# cs.CV [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Everything at Every Scale: Scale-Invariant Diffusion with Continuous Super-Resolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26032)
*Zixin Jessie Chen,Zhuo Chen,Archer Wang,Jeff Gore,William T. Freeman,Congyue Deng,Marin Soljačić*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出SKILD，一个尺度不变的K空间图像学习扩散模型（Scale-invariant K-Space Image Learning Diffusion model），通过将尺度作为扩散过程的显式坐标，在单一无条件框架下统一了图像生成与连续超分辨率任务。该方法无需任务专用架构、条件分支、无分类器引导或按尺度重训练，在CIFAR-10无条件生成和ImageNet超分辨率上均取得优异表现，并能重建临界伊辛模型（Ising model）的相关函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 图像生成（generation from noise）与超分辨率（super-resolution from coarse inputs）虽然在应用上不同，但本质上均可理解为跨尺度信息恢复。作者旨在利用自然图像与物理系统共有的尺度不变性（scale invariance），设计一个统一方法同时处理这两类任务。

Method: SKILD的前向过程（forward process）按从精细到粗糙的尺度衰减图像内容，同时注入谱匹配的高斯噪声（spectrum-matched Gaussian noise），将尺度（scale）作为扩散动力学（diffusion dynamics）的显式坐标。训练完成后，仅通过改变起始时间步（starting timestep），同一个反向过程（reverse process）即可同时执行生成和连续超分辨率，无需任务专用架构、条件分支、无分类器引导（classifier-free guidance）或按尺度重训练。

Result: 在无条件CIFAR-10上，SKILD达到FID 2.65和Inception Score 9.63；在ImageNet上，仅用单个无条件检查点即可执行2倍至8倍超分辨率，并在感知指标上超越条件模型；此外，该方法能重建临界伊辛模型，其连通四点相关函数（connected four-point correlations）与真实值高度吻合。

Conclusion: SKILD通过将尺度纳入扩散过程，成功在一个统一的无条件框架中同时实现了图像生成与连续超分辨率，且在自然图像与物理系统两类任务上均验证了有效性。

Abstract: Creating images from noise is image generation; reconstructing fine details from coarse inputs is super-resolution. Despite their practical differences, both can be understood as reversing information loss across scales. We introduce $\textbf{SKILD}$, a $\textbf{S}$cale-invariant $\textbf{K}$-Space $\textbf{I}$mage $\textbf{L}$earning $\textbf{D}$iffusion model that unifies generation and continuous super-resolution within a single unconditional framework. Both natural images and critical physical systems exhibit scale invariance, and we leverage it to design a forward process that attenuates image content from fine to coarse scales while injecting spectrum-matched Gaussian noise, making scale an explicit coordinate of the diffusion dynamics. The same trained reverse process performs generation and continuous super-resolution by varying only the starting timestep: $\textit{no task-specific architecture, no conditioning branch, no classifier-free guidance, no retraining per scale factor}$. Empirically, SKILD reaches FID $2.65$ and Inception Score $9.63$ on unconditional CIFAR-10, performs $2\times$--$8\times$ super-resolution on ImageNet from a single unconditional checkpoint while outperforming conditional models across perceptual metrics, and reconstructs critical Ising models whose connected four-point correlations closely track the ground truth.

</details>

# cond-mat.supr-con [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [A helical Rashba--exchange gauge field drives a uniaxial pair density wave in EuRbFe$_4$As$_4$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24362)
*Pengfei Li,Yi Zhou*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过理论分析，展示了在铁基超导体 EuRbFe₄As₄ 中，由 Rashba 自旋轨道耦合（Rashba spin-orbit coupling）与螺旋交换场（helical exchange field）的相互作用会生成一个层旋转的有效 U(1) 规范场（effective U(1) gauge field），该规范场与 Fe 3d_{xz}/3d_{yz} 轨道的对称性一致，从而诱导出轨道选择性配对态（orbital-selective pairing state），并自然稳定了单轴（unidirectional）的配对密度波（PDW）态，该态伴随有层间的自发环流（spontaneous loop currents），可作为未来实验的独特探测信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期在铁基超导体 EuRbFe₄As₄ 中发现了内禀的配对密度波（pair density wave, PDW），这一现象缺乏微观机制解释，构成了一个引人注目的谜题。本文旨在从理论上阐明该 PDW 态的形成机制及其物理起源。

Method: 采用唯象的金兹堡-朗道理论（Ginzburg-Landau theory），分析了诱导 Rashba 自旋轨道耦合与 Eu²⁺ 螺旋磁序的交换场之间的耦合效应，推导出对于库珀对（Cooper pairs）而言表现为层旋转的有效 U(1) 规范场，并基于该对称性机制构建轨道选择性配对模型。

Result: 该机制自然稳定了一个结构调制的布洛赫超导态（Bloch superconducting state），其特征为严格的单轴 PDW，这与近期扫描隧道显微镜（scanning tunneling microscopy, STM）实验的现象学描述一致。此外，理论预测该 PDW 态伴随有层间的自发环流。

Conclusion: 该工作为 EuRbFe₄As₄ 中的内禀 PDW 提供了清晰的对称性解释和微观机制，为理解铁基超导体中的非常规配对态提供了新视角。预测的层间自发环流可作为未来通过 μSR 或扫描 SQUID 实验进行验证的独特特征信号。

Abstract: The recent discovery of an intrinsic pair density wave (PDW) in the iron-pnictide superconductor EuRbFe$_4$As$_4$ presents a fascinating puzzle. Structurally, the FeAs layers break local inversion symmetry, while the Eu$^{2+}$ spins exhibit a period-four helical magnetic order. Here, we demonstrate that the interplay of induced Rashba spin-orbit coupling and the helical exchange field generates a layer-rotating effective $U(1)$ gauge field for the Cooper pairs. Because this gauge field shares the symmetry of the Fe $3d_{xz}/3d_{yz}$ orbitals, it explicitly induces an intertwined, orbital-selective pairing state. Using a phenomenological Ginzburg-Landau theory, we show this mechanism naturally stabilizes a structurally modulated Bloch superconducting state. This state features a strictly uniaxial (unidirectional) PDW, naturally capturing the phenomenology of recent scanning tunneling microscopy experiments. Furthermore, we predict this PDW is accompanied by spontaneous loop currents between adjacent layers, offering a distinctive signature for future $μ$SR or scanning SQUID experiments.

</details>


### [3] [Emergence of Triplet Superconductivity from Cavity Vacuum Fluctuations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24439)
*Xin-Xin Yang,Shuai Zhang,Kun Ding,Xiaopeng Li*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文证明，仅凭腔真空涨落（cavity vacuum fluctuations）即可驱动原本表现为单态超导体（singlet superconductor）的材料中出现三重态超导电性（triplet superconductivity）。真空场以极化依赖的方式重整化电子能带结构，重塑费米面（Fermi surface），改变对称性允许的配对通道之间的竞争，从而在超过临界光-物质耦合强度时引发从单态到三重态配对的对称性转变，产生母体材料中不存在的超导态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索利用腔场（cavity fields）工程化量子材料中的新奇物相，特别是验证仅凭真空真空涨落是否足以诱导非常规超导序，从而拓展腔真空工程（cavity vacuum engineering）在量子材料调控中的潜力。

Method: 通过理论分析，研究腔真空涨落对电子能带结构的重整化效应（renormalization effect），分析极化依赖的费米面重构以及由此导致的对称性允许配对通道之间竞争关系的改变，并计算不同光-物质耦合强度下的超导不稳定性（superconducting instability）。

Result: 超过临界光-物质耦合强度后，系统的主导不稳定性从单态配对（singlet pairing）转变为三重态配对（triplet pairing），产生母体材料中不存在的超导态；该真空诱导的对称性转变显著改变能隙结构（gap structure）和低能准粒子谱（low energy quasiparticle spectrum）。

Conclusion: 腔真空工程可作为产生非常规超导相和稳定三重态的一种通用机制，对拓扑超导电性（topological superconductivity）具有潜在重要意义。

Abstract: Engineering quantum materials with cavity fields has emerged as a powerful route to manipulate phases of quantum matter in solids. Here we demonstrate that cavity vacuum fluctuations alone can drive the emergence of triplet superconductivity in an otherwise singlet superconductor. The vacuum field renormalizes the electronic band structure in a polarization dependent manner, reshaping the Fermi surface and altering the competition among symmetry allowed pairing channels. As a result, multiple superconducting phases arise from the cavity vacuum fluctuations. Above a critical light matter coupling, the leading instability switches from singlet to triplet pairing, yielding a superconducting state absent in the bare material. This vacuum induced symmetry transition produces distinct modifications of the gap structure and low energy quasiparticle spectrum. Our results establish cavity vacuum engineering as a mechanism for generating unconventional superconducting phases and stabilizing triplet states of potential relevance for topological superconductivity.

</details>


### [4] [Synchronization of Bloch Oscillations in array of parallel Josephson Junctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24522)
*R. Shaikhaidarov,R. Hussain,V. N. Antonov,E. Il'ichev*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文实验演示了在弱耦合约瑟夫森结（Josephson Junctions）平行阵列中，于相干量子相位滑移（coherent quantum phase slip）工作区间实现电流量子化的同步现象。在69个平行约瑟夫森结的电压-电流特性曲线上，于19.325 GHz微波激励下首次观察到426 nA的量子化电流台阶。实验表明，量子化精度不随结数增加而下降。该研究解决了实用量子电流标准对量化电流幅度的需求问题，但量化精度的进一步提升仍需后续研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子电流标准是电学单位三角（triangle of electrical units）中尚未实现计量级精度的环节（伏特与欧姆标准已基于约瑟夫森效应和量子霍尔效应建立），本文旨在通过弱耦合平行约瑟夫森结阵列中的相干量子相位滑移效应，演示满足实用量子标准电流幅度要求的同步量子化现象。

Method: 采用69个弱耦合平行约瑟夫森结组成的阵列，在相干量子相位滑移工作区间运行，并施加频率f=19.325 GHz的微波激励，测量其电压-电流特性曲线中量子化电流台阶的位置与精度。

Result: 在电压-电流特性曲线上首次观察到量子化电流台阶位于426 nA；实验显示，随着并联约瑟夫森结数量增加至69个，量子化精度并未发生退化。

Conclusion: 该演示解决了实用量子电流标准对量化电流幅度（quantized current amplitude）的基本需求问题，表明弱耦合平行约瑟夫森结阵列有望作为量子电流标准的基础；但量化精度仍需进一步研究，以最终实现电学单位三角中可接受的计量级精度量子电流标准。

Abstract: We demonstrate the synchronization of current quantization in a parallel array of weakly coupled Josephson Junctions operating in the regime of the coherent quantum phase slip. The first quantized current step on the voltage-current characteristic of 69 parallel Josephson junctions, under microwave excitation at a frequency of f = 19.325 GHz, is observed at 426 nA. Experiments show that accuracy of quantization does not degrade with increasing number of combined Josephson junctions. This demonstration addresses the issue of quantized current amplitude requirements adopted for a practical quantum standard, while leaving the question of accuracy for further research. At present, the quantum current standard of accepted metrological accuracy in the triangle of electrical units is under development. The other two, the Volt and Ohm standards based on the Josephson and Quantum Hall effects, respectively, are already well established in metrology.

</details>


### [5] [Nonunitary triplet superconductivity in the Z2 topological metal SrPd2As2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24536)
*Aarti,Dibyendu Samanta,Kartik Panda,Devashibhai Adroja,Daloo Ram,Zakir Hossain,Rhea Stewart,Adrian Hillier,Amitava Bhattacharyya,Samar Layek,Sudeep Kumar Ghosh,Vivek Kumar Anand*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过μ子自旋旋转与弛豫（muSR）、第一性原理计算和金兹堡-朗道（Ginzburg-Landau）分析，研究了Z₂拓扑金属SrPd₂As₂的超导基态。实验发现其具有全能隙超导态且伴随时间反演对称性（TRS）破缺，理论计算表明自旋-轨道耦合（SOC）、四方对称性与开放费米面拓扑共同稳定了一种非幺正三重态超导态，该态在动量空间中无电子态的区域存在对称性要求的节点，从而同时解释全能隙热力学响应与TRS破缺。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在Z₂拓扑金属中，非平庸的能带拓扑与强自旋-轨道耦合（SOC）会对超导态施加对称性约束，可能稳定非常规超导态，即使热力学探测表明其具有各向同性能隙。作者旨在解决SrPd₂As₂中超导基态的表观矛盾——热力学显示全能隙，但常规电声耦合机制预测节线能隙并高估超导转变温度Tc。

Method: 采用横场μ子自旋旋转（transverse-field muSR）探测超导能隙结构，零场μ子自旋弛豫（zero-field muSR）检测时间反演对称性（TRS）破缺；结合第一性原理（first-principles）电子结构计算识别拓扑性质；使用各向异性Migdal-Eliashberg（Migdal-Eliashberg）计算评估电声耦合机制；并利用金兹堡-朗道（Ginzburg-Landau）分析阐释超导态的对称性。

Result: 横场muSR表明SrPd₂As₂在Tc = 0.94 K以下为全能隙超导态；零场muSR检测到Tc以下的自发内磁场，证实时间反演对称性（TRS）破缺。电子结构计算将其识别为Z₂拓扑金属，具有穿越费米能级的表面态。各向异性Migdal-Eliashberg计算预测节线能隙并高估Tc，表明纯电声配对机制不充分。

Conclusion: 自旋-轨道耦合（SOC）、四方对称性与开放费米面拓扑的共同作用稳定了一种非幺正三重态超导态（nonunitary triplet superconducting state），其对称性要求的节点位于动量空间中无电子态的区域，从而同时实现全能隙热力学响应与时间反演对称性（TRS）自发破缺。SrPd₂As₂被确立为体非幺正三重态配对的洁净平台和内禀拓扑超导的候选材料。

Abstract: In Z2 topological metals, nontrivial band topology and strong spin-orbit coupling (SOC) impose symmetry constraints that can stabilize unconventional superconducting states, even when thermodynamic probes indicate an isotropic gap. Here, we investigate the superconducting ground state of such a material, SrPd2As2, using muon spin rotation and relaxation (muSR), first-principles calculations, and Ginzburg-Landau analysis. Transverse-field muSR indicates a fully gapped superconducting state below Tc = 0.94 K, while zero-field muSR detects spontaneous internal magnetic fields below Tc, establishing time-reversal symmetry (TRS) breaking. Electronic structure calculations identify SrPd2As2 as a Z2 topological metal with surface states crossing the Fermi level. Standard anisotropic Migdal-Eliashberg calculations predict a nodal gap and overestimate Tc, indicating that a purely phonon-mediated pairing mechanism is insufficient. We resolve this apparent contradiction by showing that the interplay of SOC, tetragonal symmetry, and an open Fermi surface topology stabilizes a nonunitary triplet superconducting state whose symmetry-imposed nodes lie in momentum-space regions devoid of electronic states. This yields a fully gapped thermodynamic response while naturally breaking TRS. Our results establish SrPd2As2 as a clean platform for bulk nonunitary triplet pairing and a promising candidate for intrinsic topological superconductivity.

</details>


### [6] [Theoretical study of superconductivity in freestanding infinite-layer nickelate membranes under pressure: mitigation of excess correlation enhances $T_c$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24565)
*Mahiru Seki,Reo Kono,Naotaka Tanaka,Kensei Ushio,Daiki Nakaoka,Masayuki Ochi,Kazuhiko Kuroki,Hirofumi Sakakibara*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 基于第一性原理构建七轨道有效模型，结合涨落交换（FLEX）近似和声子计算，揭示了无限层镍酸盐Nd0.85Sr0.15NiO2在压力下超导转变温度（Tc）单调升高的微观机制，归因于压力缓解了Ni原子极低价态引起的过强电子关联，并验证了晶体结构的动力学稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解无限层镍酸盐在压力下超导转变温度（Tc）单调升高的微观机制，并验证晶体结构在压力下的动力学稳定性。

Method: 基于第一性原理（first-principles calculations）构建七轨道有效模型（seven-orbital effective model），采用涨落交换近似（fluctuation exchange approximation, FLEX）分析超导性质，并通过声子计算（phonon calculation）检验结构的动力学稳定性。

Result: 七轨道模型成功解释了实验中观测到的Tc随压力的单调升高；超导电性的增强归因于压力缓解了Ni原子极低价态导致的过强电子关联；声子计算证实了压力下晶体结构的动力学稳定性。

Conclusion: 压力通过削弱过强的电子关联，是提升无限层镍酸盐超导转变温度的关键因素，且晶体结构在压力下保持动力学稳定。

Abstract: We theoretically investigate a freestanding membrane of infinite-layer nickelate Nd$_{0.85}$Sr$_{0.15}$NiO$_2$ under pressure by constructing a seven-orbital effective model based on first-principles calculations.
  By performing the fluctuation exchange (FLEX) approximation, we demonstrate that the seven-orbital model explains a monotonic increase in $T_c$ reported in a recent experiment. This enhancement of superconductivity is attributed to the mitigation of excessively strong electron correlations caused by exceptionally low valence of Ni atom. Furthermore, we examine the dynamical stability of the crystal structure under pressure through phonon calculation.

</details>


### [7] [Prediction of 1:1 kagome metals with superconductivity and band topology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24822)
*Na Jiao,Shu-Xiang Qiao,Pan Zhou,Hong-Yan Lu,Ping Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 通过第一性原理计算，本文预测了一类新型1:1 Kagome MSn（M=过渡金属）材料，其中五种非磁性候选物（M=Mo, Hf, Nb, Ta, W）展现出声子介导的超导性（phonon-mediated superconductivity），且MoSn、HfSn和NbSn在费米能级（Fermi level）处具有非平庸拓扑能带结构（nontrivial topological band structure），从而建立了超导与拓扑序共存的平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Kagome超导体因其拓扑非平庸能带结构而备受关注，但现有FeSn和CoSn等Kagome材料虽具有内禀磁性（intrinsic magnetism），却抑制了超导性的出现。因此，寻找兼具本征超导性和拓扑特性的Kagome材料成为研究驱动力。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）对27种候选MSn（M=过渡金属）进行筛选，评估其动力学稳定性（dynamical stability）与热力学稳定性（thermodynamical stability），并进一步分析其中非磁性体系的超导性与拓扑性质。

Result: 在27种候选物中，M=Mo、Hf、Nb、Ta、W、Ti被识别为动力学和热力学稳定体系；其中五种非磁性MSn（M=Mo、Hf、Nb、Ta、W）表现出声子介导的超导性。d轨道能带在费米能级附近出现狄拉克点（Dirac points）和范霍夫奇点（van Hove singularities），促进了拓扑结构和电子-声子耦合（electron-phonon coupling, EPC）的形成。MoSn、HfSn和NbSn在费米能级处呈现非平庸拓扑能带结构。

Conclusion: 所预测的MSn材料为超导性与拓扑序共存的集成平台（platform integrating superconductivity and topological order），为后续的实验合成和功能探索提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Kagome superconductors featuring topologically nontrivial band structures have attracted extensive research interest. FeSn and CoSn is a new kind of kagome material with intrinsic magnetism, which suppresses the emergence of superconductivity. Here, we theoretically predict a new kind of 1:1 kagome MSn (M=transition metal), which exhibit intrinsic superconductivity and nontrivial band topology by first-principles calculations. Among twenty-seven candidates, MSn (M= Mo, Hf, Nb, Ta, W, Ti) are theoretically identified as both dynamically and thermodynamical stable. And, five non-magnetic MSn (M= Mo, Hf, Nb, Ta, W) exhibit phonon-mediated superconductivity. Especially, the d orbitals bands display Dirac points and van Hove singularities near the Fermi level, which contribute to the emergence of topology and the electron-phonon coupling (EPC). More interestingly, MoSn, HfSn and NbSn show nontrivial topological band structure at the Fermi level. Thus, the predicted MSn establish a platform integrating superconductivity and topological order.

</details>


### [8] [Superconductivity in Al-based high-entropy alloys TiHfNbTaAl and TaNbHfZrAl](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25048)
*Junjin Huang,Wenbo Sun,Longfu Li,Shuangyue Wang,Jingjun Qin,Rui Chen,Zaichen Xiang,Yucheng Li,Lingyong Zeng,Huixia Luo*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文报道了TaNbHfZrAl和TiHfNbTaAl两种高熵合金（HEA）超导体的超导性质与晶体结构。两种合金的价电子浓度（VEC）均为4.2，具有体心立方（BCC）结构。电阻率、磁化率和比热测量表明，两者均为体第二类超导体，临界温度Tc分别为5.5 K和3.2 K。研究发现，VEC和元素组成影响Tc，而Al的引入使高度无序的HEA超导体呈现出更类似晶体的Tc依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自2014年首次报道高熵合金（high entropy alloy, HEA）超导体以来，HEA因其显著的内部无序程度，成为研究介于晶体与非晶结构之间材料性质的理想模型。本文旨在探究TaNbHfZrAl和TiHfNbTaAl两种HEA的超导性质与晶体结构。

Method: 通过电阻率（resistivity）、磁化率（magnetic）和比热（specific heat）测量，对两种HEA样品进行了超导性质的实验表征。

Result: 两种合金均具有体心立方（body centered cubic, BCC）结构和价电子浓度（valence electron concentration, VEC）4.2。TaNbHfZrAl的临界温度Tc为5.5 K，TiHfNbTaAl的Tc为3.2 K，两者均为体第二类超导体（bulk type-II superconductor）。Tc受VEC和元素组成影响，且Al的引入使高无序HEA超导体呈现出更类似晶体的Tc依赖性。

Conclusion: TaNbHfZrAl和TiHfNbTaAl均为体第二类超导体，其超导转变温度受价电子浓度和元素组成调控，且Al的掺杂效应可增强Tc随组分变化的晶体样行为。

Abstract: Since the first report of a high entropy alloy (HEA) superconductor in 2014, HEAs have continued to captivate the interest of superconducting researchers. Owing to the significant degree of disorder inherent in these systems, they serve as exemplary models for examining the properties of materials that exist in states intermediate between crystalline and amorphous structures. Here we present the superconductivity properties and crystal structure of TaNbHfZrAl and TiHfNbTaAl HEAs, which both have the VEC of 4.2 and body centered cubic (BCC) structure. Through resistivity, magnetic, and specific heat measurements, we prove that both samples are the bulk type-II superconductors with a critical temperature Tc of 5.5 K for TaNbHfZrAl and Tc of 3.2 K for TiHfNbTaAl. The Tc of HEA superconductors is influenced by the VEC and the element composition. And the incorporation of Al in high disorder HEA superconductors causes a more crystallinelike Tc dependence.

### [9] [Light-Driven Intrinsic Perfect Superconducting Diode Effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25197)
*Makoto Ichikawa,Youichi Yanase*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过光驱动非平衡系统实现了完美的超导二极管效应（superconducting diode effect, SDE），即100%二极管效率的单向超流。单色光可在缺乏反演和时间反演对称性的系统中诱导完美SDE；多频光甚至能在中心对称系统中通过动力学对称性破缺（dynamical symmetry breaking）实现完美SDE。结果确立了基于非平衡调控与对称性工程实现单向超导输运的一般性原理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在平衡态系统中难以实现100%效率的完美超导二极管效应（SDE），该研究旨在利用光驱动的非平衡系统来克服这一限制，探索实现单向超流（unidirectional supercurrent）的新途径。

Method: 采用单色光（monochromatic light）驱动缺乏反演对称性（inversion symmetry）和时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry）的系统；进一步使用多频光（multi-frequency light）在中心对称系统（centrosymmetric systems）中通过动力学对称性破缺实现完美SDE。

Result: 单色光可在非中心对称且时间反演破缺的系统中诱导完美SDE；多频光则在中心对称系统中实现完美SDE，表明动力学对称性破缺可替代静态对称性破缺。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了基于非平衡调控（nonequilibrium control）与对称性工程（symmetry engineering）实现完美超导二极管效应的一般性原理，为设计高性能超导二极管器件提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We demonstrate the perfect superconducting diode effect (SDE) -- unidirectional supercurrent with 100% diode efficiency -- in light-driven nonequilibrium systems. Although the perfect SDE is difficult to achieve in equilibrium, monochromatic light induces the perfect SDE in systems lacking inversion and time-reversal symmetries. More strikingly, multi-frequency light enables the perfect SDE even in centrosymmetric systems via dynamical symmetry breaking. Our results establish a general principle for realizing unidirectional superconducting transport based on nonequilibrium control and symmetry engineering.

</details>


### [10] [Nitrogen-doped W0.75Re0.25 Superconducting Nanowire Single Photon Detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25597)

Method: 采用反应式直流磁控溅射（reactive DC magnetron sputtering）在Ar/N2混合气氛中沉积超薄W0.75Re0.25薄膜，并制备成70 nm线宽的曲折型（meander）SNSPD结构。

Conclusion: 实验表明氮掺杂钨铼合金薄膜可成功制备高性能SNSPD，在红外波段（1310 nm）兼具高探测效率与快速时间响应特性，验证了该材料平台的实际可行性。

Abstract: Nitrogen-doped Tungsten-Rhenium superconducting alloys were recently proposed as a promising material platform for superconducting nanowire single-photon detectors (SNSPDs), offering a favorable balance between high normal state resistivity and tunable superconducting properties. In this work, we report on the fabrication and characterization of SNSPDs based on ultrathin W0.75Re0.25 films deposited by reactive DC magnetron sputtering in a mixed Ar/N2 atmosphere. Meander detectors with 70 nm linewidth exhibit saturated internal detection efficiency up to 1310 nm at 2.5 K, with sub-nanosecond rise times, decay times of the order of a few nanoseconds, and timing jitter of 73.2 ps measured with room temperature amplifiers.

### [11] [Superconductivity and electronic structure evolution in the enforced semimetal Fe-doped ZrTe$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25898)
*L. M. Ishikura,C. F. Schuch,A. Faé Rabello,F. F. Nogueira,L. E. Corrêa,L. R. de Faria,J. Larrea Jiménez,L. T. F. Eleno,A. J. S. Machado*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究通过实验测量与第一性原理（ab initio）计算，系统探究了Fe插层（Fe intercalation）对ZrTe₂电子结构的影响。结果表明，Fe插层可诱导超导电性（最大临界温度Tc=2.74 K，x=0.03），但并未破坏体系原有的非平庸拓扑能带结构，仅在费米能级附近移动能带交叉点，并在x=0.125时观察到范霍夫奇点（van Hove singularity），暗示超导序可能与态密度（density of states）增强及能带折叠结构特征相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ZrTe₂作为层状半金属（layered semimetal），具有非平庸拓扑电子结构，但其电子演化和超导性起源尚不明确。通过在ZrTe₂中引入Fe插层，旨在探索超导态的出现及其与拓扑电子结构之间的关系。

Method: 采用实验测量与第一性原理（ab initio）计算相结合的方法，对Fe插层化合物Fe$_x$ZrTe₂（$x=0-0.25$）的电子演化进行系统研究。

Result: 实验发现Fe插层可诱导超导电性，最大临界温度$T_c=2.74$ K（$x=0.03$）；计算表明，拓扑特征对Te原子与Zr层间距敏感；Fe插层未改变非平庸电子能带（non-trivial electronic band structure），仅使能带交叉点轻微下移至费米能级（$E_F$）以下；在$x=0.125$时观察到费米能级附近的范霍夫奇点（van Hove singularity），表明超导序可能与能带折叠结构及态密度增强相关。

Conclusion: Fe插层的ZrTe₂新化合物保持强制的半金属分类（enforced semimetal classification），超导态的出现与能带结构特征及费米能级处态密度的增强密切相关。

Abstract: ZrTe$_2$ is an outstanding layered semimetal due to the topologically nontrivial electronic structure. In this work, we present an investigation of the electronic evolution of ZrTe$_2$ in the presence of Fe intercalation, namely Fe$_{x}$ZrTe$_2$ ($x= 0 - 0.25$), scrutinized by both experimental measurements and \textit{ab} initio calculations. While the first reveals a superconducting state with a maximum critical temperature $T_c = 2.74$ K ($x=$ 0.03), the latter indicates that the topological features of the pristine ZrTe$_2$ is sensitive to the distance between Te atoms and Zr layers. Also, the intercalation of Fe does not modify the non-trivial electronic band structure unlike the band crossings are now shifted slightly below $E_{F}$. In particular, a van Hove singularity near the Fermi level for a Fe content of $x=0.125$ is observed in the density of states, indicating that the superconducting order may be associated with features of the unfolded band structure and the concomitant enhancement of the density of states at $E_F$. Finally, our results reveal that the new compound with inclusion of Fe intercalation preserves the enforced semimetal classification.

### [12] [Substitution modulated transition from semimetal to superconductor in ZrTe$_{2-x}$Se$_x$ with coexistence of nontrivial electronic topology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25906)
*V. M. Fim,C. F. Schuch,L. R. de Faria,F. A. Santos,M. S. da Luz,S. S. Tsirkin,L. T. F. Eleno,A. J. S. Machado*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究通过等温化学气相传输（ICVT）技术生长高质量ZrTe$_{2-x}$Se$_x$晶体，发现硒（Se）替代碲（Te）可诱导超导态（superconducting state），并绘制了从电荷密度波（CDW）到狄拉克半金属与超导共存态、再到半导体相的完整相图。其中ZrTe$_{1.85}$Se$_{0.15}$因具有非平凡$\mathbb Z_2$拓扑不变量及非零表面态，被视为拓扑超导（topological superconductivity）的候选平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: Se替代Te可在低硒含量下同时改变电子贡献和晶格振动模式（vibrational modes）；超导临界温度（$T_c$）在$x=0.15$时达到最大值4.8 K；建立了从电荷密度波（CDW）到狄拉克半金属与超导共存态、再到半导体相的完整相图。

Conclusion: ZrTe$_{1.85}$Se$_{0.15}$体系呈现狄拉克半金属与超导共存，并具有非平凡$\mathbb Z_2$拓扑不变量及非零(001)面表面态，是拓扑超导（topological superconductivity）的候选平台。

Abstract: This study explores the emergence of superconductivity in high-quality ZrTe$_{2-x}$Se$_x$ crystals, grown via the isothermal chemical vapor transport (ICVT) technique. Resistive, structural, and thermal measurements reveal that substituting Te with Se in the ZrTe$_2$ matrix induces a superconducting state at low temperatures. The critical temperature ($T_c$) exhibits a clear dependence on the selenium concentration, peaking at $x=0.15$ with a $T_c$ of $4.8$ K. Calorimetric data indicates that even a low Se substitution range is capable of modifying both the electronic contribution and the vibrational modes of the crystal lattice. Combined with ab initio calculations and Wannier Hamiltonian interpolation between ZrTe$_2$/ZrSe$_2$, we established an extensive phase diagram mapping the transition from charge density wave (CDW) to the state with coexistence between the Dirac semimetal and superconductivity (SC), up to the semiconductor phase. This coexistence suggests that ZrTe$_{1.85}$Se$_{0.15}$ could be a candidate platform for topological superconductivity, as it hosts a nontrivial $\mathbb Z_2$ invariant, with nonvanishing surface states in its $(001)$ planes.

### [13] [Exact Single-Scale Outer Solution of the Abrikosov Vortex in the Extreme Type-II Limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25938)
*Eugene B. Kolomeisky*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究精确确定了极端第二类极限（extreme type-II limit）下Abrikosov涡旋（Abrikosov vortex）的外部结构，当Ginzburg-Landau参数κ发散时，涡核外部区域简化为一个关于超流体速度（superfluid velocity）的封闭非线性理论，受代数密度约束。结果证明在κ≫1极限下，磁场和超导密度均以London穿透深度（London penetration depth）为特征长度变化，推翻了传统的双长度尺度图像。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管已知在极端第二类极限下Ginzburg-Landau理论会在核心收缩区域之外简化，但Abrikosov涡旋在该极限下的精确外部结构尚未被严格确定。传统观点认为涡旋存在两个不同的长度尺度（相干长度与穿透深度），该研究旨在检验此图像在κ→∞极限下是否仍然成立。

Method: 作者在Ginzburg-Landau参数κ发散（κ→∞）的极端第二类极限下，对Ginzburg-Landau理论进行分析。涡核（vortex core）缩小至零后，涡核外部区域满足一个带代数密度约束的、关于超流体速度的封闭非线性方程，据此求解得到渐近精确的外部分布。

Result: 求解结果表明，在极端第二类极限下，涡核外部的磁场（magnetic field）和超导密度（superconducting density）均以London穿透深度为唯一特征长度变化。该结果严格证明了传统认知中涡旋同时具有相干长度和穿透深度两个独立尺度的图像在κ≫1时并不成立。

Conclusion: 该工作澄清了极端第二类极限下Abrikosov涡旋的外部结构，指出磁场和超导密度在涡核外共用London穿透深度这一单一长度尺度，修正了关于第二类超导体涡旋尺度分离的传统理解。

Abstract: We determine the exact outer structure of the Abrikosov vortex in the extreme type-II limit, which occurs when the Ginzburg-Landau parameter $κ$ diverges. In this limit, Ginzburg-Landau theory simplifies, outside a shrinking core, to a closed nonlinear theory for the superfluid velocity subject to an algebraic density constraint. The resulting solution is asymptotically exact everywhere outside the vanishing vortex core, demonstrating that both magnetic field and superconducting density vary on the length scale of the London penetration depth. This establishes that the conventional two-length-scale picture of the vortex does not hold in the $κ\gg 1$ limit.

</details>

### [14] [Sensing Intelligence as a Trainable Metamaterial Property](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23967)
*Kyungmi Na,Yifei Li,Xinyi Yang,Bolei Deng*

Main category: q-bio.NC

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种将传感智能（sensing intelligence）直接赋予机械本体（body）的方法，通过可微仿真（differentiable simulation）让神经网络反向传播传感损失（sensing loss）以优化超材料（metamaterial）的几何结构，从而将外部刺激重塑为更易被神经网络解释的内部信号。在数值与实验传感场景中，该方法将传感精度提升最多五倍，或将所需电子传感器数量减少近一个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统生物系统依赖本体（而非仅大脑）对刺激进行机械预处理，而工程系统的传感负担几乎全部由电子与计算承担，机械结构仅用于提供强度与稳定性。作者希望使机械本体本身具备可训练的传感智能，以减轻后续电子传感与计算的压力。

Method: 通过可微仿真（differentiable simulation），将神经网络（neural network）的传感损失（sensing loss）反向传播（backpropagate）至超材料（metamaterial）的几何设计参数，从而自动优化本体结构，使其将外部刺激重塑为便于神经网络解析的内部信号。

Result: 在数值模拟与实验传感场景中，优化后的本体使传感精度最高提升五倍，或将所需电子传感器数量减少近一个数量级（nearly an order of magnitude）。

Conclusion: 机械本体的几何结构可作为可训练属性，通过可微优化实现传感智能（sensing intelligence），在无需人工设计物理预处理的前提下显著提升传感性能或降低电子传感器依赖。

Abstract: In biological systems, sensing is not performed by the brain alone: the body deforms, vibrates, and filters external stimuli before they are transduced into neural signals. In engineered systems, this processing burden is placed largely on electronics and computation, while the mechanical body is usually designed only for strength and stability. Here, we present sensing intelligence as a trainable property of the body. We show that the geometry of a metamaterial can be optimized to reshape external stimuli into internal signals that are easier for a neural network to interpret. Rather than hand-designing this physical preprocessing, we let the neural network train its own body for sensing by backpropagating the sensing loss to the body's design parameters through differentiable simulation. Across numerical and experimental sensing scenarios, the optimized body improves sensing accuracy by up to fivefold or reduces the number of required electronic sensors by nearly an order of magnitude.

</details>


### [15] [Balancing structure and randomness: maximum entropy networks for context-dependent computations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25607)
*Ludwig Hruza,Srdjan Ostojic*

Main category: q-bio.NC

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于最大熵原理（maximum entropy principle）的规范性方法，在无需依赖特定学习算法的情况下，通过将任务需求表示为对连接权重的约束，预测神经网络连接结构。该方法在双层前馈网络的上下文相关输入选择任务中解析求解，所得的最大熵连接结构与梯度下降（gradient descent）训练的网络在定性和定量上均高度匹配，揭示了任务约束与熵最大化之间的相互作用是理解神经网络结构与功能关系的基本原理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解网络功能如何约束神经连接是神经科学中的一个核心挑战。现有方法通过梯度下降训练神经网络并分析其连接结构，但所得结构依赖于训练过程的细节，缺乏独立于特定学习算法的通用框架。

Method: 本文将连接性描述为单神经元权重的概率分布，将任务需求表达为对该分布的约束，并在满足这些约束的条件下最大化香农熵（Shannon entropy），从而确定唯一的分布。一个权重尺度参数控制随机性与任务诱导结构之间的平衡。通过将非线性网络映射为增益调制线性模型（gain-modulated linear models），使得最大熵推理在两层前馈网络（2-layer feed-forward networks）的上下文相关输入选择任务中可解析求解。

Result: 从先验均匀分布出发，最大熵方法在任务约束下涌现出由上下文增益调制（contextual gain modulation）模式定义的神经元群体。增加上下文数量会驱动从上下文特化群体（context-specialized populations）向非特化随机群体的转变；增加权重尺度则驱动从结构化向随机刺激选择性（stimulus selectivity）的平行转变。该最大熵连接结构与不同学习机制下的梯度下降训练网络在定性和定量上均高度一致。

Conclusion: 任务约束与熵最大化之间的相互作用为理解神经网络中结构与功能的关系提供了基本原理。

Abstract: Understanding how network function constrains neural connectivity is a central challenge in neuroscience. An influential approach is to train neural networks with gradient descent on cognitive tasks and characterize the resulting connectivity. A key limitation is that the resulting structure depends on the details of the training procedure. Here we propose a complementary normative approach based on the maximum entropy principle for network connectivity, independent of any particular learning algorithm. We describe connectivity as a probability distribution over single-neuron weights, express task requirements as constraints on this distribution, and determine the unique distribution maximizing Shannon entropy subject to these constraints. A weight scale parameter controls the balance between randomness and task-induced structure. We apply this framework to context-dependent input-selection tasks in 2-layer feed-forward networks, and show that maximum entropy inference becomes analytically tractable by mapping nonlinear networks onto gain-modulated linear models. Starting from an a priori homogeneous distribution, we find that maximizing entropy under task constraints leads to the emergence of populations of neurons, each defined by its pattern of contextual gain modulation. Increasing the number of contexts drives a transition from context-specialized to unspecialized, random populations. Increasing the weight scale drives a parallel transition from structured to random stimulus selectivity. Strikingly, this maximum entropy connectivity matches both qualitatively and quantitatively the structure of networks trained with gradient descent across different learning regimes. Our results suggest that the interplay between task constraints and entropy maximization provides a fundamental principle for understanding the relationship between structure and function in neural networks.

</details>

### [16] [Oscillating Imprints of Dark Matter in Mesons Decays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24090)
*Prisco Lo Chiatto,Babette Döbrich,Gilad Perez*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了超轻暗物质（ULDM）引起CKM矩阵元素振荡的两种理论框架（Nelson-Barr机制与Froggatt-Nielsen味模型），并在NA62等味工厂实验中提出了基于事件直接计数的替代观测量，以规避通量不确定度对寿命观测量灵敏度的退化，从而将味实验发展为探测ULDM时间依赖信号的新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索超轻暗物质（ultralight dark matter, ULDM）作为CKM矩阵元素振荡的物理来源，并通过味实验（flavor experiments）的时间依赖信号来间接探测ULDM，弥补传统直接探测方法的不足。

Method: 提出了两种理论框架：一是基于Nelson-Barr机制（Nelson–Barr mechanism）解决强CP问题，并将CKM相位视为伪Nambu-Goldstone玻色子（pseudo-Nambu–Goldstone boson）；二是受Froggatt-Nielsen味模型（Froggatt–Nielsen flavor models）启发，利用ULDM与标准模型的二次耦合而自然压低线性耦合。在实验方面，以NA62实验为主要候选，分析介子衰变中的振荡信号，并对比了基于寿命的观测量与基于事件直接计数的观测量。

Result: 当总粒子通量无法精确已知时，基于寿命的观测量（lifetime-based observables）的灵敏度会参量退化，显著低于朴素估计。而基于事件直接计数的观测量保留了预期的$1/\sqrt{N}$标度，提供了对振荡CKM元素的稳健探针。

Conclusion: 味实验可通过时间依赖信号（time-dependent signatures）作为ULDM的新型探测手段，其中基于事件直接计数的观测量比基于寿命的观测量更具鲁棒性。

Abstract: We study scenarios in which ultralight dark matter (ULDM) causes oscillations of the Cabibbo--Kobayashi--Maskawa (CKM) matrix elements, considering two frameworks. The first, previously proposed in the literature, employs the Nelson--Barr mechanism to solve the strong CP problem and the CKM phase is identified with a pseudo-Nambu--Goldstone boson. The second, inspired by Froggatt--Nielsen flavor models, relies on quadratic couplings of the ULDM to the Standard Model while naturally suppressing linear couplings. On the experimental side, we outline a strategy to search for such oscillations at flavor factories using meson decays, focusing on the NA62 experiment as the most promising candidate for discovery thanks to its large kaon statistics. We show that the sensitivity of lifetime-based observables is parametrically degraded when the total particle flux is not known exactly, leading to a substantial loss of sensitivity compared to naive estimates. We therefore advocate alternative observables based on direct counting of events, which retain the expected $1/\sqrt{N}$ scaling and provide a robust probe of oscillating CKM elements. Our results highlight flavor experiments as a novel probe of ULDM through time-dependent signatures.

</details>


### [17] [Associated $ZH$ production in gluon fusion process at NLO+NLL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24131)
*Pulak Banerjee,Chinmoy Dey,Niraj Koirala,M. C. Kumar,Vaibhav Pandey*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在QCD框架下通过胶子融合过程精确计算了伴随ZH产生的不变质量分布和总截面，将阈值对数求和推进到次次领头对数（NLL）精度，并与包含完整顶夸克质量依赖的次领头阶（NLO）结果匹配。在LHC 13.6 TeV能量下，NLO+NLL截面相比纯NLO提高约20%；微分分布在3000 GeV处标度不确定性从NLO的~20%降至重求和后的~12%。进一步结合Drell-Yan型过程的N³LL结果，给出了强子对撞中最精确的结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精确计算胶子融合过程（gluon fusion）中的伴随ZH产生是检验标准模型和探索新物理的重要途径。由于阈值效应和大对数项的存在，纯微扰论NLO计算在相空间边缘存在较大不确定性，需要重求和（resummation）技术来改进收敛性和精度。

Method: 采用阈值重求和（threshold resummation）方法，将阈值对数项提升至NLL精度；将重求和结果与包含完整顶夸克（top quark）质量依赖的精确NLO虚拟振幅结果进行匹配。同时将所得结果与Drell-Yan型过程的N³LL精确结果进行合并。

Result: 在LHC 13.6 TeV条件下，NLO+NLL总截面相比纯NLO增加约20%。对于微分分布，在3000 GeV处，NLO的标度不确定性约20%，而重求和后的NLO+NLL结果降至约12%，显著降低了理论误差。

Conclusion: 结合了NLL胶子融合重求和与N³LL Drell-Yan过程的结果，在强子对撞（hadron collisions）中给出了当前最精确的ZH产生截面预测，为LHC实验数据分析提供了有力理论支持。

Abstract: We present precise results for invariant mass distributions and inclusive cross-sections, of associated $ZH$ production through gluon fusion in QCD. We include threshold logarithms at next-to-leading-logarithmic (NLL) accuracy and match the results to full next-to-leading-order (NLO) results with exact top-quark mass dependence in the virtual amplitudes. At 13.6 TeV energy at LHC, the NLO+NLL cross-section increases the NLO counterpart by about $20\%$. For differential distributions, at 3000 GeV, the uncertainties arising out of the unphysical renormalization and factorization scales is about $20\%$ for NLO; whereas for the resummed results it is around $12\%$. We also combine these results to the Drell-Yan type results at N$^3$LL and present the most precise results in hadron collisions.

### [18] [Low-lying $Λ$ and $Σ$ resonances studied with the forward $K^*$ productions off the proton induced by high-momentum $π$ beam](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24412)
*H. Kamano,T. -S. H. Lee*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出利用前向K*产生反应（πN → K* MB）作为研究K̅N阈值附近及以下低能Y*共振态的补充手段，建立了基于单介子交换机制和ANL-Osaka动力学耦合道（DCC）模型的框架，预测了微分截面和角分布等可观测量，发现亚阈值区域信号显著增强，且重叠共振态（如潜在的新3/2+ Σ态与已知Σ(1385)3/2+）可在πΛ质谱中形成单一峰，角分布可通过分波干涉效应区分这些重叠态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的K⁻ p散射实验难以直接探测K̅N阈值附近及以下的低能Y*共振区域，因此需要发展新的互补性方法。本文旨在利用高动量π束流诱导的前向K*产生反应来研究这一难以触及的动力学区域。

Method: 构建了基于单介子交换机制（one-meson exchange mechanism）的模型，该机制在高能前向产生反应中占主导地位。散射振幅取自ANL-Osaka动力学耦合道（dynamical coupled-channels, DCC）模型（Model A和Model B）的半离壳（half-off-shell）形式。

Result: 预测的不变质量谱在亚阈值区域表现出显著增强。潜在的3/2+ Σ新态与已知的Σ(1385)3/2+可在πΛ质量谱中叠加形成单一峰。角分布通过分波干涉（partial-wave interference）效应可有效区分重叠共振态，t'和φM*依赖性对高能产生机制提供关键约束。

Conclusion: 该反应提供了一种有价值的Y*谱学互补方法，不能仅凭现有质谱数据排除尚未确认的亚阈值态的存在。预测的高灵敏度可观测量可在J-PARC等现代强子设施中通过高统计量实验加以检验，有助于揭示S=−1的Y*质量谱。

Abstract: We develop a novel model utilizing the forward $K^*$ production reaction off the nucleon, $πN \to K^* MB$, induced by a high-momentum $π$ beam, as a tool to study low-lying $Y^*$ resonances below and just above the $\bar{K}N$ threshold. Because conventional $K^- p$ scattering experiments face difficulties in directly accessing this kinematic region, the proposed reaction offers a valuable complementary approach for $Y^*$ spectroscopy. The constructed model is based on the one-meson exchange mechanism, which is known to dominate forward-angle production at high energies, and the half-off-shell scattering amplitudes from the ANL-Osaka dynamical coupled-channels (DCC) models (Model~A and Model~B). We predict various observables, including differential cross sections and angular distributions. Our results demonstrate significant enhancements in the sub-threshold region of the invariant mass spectra. Notably, we show that overlapping resonances, such as a potential new $3/2^+$ $Σ$ state and the well-established $Σ(1385)3/2^+$, can constitute a single peak in the $πΛ$ mass spectrum, indicating that the existence of previously unconfirmed sub-threshold states cannot be ruled out by analyzing only the existing mass spectrum data. Furthermore, we find that angular distributions provide strong discriminatory power to disentangle such overlapping states through partial-wave interference effects, while the $t'$ and $φ_M^*$ dependencies provide crucial constraints on the high-energy production mechanisms.Our predictions for these highly sensitive observables can facilitate high-statistics measurements, which are accessible at modern hadron facilities such as J-PARC, to unravel the $S=-1$ $Y^*$ mass spectrum.

### [19] [Multipole structure of the nucleon tensor form factors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24435)
*Nam-Yong Ghim,Ho-Yeon Won,June-Young Kim,Hyun-Chul Kim*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在夸克-孤子手征模型（chiral quark-soliton model）框架下，基于$1/N_c$展开，通过引入转动$1/N_c$修正，对核子张量形状因子（nucleon tensor form factors）的多极结构进行了完整分析。数值计算给出了同位旋标量张量荷（isoscalar tensor charge）、同位旋矢量反常张量磁矩（isovector anomalous tensor magnetic moment）和同位旋标量张量四极矩（isoscalar tensor quadrupole moment），并系统研究了动量转移依赖性和价夸克与Dirac海贡献的分离。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前期的领头阶分析未能完整描述核子张量形状因子的味分解（flavor decomposition），部分味分量在领头阶为零。本文旨在通过引入转动$1/N_c$修正，填补这些缺失的味分量，从而在现有阶次下完成对张量多极形状因子的完整描述。

Method: 基于$1/N_c$展开的手征夸克-孤子模型（chiral quark-soliton model），在前期领头阶分析基础上纳入转动$1/N_c$修正（rotational $1/N_c$ corrections）。通过味分解分别计算并分离价夸克贡献（valence-quark contribution）和Dirac海贡献（Dirac-sea contribution）。

Result: 数值结果：同位旋标量张量荷$g_T^{u+d}=0.81$，同位旋矢量反常张量磁矩$\kappa_T^{u-d}=1.97$，同位旋标量张量四极矩$E_T^{u+d}(0)=5.98$。同位旋标量张量荷和四极矩主要由价夸克贡献主导，而同位旋矢量反常张量磁矩则受到显著的Dirac海贡献。所有形状因子随$-t$增大单调递减，其中同位旋矢量反常张量磁形状因子在小$|t|$区域下降尤为明显。

Conclusion: 转动$1/N_c$修正提供了领头阶缺失味分量的主导非零贡献，完成了现有阶次下张量多极形状因子的味分解。Dirac海贡献在同位旋矢量反常张量磁矩中的重要性反映了Dirac海在张量偶极结构（tensor dipole structure）中的关键作用。

Abstract: We investigate the multipole structure of the nucleon tensor form factors within the chiral quark-soliton model based on the $1/N_c$ expansion. Extending the previous leading-order analysis~\cite{Ghim:2025gqo}, we include the rotational $1/N_c$ corrections. These corrections provide the leading nonvanishing contributions to the flavor components that are absent at leading order, thereby completing the flavor decomposition of the tensor multipole form factors at the present order. We numerically evaluate the isoscalar tensor charge, the isovector anomalous tensor magnetic moment, and the isoscalar tensor quadrupole moment, obtaining $g_T^{u+d}=0.81$, $κ_T^{u-d}=1.97$, and $E_T^{u+d}(0)=5.98$, respectively. The isoscalar tensor charge and quadrupole moment are mainly governed by the valence-quark contribution, whereas the isovector anomalous tensor magnetic moment receives a sizable Dirac-sea contribution. We also examine the momentum-transfer dependence of the corresponding form factors. They decrease monotonically with increasing $-t$. In particular, the isovector anomalous tensor magnetic form factor shows a pronounced falloff in the small-$|t|$ region, reflecting the importance of the Dirac sea in the tensor dipole structure.

</details>


### [20] [Emerging Nonlocal Källèn-Lehmann Higgs Spectra at the LHC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25015)
*Stathes Paganis*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出电弱对称性破缺可能源于具有多标量相互作用的哈密顿量中的涌现非局域Källèn-Lehmann谱密度。非局域标量扇区可在当前及未来LHC运行中被探测到，通过多通道全局拟合约束非局域谱密度，为高能对撞机新物理搜索提供了范式转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决电弱对称性破缺（electroweak symmetry breaking）的起源以及与之相关的层次性问题（Hierarchy problem），即在标准模型中希格斯玻色子质量对紫外截断的极端敏感性。

Method: 通过重整化（renormalization）非局域希格斯传播子，推导非微扰散射振幅的解析表达式；利用Källèn-Lehmann谱密度（spectral density）表征非局域性，并对LHC多排他道（di-Higgs、电弱双玻色子、双光子产生）进行全局拟合（global fit）。

Result: 当能量超过非局域标度$Λ_{NL}$时，散射振幅呈指数抑制；希格斯自能实部在深类空动量区域（$p^2 \sim -Λ^2_{NL}$）被压低，为层次性问题提供了解决方案。

Conclusion: 非局域Källèn-Lehmann谱密度可通过LHC数据的全局拟合加以约束，该方案代表了高能对撞机新物理搜索的一种范式转变。

Abstract: Electroweak symmetry breaking may arise from emergent nonlocal Källèn-Lehmann spectral densities in Hamiltonians with multiscalar interactions. The nonlocality scale $Λ_{NL}$ emerges naturally from the exponentially increasing degeneracy of mass eigenstates in the Higgs two-point function at scales $p^2 \geq Λ^2_{NL}$. Following the renormalization of the nonlocal Higgs propagator, we provide a framework for deriving analytic expressions for non-perturbative scattering amplitudes. We demonstrate that for energies exceeding the nonlocality scale, scattering amplitudes are exponentially suppressed. Furthermore, the real part of the Higgs self-energy is suppressed at deep spacelike momenta ($p^2 \sim -Λ^2_{NL}$), offering a solution to the Hierarchy problem. Such nonlocal scalar sectors are accessible to current and future LHC runs. We argue that the nonlocal Källèn-Lehmann spectral density can be constrained through a simultaneous global fit of LHC measurements in exclusive channels, including di-Higgs, electroweak di-boson, and di-photon production. This approach represents a paradigm shift in the search for new physics at high-energy colliders.

</details>


### [21] [Electromagnetic form factors of the nucleon from the instanton vacuum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25900)
*Hui-Jae Lee,Yongwoo Choi,Hyun-Chul Kim*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 基于QCD瞬子真空（instanton vacuum）导出的手征有效理论，在有限流夸克质量下计算核子的电磁形状因子（electromagnetic form factors）。瞬子介质产生的动量依赖动力学夸克质量自然充当正则化器，无需额外正则化。质子电荷半径与μ子氢实验值高度吻合，形状因子比率随Q²的依赖关系被很好再现，验证了该理论框架的一致性与预言能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在QCD瞬子真空框架下，检验有效手征理论能否在无自由可调参数的情况下，统一描述核子的电磁形状因子、电荷半径、磁矩等电磁结构性质，并与实验数据及其他模型结果进行对比。

Method: 基于QCD瞬子真空导出的有效手征理论（effective chiral theory），计入有限流夸克质量效应。瞬子-反瞬子介质产生的动量依赖动力学夸克质量（momentum-dependent dynamical quark mass）自然作为正则化器，处理夸克圈发散。瞬子参数（平均大小ρ̄=0.35 fm、平均间距R̄=0.86 fm）和零虚度时动力学夸克质量（M₀=385 MeV）均由手征极限外的鞍点方程（saddle-point equation）确定，计算中无自由可调参数。

Result: 计算了质子和中子的Sachs电形状因子与磁形状因子、核子电荷半径与磁化半径、磁矩以及比率μ_p,n G_E^{p,n}(Q²)/G_M^{p,n}(Q²)。质子电荷半径√⟨r²⟩_ch^p = 0.841 fm与近期μ子氢实验值吻合极好；质子形状因子比率μ_p G_E^p/G_M^p随Q²的依赖关系被很好地再现，明显优于手征夸克-孤子模型（χQSM）。

Conclusion: 与实验数据的整体一致性证实，从QCD瞬子真空导出的有效手征理论为描述核子电磁结构提供了一个自洽且具有预言能力的理论框架。

Abstract: We investigate the electromagnetic form factors of the nucleon within an effective chiral theory derived from the QCD instanton vacuum, taking into account the finite current quark mass. The momentum-dependent dynamical quark mass, generated by the instanton-antiinstanton medium, naturally plays the role of a regulator, so that no additional regularization is required to tame the divergences arising from quark loops. The instanton parameters, the average instanton size $\barρ=0.35$ fm and the average interdistance $\bar{R}=0.86$ fm, together with the dynamical quark mass at zero virtuality $M_0=385$ MeV, are all fixed by the saddle-point equation beyond the chiral limit, leaving no adjustable free parameter in the present calculation. We compute the Sachs electric and magnetic form factors of the proton and neutron, the nucleon charge and magnetization radii, the magnetic moments, and the ratios $μ_{p,n} G_E^{p,n}(Q^2)/G_M^{p,n}(Q^2)$. The present results are compared with the experimental data, the chiral quark-soliton model ($χ$QSM), and the Kelly parametrization. The proton charge radius, $\sqrt{\langle r^2 \rangle_\mathrm{ch}^p}=0.841$ fm, is in remarkable agreement with the recent muonic-hydrogen value, and the $Q^2$ dependence of the proton form-factor ratio $μ_p G_E^p/G_M^p$ is reproduced very well, in clear contrast to the $χ$QSM. The overall agreement with the experimental data confirms that the effective chiral theory derived from the QCD instanton vacuum provides a consistent and predictive framework for describing the electromagnetic structure of the nucleon.

</details>


### [22] [Odderon Form Factors in Reggeized Spin-2 Pomeron and Spin-3 Odderon Exchange in $pp$ and $p\bar p$ Elastic Scattering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25636)
*Dominador F. Vaso,,Prin Sawasdipol,Jingle B. Magallanes,Chakrit Pongkitivanichkul,Daris Samart*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过引入协变自旋投影算符，对高能弹性 pp 和 p\bar p 散射中的 Regge化张量 Pomeron 与 Odderon 交换的形态因子依赖性进行了系统研究。通过对七种 Odderon-质子形态因子参数化方案的全局拟合发现，单参数指数形式（χ²_red=0.98）显著优于其他六种参数化方案（χ²_red≈1.44–1.48），且耦合常数与 Regge 斜率保持稳定。指数形式对应高斯型横向轮廓，揭示出软 Odderon 相互作用的周边性（peripheral）特征，并随能量升高单 Regge 交换描述的 t 范围收缩，暗示吸收修正与幺正性修正的开始出现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高能弹性 pp 与 p\bar p 散射中，Odderon 交换的形态因子（form-factor）依赖性尚未被系统厘清，现有参数化方案多样但缺乏统一比较。本文旨在通过自旋结构因子化处理，分离顶点效应与轨迹动力学，从而明确 Odderon-质子顶点的最优形式及其物理含义。

Method: 采用协变自旋-2 和自旋-3 投影算符显式实现自旋结构，并将其与 Regge化标量核保持因子化。对七种 Odderon-质子形态因子参数化方案（包括偶极、多项式、高斯、混合及指数形式）进行全局拟合，数据集涵盖 TOTEM 的 pp 数据（√s=2.76, 7, 8, 13 TeV）和 Tevatron 的 p\bar p 数据（√s=1.80, 1.96 TeV）。

Result: 单参数指数形式 F_O(t)=exp[-B|t|/2] 给出 χ²_red=0.98（138 自由度），显著优于其余六种方案的 χ²_red≈1.44–1.48；拟合的耦合常数和 Regge 斜率在不同形态因子选择下保持相对稳定。指数形式在碰撞参数（impact-parameter）空间对应高斯横向轮廓，有效半径 √⟨b²⟩=√(2B)ℏc 呈强子尺度且表明 Odderon 相互作用具有周边性（peripheral）。随能量升高，单 Regge 交换描述准确的 t 范围逐渐收缩。

Conclusion: 指数形式的 Odderon-质子形态因子为 pp/p\bar p 散射中的 dip-bump 差异与 C-奇（C-odd）色单态交换的横向结构之间提供了一个紧凑的唯象学连接框架。拟合质量的改进主要由 Odderon-质子顶点而非轨迹参数的大幅补偿性偏移驱动，且t范围收缩现象暗示吸收修正与幺正性修正（unitarity corrections）的 onset。

Abstract: We investigate the form-factor dependence of Reggeized tensor Pomeron and Odderon exchanges in high-energy elastic $pp$ and $p\bar p$ scattering. The spin structure is implemented through explicit covariant spin-2 and spin-3 projectors, kept factorized from the Reggeized scalar kernels, so that vertex effects can be separated from trajectory dynamics. Seven Odderon--proton form-factor parametrizations are tested against a global dataset including TOTEM $pp$ data at $\sqrt{s}=2.76$, $7$, $8$, and $13$~TeV and Tevatron $p\bar p$ data at $\sqrt{s}=1.80$ and $1.96$~TeV. A clear hierarchy is found. Six dipole, polynomial, Gaussian, and hybrid parametrizations give comparable fit qualities, $χ^2_{\rm red}\simeq 1.44$--$1.48$, whereas a one-parameter exponential form, $F_{\mathbb O}(t)=\exp[-B|t|/2]$, yields $χ^2_{\rm red}=0.98$ for 138 degrees of freedom. The fitted couplings and Regge slopes remain comparatively stable across the form-factor choices, indicating that the improvement is driven mainly by the Odderon--proton vertex rather than by large compensating shifts in trajectory parameters. The exponential form admits an impact-parameter interpretation as a Gaussian transverse profile, with an effective radius $\sqrt{\langle b^2\rangle}=\sqrt{2B}\,\hbar c$. The extracted radii are of hadronic size and suggest a peripheral soft Odderon interaction. The shrinking $t$-range over which the single-Regge-exchange description remains accurate at increasing energy indicates the onset of absorptive and unitarity corrections. These results provide a compact phenomenological framework for connecting the $pp/p\bar p$ dip--bump difference with the transverse structure of $C$-odd color-singlet exchange.

</details>


### [23] [Predicted Exotic Doubly Heavy-Strange Pentaquarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25918)
*Albert Feijoo,Eulogio Oset*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在耦合道幺正框架下，基于隐藏局域规范（hidden local gauge）向重夸克（heavy-quark）扇区的推广，预言了夸克组分为 ūd̄sQQ′（QQ′=cc, bc, bb）的奇异双重味五夸克态（doubly heavy–strange pentaquarks），获得了由束缚态、共振态和虚态（threshold cusps）构成的稳定能谱，并揭示了以非对角跃迁为主的束缚机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将奇异五夸克态研究拓展至包含两个重夸克的新扇区（doubly heavy–strange sector），预言尚未被发现的、具有显式奇异量子数的双重味五夸克态，为未来实验搜寻提供具体目标。

Method: 采用耦合道幺正框架（coupled-channel unitary framework），相互作用来自隐藏局域规范方法（local hidden gauge approach）向重夸克扇区（heavy-quark sector）的扩展，通过考虑重子-轻介子（heavy-baryon–light-meson）道之间的离壳和非对角耦合来生成动力学。

Result: 在 us̄d̄scc、us̄d̄scb 和 us̄d̄sbb 三个扇区中分别预言了2个、3个和4个显式奇异（manifestly exotic）的五夸克态，这些态以束缚态或共振态形式出现，另有5个虚态表现为阈值尖点（threshold cusps）。非对角跃迁（off-diagonal transitions）主导束缚机制，而对角相互作用被强烈抑制。

Conclusion: 该工作将奇异强子谱学（exotic hadron spectroscopy）拓展到了双重味–奇异扇区，为实验上寻找新型五夸克态提供了可靠的能谱预测和可检验的理论靶标。

Abstract: We predict exotic doubly heavy--strange pentaquarks with minimal quark content $u\bar d sQQ'$ ($QQ'=cc,bc,bb$) within a coupled-channel unitary framework where the interaction is derived from an extension of the local hidden gauge approach to the heavy-quark sector. We obtain a robust spectrum of manifestly exotic states; two states appear in the $u\bar d scc$ sector, three in $u\bar d scb$, and four in $u\bar d sbb$. These emerge either as bound states or resonances, along with five additional virtual states manifested as threshold cusps. The binding mechanism is dominated by off-diagonal transitions among heavy-baryon--light-meson channels, while diagonal interactions are strongly suppressed. These results extend exotic hadron spectroscopy into the doubly heavy--strange sector and provide concrete targets for future experimental searches.

### [24] [Photon Calibration Techniques for High Resolution Cryogenic Detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24116)
*William J. Matava,Michael R. Williams*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文澄清了利用泊松统计（Poisson statistics）进行高分辨量热探测器（calorimetric detector）标定时隐含的假设，并分析了探测器实际性能模型对这些假设的偏离所导致的标定偏差，最后评估了各探测器参数对标定的影响并讨论了计算局限及对先进探测器的启示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在量热探测器分辨率超过单光子能量时，通常依靠泊松统计进行标定，但该方法隐含的假设缺乏明确讨论，且实际探测器性能可能违背这些假设，从而引入标定偏差。

Method: 首先明确标定方法中隐含的假设条件，然后引入更实际的探测器性能模型，分析假设被违反的情况，并逐一评估特定探测器参数对标定的影响。

Result: 指出了实际探测器模型对标定假设的违反会导致标定偏差，并量化了各探测器参数对该偏差的独立贡献。

Conclusion: 总结了计算的适用范围与局限性，并讨论了该标定偏差对当前最先进量热探测器的实际意义。

Abstract: Monoenergetic photons from a pulsed laser diode or LED are commonly used to calibrate the detector response of high-resolution calorimetric detectors. However, when the detector's resolution is larger than the energy of a single photon, a calibration is normally derived using Poisson statistics. In this paper, we clarify the assumptions implicit in this calibration method, before considering how a more realistic model of a detector's performance will violate these assumptions, biasing the calibration. Finally, we judge the individual impact of specific detector parameters on our calibration, and conclude with discussion of both the limits of our calculations and the implications for state-of-the art detectors.

</details>


### [25] [Long-term stability-degradation analysis of DUNE SiPMs in Liquid Nitrogen](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24196)
*Thomas Tsang,Flavio Cavanna,Hucheng Chen,Shanshan Gao,Lingyun Ke,Koloina Rambeloson*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文开发了一套低温光子读出系统，用于监测DUNE实验中硅光电倍增管（SiPM）在液氮（LN2）中不同过电压下运行超过三个月的性能。通过弱电容耦合到微前端电子学板（micro-FEMB）同时读出光电子信号，并采用波形片段采集方案滤除空波形。结果表明，多数参数在3个月内仅表现出约1σ的波动，且高过电压（4 V或5 V）未导致漂移加剧，但所有通道均观察到可探测的量子效率（PDE）下降，需进一步研究。此外，系统可在室温下同时读出选定SiPM组的单光子信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开发并验证一套适用于低温环境、可长期稳定运行的SiPM光子读出系统，以支持DUNE实验对大规模硅光电倍增管阵列在液氩时间投影室（LAr-TPC）中的性能监测需求。

Method: 在液氮中将DUNE SiPM阵列以不同过电压运行超过三个月，通过弱电容耦合至32通道电荷敏感读出板（micro-FEMB，工作温度范围77 K–300 K）同时读出光电子信号；采用波形片段采集方案（waveform snippet acquisition scheme），仅在信号超过预设触发电平时捕获波形，丢弃空波形。

Result: 多数SiPM参数在3个月测试期内仅表现出约1σ的波动；4 V或5 V过电压相比3 V未导致漂移增强；所有通道均出现可探测的量子效率（PDE）下降；系统在室温下可同时读出选定SiPM组的单光子信号。

Conclusion: 该低温光子读出系统能够长期稳定监测SiPM阵列，高过电压未加剧参数漂移，但PDE的持续下降需要进一步研究；系统同时具备室温下单光子读出能力。

Abstract: We developed a cryogenic photon readout system to monitor arrays of DUNE SiPMs operating at various over-voltages in liquid nitrogen (LN2) for over three months. Photoelectron signals were read out simultaneously via weak capacitive coupling to the micro-FEMB, a 32-channel charge sensitive readout board designed for 77 K to 300 K operation in liquid argon time projection chambers (LAr-TPCs). A waveform snippet acquisition scheme was implemented to capture waveform signals whenever they exceeded a predetermined trigger level; consequently, empty waveforms were discarded. Selected SiPM parameters were monitored to detect any deviations beyond statistical fluctuations. While some parameters exhibited ~1σ variations over the 3-month test period, there was no evidence of drift being enhanced when operating at 4 V or 5 V compared to a 3 V over-voltage. However, a discernible PDE drop was observed across all channels, which warrants further investigation. In addition, we demonstrated that our system can simultaneously read out single photons from a selected group of SiPMs at room temperature.

Niedzielski,Valentina Novati,Wiliam D. Oliver,Emiliano Olivieri,H. Douglas Pinckney,Denys V. Poda,Dmitrii Ponomarev,Jean-Sébastien Real,Faith C. Reyes,Alejandro Rodriguez,Sergey Rozov,Irina Rozova,Brianna Ryan,Deeksha Sabhari,Silvia Scorza,Kyle Serniak,Renaud Serra,Yegor Shevchik,Torsten Soldner,Hannah Stickler,Caitlyn Stone-Whitehead,Christian Ulysse,Wouter Van De Pontseele,Sergey Vasilyev,Paul Vittaz,Steven Weber,Evan Wolfe,Wayne Woods,Evgeny Yakushev,Jiatong Yang,Daniya Zinatulina*

TL;DR: 本文报道了用于RICOCHET实验中TES探测器读出的铝基六通道微波SQUID多路复用器（μMUX）原型的设计、制备与表征，验证了器件响应与模型的吻合，并在多种模式下测量了噪声性能，最终通过引入JTWPA实现了低于1 K的有效系统噪声温度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为RICOCHET实验中的超导转变边缘传感器（transition-edge sensor, TES）读出示波器（readout）开发低噪声、可扩展的微波SQUID多路复用（$μ$MUX）技术，以满足低温探测器阵列的读出需求。

Method: 设计并制备了基于铝的共面波导谐振器（coplanar-waveguide resonator）与射频SQUID（RF SQUID）器件，采用Dolan式Al/AlO$_x$/Al约瑟夫森结（Josephson junction）。通过测量谐振器在不同探测音频率、功率和磁通偏置点下的散射参数，与现有多路复用器模型进行对比验证；并在开环（open-loop）与磁通斜坡（flux-ramping）两种模式下进行噪声表征，同时引入约瑟夫森行波参量放大器（Josephson traveling-wave parametric amplifier, JTWPA）以降低读出噪声。

Result: 开环模式下使用HEMT放大器测得磁通灵敏度为1-1.5 $μΦ_0/\sqrt{Hz}$；采用磁通斜坡调制后抑制了低频1/f噪声，磁通灵敏度约为3-4 $μΦ_0/\sqrt{Hz}$，对应输入线圈电流灵敏度为24-33 $pA/\sqrt{Hz}$。加入JTWPA后，开环磁通灵敏度提升至0.3-0.6 $μΦ_0/\sqrt{Hz}$，有效系统噪声温度低于1 K。

Conclusion: 铝基μMUX器件可作为低噪声低温探测器阵列的一种可行且可扩展的读出技术方案，尤其适用于RICOCHET实验中的TES探测器读出示波器需求。

Abstract: We present the design, fabrication, and characterization of an aluminum-based six-channel microwave SQUID multiplexer ($μ$MUX) prototype for transition-edge sensor (TES) readout in the RICOCHET experiment. The device consists of aluminum coplanar-waveguide resonators and RF SQUIDs with Dolan-style Al/AlO$_x$/Al Josephson junctions. By measuring the resonator scattering parameters at a range of probe tone frequencies, powers, and flux bias points, we demonstrate agreement between the device response and existing multiplexer models. We also characterize the noise performance in both open-loop and flux-ramping modes. With a high electron mobility transistor (HEMT) amplifier, open-loop measurements yield a flux sensitivity of 1-1.5 $μΦ_0/\sqrt{Hz}$. With flux-ramp modulation, low-frequency 1/f noise is suppressed, and the flux sensitivity is around 3-4 $μΦ_0/\sqrt{Hz}$, corresponding to a current sensitivity of 24-33 $pA/\sqrt{Hz}$ at the input coil. We further demonstrate a reduction in readout noise by incorporating a Josephson traveling-wave parametric amplifier (JTWPA) between the $μ$MUX and the HEMT. This achieves an open-loop flux sensitivity of 0.3-0.6 $μΦ_0/\sqrt{Hz}$ and an effective system noise temperature below 1 K. These results establish aluminum $μ$MUX devices as a viable and extensible readout technology for low-noise cryogenic detector arrays.

### [27] [Towards 6D Tracking: A Study Of Using Fast-Timing For Measuring Track Position, Time, And Angles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24736)
*Victor Turbiner,Elena Villhauer,Abhiraj Gupta,Michael Cardiff,Julie Segal,Christopher J. Kenney,Mark Horowitz,Ariel Schwartzman,Angelo Dragone*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文通过TCAD模拟LGAD探测器，发现斜入射会导致跨像素定时偏差达数百皮秒，据此建立解析线性模型实现单层角度重建（精度约几度），并指出朗道涨落是分辨率的基本限制因素，且线性模型性能接近神经网络最优结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前及下一代粒子径迹探测器（particle tracking detector）需具备数十皮秒量级的时间精度，但斜入射（oblique incidence）引起的像素间定时偏差可能限制性能，亟需理解其物理机制并开发有效的角度重建方法。

Method: 基于低增益雪崩二极管（Low-Gain Avalanche Diode, LGAD）探测器的技术计算机辅助设计（Technology Computer-Aided Design, TCAD）模拟，推导出描述像素间定时差与入射角度关系的解析线性模型，并与神经网络方法进行性能对比。

Result: 斜入射会引起数百皮秒的系统性像素间定时变化；线性模型可实现单层角度重建，精度达几度；随机能量损失涨落（朗道涨落，Landau fluctuations）对角度分辨率和重建效率施加了基本极限；线性模型的角度分辨率接近神经网络方法的最优结果。

Conclusion: 在LGAD探测器的角度重建任务中，物理上由电荷收集几何（charge collection geometry）决定的可达性能，而非算法复杂度；线性模型已达到近最优角度分辨率，神经网络等复杂算法提升空间有限。

Abstract: Current and next-generation particle tracking detectors will incorporate precision timing capabilities with resolutions approaching tens of picoseconds. Using Technology Computer-Aided Design (TCAD) simulations of Low-Gain Avalanche Diode (LGAD) detectors, we demonstrate that oblique particle incidence induces systematic timing variations of hundreds of picoseconds across multiple pixels. We derive an analytical linear model relating inter-pixel timing differences to incident track angles, enabling single-layer angular reconstruction with few-degree precision. Stochastic energy loss fluctuations (Landau fluctuations) impose fundamental limits on both angular resolution and reconstruction efficiency. Comparison with neural network approaches demonstrates that the linear model achieves near-optimal angular resolution, indicating that the physics of charge collection geometry, rather than algorithmic sophistication, dominates the achievable performance.

### [28] [3D Magnetic Field Reconstruction and Mapping with Physics-Informed Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25640)
*Haohan Yu,Zhanxu Hao,Bingzhi Li,Zejia Lu,Xiang Chen,Liang Li*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 提出一种改进的物理信息神经网络（PINN, Physics-Informed Neural Network）框架，通过将麦克斯韦方程组直接嵌入损失函数并在测量点添加显式物理残差损失，实现了对不可达区域三维磁场的高精度重建，仿真精度达到 $10^{-4}$，实验精度达到 $10^{-3}$ 量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在众多高精度物理实验中，重建不可达区域的磁场分布至关重要，而传统的球谐展开（spherical harmonic expansion）等方法受截断误差（truncation errors）限制，精度不足。

Method: 提出一种改进的物理信息神经网络（PINN）框架，将麦克斯韦方程组（Maxwell's equations）中的散度为零（divergence-free）和旋度为零（curl-free）条件直接融入损失函数，并在测量位置加入显式物理残差损失（explicit physics-residual losses），以替代常规的随机配点采样，确保全域物理一致性。

Result: 在模拟数据上重建精度达到 $10^{-4}$，较现有PINN基准提升十倍；在自制线圈装置的实验验证中，环境条件下相对精度达到 $10^{-3}$ 量级（sub-percent relative accuracy）。

Conclusion: 该AI驱动方法为传感器受限的复杂实验环境中磁场监测与测量提供了稳健且高精度的解决方案。

Abstract: Accurate reconstruction of magnetic fields in inaccessible regions is vital for many high-precision experiments in physics. Traditional methods, such as spherical harmonic expansion, often suffer from truncation errors that limit their precision. This study proposes an advanced Physics-Informed Neural Network (PINN) framework for high-precision 3D magnetic field mapping. Unlike conventional data-driven models, the proposed PINN integrates Maxwell's equations directly into the loss function, enforcing divergence-free and curl-free conditions across the entire domain. A key innovation is the inclusion of explicit physics-residual losses at measurement locations, ensuring rigorous physical consistency beyond random collocation sampling. Validation using simulated data achieves a reconstruction accuracy of $10^{-4}$, a tenfold improvement over existing PINN benchmarks. Furthermore, experimental validation using a custom coil assembly demonstrates robust reconstruction with sub-percent relative accuracy, reaching the $10^{-3}$ level under ambient conditions. This AI-driven methodology provides a robust, high-precision solution for field monitoring and measurement in complex experimental environments where direct sensor placement is restricted.

</details>

### [29] [Pulse magnet of 10 T for power laser experiments with x-ray free-electron laser diagnostics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25697)
*Akihiko Ikeda,Kosuke Noda,Yutaro Yamanaka,Yuma Urabe,Keiichiro Kawai,Yasuhiro H. It flows through a split-pair coil to generate a high magnetic field (10 T at 6 kA) which has 1 cm access every 45$^{\circ}$ in the equatorial plane and 90$^{\circ}$ in the poloidal one. This platform offers new opportunities to study high-energy-density matter in strong magnetic fields, including shock propagation, instability growth, and turbulent plasma dynamics.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 首先推导该系统的双线性形式（bilinear form），然后基于该形式构造基本孤子、基本呼吸子及复合呼吸子（composite breather），并进一步获得双孤子、双呼吸子以及孤子与呼吸子组合的解；通过显式公式推导、可视化及长时间渐近行为（long-time asymptotic behavior）分析讨论所有“两体”相互作用（two-body interactions）性质。

Result: 成功构造了基本孤子、基本与复合呼吸子、双孤子、双呼吸子以及孤子-呼吸子组合等多种解，并通过分析确认了这些结构在相互作用中表现出的高度非平凡性质。

Conclusion: Hirota双线性方法可有效应用于可积离散Manakov系统，所构造的孤子与呼吸子解及其相互作用性质得到了严格的理论确认，深化了对该系统中相干结构行为的理解。

Abstract: The aim of this paper is to apply Hirota's bilinear method to the integrable discrete Manakov system in the focusing dispersion regime in order to construct and analyze soliton and breather solutions. After deriving the general bilinear form of the system, we show how to obtain fundamental solitons, as well as fundamental and composite breathers. We then obtain solutions exhibiting 2 solitons and 2 breathers and combinations of a soliton and a breather, and discuss all ``two-body'' interactions properties, with particular emphasis on explicit formulas, visualization, and long-time asymptotic behavior, thus rigorously confirming the highly nontrivial interaction properties of these coherent structures.

### [31] [QPEs from Warped Disk Collisions with EMRIs: Brightness-Recurrence Diagram and Gravitational-Wave Follow-up](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24905)
*Bo-An Chen,Bei You,Giovanni Miniutti,Ning Jiang,Zhen Pan,Tao Yang,Xi-Long Fan,Kai Liao,Xu-Heng Ding,Zong-Hong Zhu,Shuai-Kang Yang,Sai-En Xu,Han He,Xiao Fan*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文提出，准周期爆发（QPEs）的长短/强弱相关模式并非由现有的平盘碰撞模型解释，而是源于极端质量比旋进（EMRI）与翘曲吸积盘（warped accretion disk）的碰撞。盘翘曲调制了复发时间与爆发能量，将中心超大质量黑洞（SMBH）的自旋信息编码进X射线光变曲线；作者引入亮度-复发图（BRD）可视化这一相关性，并通过对原型源GSN 069的建模成功复现观测特征。数据支持两种情形：顺行恒星伴星或逆行恒星质量黑洞；若为后者，轨道衰减可在数十年内使LISA探测到该EMRI，实现引力波多信使约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有平盘碰撞模型无法解释QPEs中观测到的长短/强弱相关模式，亟需一个能够同时解释时间调制与能量调制的物理机制。

Method: 提出EMRI与翘曲吸积盘碰撞模型：盘翘曲通过改变碰撞几何同时调制复发间隔与爆发能量；引入亮度-复发图（BRD）来可视化这种相关性，其中EMRI的近星点进动（apsidal precession）驱动QPE爆发在BRD上形成椭圆轨迹，椭圆倾斜方向指示EMRI相对于SMBH自旋的顺行或逆行轨道。

Result: 将模型应用于原型源GSN 069，成功复现了观测到的长短/强弱相关模式。数据与两种轨道构型一致：顺行的恒星级伴星，或逆行的恒星质量黑洞。若为黑洞情形，轨道衰减可使其在未来数十年内被LISA探测到。

Conclusion: 翘曲盘碰撞模型为解释QPEs的相关模式提供了统一框架，并可将X射线观测与引力波探测（LISA）衔接，为系统（尤其是SMBH自旋与EMRI轨道几何）提供独立的多信使约束。

Abstract: Quasi-Periodic Eruptions (QPEs) display correlated long/short and strong/weak patterns that remain unexplained by existing flat-disk collision models. We propose that these features arise from an extreme-mass-ratio inspiral (EMRI) colliding with a warped accretion disk, likely formed after a tidal disruption event. The warp modulates both recurrence time and burst energy, encoding the disk geometry -- and thus the spin of the central supermassive black hole (SMBH) -- into the X-ray light curve. We introduce the Brightness-Recurrence Diagram (BRD) to visualize this correlation, where QPE bursts trace an elliptical trajectory driven by the EMRI's apsidal precession; the tilt of this ellipse encodes whether the EMRI is prograde or retrograde relative to the SMBH spin. Applying this model to the prototypical QPE source GSN 069 successfully reproduces the observed patterns. The data are consistent with either a prograde stellar secondary or a retrograde stellar-mass black hole. In the stellar-mass black hole scenario, ongoing orbital decay could render the EMRI detectable by LISA within a few decades, facilitating gravitational-wave follow-up and independent multimessenger constraints on the system.

### [32] [Core-collape supernovae and supernova neutrinos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25879)
*B. Mueller,B. Sykes*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解核塌缩超新星的形成机制和爆炸驱动过程，尤其是中微子和多维流体力学在能量提取中的角色，并强调核物理与中微子相互作用率在这一问题中的关键性。

Method: 通过综述恒星演化与瞬变观测的天体物理背景，采用现代中微子驱动爆炸的理论框架，结合核物理和中微子反应率进行分析，并讨论中微子与引力波作为超新星核心的探测手段。

Result: 指出核塌缩超新星爆炸的动能约为10^51 erg，中微子和多维流体流动是从塌缩核心提取能量以驱动爆炸的关键机制。

Conclusion: 中微子与引力波可作为探测超新星核心内部物理过程的有效探针；核物理与中微子相互作用率是理解超新星爆发现象的核心要素。

Abstract: Core-collapse supernovae are the terminal explosions of massive stars. After successive phases of nuclear fusion proceeding up to silicon burning, these stars form an iron core that is supported by electron degeneracy pressure. The core eventually collapses to a proto-neutron star, and in most cases the outer layers of the star are ejected by a shock wave, with a kinetic energy of order $10^{51}\,\mathrm{erg}$. Neutrinos and multi-dimensional fluid flow play a key role in extracting energy from the collapsed core to drive the explosion. After adumbrating the astrophysical context of stellar evolution and transient observations, this chapter sketches the modern theory of neutrino-driven supernova explosions, and discusses the key role of nuclear physics and neutrino interaction rates in the supernova problem. It also outlines the role of neutrinos and gravitational waves as probes into the supernova core.

### [33] [Reversible-jump MCMC reveals binary black hole subpopulations with distinct redshift evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25980)
*April Qiu Cheng,Alexandre Toubiana,Sylvia Biscoveanu,Jonathan Gair*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文利用可逆跳跃马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（reversible-jump Markov chain Monte Carlo）方法，在LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA观测的双黑洞（binary black hole, BBH）并合数据中发现了三个质量-自旋子族群，并首次独立约束了各子族群的 redshift 演化，为数据驱动的 BBH 形成机制推断奠定了基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着 LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA 探测器观测到的双黑洞（BBH）并合事件样本不断增长，其质量、自旋和红移（redshift）分布开始显现出特征结构，揭示驱动 BBH 形成与演化的天体物理过程印记。现有分析需要一种能够在最小先验假设下提供可解释结果的子族群搜索方法。

Method: 采用可逆跳跃马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（reversible-jump Markov chain Monte Carlo, RJMCMC）方法，在数据中自动搜索子族群，该方法能够在不预先指定子族群数量的情况下进行模型比较，并提供可解释的结果且对先验假设的需求最低。

Result: 发现了三个子族群：（1）窄的主质量峰位于 ~10 M☉，自旋优先对齐，质量比不相等，符合孤立双星演化（isolated binary evolution）；（2）主质量广泛分布在 ~30 M☉附近，自旋各向同性分布，强烈偏好相等质量比，符合动力学形成（dynamical formation in clusters）；（3）高自旋子族群在质量上连续分布，被解释为多个次要形成通道的汇聚。允许各子族群独立红移演化时，~10 M☉子族群的演化速率快于 ~30 M☉子族群，对延迟时间分布（delay-time distribution）和金属丰度依赖的 BBH 形成效率具有重要含义。

Conclusion: 这项工作为建立一种新颖的、数据驱动的框架来推断双黑洞（BBH）的形成机制奠定了基础，展示了通过子族群分析直接约束不同天体物理形成通道贡献的可行路径。

Abstract: Analyses of the growing catalog of binary black hole (BBH) mergers observed by the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA detectors are beginning to resolve features in their population-level mass, spin, and redshift distributions, revealing imprints of the astrophysical processes driving their formation and evolution. We present a novel method to search for subpopulations in the data using reversible-jump Markov chain Monte Carlo, providing interpretable results while making minimal prior assumptions. We find evidence for three subpopulations: a narrow subpopulation in primary mass at $\sim 10~M_\odot$ with preferentially aligned spins and unequal masses, consistent with isolated binary evolution; a subpopulation broadly distributed around $\sim 30~M_\odot$ with isotropically-distributed spins and a strong preference for equal mass ratios, consistent with dynamical formation in clusters; and a high-spin subpopulation spanning the continuum in mass, which we interpret as the confluence of multiple subdominant formation channels. When we allow for the independent redshift evolution of each subpopulation, we find that the subpopulation encompassing the $10~M_\odot$ peak evolves more quickly than the $30~M_\odot$ subpopulation, with implications for the delay-time distribution and metallicity-dependent BBH formation efficiency. Our work lays the foundation for a novel data-driven framework to infer the formation mechanisms of BBHs.

</details>


### [34] [Superfluid fraction and effective ion mass in the crystalline crust of a neutron star: role of interband response](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25600)
*Nicolas Chamel*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本论文通过线性响应理论与时间依赖的 Hartree-Fock-Bogoliubov 方程的自洽计算，首次系统分析了中子星内壳层中子超流中带间响应（interband response）对超流分数和离子有效质量的影响，并在统一微观框架下将夹带效应（entrainment effect）的描述从中子星内壳层扩展至外壳层。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 进一步完善中子星内壳层中子超流体的理论描述，澄清此前分析中忽略带间响应的问题，并探索带间响应如何影响超流分数和离子有效质量，最终实现内壳层与外壳层夹带效应的统一微观描述。

Method: 采用线性响应理论（linear response theory）处理自洽的时间依赖 Hartree-Fock-Bogoliubov 方程，基于 Skyrme 核能量密度泛函（Skyrme nuclear energy density functionals）并在 Bardeen-Cooper-Schrieffer（BCS）近似下进行计算；通过三维能带结构计算（three-dimensional band-structure calculations）数值评估带内响应（intraband response）与带间响应在不同壳层区域的相对重要性，并考虑离子在其平衡位置附近的量子零点运动（quantum zero-point motion）。

Result: 带间响应增强了中子超流分数（neutron superfluid fraction）；在真实中子对能隙下，带间响应的引入使有效离子质量（effective ion mass）保持在量子力学束缚核子的质量附近。与经典流体动力学（classical hydrodynamics）中不同离子渗透性（permeability of ions to superfluidity）预设的预测结果进行了比较。

Conclusion: 中子超流密度在形式上与先前均匀中子-质子超流混合物中导出的夹带矩阵一致，从而在同一微观框架内实现了中子星内壳层与外壳层夹带效应的统一描述。

Abstract: Neutron superfluidity in the inner crust of a neutron star is further investigated, focusing on the role of the interband response in the superfluid fraction and the effective mass of crustal ions induced by their motion through the superfluid. Calculations are performed within the linear response theory of the self-consistent time-dependent Hartree-Fock-Bogoliubov equations with Skyrme nuclear energy density functionals in the Bardeen-Cooper-Schrieffer approximation. The absence of interband response in previous analyses is clarified. The neutron superfluid density is formally shown to be consistent with the entrainment matrix derived earlier in homogeneous neutron-proton superfluid mixture, thus providing a unified description of entrainment effects in the inner crust and outer core of a neutron star within the same microscopic framework. The relative importance of the intraband and interband responses in different regions of the crust is numerically assessed from three-dimensional band-structure calculations, taking into account quantum zero-point motion of ions about their equilibrium position. The neutron superfluid fraction is found to be enhanced by the interband response, resulting in effective ion masses that remain close to the mass of quantum mechanically bound nucleons for realistic neutron pairing gaps. Results are compared to predictions from classical hydrodynamics with different prescriptions for the permeability of ions to superfluidity.

### [35] [Geometry, elasticity, and activity in the transport of self-propelled filaments in turbulence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24901)
*Kunal Kumar,Aliv Sahoo,Rahul Kumar Singh,Samriddhi Sankar Ray*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文通过珠-弹簧模型（bead-spring model）研究了弹性活性细丝（elastic active filaments）在二维湍流中的输运行为，发现推进几何结构（propulsion geometry）是决定输运的关键控制参数：当推进方向与细丝构象耦合时，涡旋捕获占主导，运动呈扩散性；当推进沿固定外部方向时，则出现超扩散输运。活性、弹性与流动诱导形变之间的竞争共同决定了最终的输运特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解活性物质（active matter）在复杂流动中的行为，特别是弹性活性细丝在湍流环境下的涡旋捕获与输运机制，揭示推进几何结构与弹性如何相互作用并影响细丝动力学。

Method: 采用珠-弹簧模型，在细丝头部施加活性（activity），对比两种推进模式：一是推进方向跟随细丝瞬时构象（instantaneous filament conformation），二是推进沿固定外部方向（fixed external direction）。在二维湍流场中模拟细丝运动，分析其输运行为与构象变化。

Result: 活性并不普遍增强输运：当推进与细丝骨架耦合时，涡旋捕获主导，运动呈有效扩散（diffusive）；固定方向推进则使细丝能够持续穿越流动结构，产生超扩散（superdiffusive）输运。两种情况下活性均使细丝构象向更伸展状态偏移，但并未消除对相干涡旋区域的优先采样。低韦森伯格数（Weissenberg number）下，活性与弹性协同增强对涡旋区域的优先采样，强化涡旋捕获。

Conclusion: 输运行为源于活性、弹性与流动诱导形变之间的竞争；弹性决定了活性引起的伸展能否在湍流捕获中持续存在。推进几何结构是输运的关键控制参数，弹性与活性以协同而非独立的方式共同塑造湍流中细丝的动力学行为。

Abstract: We investigate the transport of elastic active filaments in two-dimensional turbulence, focusing on how propulsion geometry and elasticity determine vortex trapping and transport. Using a bead-spring model with activity applied at the filament head, we compare propulsion that follows the instantaneous filament conformation with propulsion imposed along a fixed external direction. We find that activity does not generically enhance transport: when propulsion remains coupled to the filament backbone, vortex trapping remains dominant and motion stays effectively diffusive, whereas fixed-direction propulsion enables persistent excursions across flow structures and leads to superdiffusive transport. In both cases, activity shifts filament conformations toward more extended states, effectively opposing elastic relaxation without eliminating preferential sampling of coherent vortical regions. At low Weissenberg number, this conformational change is amplified: activity cooperates with elasticity to enhance preferential sampling of vortical regions and strengthen vortex trapping. Transport therefore emerges from a competition between activity, elasticity, and flow-induced deformation, with elasticity determining how effectively activity-induced extensions can persist against turbulent trapping. These results establish propulsion geometry as the key control parameter for transport, with elasticity and activity acting cooperatively rather than independently to shape filament dynamics in turbulent flows.

</details>


### [36] [Time-Symmetry of Lagrangian Coherent Structures in Active Turbulence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25056)
*Suvarchalanjan Bellaganti,Amal Manoharan,Kirti Kashyap,Siddhartha Mukherjee*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文利用拉格朗日相干结构（Lagrangian Coherent Structures, LCS）揭示了活性湍流（active turbulence）中驱动混合的吸引性与排斥性双曲曲面网络，发现尽管涡度主导流动，极端混沌混合却源于应变区域，且LCS网络随活性增加发生形态简化但保持各向同性交叉，最后指出拉格朗日不可逆性（Lagrangian irreversibility）在吸引性与排斥性LCS中并未明显体现，反而存在显著的时间对称性（time-symmetry）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 活性流动（active flows）在生命系统中的混合与输运中至关重要，但驱动混合的时空持久结构尚不明确，该研究旨在揭示这些结构及其与活性增加之间的关系。

Method: 采用拉格朗日相干结构（Lagrangian Coherent Structures, LCS）方法，研究吸引性与排斥性双曲曲面网络，分析有限时间李雅普诺夫指数（Finite-Time Lyapunov Exponent, FTLE）场的分布与谱随活性增加的变化，并计算LCS脊线的分形维数（fractal dimensions）。

Result: 尽管流场中涡度（vorticity）占主导，极端正向与反向时间混沌混合却起源于应变区域（straining regions），强调鞍点（saddles）的作用；随活性增加，LCS网络发生形态简化但保持各向同性交叉（isotropic crossing）；吸引性与排斥性LCS之间表现出显著的时间对称性，而非预期的拉格朗日不可逆性。

Conclusion: 该工作首次将活性湍流中的流场结构与不变混合曲面（invariant mixing surfaces）联系起来，为通过调节活性来调控流场结构及混合行为、进而控制活性湍流以服务于多种应用提供了基础。

Abstract: Active flows are central to mixing and transport across living systems. While Newtonian fluids remain laminar, diffusive and predictable at the microscale, living fluids like dense bacterial suspensions can exhibit highly chaotic flows like active turbulence, with anomalous transport capabilities. The underlying spatiotemporally persistent structures that drive mixing in active flows, however, remain uncharted. Using Lagrangian Coherent Structures, we now uncover networks of attracting and repelling hyperbolic surfaces. We study changes in the distribution and spectra of Finite-Time Lyapunov Exponent fields in response to increasing activity. Despite the dominance of vorticity in the flow, extreme forward and backward time chaotic mixing is found to originate from straining regions, emphasizing the role of saddles. Fractal dimensions of ridges reveal a morphological simplification of LCS networks with increasing activity, while retaining isotropic crossing. Throughout our work, we also probe a hitherto unasked question-Are signatures of Lagrangian irreversibility manifest in attracting and repelling LCS? To the contrary, we find there is a striking time-symmetry. Our work takes the first steps towards linking flow structures in active turbulence to invariant mixing surfaces. These findings will crucially help in designing activity modulation protocols to seed or inhibit flow structures, and thence mixing, in a bid to tame active turbulence for varied applications.

</details>
