### [37] [Signature of spin liquid state in a frustrated 3D antiferromagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24119)
*Satish Kumar,U. Jena,A. Bandhopadhay,G. B. G. Stenning,D. T. Adroja,S. Petit,P. Khuntia*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文报道了ZnCrGaO₄——一种具有内在阳离子无序的三维阻挫烧绿石（pyrochlore-like）磁体的合成与表征。尽管存在强反铁磁交换相互作用（J/k_B ∼ 55 K），但该材料在低至125 mK的极低温下未出现长程磁有序（long-range magnetic ordering）或自旋冻结（spin freezing）。比热和交流磁化率测量在低温下表现出宽峰，暗示短程自旋关联（short-range spin correlations）的形成；低温比热在1 K以下呈现幂律行为，表明存在非常规低能激发和代数自旋关联（algebraic spin correlations），为动态关联基态和潜在的自旋液体（spin-liquid）行为提供了有力证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 过渡金属氧化物中的阻挫烧绿石晶格（frustrated pyrochlore lattice）为实现奇异量子态（如自旋液体）提供了理想平台，而具有S > 1/2的高自旋三维阻挫磁体中自旋液体态的探索仍相对有限。本文旨在合成一种新型阻挫三维磁体ZnCrGaO₄，并系统研究其磁性和热力学性质，以探索高度阻挫S > 1/2三维量子磁体中潜在的自旋液体行为。

Method: 通过合成得到ZnCrGaO₄多晶样品，利用Curie–Weiss分析（Curie–Weiss analysis）高温磁化率数据估算交换相互作用强度；采用比热（specific-heat）测量、直流磁化率（dc susceptibility，包括零场冷ZFC和场冷FC测量）和交流磁化率（ac susceptibility）测量，在低至125 mK的极低温范围内表征该材料的磁性和热力学性质。

Result: 高温磁化率Curie–Weiss分析得出大负Curie–Weiss温度θ_CW ≈ −205 K，表明Cr³⁺（S = 3/2）矩之间的主导反铁磁交换相互作用（J/k_B ∼ 55 K）。比热和交流磁化率测量显示，即便在125 mK下也未出现长程磁有序迹象；0.01 T下ZFC和FC直流磁化率无分叉，且交流磁化率在低至250 mK下与频率无关，表明无自旋冻结。低温下磁比热和交流磁化率出现宽峰，指示动态磁态中短程自旋关联的发展。此外，低温比热在1 K以下遵循幂律行为，暗示非常规低能激发和代数自旋关联的存在。

Conclusion: ZnCrGaO₄展现出动态关联基态，未出现长程磁有序或自旋冻结，且低温比热呈现幂律行为，这些特征强烈支持其作为高度阻挫S > 1/2三维量子磁体和潜在自旋液体行为的候选平台。该结果拓展了阻挫量子磁体的研究范畴，为探索高自旋三维体系中自旋液体态提供了重要实验依据。

Abstract: Frustrated pyrochlore lattices in transition-metal oxides provide an ideal platform for realizing exotic quantum states, including spin liquids with unconventional low-energy excitations arising from the macroscopic ground-state degeneracy of corner-sharing tetrahedral networks. Here, we report the synthesis and comprehensive characterization of ZnCrGaO$4$, a frustrated three-dimensional pyrochlore-like magnet in which intrinsic cation ordering gives rise to unavoidable atomic-site disorder. A Curie--Weiss analysis of the high-temperature magnetic susceptibility yields a large negative Curie--Weiss temperature, $θ{\mathrm{CW}} \approx -205$ K, indicating dominant antiferromagnetic exchange interactions ($J/k_{\mathrm{B}} \sim 55$ K) between Cr$^{3+}$ ($S = 3/2$) moments. Despite the presence of strong antiferromagnetic interactions, no signature of long-range magnetic ordering is observed down to 125 mK, as evidenced by specific-heat and ac-susceptibility measurements. Furthermore, the absence of bifurcation between zero-field-cooled and field-cooled dc magnetic susceptibilities measured at 0.01 T indicates the absence of spin freezing, which is further supported by the frequency-independent ac susceptibility down to 250 mK. The presence of broad maxima in the magnetic specific heat and ac susceptibility at low temperatures suggests the development of short-range spin correlations within a dynamic magnetic state. In addition, the low-temperature specific heat follows a power-law behavior below 1 K, indicating the presence of unconventional low-energy excitations and algebraic spin correlations. These results provide compelling evidence for a dynamic correlated ground state in ZnCrGaO$_4$, establishing it as a promising platform for exploring highly frustrated $S > 1/2$ three-dimensional quantum magnets and potential spin-liquid behavior.

</details>


### [38] [Charge density wave in a band insulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24153)
*Md Shafayat Hossain,Wenhao Liu,Yuqi Zhang,Qi Zhang,Chao Lei,Nana Shumiya,Kouta Dagnino,Maksim Litskevich,Yu-Xiao Jiang,Jia-Xin Yin,Nikhil Dhale,Zi-Jia Cheng,Byunghoon Kim,Yongkai Li,Tyler A. Cochran,Xian P. Yang,Fan Zhang,Yugui Yao,Zhiwei Wang,Bing Lv,Titus Neupert,Luis Balicas,M. Zahid Hasan*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文在无费米面的能带绝缘体Bi4Br4中发现了电荷密度波（CDW）态，该CDW在40 K以下出现，打破了晶格平移对称性，并在原有绝缘能隙之上叠加了一个新能隙；同时观测到与滑动或相子模相关的非线性电导现象。这些发现代表了一类新型CDW，需要新的理论框架来解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为电荷密度波（CDW）起源于费米面（Fermi surface）的不稳定性，通常出现在金属体系中。本文旨在探索在无费米面的能带绝缘体（band insulator）中是否可能存在CDW态，以挑战现有的CDW理论框架。

Method: 以Bi4Br4为材料平台，利用低温拓扑成像（topographic imaging）和能谱成像（spectroscopic imaging）技术观测原子尺度的电荷调制；同时结合输运测量（transport measurements）研究电导特性。

Result: 在Bi4Br4的整个布里渊区（Brillouin zone）中，体相和表面均为能隙态。然而，在40 K以下观测到单向电荷调制（unidirectional charge modulation），打破了晶格平移对称性（lattice translation symmetry），并在原有绝缘能隙之上叠加了一个新的能隙。输运测量还发现了非线性电导（nonlinear electrical conduction），这一现象传统上与不相称CDW的滑动模（sliding mode）或相子模（phason mode）相关。

Conclusion: 这些高度反常的观测结果表明，在无费米面的能带绝缘体中存在一类新型CDW，无法被现有的CDW理论所解释，因此需要建立新的理论框架来理解这一现象。

Abstract: Charge density wave (CDW) implies a periodic modulation of the charge density. Typically observed in metallic systems, CDWs arise from Fermi surface instabilities, resulting in the total or partial gapping of the Fermi surface. Here, we present experimental evidence for a CDW state emerging in a band insulator which has no Fermi surface. The bulk and surface of our material platform, Bi4Br4, is gapped over the entire Brillouin zone. Through topographic and spectroscopic imaging at low temperatures, we unveil an unexpected unidirectional charge modulation in Bi4Br4, breaking the lattice translation symmetry. The CDW develops at temperatures below 40 K and adds an energy gap atop the existing insulating gap of Bi4Br4. Furthermore, our transport measurements reveal nonlinear electrical conduction, a phenomenon conventionally associated with the sliding or phason mode of incommensurate CDWs. These highly unusual observations represent a new type of CDW and demand a new theoretical framework for CDWs.

</details>


### [39] [Superconfined Antiferromagnons on the Two-Dimensional Penrose Lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24430)
*Takashi Inoue,Shoji Yamamoto*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 在二维彭罗斯晶格（Penrose lattice）上的自旋-S 近邻反铁磁海森堡模型（Heisenberg model）中，发现了新型局限态——线性自旋波（linear spin waves）具有大量简并的、严格局限在三配位（tricoordinated）位点上的本征态。与紧束缚模型（tight-binding model）中电子可同时局限在三配位和五配位（pentacoordinated）位点不同，自旋波仅局限在最小配位位点，其局限态由四种基本构建块（building blocks）构成（紧束缚模型中为六种），且对 1/S 修正鲁棒，并可通过 O(S⁰) 相互作用实现“超局限”（superconfinement）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索准晶（quasicrystal）系统中超越电子系统的磁激发（magnetic excitation）局限现象，揭示自旋波局限态与电子局限态的本质差异，并验证其在高阶修正下的稳定性。

Method: 基于线性自旋波理论（linear spin-wave theory）分析二维彭罗斯晶格上的自旋-S 反铁磁海森堡模型，通过对比紧束缚模型中的电子局限态，识别自旋波哈密顿量中的位点势（site potentials）来源，并系统分类两种模型中的局限态构建块类型。

Result: 自旋波局限态仅存在于三配位位点，且简并度高；紧束缚模型中的局限态则同时存在于三配位和五配位位点。自旋波局限态仅由四种构建块组成，而电子局限态有六种。自旋波局限态对 1/S 修正鲁棒，并可在三配位位点内进一步被 O(S⁰) 相互作用“超局限”为两组。

Conclusion: 自旋波局限态的构型、构建块数量和配位选择性均与电子局限态有本质区别，根源在于自旋波哈密顿量中的库仑相互作用（Coulomb interaction）起源的位点势；这些局限态在量子修正下依然稳定，并在高阶相互作用下表现出更精细的“超局限”结构。

Abstract: We find novel confined states in the spin-$S$ nearest-neighbor antiferromagnetic Heisenberg model on the two-dimensional Penrose lattice. Linear spin waves have massively degenerate eigenstates strictly confined to tricoordinated sites. They contrast with the well-known itinerant analogs in the tight-binding model, where electrons are confined but extended to both tricoordinated and pentacoordinated sites. It is the site potentials in the spin-wave Hamiltonian, originating from Coulomb interactions between electrons, that confine spin waves to minimally coordinated sites only. Confined states in the tight-binding Hamiltonian consist of six types of building blocks, whereas those in the spin-wave Hamiltonian consist of only four of them. Confined spin waves are robust against $1/S$ corrections. Emergent $O(S^{0})$ interactions further confine -- superconfine -- spin waves into two separate groups within tricoordinated sites.

</details>


### [40] [1/9 Magnetization Plateau in a Classical Kagome Ising Ferromagnet with Competing Further-Neighbor Interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24372)
*Yixin Guan,Kan Zhao,Nvsen Ma*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过模拟退火蒙特卡洛方法，系统研究了一类具有铁磁最近邻（J1）和反铁磁次近邻（J2）及第三近邻（J3）耦合的经典kagome伊辛模型，发现J3耦合通过扩展几何阻挫（geometric frustration）稳定了一种具有1/9磁化平台和3×3超大磁超胞（magnetic supercell）的新型分数有序相（fractional ordered phase），其临界温度几乎独立于J3耦合强度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索几何阻挫系统中复杂分数磁有序的产生机制，特别是kagome格点上超越最近邻相互作用的扩展竞争耦合如何诱导非平庸的低温相图行为。

Method: 采用模拟退火蒙特卡洛方法（simulated annealing Monte Carlo），系统扫描具有铁磁J1、反铁磁J2和J3耦合的经典kagome伊辛模型（classical kagome Ising model）的相空间。

Result: J2耦合仅抑制常规铁磁序，而J3耦合从根本上重构了低温相图，稳定了一种具有1/9磁化平台和3×3磁超胞的分数有序相；该相的临界温度几乎不依赖于J3的耦合强度；静态自旋结构因子（static spin structure factor）呈现清晰的Z6对称倒易空间特征。

Conclusion: 纯经典几何阻挫在扩展竞争相互作用下足以产生复杂的分数磁有序，为理解实际阻挫磁体中的分数有序态提供了新的机制。

Abstract: The two-dimensional kagome lattice is a paradigmatic platform for exploring geometrically frustrated magnetism. While the nearest-neighbor ferromagnetic Ising model on this lattice is theoretically trivial, competing further-neighbor interactions can reintroduce severe frustration. In this work, we systematically investigate a classical kagome Ising model with ferromagnetic nearest-neighbor (J1) and antiferromagnetic second- (J2) and third-neighbor (J3) couplings using simulated annealing Monte Carlo methods. We demonstrate that while J2 couplings merely suppress the conventional ferromagnetic order, the inclusion of J3 fundamentally reconstructs the low-temperature phase diagram. This extended geometric frustration stabilizes a novel ordered phase characterized by a robust 1/9 magnetization plateau and a massively enlarged 3 by 3 magnetic supercell. Crucially, this fractional ordered phase manifests as a stability plateau in the phase diagram, where its critical temperature becomes nearly independent of the coupling strength J3. We also calculate the corresponding static spin structure factor, revealing a distinct Z6-symmetric reciprocal-space signature for experimental identification. Our findings reveal that complex fractional magnetic orders can emerge purely from classical geometric frustration induced by competing extended interactions, providing a distinct mechanism for understanding fractionally ordered states in real frustrated magnets.

</details>


### [41] [Analytic Origin of Green-Function Compression in the Intermediate Representation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24814)
*Takahiro Misawa*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文揭示了中间表示（intermediate representation, IR）基底下压缩虚时格林函数（imaginary-time Green functions）的分析起源，发现其核函数具有有限拉普拉斯变换（finite-Laplace-transform）结构，并证明其本征函数可自然展开为扁长椭球波函数（oblate spheroidal wave functions），从而为压缩机制提供了严格的数学基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管中间表示（IR）基已在量子多体计算中被广泛用于压缩虚时格林函数，但其高效压缩能力的分析起源（analytic origin）一直未被阐明。理解这一机制对于建立更坚实的理论基础至关重要。

Method: 通过揭示IR核函数（IR kernel）潜在的有限拉普拉斯变换（finite-Laplace-transform）结构，证明其本征函数（eigenfunctions）可自然展开为经典特殊函数中的扁长椭球波函数（oblate spheroidal wave functions），从而分析性地阐明压缩机制。

Result: 发现了IR基底下压缩能力源于有限拉普拉斯变换结构，该结构使本征函数与扁长椭球波函数建立了直接关联，并据此从分析上澄清了压缩机制的物理根源。

Conclusion: 研究为虚时格林函数的压缩提供了数学基础，将量子多体物理学（quantum many-body physics）与信息压缩理论及有限积分变换（finite integral transforms）理论联系起来。

Abstract: Information compression plays a central role in diverse fields of modern science and technology, from communication theory to machine learning. In condensed-matter physics, the intermediate representation (IR) basis has recently been developed as an efficient method for compressing imaginary-time Green functions, which are fundamental quantities for describing quantum many-body systems. This compression relies on the rapid decay of the singular values with the basis index and the unusually weak growth of the effective rank with inverse temperature. Because of these useful features, the IR basis is now widely used as a standard method in quantum many-body calculations. However, the analytic origin of its compression capability has remained unclear. Here we uncover a finite-Laplace-transform structure underlying the IR kernel, which reveals that the eigenfunctions of the IR kernel admit a natural expansion in terms of classical special functions, the oblate spheroidal wave functions. This finite-Laplace-transform structure also enables us to analytically clarify the compression mechanism of the IR basis. Our results provide a mathematical foundation for the compression of imaginary-time Green functions, connecting quantum many-body physics with theories of information compression and finite integral transforms.

</details>


### [42] [Spiral and Mixed Plaquette-Dimer Phases in the $S=1$ and $3/2$ Shastry-Sutherland Heisenberg Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24409)
*Han-Qing Wu,Muwei Wu,Shou-Shu Gong*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文利用密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）和团簇平均场理论（CMFT），研究了二维Shastry-Sutherland晶格（SSL）上自旋S=1和S=3/2海森堡模型的基态相图。在二聚体相和Néel反铁磁相之间，识别出两种中间相：混合plaquette-二聚体（MPD）相和螺旋相。结合已有S=1/2和经典极限S→∞的边界，构建了全局S-g相图，揭示了量子效应随S增大而逐渐被抑制的规律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究主要集中于S=1/2的Shastry-Sutherland晶格（SSL）海森堡模型，但对更大自旋（S≥1）体系的基态相图尚缺乏系统理解。本文旨在填补这一空白，通过研究S=1和S=3/2情形，并结合已知结果构建全局相图，从而揭示自旋量子数S对相图结构的影响。

Method: 采用密度矩阵重整化群（density matrix renormalization group, DMRG）和团簇平均场理论（cluster mean-field theory, CMFT）进行数值计算。通过键能和自旋-自旋关联函数（spin-spin correlation functions）表征各相，利用基态能量导数和纠缠熵（entanglement entropy）定位相边界。

Result: 在二聚体相（dimer phase）和Néel反铁磁相之间的区域，识别出两个中间相：混合plaquette-二聚体（mixed plaquette-dimer, MPD）相和螺旋相（spiral phase）。MPD相表现出强二聚体关联和空plaquette上的弱四聚化，其到二聚体相和螺旋相的相变均为一级相变（first order）。

Conclusion: 通过整合S=1/2、S=1、S=3/2及经典极限S→∞的相边界，构建了全局S-g相图。该相图揭示了量子效应随自旋S增大而逐步被抑制的规律，并为更大自旋的SSL材料研究提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We investigate the ground-state phase diagram of the $S=1$ and $S=3/2$ Heisenberg model on the two-dimensional Shastry-Sutherland lattice (SSL) using density matrix renormalization group (DMRG) and cluster mean-field theory (CMFT). Between the dimer phase and Néel antiferromagnetic phases, we identify two intermediate phases: a mixed plaquette-dimer (MPD) phase and a spiral phase. These phases are characterized via bond energies and spin-spin correlation functions; phase boundaries are located from the ground-state energy derivative and entanglement entropy. The MPD phase exhibits strong intradimer correlations and weak tetramerization on the empty plaquettes, and its transitions to the dimer and spiral phases are first order. Combining our results with the known boundaries for $S=1/2$ and the classical limit $S\to\infty$, we construct a global $S$-$g$ phase diagram. This diagram reveals the progressive suppression of quantum effects with increasing $S$ and offers a theoretical framework for larger-$S$ SSL materials.

</details>


### [43] [Emergent Dispersive Multipolar Excitations in NaErSe$_{2}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24527)
*Zheng Zhang,Mingfang Shu,Mingtai Xie,Weizhen Zhuo,Yanzhen Cai,Christian Balz,Jianting Ji,Feng Jin,Jie Ma*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本论文通过中子谱学（neutron spectroscopy）与总角动量建模（total angular momentum modeling）相结合的方法，在三角晶格反铁磁体NaErSe₂中发现了局域激发与集体激发之间的耦合现象，揭示了由强自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）驱动的多极（multipolar）激发行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大多数凝聚态系统中，局域激发与集体激发因能量尺度不同而保持解耦状态。本文旨在探索是否存在两者耦合的例外情形，特别是在具有强自旋-轨道耦合的阻挫磁体（frustrated magnet）中。

Method: 采用中子谱学实验与总角动量建模相结合的方法，对三角晶格反铁磁体（triangular antiferromagnet）NaErSe₂ 进行高分辨率谱学测量与分析。

Result: 低能晶场（crystalline electric field, CEF）双重态包含具有偶极（dipolar）特性的 Γ₄ 基态（形成条纹-x 序）和具有偶极-八极（dipole-octupole）特性的 Γ₅,₆ 激发态。高分辨率谱显示对称性选择的色散现象：来自基态的自旋波（magnon）支在更高 Γ₄ 能级上复制，但与 Γ₅,₆ 能级耦合形成独特的多极带（multipolar band）。外加磁场可重构 CEF 波函数，将系统极化为多极铁磁态（multipolar ferromagnet），进一步重塑谱结构。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了由强自旋-轨道耦合驱动的局域激发与集体激发的涌现耦合现象，并确立了 NaErSe₂ 作为阻挫磁体中可通过场调控的多极激发平台。

Abstract: In most condensed-matter systems, local and collective excitations remain decoupled due to their distinct energy scales. Here, we identify coupled local-collective excitations in the triangular antiferromagnet NaErSe$_2$ by combining neutron spectroscopy with total angular momentum modeling. The low-lying crystalline electric field (CEF) doublets include a dipolar $Γ_4$ ground state forming stripe-$x$ order and a $Γ_{5,6}$ excited state with dipole-octupole character. High-resolution spectra reveal emergent symmetry-selected dispersions, where magnon branches from the ground state are replicated on higher $Γ_4$ levels but couple with the $Γ_{5,6}$ levels to form a distinct multipolar band. An applied magnetic field reconstructs the CEF wavefunctions and polarizes the system into a multipolar ferromagnet, further reshaping the spectra. This study demonstrates the emergent coupling of local and collective excitations driven by strong spin-orbit coupling and establishes NaErSe$_2$ as a platform for field-tunable multipolar excitations in frustrated magnets.

</details>


### [44] [Revisiting spin Hamiltonian parameters in a Kitaev material via Bayesian optimization of magnetization curves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24857)
*Takahiro Misawa,Ryo Tamura,Kazuyoshi Yoshimi,Youhei Yamaji*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出一种数据驱动方法，通过贝叶斯优化（Bayesian optimization）实验磁化曲线来替代传统第一性原理计算，以确定α-RuCl₃的自旋哈密顿量参数；优化得到的最优参数集为(K,Γ,Γ′,J,g_c)=(-6.0, 7.5, -0.3, -1.75, 2.3)，并发现该参数集对基塔耶夫耦合（Kitaev coupling）K的绝对值不敏感，且偏好大Γ值场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于第一性原理（ab initio）计算确定自旋哈密顿量（spin Hamiltonian）的方法对计算细节高度敏感，这在候选基塔耶夫材料（Kitaev material）α-RuCl₃中尤为突出。因此，需要一种替代方案，能够从实验数据出发更稳健地确定模型参数。

Method: 采用数据驱动方法，通过贝叶斯优化对α-RuCl₃沿b轴和c轴方向的实验磁化曲线进行优化，拟合五个参数：基塔耶夫相互作用K、非对角相互作用Γ和Γ′、海森堡相互作用（Heisenberg interaction）J以及c轴g因子g_c。结合精确低能求解器（accurate low-energy solvers）计算代价函数（cost function）。

Result: 最优参数集为(K,Γ,Γ′,J,g_c)=(-6.0, 7.5, -0.3, -1.75, 2.3)（交换耦合单位meV）。代价函数对K的绝对值不敏感，对Γ′和J依赖较弱，但强烈偏好大正Γ值。通过静态自旋结构因子、磁化率和比热计算，大Γ场景比小g_c场景更符合实验。

Conclusion: 贝叶斯优化结合精确低能求解器为从实验数据确定自旋哈密顿量参数提供了一种有效方法，为量子磁体中自旋哈密顿量的系统确定开辟了系统性途径。

Abstract: Determining the spin Hamiltonian of a magnetic compound is crucial for understanding its magnetic properties. A standard approach is to derive model parameters from $ab$ $initio$ calculations based on the crystal structure. However, the resulting Hamiltonian can depend sensitively on methodological details of the $ab$ $initio$ procedure. This issue is particularly evident in $α$-RuCl$_3$, a candidate Kitaev material. Here, we present an alternative, data-driven approach to determine the spin Hamiltonian parameters of $α$-RuCl$_3$ by Bayesian optimization of experimental magnetization curves along the $b$- and $c$-axis directions. We optimize five parameters, namely the Kitaev interaction $K$, off-diagonal interactions $Γ$ and $Γ'$, the Heisenberg interaction $J$, and the $c$-axis $g$-factor $g_c$. The parameter set that minimizes the cost function is $(K,Γ,Γ',J,g_c)=(-6.0,\,7.5,\,-0.3,\,-1.75,\,2.3)$, where the exchange couplings are in meV. We find that the cost function is insensitive to the absolute value of the Kitaev coupling $K$. Thus, the magnetization data alone do not determine its energy scale. The cost function also depends only weakly on $Γ'$ and $J$, while the optimization favors a large positive $Γ$. By computing the static spin structure factor, magnetic susceptibility, and specific heat, we show that these quantities favor the large-$Γ$ scenario over the small-$g_c$ scenario and that the parameter set that minimizes the cost function yields good agreement with experiment. The combination of Bayesian optimization and accurate low-energy solvers provides an effective approach for determining parameters of spin Hamiltonians. This methodology opens a systematic route to determining spin Hamiltonians in quantum magnets from experimental data.

</details>

Conclusion: 该模型在强关联下展现出从关联半金属到能带绝缘体的Lifshitz相变，且空穴掺杂可在绝缘相中诱导出与掺杂Mott绝缘体类似的隙态及关联半金属行为，揭示了电子-空穴关联体系中金属-绝缘体转变的丰富物理。

Abstract: We investigate the strong correlation effect in the spinless electron-hole two-band Hubbard model using the dynamical mean-field theory. At half filling, both the renormalization factor $Z$ and the number of conduction electrons (valence holes) $n_c$ decrease with increasing the interband Coulomb interaction $U$ down to $Z\sim 0.15$ and $n_c\sim 0.1$ for $U_c \sim \mbox{bandwidth}$ at which the first-order Lifshitz transition occurs from a correlated semimetal with a large effective mass $m^*/m=Z^{-1}$ to a band insulator with a finite gap due to the Hartree shift. A slight hole doping $x$ in the band insulator with a large $U>U_c$ yields a remarkable correlated semimetal with $Z\sim 0.1$ at $x\sim 0.01$, where in-gap states emerge above the valence band top and those weights increase with increasing $x$ together with the increase in $Z$ similar to the in-gap states observed in doped Mott insulators.

### [46] [Dynamical susceptibility and quantum Fisher information in the Su-Schrieffer-Heeger model with Hatsugai-Kohmoto interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25231)
*Sepide Mohamadi,Jahanfar Abouie*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文在Hatsugai-Kohmoto相互作用下的Su-Schrieffer-Heeger模型中，系统研究了动力学自旋和电荷磁化率及其关联的量子Fisher信息。通过与单带Hubbard和SSH-Hubbard模型的对比，展示了SSH-HK模型因SSH二聚化与HK相互作用的动量对角性而产生的独特物理行为，并揭示了量子Fisher信息可作为填充区间的有效探针，但对拓扑转变不敏感。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用随机相位近似（random-phase approximation）处理单带Hubbard和SSH-Hubbard模型作为比对基准；利用Hatsugai-Kohmoto（HK）相互作用的精确可解性，推导动力学磁化率的闭式表达式，并基于磁化率虚部的频率积分定义量子Fisher信息。

Result: SSH-HK模型展现出与标准Hubbard型相互作用截然不同的行为，包括零波矢下的有限响应以及整数和分数填充区间光谱权重的显著重构。量子Fisher信息在不同填充区间呈现分段特征，能有效区分整数与分数填充，但对均匀密度区内的拓扑转变不敏感。

Conclusion: SSH-HK模型为探索拓扑与强关联竞争提供了强大的解析平台；动力学磁化率与量子Fisher信息可作为互补的可实验观测的多体物理探针，但标准动力学响应函数在表征能带拓扑方面存在固有局限。

Abstract: We investigate the dynamical spin and charge susceptibilities and the associated quantum Fisher information in a class of interacting lattice models, with a primary focus on the Su-Schrieffer-Heeger model in the presence of Hatsugai-Kohmoto interactions. To provide a rigorous analytical benchmark, we contrast the response properties of the SSH-HK system with those of the single-band Hubbard and SSH-Hubbard models, treated within the random-phase approximation. While standard Hubbard-type interactions typically suppress excitation strength, we demonstrate that the SSH-HK model displays qualitatively distinct physical behavior arising from the interplay between SSH dimerization and the momentum-diagonal nature of the HK interaction. Leveraging the exact solvability of the HK term, we derive closed-form expressions for the dynamical susceptibility, revealing unique filling-controlled characteristics such as a finite response at zero wave vector and a pronounced restructuring of spectral weight across integer and fractional filling sectors. We show that the quantum Fisher information, defined as the frequency integral of the imaginary part of the susceptibility, serves as an efficient probe of these filling sectors, exhibiting distinct piecewise behavior that distinguishes integer from fractional fillings. Notably, our results indicate that the quantum Fisher information remains insensitive to topological transitions within uniform-density regimes, highlighting the limitations of standard dynamical response functions in characterizing band topology. These findings establish the SSH-HK model as a powerful analytical platform for exploring the competition between topology and strong correlations, demonstrating how dynamical susceptibilities and the quantum Fisher information provide complementary, experimentally accessible probes of many-body physics.

### [47] [Non-local low energy neutral excitations in a strongly disordered triangular Mott magnet Cr$_3$Se$_2$Br$_5$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25269)
*Wenhao Liu,Dechen Zhang,Yuanqi Lyu,Lebing Chen,Lifang Hu,Keith M. Teddei,Yuting Zhang,Steve Shelton,Moon Kim,Xiqu Wang,Michael A. Susner,James G. Analytis,Dung-Hai Lee,Lu Li,Bing Lv,Robert J. Birgeneau*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 对范德华化合物Cr₃Se₂Br₅——一种具有受挫三角晶格（triangular lattice）的S=3/2莫特绝缘体（Mott insulator）——进行结构分析、磁性测量以及磁比热C_mag/T和热导率κ_xx/T的输运表征。

Result: 结构分析表明存在由Cr位缺失和Se/Br位混合导致的显著内在无序。未观察到长程磁有序（long-range magnetic order）或常规玻璃态行为（glassy behavior）。磁场无关的残余热导项κ/T ≈ 0.03 W m⁻¹ K⁻²被观测到，且磁比热和热导率均呈现线性温度依赖并具有显著有限截距。

Conclusion: 这些发现从概念上推进了对量子物质（quantum matter）的理解，展示了一种罕见相态，其中无序、受挫和电子关联（electronic correlations）的相互作用主动重塑了低能激发的性质，使得巡游中性激发与强内在无序得以共存。

Abstract: Understanding if low-energy excitations can remain itinerant in the presence of strong disorder remains a central challenge in frustrated quantum magnets, where disorder is generally expected to localize excitations through Anderson-like mechanisms. Here we report the emergence of charge-neutral itinerant excitations in a van der Waals compound Cr$_3$Se$_2$Br$_5$, a strongly disordered $S = 3/2$ Mott insulator with a frustrated triangular lattice. Structural analysis reveals substantial intrinsic disorder arising from Cr-site deficiency and Se/Br-site mixing, which appear to be fixed and cannot be readily tuned. No long-range magnetic order or conventional glassy behavior is observed. In addition to its highly insulating nature, the magnetic specific heat C_mag/T and thermal conductivity \k{appa}_xx/T both exhibit linear temperature dependencies with substantial finite intercepts. In particular, a sizeable field-independent residual term $κ/T \approx 0.03~\mathrm{W\,m^{-1}\,K^{-2}}$ is observed, providing compelling evidence of itinerant low-energy excitations that carry entropy without charge. These findings conceptually advance our understanding of quantum matter by demonstrating a rare regime where the interplay of disorder, frustration, and electronic correlations actively reshapes the nature of low-energy excitations, allowing itinerant neutral excitations to coexist with strong intrinsic disorder.

### [48] [Magnetoelastic effects in the metallic frustrated antiferromagnet CrB$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25564)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 六方CrB₂是一种金属阻挫反铁磁体（frustrated antiferromagnet），其Cr 3d电子同时贡献局部磁矩和金属导电性。研究旨在通过弹性性质测量，理解磁阻挫与电子-晶格耦合的关联机制。

Result: ab面剪切弹性模量在冷却至尼尔温度（Néel temperature, T_N）过程中表现出居里型软化（Curie-type softening），解释为T_N处对称性降低晶格畸变的前驱效应；a轴和c轴压缩弹性模量在冷却时出现异常软化和抑制行为，由费米面嵌套及其冷却抑制自然解释。

Abstract: Hexagonal chromium diboride CrB$_2$ is a metallic frustrated antiferromagnet with a Néel temperature $T_N \sim$ 88 K. In CrB$_2$, Cr 3$d$ electrons not only give rise to localized magnetic moments but also contribute to metallic conduction. We perform ultrasound velocity measurements on a single crystal of hexagonal CrB$_2$ to determine its elastic properties. The temperature dependence of the $ab$-plane shear elastic modulus exhibits Curie-type softening upon cooling from $\sim$120 K down to $T_N$. This behavior is interpreted as a precursor to a symmetry-lowering lattice distortion at $T_N$, indicating that magnetic frustration is relieved via transverse magnetoelastic coupling. In addition, the $a$-axis and $c$-axis compressive elastic moduli show unusual softness and their suppression upon cooling, which are naturally explained by Fermi-surface nesting and its suppression upon cooling. The present results suggest that, in CrB$_2$, longitudinal magnetoelastic coupling suppresses Fermi-surface nesting and enhances frustrated exchange interactions, while transverse magnetoelastic coupling plays a key role in relieving the frustration.

### [49] [On the Relation Between String Order Parameters, Entanglement, and Dynamical Quantum Phase Transitions in Topological Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25611)
*Sirshendu Bhattacharyya,Szczepan Głodzik,Nicholas Sedlmayr*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究一维拓扑模型淬火后，弦序参量（string order parameter）和纠缠谱（entanglement spectrum）的非平衡动力学，发现弦序参量的零点与动力学量子相变（dynamical quantum phase transition）的临界时间之间不存在普遍的定量或定性联系，与纠缠谱中心交叉也仅偶有相关性，质疑了此类模型中存在真正动力学相的观点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前研究建议弦序参量可作为动力学量子相变的实验探针，本文旨在系统检验弦序参量和纠缠谱在非平衡淬火（quench）动力学中是否与动力学量子相变的临界时间存在严格关联。

Method: 基于一维具有$\mathbb{Z}$拓扑不变量（topological invariant）的拓扑模型，通过淬火驱动系统远离平衡，分析弦序参量的时间演化和纠缠谱（entanglement spectrum）的中心交叉行为，并与动力学量子相变的临界时间进行对比。

Result: 弦序参量在临界时间出现清晰的零点，但与动力学量子相变临界时间无普遍的定量或定性联系；纠缠谱中心交叉与弦序参量零点有时相关，但非典型情形。此外，标记某一拓扑相的弦序参量在另一拓扑相之间的淬火中也能展现非平凡动力学。

Conclusion: 弦序参量零点、纠缠谱中心交叉和动力学量子相变临界时间各自的临界行为彼此独立，仅临界时间量级相近；这些结果对一维$\mathbb{Z}$拓扑模型中存在真正动力学相的观点提出质疑。

Abstract: Topological order is defined by topological invariants, rather than symmetries and local order parameters. Nonetheless some topological phases can be characterized by string order parameters and entanglement. In this article we study how string order parameters and entanglement spectra behave out-of-equilibrium following quenches in one dimensional topological models with $\mathbb{Z}$ invariants. Previously it has been suggested that string order parameters could serve as an experimental probe of dynamical quantum phase transitions. Despite the existence of clear zeroes in the order parameters at critical times, we show that in general there is no exact quantitative or qualitative connection with the critical times of dynamical quantum phase transitions. Another possible connection is of dynamical string order parameter zeroes and dynamical crossings at the center of entanglement spectra. Here we see that there can sometimes be a connection, but it is not typical. Again there is no general quantitative or qualitative connection. Each dynamical form of criticality behaves independently, though we do see that critical times tend to be of the same order of magnitude and give an argument for why this is the case. We also find that a string order parameter which labels one topological phase can undergo non-trivial dynamics even following a quench between \emph{other} topological phases. We elucidate where connections can be made, and where they result from a consideration of insufficiently general models. These results cast doubt on the idea of genuine dynamical phases following quenches in such models.

### [50] [The evolution of pairing correlation with $3d_{z^{2}}$ electron filling in a bilayer two-orbital model for La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25654)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高压双层镍酸盐La₃Ni₂O₇中高温超导的发现为非传统配对机制（unconventional pairing mechanisms）提供了新的研究平台。其中Ni的3d_{z²}轨道所扮演的具体角色尚不清楚——其层间超交换反铁磁耦合被广泛认为对超导至关重要，但该轨道的巡游性（itinerancy）的作用仍悬而未决。早期与近期实验给出了相互矛盾的结果，促使作者通过理论模型系统研究其作用。

Method: 采用密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）方法，在一维最小几何构型（minimal one-dimensional geometry）下，对La₃Ni₂O₇的有效双层双轨道模型（effective bilayer two-orbital model）进行数值研究。通过系统变化3d_{z²}轨道填充从1/12掺杂到半填充（half-filling），考察超导关联的演化。

Result: 在半填充附近观察到超导关联（superconducting correlations）被显著抑制。3d_{z²}轨道的巡游性有利于双层双轨道模型中的配对。此外，在电荷涨落（charge fluctuations）较大的区域，配对关联（pairing correlation）得到增强。

Conclusion: 结果表明，3d_{z²}轨道的巡游性对La₃Ni₂O₇中的超导配对是有利的；同时，电荷序（charge order）与超导之间在该模型中存在竞争关系。

Abstract: The discovery of high-${T_c}$ superconductivity in pressurized bilayer nickelate La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ presents a new arena for exploring unconventional pairing mechanisms. A pivotal yet unresolved issue is the specific role of the $3d_{z^{2}}$ orbital of Ni. While its inter-layer super-exchange antiferromagnetic coupling is widely considered crucial for superconductivity, the role of its itinerancy remains undetermined. Early studies showed that the superconductivity is accompanied by the emergence of a small Fermi pocket of the $3d_{z^{2}}$ orbitals. However, recent experiments show controversial results on the role of the $3d_{z^{2}}$ Fermi pocket on superconductivity. Motivated by these experimental results, we investigate an effective bilayer two-orbital model for La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ using density-matrix renormalization group (DMRG) on a minimal one-dimensional geometry. By systematically varying the $3d_{z^{2}}$ orbital filling from $1/12$ doping to half-filling, we observe a pronounced suppression of superconducting correlations near half-filling. Our results demonstrate the itinerancy of $3d_{z^{2}}$ orbital is favorable for the pairing in the bilayer two-orbital model for La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$. Moreover, we observe that the pairing correlation is enhanced in regions where charge fluctuations are large, suggesting a competition between charge order and superconductivity in the model.

</details>


### [51] [Near-Room-Temperature Antiferromagnetic Ordering in the Quadruple Perovskite Sr4NaRu3O12](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25694)
*Subham Naik,Biswajit Singh,Hiranmayee Senapati,Akshay K. U.,Ramesh C. Nath,Soumyojit Chatterjee,Rahul Sharma,Thomas Doert,Walter Schnelle,Manfred Reehuis,Thomas C. Hansen,Michael Ruck,Gohil S. Thakur*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文报道了两种1:3有序四重钙钛矿（quadruple perovskite）Sr4MRu3O12（M = Li和Na）的合成、结构和磁性。Sr4NaRu3O12在~265 K以下发生反铁磁（antiferromagnetic）相变，而Sr4LiRu3O12在110 K以下表现出磁性异常，可能源于铁磁与反铁磁相互作用的竞争。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索新型1:3有序四重钙钛矿材料的结构与磁性性质，特别是B位阳离子有序排列对磁有序和电子性质的影响。

Method: 通过粉末X射线衍射（PXRD）、磁化率测量、差示扫描量热法（DSC）和中子衍射（neutron diffraction）对Sr4MRu3O12（M = Li, Na）进行结构和磁性表征；结合能带结构计算（band structure calculation）分析电子性质。

Result: Sr4NaRu3O12属于中心对称空间群R-3，具有较大的单胞（a = 11.25 Å, c = 27.6 Å），在TN ≈ 265 K以下进入共线反铁磁态，磁传播矢量（propagation vector）k = (0, 0, 1.5)，Ru磁矩沿六方c轴排列，位于三重复反演轴（three-fold roto-inversion）上的Ru磁矩由于几何阻挫（geometric frustration）对磁序贡献很小。Sr4LiRu3O12在110 K以下出现磁性异常，可能涉及铁磁（ferromagnetic）与反铁磁相互作用的竞争。

Conclusion: Sr4NaRu3O12呈现反铁磁基态和半导体行为，其磁结构由B位有序排列和几何阻挫共同决定；Sr4LiRu3O12则表现出更复杂的磁性竞争。

Abstract: We report the synthesis, structure and magnetic properties of two 1:3 ordered quadruple perovskites Sr4MRu3O12 (M = Li and Na). Sr4NaRu3O12 crystallizes in the centrosymmetric space group R-3 and Sr4LiRu3O12 appears to be isostructural to the Na compound based on the PXRD data. In Sr4NaRu3O12, both Na and Ru are predominantly ordered at the B sites (here Na/Li and Ru) and the structure contains only corner-connected RuO6 and NaO6 octahedra. This atomic ordering also leads to a rather large unit cell with a = 11.25 Å and c = 27.6 Å compared to the basic 12R structure (a = 5.5 Å and c ~ 27 Å). Magnetic measurements reveal that Sr4NaRu3O12 undergoes a magnetic transition to an antiferromagnetic state below TN ~ 265 K which is confirmed by DSC and neutron diffraction. The Ru moments show a collinear antiferromagnetic spin alignment along the hexagonal c axis with a propagation vector k = (0, 0, 1.5). Interestingly, those Ru moments lying on the three-fold roto-inversion do not significantly contribute to the magnetic order, since they are located between antiferromagnetically coupled Ru atoms and are therefore probably highly frustrated. Band structure calculations on Sr4NaRu3O12 complement the observed magnetic ground state and a semiconducting behavior in the compound. Sr4LiRu3O12 shows a magnetic anomaly below 110 K, possibly associated with competing ferromagnetic and antiferromagnetic interactions.

</details>


### [52] [Trimerized Spin-$1/2$ Chain: Emergent Low-Energy Hamiltonian, Higher-Energy Excitations, and Magnetic and Thermodynamic Responses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25960)
*Snehasish Sen,Sudhansu S. Mandal*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究了与Na₂Cu₃Ge₄O₁₂相关的自旋-1/2三聚化反铁磁链，通过将低能希尔伯特空间映射为有效海森堡链（Heisenberg chain），并发展自洽的Jordan-Wigner平均场理论（self-consistent Jordan-Wigner mean-field theory），建立了连接低能和高能激发的统一理论框架。该理论精确再现低能自旋子连续谱，预言了两个额外的高能激发带，并成功解释了1/3磁化平台等实验现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三聚化量子自旋链中低能和高能激发之间的统一描述一直缺乏系统的理论框架，现有方法难以同时精确刻画两个能量尺度的物理行为。

Method: 首先将低能希尔伯特空间映射为具有正耦合的有效复合自旋-1/2三聚体海森堡链，通过Bethe拟设（Bethe ansatz）精确求解自旋子激发；为进一步获取高能动力学，发展了自洽的Jordan-Wigner平均场理论，得到反映三聚体结构的三条费米子能带。

Result: 该平均场理论精确再现了低能自旋子连续谱，同时预言了两个额外的高能激发带，与实验观测和先前的数值模拟一致；理论还捕获了外加磁场下的1/3磁化平台（magnetization plateau），并在磁化率（magnetic susceptibility）和比热（specific heat）方面提供了可检验的预言。

Conclusion: 建立了统一描述三聚化量子自旋链中低能和高能激发的理论框架，验证了该方法的有效性，并为后续实验探测提供了明确的理论预测。

Abstract: We investigate a spin-1/2 antiferromagnetic chain with trimerized exchange couplings relevant to Na$_2$Cu$_3$Ge$_4$O$_{12}$. We show that the low-energy Hilbert space maps onto an effective Heisenberg chain of composite spin-1/2 trimer degrees of freedom with positive coupling, enabling an exact spinon excitations via the Bethe ansatz. To access higher-energy dynamics, we develop a self-consistent Jordan-Wigner mean-field theory that yields three fermionic bands reflecting the underlying trimer structure. Remarkably, this approach reproduces the exact low-energy spinon continuum while predicting two additional higher-energy excitation bands consistent with the experimental observations and previous numerical simulations. The theory further captures the 1/3 magnetization plateau under an applied magnetic field, and provides testable predictions in magnetic susceptibility and specific heat. Our results establish a unified framework connecting low- and high-energy excitations in trimerized quantum spin chains.

### [53] [Demagnetization effect on magnetic noise measurements in spin ice materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25993)
*F. Morineau,C. Paulsen,G. Balakrishnan,D. Prabhakaran,K. Matsuhira,S. R. Giblin,E. Lhotel*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过实验与理论分析，证明自旋冰（spin ice）中的磁噪声谱（magnetic noise spectroscopy）受到退磁场（demagnetizing field）和样品几何形状的强烈重整化（renormalization），导致测量到的噪声谱不能直接反映本征涨落谱，必须将样品几何作为中心控制参数才能获取本征动力学信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁噪声谱是研究关联磁系统（如自旋液体、自旋冰、自旋玻璃）中自发时变磁化涨落的直接工具，但退磁场如何影响自旋冰中的噪声谱尚不清楚，需要系统探究样品几何对噪声测量的作用。

Method: 结合磁噪声测量和交流磁化率（ac susceptibility）测量，对具有不同尺寸和形状的单晶自旋冰样品进行研究，通过对比噪声数据与线性响应结果来分析样品几何的效应。

Result: 磁噪声与线性响应类似，都受到样品几何的强烈重整化；测量得到的噪声谱并不直接给出本征涨落谱，且仅凭噪声数据无法普遍确定退磁修正（demagnetization correction）。

Conclusion: 样品几何必须被视作获取本征动力学（intrinsic dynamics）的核心实验控制参数；该结果确立了边界条件（boundary condition）在涨落谱学（fluctuation spectroscopy）中的关键角色，为将噪声测量与自旋动力学的微观理论进行定量比较提供了框架。

Abstract: Magnetic noise spectroscopy provides direct access to spontaneous time-dependent magnetization fluctuations in correlated magnetic systems, including spin liquids, spin ices, and spin glasses. Here we investigate how demagnetizing fields shape the magnetic noise spectra measured in spin ice. By combining magnetic noise and ac susceptibility measurements on single-crystal spin ice samples with different sizes and shapes, we show that magnetic noise, like linear response, is strongly renormalized by sample geometry. As a consequence, measured noise spectra do not directly yield the intrinsic fluctuation spectrum, and demagnetization corrections cannot in general be determined from noise data alone. Instead, sample geometry must be treated as a central experimental control parameter for accessing intrinsic dynamics. These results establish the role of boundary conditions in fluctuation spectroscopy and provide a framework for quantitatively comparing noise measurements with microscopic theories of spin dynamics.

</details>


### [54] [Magnetic ground state of a prototype quasicrystal approximant: a candidate for octahedral spin ice physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26044)
*Leonie Woodland,Farid Labib,Dmitry Khalyavin,Pascal Manuel,Fabio Orlandi,Hubertus Luetkens,Ryuji Tamura*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本研究通过中子衍射和μ子自旋旋转实验，发现准晶近似相Cd6Tb中存在由Ising型Tb矩构成的非共面多k磁基态，其中仅三分之一的Tb矩形成长程磁序，其余矩保持动态涨落，实现了准晶关联材料中的八面体自旋冰（octahedral spin-ice）磁碎裂（magnetic fragmentation）现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准晶（quasicrystals）中的磁有序为发现超越周期性晶格框架的非传统磁态提供了新机遇，但由于准晶固有的非周期性（aperiodicity），阐明这些磁态的微观起源极具挑战性。

Method: 以典型Tsai型准晶近似相（quasicrystal approximant）Cd6Tb为研究对象，该材料保留了二十面体准晶（icosahedral quasicrystals）的局域几何与连接性，同时因平移周期性（translational periodicity）允许详细的结构与磁性表征；采用中子衍射（neutron diffraction）和μ子自旋旋转（muon spin rotation）实验进行测量。

Result: 发现一个由Ising型Tb矩构成的非共面多k磁基态（noncoplanar multi-k magnetic ground state），Tb矩排列在共角八面体（corner-sharing octahedra）网络上；仅约三分之一Tb矩形成长程磁序（long-range magnetic order），其余矩表现出显著降低的静态序伴随微秒时间尺度的持续自旋动力学（persistent spin dynamics）。

Conclusion: 这种有序与涨落矩的共存构成了八面体自旋冰物理学中关键预言——磁碎裂——在准晶关联材料中的潜在实现。

Abstract: Magnetic ordering in quasicrystals has recently emerged as a fertile ground for discovering unconventional magnetic states beyond the framework of periodic crystals. However, elucidating the microscopic origin of such states remains challenging due to the intrinsic aperiodicity of quasicrystals. Here, we address this issue by investigating the prototypical Tsai-type quasicrystal approximant Cd6Tb, which preserves the essential local geometry and connectivity of icosahedral quasicrystals while allowing detailed structural and magnetic characterization due to its translational periodicity. Using neutron diffraction measurements, we find a noncoplanar multi-k magnetic ground state composed of Ising-like Tb moments arranged on a network of corner-sharing octahedra, the ingredients required to host octahedral spin-ice physics. Remarkably, only one third of the Tb moments develop long-range magnetic order, whereas the remaining moments display strongly reduced static order accompanied by persistent spin dynamics on microsecond timescales, as evidenced by muon spin rotation. This coexistence of ordered and fluctuating moments constitutes a potential realization of magnetic fragmentation - a key prediction of octahedral spin-ice physics - in a quasicrystal-related material.

</details>

### [55] [High Statistics Measurements of $ν_μ$ Charged-Current Single $π^{+}$ Production with Zero Pion Kinetic Energy Threshold in MINERvA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24224)
*E. Granados,B. Messerly,S. Akhter,M. Sajjad Athar,S. A. Dytman,J. Felix,L. Fields,P. K. Gaur,S. M. Gilligan,R. Gran,D. A. Harris,A. L. Hart,J. Kleykamp,A. Klustová,M. Kordosky,D. Last,S. Manly,W. A. Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该研究利用MINERvA探测器测量中微子-核子带电电流单π⁺产生过程的单微分截面，覆盖0–350 MeV动能范围，共选取91843个事件，并将结果与多个中微子事件生成器预测进行比较，发现现有模型在主相空间区域与数据存在显著偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中微子振荡实验（neutrino oscillation experiments）的精度提升依赖于对中微子-核子相互作用中单π⁺产生过程的准确建模，而现有事件生成器在关键相空间区域仍存在较大不确定性。

Method: 利用MINERvA探测器在费米实验室（Fermilab）获取数据，采用传统基于径迹（track-based）的π介子重建以及仅通过Michel电子衰变（Michel electron decays）识别π介子的方法，测量了动能范围为0–350 MeV的单π⁺产生截面，并基于W_exp < 1.4 GeV/c条件筛选出91843个事件。

Result: 微分截面（differential cross sections）作为π介子和缪子（muon）运动学变量的函数被呈现，与现代π产生模型（pion production models）在运动学区域末端基本一致，但在主相空间区域存在偏差：缪子观测量偏差高达15%，π介子观测量偏差高达20%。

Conclusion: 现有模型均无法充分描述任何变量，该结果凸显了下一代中微子振荡实验所需的模型改进方向。

Abstract: This Letter presents measurements of single-differential cross sections of $ν_μ$-induced charged-current 1 $π^{+}$ production on scintillator using the MINERvA detector at Fermilab. These measurements use traditional track-based pion reconstruction as well as pions identified solely via Michel electron decays, allowing measurement of kinetic energies from 0 to 350 MeV. In total, 91,843 events were selected with $W_{exp}$ $<$ 1.4 GeV/c. Differential cross sections as a function of pion and muon kinematic variables are presented and compared with the predictions of several neutrino event generators. Overall, modern pion production models tend to agree with data at the ends of the kinematic regions probed, but are discrepant with the main regions of the phase space probed by up to 15% in muon observables and up to 20% in pion observables. No model describes any of the variables well, and this result highlights model areas that require improvement for the next generation of neutrino oscillation experiments.

*Anne-Mazarine Lyon*

Conclusion: 这些结果充分利用了LHC Run 2及部分Run 3的数据，有效推动了味物理（flavour physics）测量精度的前沿进展，为检验标准模型和寻找新物理提供了重要实验依据。

Abstract: A review of recent results in flavour physics at the ATLAS and CMS experiments is presented. These include measurements of quarkonia and charm production cross sections, the B0 lifetime, and the mass splittings between excited and ground B meson states. Results targeting the characterisation of all-charm tetraquarks are also discussed. Finally, studies of rare heavy-flavour decays are reported. The various analyses exploit Run 2 and partial Run 3 LHC data and contribute to pushing the precision frontier in flavour physics.

### [57] [Search for low-mass resonances decaying to $ττ$ and measurement of the $Υ$ $\to$ $ττ$ decay in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13.6 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25103)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文利用CMS探测器在13.6 TeV质子-质子对撞数据中，对20–60 GeV质量范围内自旋零玻色子衰变至ττ对进行了首次全包容搜寻，并基于高率触发流（trigger stream）与新型低动量强子τ重建算法，首次在强子对撞机环境中以5.8σ显著性测量了Υ(1S,2S,3S) → τ⁺τ⁻过程，未发现超出标准模型背景的显著信号，在95%置信水平上设定了自旋零共振产生截面与ττ分支比乘积的上限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前20–60 GeV质量范围内自旋零玻色子衰变至ττ的搜寻尚属空白，且Υ(1S,2S,3S) → τ⁺τ⁻过程在强子对撞机环境中因低动量τ轻子重建困难而从未被直接测量。本文旨在填补这一质量区间的实验空白，并验证新型低动量τ重建算法的可行性。

Method: 使用CMS在2022–2023年采集的质心能量√s = 13.6 TeV、积分亮度61.9 fb⁻¹的质子-质子对撞数据。采用高率触发流（high-rate trigger stream）结合新型低动量强子τ重建算法（low-momentum hadronic tau reconstruction algorithm），针对20–60 GeV质量范围的自旋零共振（spin-zero boson）衰变至ττ过程进行全包容搜索。

Result: 在可见快度|y_vis| < 1.2、可见横动量p_T^vis > 15 GeV条件下，Υ(1S,2S,3S) → τ⁺τ⁻过程以5.8σ显著性被观测到，产生截面为3.5 ± 0.7 (stat) ± 0.7 (syst) nb。未观察到超出标准模型背景的显著信号，在95%置信水平上对自旋零共振产生截面与ττ分支比乘积设定了40–400 pb的上限。

Conclusion: 新型低动量τ重建算法成功使强子对撞机中低质量ττ共振的测量成为可能，但对20–60 GeV范围内的新自旋零玻色子未发现显著信号，所设上限对未来的新物理搜寻具有约束意义。

Abstract: An inclusive search is presented for spin-zero bosons decaying to $ττ$ in a previously unexplored mass range between 20 and 60 GeV using proton-proton collision data at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13.6 TeV, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 61.9 fb$^{-1}$ recorded by CMS in 2022$-$2023. A high-rate trigger stream in combination with a novel low-momentum hadronic tau reconstruction algorithm have enabled a measurement of the $Υ$(1S,2S,3S) $\to$ $τ^+τ^-$ process in the challenging environment of a hadron collider, with a 5.8$σ$ significance above background and production cross section of 3.5 $\pm$ 0.7 (stat) $\pm$ 0.7 (syst) nb for visible rapidity $\lvert y_{\text{vis}}\rvert$ $\lt$ 1.2 and visible transverse momentum $p_\mathrm{T}^\text{vis}$ $\gt$ 15 GeV. No significant excess above the standard model background is observed. Upper limits on the product of the spin-zero resonance production cross section and branching fraction to $ττ$ are set at 95% confidence level between 40 and 400 pb.

</details>


### [58] [Studies of Z $\to$ 4$\ell$ decays in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 8 and 13 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25158)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 基于CMS探测器在LHC上收集的质心能量8 TeV（积分亮度19.7 fb⁻¹）和13 TeV（积分亮度138 fb⁻¹）的质子-质子对撞数据，测量了Z玻色子衰变到四个带电轻子（电子和缪子）的分支比和微分衰变率，结果与标准模型预言一致，并用于限制新规范玻色子的产生。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精确测量Z玻色子到四轻子的稀有衰变，检验标准模型（Standard Model）预言的完整性，并寻找超出标准模型的新物理信号，例如新规范玻色子（new gauge bosons）的产生或电荷共轭-宇称（CP）不变性的可能破坏。

Method: 基于CMS探测器在LHC上收集的质子-质子对撞数据，质心能量$\sqrt{s}$ = 8 TeV（积分亮度19.7 fb⁻¹）和13 TeV（积分亮度138 fb⁻¹）。测量了Z → 4ℓ通道的包含性分支比以及各个子通道（Z → 4μ、Z → 4e、Z → 2μ2e）的分支比；在Z玻色子静止系中，构建了运动学和角量相关的微分衰变率，并进行了三乘积不对称性（triple-product asymmetries）测量以检验电荷共轭-宇称（CP）不变性。

Result: Z → 4ℓ的包含性分支比测量值为[4.67 ± 0.11（统计）± 0.10（系统）] × 10⁻⁶，精度约为3%，统计和系统不确定度相当。同时报告了各子通道的分支比测量结果、微分衰变率以及三乘积不对称性测量结果。所有测量结果与标准模型预言一致，并用于设定新规范玻色子产生的限制。

Conclusion: 该研究以约3%的精度首次在CMS实验上完成了Z → 4ℓ分支比的系统测量，验证了标准模型的可靠性；基于三乘积不对称性未观测到CP破坏迹象；所得限制有效约束了超出标准模型的新规范玻色子产生截面。

Abstract: Decays of Z bosons to four charged leptons (electrons and muons) are studied in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 8 and 13 TeV. The analysis is based on data collected with the CMS detector at the LHC corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 19.7 fb$^{-1}$ at 8 TeV and 138 fb$^{-1}$ at 13 TeV. The measured value of the inclusive branching fraction for all four-lepton decay modes, $\mathcal{B}$(Z $\to$ 4$\ell$), is [4.67 $\pm$ 0.11 (stat) $\pm$ 0.10 (syst)] $\times$ 10$^{-6}$, which has a precision of about 3% limited by both statistical and systematic uncertainties. Measurements of the individual branching fractions for the decays Z $\to$ 4$μ$, Z $\to$ 4e, and Z $\to$ 2$μ$2e are also reported. Differential decay rates are presented as functions of kinematic and angular quantities in the Z boson rest frame. Measurements of triple-product asymmetries, which are sensitive to possible violations of charge conjugation and parity invariance, are performed for Z $\to$ 4$\ell$ decays. The results are compared with standard model predictions and used to set limits on the production of new gauge bosons.

*Fakhar Ul Haider,Ramni Gupta,Salman Khurshid Malik,Balwan Singh,Zarina Banoo*

TL;DR: 该论文利用间歇性（intermittency）方法，通过分析归一化阶乘矩（normalized factorial moments）的标度行为，研究了PYTHIA和EPOS4（UrQMD ON/OFF）模拟下Pb-Pb碰撞中带电粒子数密度涨落的标度律与分形性质，并报告了与相变相关的标度指数及分形参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 带电粒子的大密度涨落被认为是探索重离子碰撞中QCD相变（phase transition）和临界点（critical point）的重要信号，这类涨落预期会表现出分形（fractal）和标度不变（scale invariant）行为，亟需通过间歇性方法进行定量探测。

Method: 采用间歇性方法，即研究归一化阶乘矩F_q随相空间划分（phase space partitioning）的缩小而呈现的幂律增长行为，并分析二阶矩（second order moments）的标度性质，以量化PYTHIA和EPOS4（UrQMD ON/OFF）两种模型在默认约束下的粒子产生特性。

Result: 报告了两种模型中与相变相关的标度指数（scaling exponent）以及与分形性质相关的参数（fractal nature parameters）。

Conclusion: 通过间歇性分析可以提取出反映相变和分形特征的标度指数与参数，从而在模拟层面量化重离子碰撞中带电粒子涨落的标度行为。

Abstract: Large density fluctuations of charged particles are the promising signatures for exploring the QCD phase transition and critical point in heavy ion collisions. These fluctuations are expected to exhibit fractal and scale invariant behaviour, which is probed using intermittency methodology. Intermittency is the phenomenon of power law growth of the normalized factorial moments ($F_{\rm{q}}$) of the number density distributions over decreasing bin size. This is studied for the charged particles simulated using PYTHIAN and EPOS4 (UrQMD ON/OFF) for Pb Pb collisions at $\sqrt{s_{\text{NN}}}$ = 5.02 TeV. Scaling behaviour of $F_{\rm{q}}$ are studied as a function of phase space partitioning and second order moments to quantify the particle production nature within the default constraints of the two models. The scaling exponent related to the phase transition and parameters connected to fractal nature obtained for these models are also reported.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 该方法预期能够抑制质子多重数涨落研究中的自相关效应，并且通过两个探测器的数据组合，可在全中心度范围内实现无歧义的中心度事件分类。

In this work, we propose a novel approach based on the combined use of signals from the forward hadron calorimeter (FHCal) and the electromagnetic calorimeter (ECal). This method is expected to suppress autocorrelation in the study of proton multiplicity fluctuations, while the combination of data from both detectors will enable unambiguous centrality event classification across the full centrality range.

### [61] [Methods for Centrality Determination Using Forward Detectors in the BM@N Experiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25729)
*Dim Idrisov,Fedor Guber,Nikolay Karpushkin,Peter Parfenov*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文改进了基于贝叶斯定理的带电粒子多重数中心度确定方法，提出了两种利用前向探测器（FHCal和石英闪烁体）的中心度确定方案，并在BM@N实验的Xe+CsI碰撞数据中与经典蒙特卡洛Glauber方法对比，验证了5%以内的一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 碰撞中心度（collision centrality）是研究核物质性质的关键参数，精确的中心度确定对于不同实验间的数据对比和理论模型基准检验至关重要。现有方法需要改进以更准确地估计事件注册效率并减少自关联效应（autocorrelation effects）。

Method: 基于贝叶斯定理（Bayes' theorem）改进了利用带电粒子多重数（charged particle multiplicity）确定中心度的方法，使得可以估算作为碰撞参数（impact parameter）函数的事件注册效率。此外提出了两种利用前向探测器的方案：一是结合径迹击中计数与前向强子量热器FHCal中旁观者沉积能量的二维方法，二是采用石英闪烁体（quartz hodoscope）与FHCal信号的方法。

Result: 上述方法被应用于BM@N实验首次物理运行中氙束流（xenon beam）能量为3.8 A GeV的Xe+CsI碰撞数据。与经典蒙特卡洛Glauber方法（Monte Carlo Glauber approach）的比较显示，所有方法在5%以内保持一致，验证了其可靠性和相互一致性。

Conclusion: 利用前向探测器进行中心度确定可作为评估初始碰撞几何的独立工具，并能减少质子多重数涨落研究中的自关联效应。所发展的方法可用于BM@N实验的数据处理，以及其它中等能量（intermediate energies）的重离子实验。

Abstract: Collision centrality is a key parameter for studying nuclear matter properties, as it determines the initial interaction geometry and the size of the produced system. Accurate centrality determination is essential for comparing experimental data obtained from different experiments and for benchmarking against theoretical models. This work presents a modification of the approach for centrality determination using charged particle multiplicity based on Bayes' theorem. The proposed improvements enable an estimation of event registration efficiency as a function of the impact parameter. Furthermore, two approaches utilizing forward detectors are proposed: a two-dimensional method based on the combined analysis of track hit counts and spectator deposited energy in the Forward Hadron Calorimeter FHCal, and a method employing signals from the quartz hodoscope and FHCal. These methods were applied to data from the first physics run Xe+CsI of the BM@N experiment (Baryonic Matter at Nuclotron) with a xenon beam at the energy of 3.8 A GeV. A comparison of the developed methods with the classical Monte Carlo Glauber approach demonstrates agreement within 5% across all considered methods, confirming their reliability and mutual consistency. The use of forward detectors for centrality determination may serve as an independent tool for assessing the initial collision geometry and can reduce autocorrelation effects in studies of proton multiplicity fluctuations. The developed approaches can be employed for data processing in the BM@N experiment, as well as in other heavy-ion experiments at intermediate energies.

### [62] [Pointwise behavior of SU(1,1) nonlinear Fourier transform](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25108)
*Sergey A. Denisov*

Main category: math.CA

TL;DR: 本文证明了SU(1,1)非线性傅里叶变换（NLFT）在平方可和系数下可能逐点发散，并由此推出单位圆上正交多项式的经典逐点渐近行为在Szegö类测度中可能失效，同时讨论了一些逐点收敛成立的特例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典理论认为，对于Szegö类（Szegö class）中的测度，单位圆上的正交多项式（orthogonal polynomials on the unit circle）具有逐点渐近行为。本文旨在考察该结论在更一般的条件下（即SU(1,1)非线性傅里叶变换框架下）是否依然成立。

Method: 通过分析SU(1,1)非线性傅里叶变换（nonlinear Fourier transform, NLFT）在平方可和（square-summable）系数条件下的逐点收敛性质，以此检验单位圆上正交多项式经典逐点渐近行为的稳健性。

Result: 发现SU(1,1) NLFT在平方可和系数条件下可以逐点发散；基于这一事实，证明了单位圆上正交多项式的经典逐点渐近行为在Szegö类测度中确实可以失败。

Conclusion: 经典逐点渐近结果在Szegö类测度中并非普遍成立，存在反例；但文中也识别了一些特殊条件下逐点收敛仍然成立的情形，为后续研究提供了边界条件。

Abstract: We show that SU(1,1) NLFT can diverge pointwise for square-summable coefficients. As a consequence, we prove that the classical pointwise asymptotics of polynomials orthogonal on the unit circle can fail for measures in the Szegö class. We also discuss some special cases when the pointwise convergence holds.

### [63] [DNA end tethering through break-induced DNA--protein condensation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24987)
*Rakesh Das,Tarun Mascarenhas,Nagaraja Chappidi,Simon Alberti,Frank Jülicher*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出DNA断裂末端可触发蛋白质从可溶态向凝聚态（condensate-competent state）转换，结合布朗动力学模拟（Brownian dynamics simulations）与理论分析，揭示了DNA-蛋白质凝聚体（DNA--protein condensate）可靠捕获断裂末端的物理机制，认为该过程由聚合物松弛与凝聚动力学之间的动力学竞争（kinetic competition）所决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DNA双链断裂（double-strand break）后，DNA-蛋白质凝聚体能够在断裂末端扩散前将其束缚在一起，这是后续修复生化过程的关键步骤；然而，在内在随机性（stochasticity）存在的情况下，这种凝聚如何可靠地在断裂位点实现时空定位并捕获双端，仍是一个未解之谜。

Method: 提出断裂末端触发蛋白质从可溶态向凝聚态转换的假设，并基于此构建布朗动力学模拟（Brownian dynamics simulations）与理论模型；通过模拟观察局部DNA-蛋白质凝聚的两种可能结果（成功或失败束缚），进而构建有效自由能景观（effective free energy landscape），识别对应的定态（stationary states）。

Result: 模拟表明，断裂诱导的蛋白质状态转换可驱动局部DNA-蛋白质凝聚，产生成功或失败两种束缚结果；进一步分析揭示束缚过程受聚合物松弛（polymer relaxation）与凝聚动力学（condensation dynamics）之间的动力学竞争（kinetic competition）所调控。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，DNA末端依赖性蛋白质状态转换与DNA-蛋白质凝聚过程相耦合，能够可靠地实现DNA断裂末端的束缚，从而为理解DNA损伤修复中的物理原理提供了机制性解释。

Abstract: Cells deploy robust mechanisms to repair DNA damage, safeguarding genomic stability and cellular health, but the physical principles underlying these processes remain incompletely understood. Experiments show \emph{in vitro} that upon a DNA double-strand break, a DNA--protein condensate can tether the broken DNA ends before they disperse away, a critical step for subsequent repair biochemistry. However, it remains puzzling how such condensation reliably achieves spatiotemporal localization at the break site and captures both broken ends despite intrinsic stochasticity. Here, we propose that broken DNA ends can trigger a conversion of proteins from a soluble state to a condensate-competent state. Combining this idea with Brownian dynamics simulations and theory, we propose a physical mechanism for reliable DNA-end tethering. Simulations show that such break-induced conversion can drive local DNA--protein condensation with two possible outcomes: successful or failed tethering. To rationalize this, we construct an effective free energy landscape, identify the corresponding stationary states, and demonstrate that tethering is governed by a kinetic competition between polymer relaxation and condensation dynamics. Together, our study shows that DNA end-dependent conversion, coupled with DNA--protein condensation, can reliably tether broken DNA ends.

</details>


### [64] [Hydrodynamics constrain choanoflagellate collar geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25337)
*Tasawar Iqbal,Catherine Penington,Christian Thomas,Lyndon Koens*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过构建简化降阶模型，研究水力约束如何影响领鞭毛虫（choanoflagellate）微绒毛领（microvilli collar）的几何结构。研究发现物种间压降存在显著差异，且微绒毛半径与间隙的相空间中存在通量脊和耗散脊，不同物种围绕这些脊状结构聚类，表明其几何结构受最大化通量与最小化耗散之间的竞争驱动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 领鞭毛虫作为动物现存最近亲，其微绒毛领在种间呈现显著多样性，已有水动力学研究暗示不同物种的压降相似。本文旨在探究水力约束是否对领鞭毛虫微绒毛领施加额外的几何限制，并揭示种间几何多样性背后可能的物理机制。

Method: 作者构建了一个忽略有限领长的简化降阶模型（reduced-order model），用于研究微绒毛半径（microvillus radius）与微绒毛间间隙（gap）对流体流动的影响。通过将模型预测与生物学观测数据对比，分析压降、有效通量（effective flux）和功率耗散（power dissipation）在相空间中的分布。

Result: 模型揭示微绒毛半径-间隙相空间中出现一条脊状结构（ridge），沿该脊有效通量和功率耗散均达到最大化。多个物种在通量脊附近聚集，但远离功率耗散脊。此外，不同物种间的压降存在显著差异，而非之前认为的相似。

Conclusion: 领鞭毛虫微绒毛领的几何结构并非遵循统一的压降特征，而是受最大化通量与最小化功率消耗这对竞争需求的共同影响。脊状结构的存在使得种间广泛的几何变异成为可能，体现了水力约束与适应性权衡的协同作用。

Abstract: As the closest living relatives of animals, choanoflagellates exhibit remarkable diversity. Even their microvilli collar, used to filter and capture food, varies significantly among species. This diversity suggests either strong environmental adaptation or an insensitivity to the collar geometry. Previous hydrodynamic studies have suggested that the pressure change across the collar is similar across species. In this study, we show that hydrodynamics imposes additional geometric constraints on the choanoflagellate collar. We create a simplified, reduced-order model that neglects finite collar length to investigate how the microvillus radius and the gap between microvilli influence the flow. Comparing with biological data reveals significant variation in the pressure drop between species. Additionally, a ridge emerges in the microvilli radius-gap phase space, along which both effective flux and power dissipation are maximised. Notably, several species cluster near the flux ridge but lie away from the power dissipation ridge. These observations suggest that choanoflagellate collars do not necessarily share a similar pressure drop. Instead, their geometry is influenced by the competing demands of maximising flux and minimising power costs. The broad variation observed among species is made possible by these ridge-like structures.

</details>

### [65] [Anderson Localization: A Floquet operator Krylov space perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24115)
*Hsiu-Chung Yeh,Aditi Mitra*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文利用算子Krylov空间方法研究Anderson局域化及Aubry-André模型的单粒子局域化-去局域化相变，证明在离散时间（stroboscopic）动力学下可映射为有效的Floquet问题，从而更高效地计算谱函数等物理量。研究发现，去局域化（局域化）相对应于Porter-Thomas分布的出现（缺失）、波前在Krylov空间中的弹道传播（局域）以及光滑（离散）的Berstein-Szegö功率谱，且在临界点处观察到多分形标度行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Anderson局域化（Anderson localization）及Aubry-André模型中的单粒子局域化-去局域化相变（localization-delocalization transition）是凝聚态物理中的核心问题。本文旨在探索利用算子Krylov空间方法（operator Krylov space methods）研究该问题的新途径，特别关注离散时间（stroboscopic）动力学相较于连续时间动力学的优势。

Method: 将连续时间动力学映射为有效的Floquet问题（effective Floquet problem），从而在算子Krylov空间中描述动力学过程。存在一种矩方法（moment method），可直接从离散时间自相关函数（discrete time autocorrelation function）提取Krylov参数。对于离散时间动力学，算子Krylov空间对应于非均匀Floquet横场Ising模型（inhomogeneous Floquet transverse field Ising model）的边算符动力学，有效模型参数通过递归方式生成。

Result: Krylov参数表现出无序平均的重整化（disorder-averaged renormalization），且随递归步数增加其分布变窄。从无序平均自相关函数获得的Krylov参数比无序平均Krylov参数能导出更物理的谱函数。去局域化相应于Porter-Thomas分布（Porter-Thomas distribution）的出现、Krylov空间中弹道传播的波前（ballistically propagating wavefront）以及光滑的Berstein-Szegö功率谱；局域化相则表现为这些特征的缺失。临界点附近也观察到Porter-Thomas分布，且长时间动力学和反参与比（inverse participation ratio）表现出与系统尺寸相关的多分形标度（multi-fractal scaling）行为。

Conclusion: 算子Krylov空间方法能够有效描述和区分局域化与去局域化相，并通过谱函数、波前传播特性及功率谱结构等物理可观测量明确揭示局域化-去局域化相变。临界点处的多分形行为进一步验证了该方法的有效性。

Abstract: The problem of Anderson localization, as well as the single particle localization-delocalizaton transition of the Aubry-André model, is studied employing operator Krylov space methods. It is shown that even when the dynamics is generated by a Hamiltonian, studying the dynamics at stroboscopic rather than continuous times has its advantages. In particular, mapping the dynamics to an effective Floquet problem results in an operator Krylov space description where quantities such as the spectral function can be computed with fewer computational resources, while a moment method exists that allows for the extraction of Krylov parameters directly from the discrete time autocorrelation function. For stroboscopic dynamics, the operator Krylov space corresponds to the dynamics of an edge operator of an inhomogeneous Floquet transverse field Ising model, with the parameters of this effective model generated recursively. The Krylov parameters show disorder-averaged renormalization with their distribution narrowing as the recursion step increases. It is shown that a more physical spectral function is obtained from the Krylov parameters obtained from the disorder-averaged autocorrelation function, rather than the disorder-averaged Krylov parameters. The delocalized (localized) phase is shown to correspond to the appearance (absence) of a Porter-Thomas distribution, a ballistically propagating (localized) wavefront in operator Krylov space, and a smooth (discrete) Berstein-Szegö power-spectrum. The localization-delocalization transition is also demonstrated in operator Krylov space. A Porter-Thomas distribution is also observed at the critical point. The long-time dynamics and the inverse participation ratio at the critical point is shown to exhibit behavior consistent with a multi-fractal scaling with system size.

</details>


### [66] [Lateral Shift as a Control Knob for Localization Transitions in a Quasiperiodic Ladder](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25033)
*Bing Shao,Guangjie Zhang,Longwen Zhou,Jiangbin Gong,Weiwei Zhu*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文报道了准周期梯子（quasiperiodic ladder）中由两条腿之间的横向偏移（lateral shift）引起的丰富局域化-去局域化转变现象，横向偏移可在倒易动量空间中有效产生磁通量，从而实现对局域化行为的调控。作者基于能带结构分析（band-structure analysis）和可公度近似（commensurate approximation），定性和定量地理解了相边界与物理机制，为实现可调局域化平台提供了理论和计算基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准周期系统中的局域化-去局域化转变是一个重要的物理问题，但如何在单一平台上灵活且系统地调控这类转变仍具有挑战性。本文旨在探索由准周期梯子中两条腿之间的横向偏移所引入的有效磁通量对局域化行为的影响，并建立相应的理论框架。

Method: 使用可公度近似（commensurate approximation）将准周期势近似为周期势，从而在有限尺寸元胞下进行能带结构分析（band-structure analysis）。通过调节两条腿之间的横向偏移来模拟有效磁通量的变化，并研究局域化、混合相和扩展相之间的相边界。

Result: 横向偏移在倒易动量空间中有效产生磁通量，从而实现了三种物理现象：磁通增强的局域化（magnetic-flux-enhanced localization）、磁通抑制的局域化（magnetic-flux-suppressed localization）、以及磁通诱导的再入式局域化转变（magnetic-flux-induced reentrant localization transitions）。相边界和物理机制得到了定性和定量解释。

Conclusion: 该准周期梯子为探索局域化物理提供了一个高度可调的平台，具有量子开关等应用前景；同时，基于能带结构分析与可公度近似的方法为准周期系统中的局域化-去局域化转变提供了广泛适用的理论工具。

Abstract: This work reports rich localization-delocalization transitions in a quasiperiodic ladder, of which the two legs are subject to the same quasiperiodic onsite potential but can be shifted laterally relative to each other. It is found that the lateral shift between the two legs effectively generates a magnetic flux in the reciprocal momentum space. The lateral shift thus offers a control knob, allowing us to access and simulate rich phenomena including magnetic-flux-enhanced localization, magnetic-flux-suppressed localization, and magnetic-flux-induced reentrant localization transitions. The underlying physical mechanisms as well as the phase boundaries separating localized, mixed, and extended phases are both qualitatively and quantitatively understood, based on a band-structure analysis that employs a commensurate approximation to the quasiperiodic potential, requiring only unit cells of small to modest sizes. Our work provides a highly tunable platform for exploring localization physics with promising applications such as quantum switching, and a broadly applicable approach for understanding localization-delocalization transitions in quasiperiodic systems.

</details>


### [67] [Topological metal-insulator transitions in one-dimensional non-Hermitian quasicrystals: beyond PT-symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25072)
*Guangjie Zhang,Bing Shao,Longwen Zhou,Jiangbin Gong,Weiwei Zhu*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该论文提出一个不保留PT对称性的非厄米准周期模型，证明在大多数参数区域中系统支持包含局域化、拓扑和简并破缺的三重相变，扩展了PT对称系统中拓扑金属-绝缘体转变的研究至更一般的非厄米情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 具有PT对称性的一维非厄米准晶（non-Hermitian quasicrystals）可同时展示局域化-退局域化转变、拓扑相变和PT对称性破缺转变。该工作旨在探究当PT对称性缺失时，这些相变在非厄米准晶中如何发生变化。

Method: 提出一个一般不保留PT对称性的非厄米准周期模型（non-Hermitian quasiperiodic model），通过分析不同参数区域中的局域化、拓扑以及简并破缺（degeneracy-breaking）行为来研究相变特性。

Result: 在大部分参数区域中，系统支持三重的相变（triple phase transitions），涵盖局域化、拓扑和简并破缺；此外，在特定参数条件下，系统可展现出类似于厄米情形（Hermitian case）的纯局域化-退局域化转变，而不伴随拓扑相变或简并破缺转变。

Conclusion: 该工作将先前在PT对称系统中研究的拓扑金属-绝缘体转变（topological metal-insulator transitions）扩展至更一般的非厄米体系，并揭示了非厄米系统可以承载不同类型的局域化行为。

Abstract: One-dimensional non-Hermitian quasicrystals with parity and time-reversal (PT) symmetry can simultaneously exhibit localization-delocalization transition, topological phase transition, and PT-symmetry-breaking transition. This motivates this work to investigate how the absence of PT symmetry impacts topological metal-insulator transitions in non-Hermitian quasicrystals. We propose a non-Hermitian quasiperiodic model that generally does not preserve PT symmetry and demonstrate that, in most parameter regions, such a system supports triple phase transitions that encompass localization, topology, and degeneracy-breaking. The system may also exhibit a particular type of localization-delocalization transition analogous to the Hermitian case, namely, without activating topological phase transitions or degeneracy-breaking transitions. Our work extends the topological metal-insulator transitions previously studied in PT-symmetric systems to a more general class of non-Hermitian setting, and further reveals that non-Hermitian systems can host distinct types of localization behavior.

</details>


### [68] [Sensitivity to perturbations in the three-dimensional Anderson model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25594)
*Piotr Tokarczyk,Lev Vidmar,Anatoli Polkovnikov,Patrycja Łydżba*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文通过研究三维安德森模型（Anderson model）中的保真度磁化率（fidelity susceptibility），发现该物理量随无序强度（disorder strength）W的变化会出现两个不同的峰：第一个峰对应弱无序下的交叉行为，第二个峰精确对应于安德森局域化转变（Anderlson localization transition）的临界点，并揭示了两个峰的散度标度行为差异及其与非遍历性（nonergodic behavior）的关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 保真度磁化率能够量化单粒子本征态对微扰的敏感性，本文旨在通过这一工具深入理解三维安德森模型中的无序诱导的局域化转变及其相关的量子混沌（quantum chaos）与非遍历行为。

Method: 本文对三维安德森模型进行数值研究，计算保真度磁化率作为无序强度W的函数，分析其峰值位置和散度标度；同时研究安德森转变以上区域中典型保真度磁化率的标度行为，以区分不同的非遍历性区域。

Result: 保真度磁化率在弱无序区出现第一个峰，标志着从平面波态到单粒子量子混沌的交叉，其在热力学极限下位置趋近于W→0；第二个峰高精度地位于安德森局域化转变临界无序强度处。第一个峰呈最大散度（maximal divergence），标度为频率截止平方的倒数；第二个峰呈次最大散度（submaximal divergence），该抑制与临界点单粒子本征态的分形结构（fractal structure）有关。在安德森转变以上区域，典型保真度磁化率的标度行为揭示出两种不同的非遍历性区域。

Conclusion: 保真度磁化率中的两个峰分别对应量子混沌交叉与局域化转变临界点，且其散度标度差异可归因于临界态的分形性质；此外，安德森局域化转变以上的非遍历行为存在两个不同的区域，为无序系统的相图提供了更精细的刻画。

Abstract: We investigate the fidelity susceptibility, which quantifies the sensitivity of single-particle eigenstates to perturbations, in the three-dimensional Anderson model. As a function of disorder strength $W$, it exhibits two distinct peaks. The first peak signals a crossover at weak disorder strength from plane-wave states to single-particle quantum chaos, and its position shifts toward $W\to 0$ in the thermodynamic limit. The second peak emerges, to high numerical accuracy, at the critical disorder strength associated with the Anderson localization transition. We further show that the divergence of the first peak is maximal, scaling as the square of the inverse frequency cutoff, whereas the divergence of the second peak is submaximal. We relate the latter suppression to the fractal structure of single-particle eigenstates at criticality. We discuss two distinct scenarios that give rise to the peaks in the fidelity susceptibilities. Moreover, studying the scaling of typical fidelity susceptibilities above the Anderson transition, we find evidence of two distinct regimes of nonergodic behavior.

</details>


### [69] [Spectral properties of non-Hermitian real random matrices with long-range correlations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25736)
*Ulysse Marquis*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本论文研究了具有长程相关性（decaying as |r-r'|^{-α}）的非厄米实随机矩阵（non-Hermitian real random matrices）的谱性质，发现圆律（circular law）随 α 减小而逐渐失效，并在 α < 1 时出现谱半径（spectral radius）的幂律增长，揭示了一个由相关性驱动的相变（correlation-driven transition）及新的普适类（universality class）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索非厄米随机矩阵中长程相关性（long-range correlations）对谱性质的影响，特别是圆律在何种条件下被破坏，以及是否存在新的普适行为。

Method: 通过数值和解析手段，分析矩阵元具有幂律衰减长程相关性（decaying as |r-r'|^{-α}）的非厄米实随机矩阵的特征值分布（eigenvalue distribution），考察径向密度（radial eigenvalue density）、谱半径（spectral radius）随矩阵大小和参数 α 的变化。

Result: 径向特征值密度从原点向外递减。α > 1 时存在与圆律相似的有效半径（effective radius）；α < 1 时特征值分布随矩阵大小展宽，谱半径以幂律方式增长，幂指数数值上接近扩展中心极限定理（extended central limit theorem）中的涨落控制指数。α = 1 时出现自相似（self-similar）的特征值密度和缓慢增长的谱半径。长程相关性还增强实数特征值的聚集并减缓土星效应（Saturn effect）的消退。

Conclusion: 长程相关性在非厄米随机矩阵中驱动了一个从圆律行为到幂律展宽行为的相变，暗示了相关非厄米随机矩阵存在一个新的普适类（universality class）。

Abstract: We investigate the spectral properties of non-Hermitian real random matrices whose entries exhibit long-range correlations decaying as~$|r-r'|^{-α}$. We find a progressive breakdown of the circular law, controlled by the decrease of~$α$. In all cases, the radial eigenvalue density decreases away from the origin. At~$α>1$, an effective radius, reminiscent of the circular law, is retrieved, while instead, for~$α<1$, the eigenvalue distribution broadens with matrix size and its spectral radius grows like a power law, with exponents numerically close to the exponents controlling the magnitude of fluctuations in the extended central limit theorem. The case~$α=1$ appears as a case with self-similar eigenvalue density, and slowly growing spectral radius. Long-range correlations also enhance clustering of real eigenvalues and slow the resorption of the Saturn effect. These results reveal a correlation-driven transition and suggest the emergence of a new universality class for correlated non-Hermitian random matrices.

</details>


### [70] [Cluster moves with an entropic reservoir accelerate low-temperature simulations of three-dimensional spin glasses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25872)
*Claudio Chilin,Enzo Marinari,Víctor Martín-Mayor,Giorgio Parisi,Juan J. Ruiz-Lorenzo,David Yllanes*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 提出一种结合平行回火、Houdayer移动和熵库（PTHR）的三维自旋玻璃低温模拟算法，在$L=16$、高斯耦合、$T\geq 0.2$条件下实现高效平衡，计算复杂度优于标准平行回火，速度提升约64倍，且复杂度与温度混沌（temperature chaos）密切相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三维自旋玻璃（spin glass）在低温相（low-temperature phase）的数值模拟面临严重的平衡困难，现有算法（如标准平行回火和团簇算法）在计算效率和规模扩展性上存在局限，亟需更具扩展性的高效模拟方法。

Method: 提出平行回火增强算法PTHR（Parallel Tempering enhanced with Houdayer moves and entropic reservoir），在标准平行回火（Parallel Tempering）框架中引入Houdayer移动和熵库（entropic reservoir）；与标准Houdayer算法相比改动较小，但显著提升了低温下的采样效率。

Result: 在$L=16$格点、高斯耦合（Gaussian couplings）、温度$T\geq 0.2$条件下成功平衡大量样本；计算复杂度的尺寸标度（size scaling）优于标准平行回火；相比其他团簇算法（cluster algorithms），可获得约64倍的加速比。

Conclusion: PTHR是一种高效的三维自旋玻璃低温模拟方法，其计算复杂度与温度混沌（temperature chaos）紧密相关，这一特性与标准平行回火类似，为理解自旋玻璃的低温行为提供了新的数值工具。

Abstract: We present an algorithm for the simulation of three-dimensional spin glasses deep in the low-temperature phase: Parallel Tempering enhanced with Houdayer moves and with an entropic reservoir (PTHR). Although differences with the standard Houdayer algorithm are small, PTHR allows us to equilibrate a large number of samples of $L=16$ lattices with Gaussian couplings for temperatures $T\geq 0.2$. We show that the computational complexity displays better size scaling than standard Parallel Tempering. For finite sizes, our method outperforms other cluster algorithms by a speedup factor of around 64. In close analogy with standard Parallel Tempering, PTHR's computational complexity strongly relates to temperature chaos.

</details>

### [71] [Supersymmetry Without Time-Reversal Invariance in Model A: A FRG perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24029)
*Sankarshan Sahu,Bertrand Delamotte,Adam Rançon,Matthieu Tissier*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文揭示了在Model A动力学中，超对称性（supersymmetry）本身并不足以确保系统弛豫至满足时间反演不变性（TRI）的稳态，并指出了所需的附加条件。通过具体反例模型、泛函重整化群（FRG）分析以及伊辛模型（Ising model）的应用，论证了时间反演不变性在大尺度上作为有效对称性涌现，并建立了动力学有效作用量与平衡态有效作用量之间的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 挑战一个普遍持有的观点：在Model A动力学中，超对称性单独是否足以保证系统最终弛豫至满足时间反演不变性（TRI）的稳态。论文旨在检验这一假设并澄清超对称性与TRI之间的精确关系。

Method: 通过构造一个具有超对称性但违反TRI的显式反例模型来论证；利用泛函重整化群（FRG）分析动力学有效作用量 $\Gamma[\varphi,\tilde\varphi]$ 与平衡态有效作用量 $\Gamma^{\mathrm{eq}}[\varphi]$ 之间的关系，证明后者在导数展开中各阶次的RG流与平衡理论相同。

Result: 超对称性不是保证TRI的充分条件，需要额外的附加条件；尽管存在违反TRI的超对称模型，但在微扰意义下TRI仍作为大尺度有效对称性涌现；动力学有效作用量包含平衡态有效作用量的导数项，且后者的RG流与平衡理论一致；伊辛模型总磁化强度的概率分布可以在Model A框架内恢复。

Conclusion: 约化模型（Model A）中超对称性与时间反演不变性之间的关系比先前认为的更复杂，但大尺度上TRI的有效涌现仍然成立，且动力学与平衡态理论之间存在深刻联系。

Abstract: We show that, contrary to common belief, supersymmetry alone is not sufficient in Model A dynamics to ensure relaxation toward a stationary state satisfying time-reversal invariance (TRI). An additional condition on top of supersymmetry is required for TRI, which we analyze in detail. We explicitly construct a model that is supersymmetric but violates TRI, and argue that, at least perturbatively, TRI nevertheless emerges as an effective large-scale symmetry. Using the functional renormalization group (FRG), we further show that the dynamical effective action, $Γ[\varphi,\tilde\varphi]$, contains the derivative of the equilibrium effective action, $Γ^{\mathrm{eq}}[\varphi]$, whose renormalization-group flow is identical to that of the equilibrium theory order by order in the derivative expansion. Finally, extending the same line of reasoning, we show that the probability distribution of the total magnetization in the Ising model can be recovered within the Model A framework.

</details>


### [72] [Universal classification of continuous phase transitions with two order parameters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24061)
*Yilun Xu,Feng-xiao Sun*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 基于金兹堡-朗道（Ginzburg-Landau）范式，本文通过自由能耦合项对具有两个序参量（order parameter）的系统进行分类，揭示了不同耦合模式下相图（phase diagram）与临界标度（critical scaling）的多样性，为复杂系统的研究提供了新路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典的金兹堡-朗道范式虽能很好地描述单一序参量（order parameter）的连续相变（continuous phase transition），但实际系统中常存在两个或更多序参量，其相图与临界现象（critical phenomena）远比单一序参量系统丰富，缺乏系统的分类框架。

Method: 依据自由能（free energy）中序参量之间的耦合项（coupling terms）对具有两个序参量的系统进行分类，并分析不同耦合类型下所对应的相图模式与临界标度行为。

Result: 将双序参量系统划分为若干类别，每类分别呈现出不同的相图模式与临界标度特征。

Conclusion: 仅基于自由能表达中的耦合项即可对复杂系统进行分类与研究，为理解和评估具有多个序参量的复杂系统提供了新途径。

Abstract: The continuous phase transition, indicated by the macroscopic order parameter and the occurrence of the spontaneous symmetry breaking, is well illustrated based on the Ginzburg-Landau's paradigm. In systems described by one order parameter, the phase diagram is only composed of the normal phase and the ordered phase. However, in systems with two or more order parameters, much richer phase diagrams and critical phenomena may emerge. According to coupling terms of the free energy, we classify the systems with two order parameters into several categories, featuring different patterns of phase diagrams and critical scalings respectively. Our work propose the new avenue to studying and evaluating the complex systems only based on the coupling terms in expressions of free energy.

</details>


### [73] [Theory of supercooled water](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24105)
*Jacobo Troncoso,Claudio A. Cerdeiriña*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出一个过冷水模型，通过数值解再现了从Speedy-Angell稳定极限图像到Poole等人的亚稳态液-液临界性，并基于与焦耳-汤姆逊气体节流过程的“逆转变热力学”以及黑洞等效现象学的类比，为液-液临界点（liquid-liquid critical point）的真实存在提供了理论依据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出一个能够描述过冷液体状态的模型，该状态相对于晶体固体是亚稳态的（metastable）；通过数值求解该模型获得结果；并引入与焦耳-汤姆逊气体节流过程（Joule-Thomson gas throttling process）的“逆转变热力学”（inversion thermodynamics）以及黑洞（black holes）等效现象学的类比分析。

Result: 数值解同时再现了Speedy-Angell的稳定极限图像（stability-limit picture）和Poole等人的亚稳态液-液临界性；发现液-液临界点的真实存在从与焦耳-汤姆逊过程的类比中获得了显著的理论可信度。

Conclusion: 液-液临界点的真实存在具有重要的理论合理性，该合理性源于一个迄今未被注意的类比，涉及焦耳-汤姆逊过程的逆转变热力学及其在黑洞现象学中的延伸。

Abstract: We introduce a model of water contemplating true supercooled-liquid states that, as such, are metastable with respect to the crystalline-solid ones. Its numerical solutions reproduce from Speedy-Angell's stability-limit picture to Poole et al.'s metastable liquid--liquid criticality. The real existence of a liquid--liquid critical point is found to gain significant theoretical plausibility from a hitherto unnoticed analogy with the ``inversion thermodynamics'' of Joule-Thomson gas throttling process and, by extension, with the equivalent phenomenology exhibited by black holes.
