### [74] [Long-range correlations in a locally constrained exclusion process](https://arxiv.org/abs/2503.12632)
*Stefan Großkinsky,Gunter Schütz,Ali Zahra*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出一种具有简单局域动力学约束（local kinetic constraint）的新型排斥过程（exclusion process），该过程展现出从短程关联（short-range correlations）的均匀相（homogeneous phase）到长程关联（long-range correlations）且自发破缺平移不变性（spontaneous breaking of translation invariance）的成簇相（clustered phase）的显著相变。粒子团簇的亚稳动力学（metastable dynamics）引发了粗化级联（coarsening cascade）和玻璃态动力学（glassy dynamics），并产生了一个有趣的“越快越慢”（faster-is-slower）效应——流向不对称性增加反而导致稳态流（stationary current）减小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索简单局域动力学约束如何导致非平衡系统中出现非平凡的相变行为，包括长程关联、平移对称性自发破缺以及反常动力学现象。

Method: 引入一种新颖的排斥过程（exclusion process），其核心是设置简单的局域动力学约束（local kinetic constraint），通过该约束调控粒子运动和团簇形成。

Result: 发现了均匀相到成簇相的相变，其中成簇相具有长程关联和自发平移对称性破缺；团簇的亚稳动力学导致粗化级联和玻璃态动力学；观察到“越快越慢”效应，即流向不对称性增大反而降低稳态流。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了简单局域约束如何在非平衡系统中引发复杂的集体行为，为理解玻璃态动力学和反常输运现象提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: We introduce a novel exclusion process with a simple local kinetic constraint that leads to a remarkable transition between a homogeneous phase with short-range correlations and a clustered phase with long-range correlations and spontaneous breaking of translation invariance. The metastable dynamics of particle clusters lead to a coarsening cascade and glassy dynamics, as well as an intriguing faster-is-slower effect where an increasing asymmetry in the flow direction leads to a decrease of the stationary current.

</details>


### [75] [Resonant interactions in the $α$-FPUT lattice with site-dependent coefficients](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24268)
*Lorenzo Migliorelli,Giovanni Dematteis,Sergio Chibbaro,Miguel Onorato*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文将波湍流（wave turbulence）框架推广到具有空间依赖系数的α-FPUT问题，推导出新的动力学方程（kinetic equation）。该方程表明热化（thermalization）速度可能显著快于常系数情形，并包含一个与布拉格散射（Bragg scattering）机制相关的额外项，促进波作用谱密度函数（wave-action spectral density function）的各向同性化（isotropization）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 波湍流框架已被证明是分析一维非线性链中非线性能量转移特征的有效工具，但此前尚未被应用于系数随空间位置变化的α-FPUT问题。本文旨在将该框架扩展至弹簧刚度χ和非线性系数α具有空间依赖性的情形。

Method: 基于波湍流框架，针对空间调制（spatial modulation）下的α-FPUT问题，分析三波相互作用（three-wave interactions）的共振条件。尽管常系数情形下三波相互作用是非共振的，但空间调制导致非平凡共振流形（non-trivial resonant manifold），并由此推导新的动力学方程。

Result: 推导出新的动力学方程，该方程暗示热化速度可能显著快于常系数情形。方程中还包含一个可归因于布拉格散射机制的额外项，该机制促进波作用谱密度函数的各向同性化。

Conclusion: 空间依赖系数条件下的波湍流框架能描述更快的热化过程，布拉格散射机制的引入为理解波作用谱的各向同性化提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: The wave turbulence framework has proven to be an effective tool for analyzing certain features of nonlinear energy transfer in one-dimensional nonlinear chains. In this work, we extend this approach to the $α$-FPUT problem when the spring stiffness $χ$ and the nonlinear coefficient $α$ are site-dependent. Although three-wave interactions are non-resonant for constant coefficients, their spatial modulation gives rise to a non-trivial resonant manifold. In this framework, we derive a new kinetic equation that suggests the possibility of substantially faster thermalization with respect to the constant coefficient case. The new kinetic equation includes also an extra term that can be associated to the Bragg-scattering mechanism, which promotes the isotropization of the wave-action spectral density function.

### [76] [Streaming Molecular Dynamics Simulation Data for On-the-fly Processing and Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24271)
*Amruthesh Thirumalaiswamy,Lawson J. Woods,Heekun Cho,Hugo MacDermott-Opeskin,Jennifer Clark,Irfan Alibay,Yuxuan Zhuang,Oliver Beckstein,Matthias Heyden*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种面向全原子多微秒分子动力学（MD）模拟的数据流框架（streaming framework），通过扩展交互式分子动力学（IMD）协议为IMDv3，并集成到GROMACS、NAMD、LAMMPS等主流MD软件包中，结合Python包imdclient和MDAnalysis接口，实现对模拟数据的实时访问与分析，避免了传统高频轨迹存储带来的数据丢失与存储瓶颈问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在全原子多微秒分子动力学（MD）模拟中，飞秒级积分步长产生的海量数据（PB量级）远超实际存储能力，导致只能以10-100 ps间隔保存部分帧。这种方式虽然足以分析系综平均和慢动力学，但丢弃了分子振动、溶剂动力学、短寿命过渡态及输运现象等快速过程的微观信息，而这些信息与宏观性质和实验可观测量直接相关。

Method: 本文提出一个流式框架（streaming framework），核心创新包括：(1) 扩展交互式分子动力学（IMD）协议为IMDv3，允许实时访问模拟数据；(2) 在GROMACS、NAMD和LAMMPS三个主流MD软件包中实现IMDv3；(3) 开发Python包imdclient，接收IMDv3数据流并对外暴露接口；(4) 在MDAnalysis包中增加基于imdclient的读取器，使流式模拟数据可与传统轨迹文件协同分析。

Result: 基准测试结果表明，流式方法相比高频轨迹输出方式具有性能优势。示例应用展示了流式框架在实时监测自定义变量、快速振荡的速度时间相关函数（velocity time-correlation function）评估以及膜孔电流实时分析等场景中的有效性。

Conclusion: 该流式框架为全原子MD模拟提供了一种替代传统轨迹存储的新范式，能够在无需写入磁盘的前提下实时访问所有生成的模拟数据，同时兼顾计算性能。该方法有望弥合MD模拟中快速微观过程数据丢失的缺口，促进模拟与实验可观测量之间的直接关联。

Abstract: Only a small fraction of the data generated in state-of-the-art all-atom multi-microsecond molecular dynamics (MD) simulations is typically analyzed. With femtosecond integration steps, microsecond simulations generate billions of time steps containing atomic positions, velocities, and forces, often corresponding to petabytes of data. Since this exceeds practical storage capacities, only a subset of frames is usually written to trajectory files at intervals of 10-100 ps. While sufficient for ensemble averages and slow dynamics, this approach discards information on fast processes such as molecular vibrations, solvent dynamics, short-lived transition states, and transport phenomena that are directly related to macroscopic properties and experimental observables. Here, we introduce a streaming framework for MD simulations that provides direct access to all data generated during a running simulation. Instead of writing high-frequency output to disk, the framework enables user-defined analysis and processing routines to access simulation data in real time. To achieve this, we extend the Interactive Molecular Dynamics (IMD) protocol and implement an enhanced version, termed IMDv3, in the MD packages GROMACS, NAMD, and LAMMPS. We further introduce the Python package imdclient, which receives IMDv3 data streams and exposes them to external applications. To maximize usability, we add an imdclient-based reader to the MDAnalysis package, enabling streamed simulation data to be analyzed alongside conventional trajectory files. Benchmark results show that streaming can improve performance compared to simulations with high-frequency trajectory output. Example applications include live monitoring of custom variables, evaluation of velocity time-correlation functions with fast fluctuations, and real-time analysis of membrane pore currents.

</details>


### [77] [Thermodynamics of classifiers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24365)
*Yoshihiko Hasegawa*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本研究推导了二元分类器（binary classifier）中分类误差与热力学成本（thermodynamic cost）之间的基本权衡关系，证明当熵产生（entropy production）或动力学活性（dynamical activity）为零时，贝叶斯误差（Bayes error）达到1/2（即随机猜测），而更大的热力学成本允许更低的误差。文章还讨论了量子推广，指出量子分类器的贝叶斯误差受哈密顿量方差（variance of the Hamiltonian）的下界约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着计算能耗持续增长，近似计算（approximate computing）受到广泛关注，其核心理念是通过牺牲计算精度来降低能耗。这引出了一个基本问题：信息处理中误差与热力学成本之间究竟存在何种关系？本研究旨在从热力学角度回答这一问题。

Method: 基于马尔可夫过程（Markov processes）对二元分类（binary classification）进行建模，从热力学量（熵产生和动力学活性）出发推导贝叶斯误差的下界（lower bounds）。

Result: 推导出贝叶斯误差的热力学下界：当熵产生或动力学活性为零时，贝叶斯误差达到1/2（等同于随机猜测）；热力学成本越大，可实现的最低误差越低。在量子情形下，量子分类器的贝叶斯误差受哈密顿量方差的下界约束。

Conclusion: 在热力学系统中，信息处理存在误差与成本之间的基本权衡（fundamental trade-off）。由于贝叶斯误差是所有可能分类器所能达到的最低误差，给定熵产生或动力学活性时，分类误差无法低于所得到的下界。这一结果为近似计算中的能耗-精度权衡提供了热力学层面的理论约束。

Abstract: The Landauer principle bridges the energetic cost and information processing, showing that irreversible computation inevitably demands energy dissipation. As energy demands from computation continue to rise, approximate computing has attracted considerable attention. Approximate computing is based on the idea that energy consumption can be reduced by sacrificing computational accuracy. This raises a fundamental question about the relationship between error and thermodynamic cost in information processing. In this study, we derive the error-cost trade-off in the binary classifier by considering classification based on Markov processes. We obtain the lower bounds on the Bayes error in terms of thermodynamic costs such as entropy production and dynamical activity. Our results show that when entropy production or dynamical activity vanishes, the Bayes error reaches $1/2$, equivalent to random guessing, while greater thermodynamic costs enable lower error. This establishes a fundamental trade-off between error and cost in information processing by thermodynamic systems. Because the Bayes error provides the lowest achievable error among all possible classifiers, the classification error cannot fall below the obtained bounds given the entropy production or dynamical activity. We also discuss the quantum generalization and show that the Bayes error of the quantum classifier is bounded from below by the variance of the Hamiltonian.

### [78] [Rare events of small-noise Doob conditioned processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24537)
*Iago N. Mamede,Francesco Coghi*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过弱噪声大偏差（weak-noise large deviation）框架，研究Doob固定时间条件（Doob fixed-time conditioning）下马尔可夫过程（Markov process）路径系综（path ensemble）的统计特性，并提出一种避免显式构造Doob变换（Doob transform）的最优控制（optimal control）变分表示，用于计算生成函数（generating function）的主要指数贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Doob固定时间条件化能够通过修改漂移项来确保马尔可夫过程在给定时间到达指定目标，从而实现对稀有轨迹（rare trajectories）的采样。然而Doob漂移（Doob drift）很少能以闭式（closed form）获得，这限制了该方法在实际问题中的应用。本文旨在提出一种无需显式构造Doob变换的分析框架。

Method: 将条件化路径系综重新解释为原始过程在终端约束下的后选择（post-selected）系综，从而绕过Doob变换的显式构造。基于此观点，推导出生成函数主导指数贡献的最优控制表示，该表示表现为一个具有由Doob端点约束（end-point constraint）设定的终端边界条件的变分原理（variational principle）。

Result: 通过两个解析算例验证了所提出的框架。此外，将该方法应用于生物分子折叠（biomolecular folding）最小模型的热耗散（heat dissipation）问题，展示了其实用性。

Conclusion: 所提出的后选择视角与最优控制变分表示为研究条件化马尔可夫过程的统计特性提供了一种有效途径，在无需显式计算Doob漂移的情况下即可获得生成函数的主要指数贡献，并适用于实际物理系统。

Abstract: Doob fixed-time conditioning enables the sampling of rare trajectories of Markov processes by modifying the drift so that reaching a prescribed target at a given time is guaranteed. We study the statistics of this conditioned path ensemble through the moment generating function in the weak-noise large deviation regime. Since the Doob drift is rarely available in closed form, we reinterpret the conditioned ensemble as the original process post-selected on the terminal constraint, thereby avoiding explicit construction of the Doob transform. This viewpoint then yields an optimal-control representation for the leading exponential contribution to the generating function, expressed as a variational principle with terminal boundary conditions set by the Doob end-point constraint. We illustrate the framework with two analytical examples and with an application to heat dissipation of a minimal model of biomolecular folding.

### [79] [The peculiar response of Kelvin-Voigt chains with a free end](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24467)
*Rupayan Saha,Matthias Krüger*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文精确求解了一个由过阻尼谐振耦合粒子组成的异质链模型，该模型具有动量守恒耗散机制。通过前向差分变换实现了非对称漂移算符的解析对角化，揭示了响应矩阵的阶梯结构，并建立了自由子空间与约束子空间在稳态响应和弛豫过程中的不同物理作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究具有动量守恒耗散（momentum-conserving dissipation）的异质过阻尼耦合粒子链（heterogeneous chain of overdamped, harmonically coupled particles）的精确解，这类系统由非对称漂移算符（non-symmetric drift operator）控制，传统方法难以解析处理。

Method: 采用前向差分变换（forward-difference transformation）对非对称漂移算符进行解析对角化（analytical diagonalization），并针对秩亏相互作用矩阵（rank-deficient interaction matrices）将状态空间分解为自由子空间（free subspace）和约束子空间（constraint subspace）。

Result: 在链的一端自由的情况下，响应矩阵（response matrix）呈现奇特的阶梯形式（staircase form）：粒子 i 对作用于粒子 j 的力的响应与 i 和 j 之间链段的属性及长度无关。自由子空间控制稳态响应（steady state responses），而约束子空间控制外力停止后的弛豫（relaxation）。

Conclusion: 该结果建立了一个用于分析具有动量守恒的异质过阻尼动力学（heterogeneous overdamped dynamics）的框架，明确了自由与约束子空间分离的物理意义。

Abstract: We exactly solve a model of a heterogeneous chain of overdamped, harmonically coupled particles with momentum-conserving dissipation. Despite being governed by a non-symmetric drift operator, the system admits an analytical diagonalization by use of a forward-difference transformation. In case of one free end, the response matrix shows a peculiar staircase form: the response of particle i to a force acting on particle j is independent of the properties and the length of the chain-part between i and j. For rank-deficient interaction matrices, the state space is decomposed into free and constrained subspaces. We demonstrate that this separation has clear physical consequences: the free subspace governs steady state responses, while the constraint subspace governs the relaxation after cessation of forcing. These results establish a framework for analyzing heterogeneous overdamped dynamics with momentum conservation.

Method: 将离散二元变量参数化为复单位圆上的连续波状状态（complex phases），从而平滑非凸能量景观。从这一表示中提取出一种隐式正则化机制，并将其显式应用于标准实数优化框架中。

Abstract: We introduce a physics-inspired continuous relaxation framework that yields substantially improved solutions for NP-hard combinatorial optimization problems, including Quadratic Unconstrained Binary Optimization (QUBO), binary sparse coding, and planted-solution Ising models. By parameterizing discrete binary variables as continuous wave-like states on the complex unit circle, we inherently smooth highly non-convex energy landscapes. We show that representing binary variables as complex phases reveals an implicit regularization mechanism that promotes convergence toward discrete states. Extracting this mechanism yields significant improvements even within standard real-valued optimization frameworks, using this regularizer explicitly. Empirically, this regularization yields vastly higher ground-state convergence rates than standard real-valued alternatives. Our models achieved zero error in large-scale 160x160 QUBO tasks under severe noise (sigma=0.25), and outperformed traditional algorithms (OMP and LASSO) in underdefined sparse coding with perfect recovery at sigma=0.15. ### [81] [Strong Eigenstate Thermalization from Mean-Ergodic Non-chaotic Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24510)
*Avadhut V. Purohit,Harshit Sharma,Udaysinh T. Bhosale*

TL;DR: 该研究通过一个源于双踢顶（double kicked top, DKT）的多体系统，展示了即使动力学非混沌但具有平均遍历性（mean-ergodic），仍可在量子区域展现强本征态热化假说（strong eigenstate thermalization hypothesis, strong ETH），从而回答了强ETH是否为遍历性（ergodicity）或平均遍历性的量子类比这一开放问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决一个关键开放问题：强本征态热化假说（strong ETH）是否是遍历性（ergodicity）或平均遍历性（mean-ergodicity）的量子类比。

Method: 基于双踢顶（DKT）构造一个非混沌但平均遍历的多体系统，在量子框架下分析可观测量的对角矩阵元涨落标度以及非对角矩阵元的统计性质。

Result: 可观测量对角矩阵元的涨落按希尔伯特空间维度（Hilbert space dimension）$D^{-1/2}$标度；非对角矩阵元呈现高斯统计，并伴随一个在大$k_θ$区域近似均匀的光滑函数$f_O(\bar{E}, \omega)$。

Conclusion: 即使动力学非混沌、仅具有平均遍历性，系统仍可展现强ETH，表明强ETH并不局限于混沌系统，而是与平均遍历性存在更深层的联系。

Abstract: We report an example of a many-body system, derived from the double kicked top (DKT), with non-chaotic yet mean-ergodic dynamics that displays \textit{strong} eigenstate thermalization hypothesis (ETH) in the quantum regime. The analysis addresses a key open question: whether \textit{strong} ETH is a quantum analog of ergodicity (or mean-ergodicity). Despite non-chaotic dynamics, the fluctuations of the diagonal matrix elements of an observable scale as $D^{-1/2}$, where $D$ denotes the Hilbert space dimension. Furthermore, the off-diagonal matrix elements show Gaussian statistics together with a smooth function $f_O(\bar{E}, ω)$ that becomes nearly uniform in the large-$k_θ$ domain. Our findings show that even mean-ergodic and non-chaotic systems can exhibit \textit{strong} ETH.

### [82] [Manipulation of information flow and thermodynamic performance in nonreciprocal quantum dot information engines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24554)
*Hao Feng,Junjie Liu*

TL;DR: 本文研究基于双量子点（double-quantum-dot）的自主信息引擎（autonomous information engine），揭示了非互易耦合（nonreciprocal coupling）可作为调控量子点间信息流（inter-dot information flow）的有效控制手段，从而提升引擎性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子信息引擎以信息作为热力学资源进行能量转换，其运行关键在于工作物质与控制器之间的信息流，但目前缺乏高效调控信息流策略的研究。

Method: 采用双量子点结构：下游量子点耦合两个电子库（reservoirs）作为工作物质，上游量子点耦合单个电子库作为控制器；通过将热力学第二定律推广至包含非互易耦合效应，建立热力学框架（thermodynamic framework）。

Result: 非互易性可显著调控量子点间的信息流，提供鲁棒控制机制；其影响可通过重参数化化学势和电子-电子耦合强度映射为等效互易系统（effective reciprocal system）来理解；非互易耦合能超越传统互易构型的性能限制。

Conclusion: 非互易耦合可作为设计和优化量子点信息引擎的有效控制旋钮（control knob），为突破传统互易构型能力边界提供了新途径。

Abstract: Quantum information engines leverage information as a thermodynamic resource to facilitate energy conversion. In the operation of such engines, the information flow between the working substance and the controller is pivotal, however, strategies for its efficient manipulation remain largely unexplored. Here, we investigate an autonomous information engine based on a double-quantum-dot setup, where a downstream dot coupled to two reservoirs acts as the working substance, and an upstream dot coupled to a single reservoir serves as the controller. By extending the second law of thermodynamics to incorporate the effects of nonreciprocal couplings between the dots and their electronic reservoirs, we develop a thermodynamic framework that allows us to demonstrate that nonreciprocity can significantly modulate the inter-dot information flow, thereby providing a robust control mechanism. We show that the influence of nonreciprocity can be equivalently understood through a mapping to an effective reciprocal system upon a reparameterization of chemical potentials and the electron-electron coupling strength. We further analyze the impact of nonreciprocity on the engine's performance and operation regime. Our findings establish nonreciprocal coupling as an effective control knob for designing and optimizing quantum dot information engines, surpassing the capabilities of conventional reciprocal configurations.

Abstract: The symmetric simple exclusion process (SSEP) is a paradigmatic model of classical non-equilibrium dynamics. In this Article, we discuss how these results are modified in the presence of localized slow bonds. For each case, we present exact expressions for the large deviation function of current and validate them through rare-event simulations based on the cloning algorithm. ### [84] [A particle-resolved rheological study of chirality transfer and odd transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25136)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用桌面流变实验、多体模拟（many-body simulations）以及约化粗粒化理论（reduced coarse-grained theory）相结合的方法，研究对称被动示踪物在非平衡手性活性浴（non-equilibrium chiral bath）中的受驱行为。

Result: 局部碰撞将手性活性动力学传递给示踪物，使其呈现圆形轨迹；在恒定拉力下产生系统性横向漂移；非线性摩擦是整流手性活性涨落为宏观奇数响应的关键因素。

Abstract: Chirality, or the breaking of mirror symmetry, appears across all scales in nature, from molecular conformations to the dynamics of bacterial collectives. Environments composed of such symmetry-breaking constituents can give rise to emergent physical phenomena, particularly in the transport and response of embedded tracers. Yet it remains unclear how chiral environments influence such tracers and through which microscopic mechanisms anomalous responses emerge. Here, we present a particle-resolved study of these systems, demonstrating chirality transfer and odd transport of an object embedded in a chiral active bath. In a rheological experiment, a symmetric passive tracer is driven through collisions with the particles of a non-equilibrium chiral bath. Combining table-top experiments, many-body simulations, and a reduced coarse-grained theory, we demonstrate that local collisions transfer chiral active dynamics to the tracer, which displays circular trajectories. We show that the same mechanism gives rise to a systematic transverse drift under a constant pulling force. ### [85] [First-passage time distribution of a Brownian particle harmonically confined in a viscoelastic bath](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25215)
*Brandon R. Ferrer,Juan Ruben Gomez-Solano*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文从理论和实验两方面研究了在恒温流体中受简谐势（harmonic trap）约束的球形布朗粒子（Brownian particle）的首次通过时间（first-passage time）性质。基于过阻尼广义朗之万方程（generalized Langevin equation），推导了首次到达势能最小位置的时间概率密度函数的一般表达式，并通过光学镊子（optical tweezers）捕获胶体球在多种非马尔可夫（non-Markovian）和马尔可夫（Markovian）介质中的实验进行了验证。结果表明，粘弹性（viscoelastic）介质中的平均首次通过时间可能超过相同零剪切粘度（zero-shear viscosity）的粘性介质，原因在于前者首次通过时间概率密度出现缓慢衰减的拖尾。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对首次通过时间的研究大多局限于马尔可夫粘性介质，但对非马尔可夫介质（如粘弹性聚合物溶液）中该问题的理论理解和实验验证仍不充分。本文旨在建立一种适用于一般非马尔可夫浴（non-Markovian bath）的首次通过时间理论框架，并通过实验加以验证。

Method: 采用过阻尼版本的广义朗之万方程（overdamped generalized Langevin equation）进行理论推导，得到首次通过时间概率密度函数（probability density function）的隐式表达式，该表达式与摩擦记忆核（friction memory kernel）相关。实验上使用光学镊子捕获胶体球，在粘弹性聚合物溶液、胶束溶液（micellar solutions）以及粘性甘油/水混合物和纯水等多种介质中测量首次通过时间，并与理论结果进行定量对比。

Result: 推导出的首次通过时间分布表达式在马尔可夫粘性浴（Markovian viscous bath）情形下正确约化为已有结果。实验测量结果与理论表达式定量一致。关键发现是：在粘弹性介质中，由于首次通过时间概率密度出现缓慢衰减的拖尾（slowly decaying tails），其平均首次通过时间（mean first-passage time）可能超过相同零剪切粘度的纯粘性介质。

Conclusion: 本文建立的首次通过时间理论框架适用于一般非马尔可夫环境，在多种介质中获得了实验验证。粘弹性介质中平均首次通过时间的增大现象揭示了记忆效应（memory effect）在随机动力学中的重要影响，对理解复杂流体中的输运过程具有意义。

Abstract: We investigate theoretically and experimentally the first passage-time properties of a spherical Brownian particle that is harmonically trapped at thermal equilibrium in a fluid at constant temperature. By using the overdamped version of the generalized Langevin equation, we derive a general expression for the probability density function of the time that the particle takes to reach for the first time the minimum of the potential starting from an arbitrary position. We show that such a first-passage time distribution can be implicitly expressed in terms of the friction memory kernel that encodes the interaction of the particle with its surroundings, and correctly reduces to previously found expressions in the case of a Markovian viscous bath. We validate our theoretical results by measuring the first-passage time of colloidal beads optically trapped in non-Markovian baths such as viscoelastic polymer and micellar solutions, as well as in a viscous glycerol/water mixture and water, which behave as Markovian media, having quantitative agreement with the derived expressions. In particular, we find that the mean first-passage time in a viscoelastic bath can surpass that in a viscous medium of the same zero-shear viscosity due to the emergence of slowly decaying tails in the first-passage time probability density of the former.

### [86] [Beyond Local Detailed Balance: Microscopic Rates Reshape Nonequilibrium Phase Behavior](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25406)
*Takahiro Kanazawa,Kyogo Kawaguchi,Kyosuke Adachi*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文发现，在强相互作用驱动晶格气体系统中，即使遵循相同的局域细致平衡（Local Detailed Balance, LDB）条件，不同的跃迁速率函数形式也能定性地改变系统的相行为，包括结构因子的各向异性、相分离模式的取向及其长时间稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 局域细致平衡（LDB）是非平衡随机动力学建模的核心原则，但它仅约束正反向跃迁速率的比值而不固定稳态。虽然已知在弱相互作用系统中，相同LDB下速率的不同函数形式会影响关联性质，但在强相互作用系统中是否会影响相行为仍不清楚。

Method: 研究针对一个具有吸引性最近邻相互作用的二维驱动晶格气体（driven lattice gas），考虑了含有一个可调参数的跃迁速率，该参数在保持相同LDB的同时调节沿驱动力的不对称性。通过分析结构因子不连续性、各向异性密度关联以及相分离模式的取向和稳定性，并结合近似的涨落流体动力学方程（fluctuating hydrodynamic equation）进行解释。

Result: 该参数控制了定性的相行为：在均匀相中，它反转了结构因子不连续性的符号，从而改变了长程密度关联的各向异性；在相分离区域，它切换了各向异性模式的取向及其长时间稳定性。这些效应均能被近似的涨落流体动力学方程一致地捕捉。

Conclusion: 与平衡系统形成鲜明对比，非平衡相行为取决于具体的动力学规则，即使在遵循相同LDB条件下也是如此。

Abstract: Local detailed balance (LDB) is a central guiding principle for modeling nonequilibrium stochastic dynamics, yet it only constrains the ratio of forward and backward transition rates and does not fix the steady state. Although the functional form of rates under the same LDB has been shown to affect correlation properties in weakly interacting systems, whether it can reshape phase behavior in strongly interacting systems remains unclear. Here, for a two-dimensional driven lattice gas with attractive nearest-neighbor interactions, we consider hopping rates with a parameter that preserves the same LDB but tunes asymmetry along the driving force. We find that this parameter controls qualitative phase behavior: in the homogeneous phase, it reverses the sign of the structure-factor discontinuity and hence the anisotropy in long-range density correlations; in the phase-separated regime, it switches the orientation of anisotropic patterns and their long-time stability. Both effects are coherently captured by an approximate fluctuating hydrodynamic equation. The results demonstrate that, in contrast to equilibrium systems, nonequilibrium phase behavior depends on specific dynamical rules even when following the same LDB.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用精确实空间重整化群（exact real-space renormalization group）计算，在自对偶层级晶格（self-dual hierarchical lattices）上数值确定了有限副本临界点（finite-replica critical points），涵盖 $q=mn=2,\ldots,6$。将结果与基于对称群傅里叶变换的对偶性预测（duality prediction）进行比较，并对 $b=3$ 数据向外推至副本极限 $mn\to0$（此时有效维度为二维）。

Result: 对偶性预测在数值比较中得到支持，同时研究揭示了外推公式（extrapolation formula）带来的系统不确定性（systematic uncertainty）。

Conclusion: 研究结果支持基于对称群傅里叶变换的对偶性估计，并澄清了外推过程中的系统不确定性，为理解置换模型相变与纠缠熵转变之间的关系提供了更可靠的数值依据。

Abstract: The permutation model is a classical spin system where elements of the symmetric group interact with one another. The partition function of this model is directly related to the entanglement structure of random quantum circuits and random tensor networks. In these contexts, the entanglement entropy undergoes a transition between area-law and volume-law scaling, depending on the model parameters. This transition point has attracted considerable attention. In the present work, we investigate the ferromagnetic-paramagnetic phase transition of the permutation model, which corresponds to the entanglement entropy transition. Using exact real-space renormalization group calculations on self-dual hierarchical lattices, we numerically determine finite-replica critical points for (q=mn=2,...,6). We compare the results with the duality prediction based on the Fourier transform of the symmetric group and then extrapolate the b=3 data toward the replica limit $mn\to0$, where the effective dimension is two. The comparison supports the duality-based estimate while also clarifying the systematic uncertainty associated with the extrapolation formula.

### [88] [Equivalent-neighbor $k$-core percolation in two dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25812)
*Qiyuan Shi,Ming Li,Youjin Deng*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 通过大规模数值模拟，本文研究了二维空间中具有扩展相互作用范围 $r$ 的 $k$-核逾渗（$k$-core percolation）的临界行为。与无限维情形不同，二维中未发现混合相变，相图仅包含连续相变区域和一阶相变区域，两者由三临界或临界端点分隔；在一阶相变区域中，赝临界点随系统尺寸的对数倒数漂移，表现出独特的有限尺寸标度行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: $k$-核逾渗在无限维中表现出混合相变（hybrid transition），但在有限维中其临界行为是否发生变化尚不清楚。本文旨在通过系统改变核心指数 $k$ 和相互作用范围 $r$，在二维系统中考察 $k$-核逾渗的相变性质，特别是探究几何约束对相变本质的影响。

Method: 采用大规模数值模拟方法，系统变化核心指数 $k$ 与相互作用范围 $r$，在 $(k,r)$ 平面中构建完整的二维 $k$-核逾渗相图，并分析不同区域的临界行为与有限尺寸标度（finite-size scaling）特征。

Result: 二维中未观察到混合相变，相图仅包含连续相变区域（属于标准二维逾渗普适类）和严格一阶相变区域，两者由三临界或临界端点 $(k_s,r_s)$ 分隔。在一阶区域内，赝临界点以 $1/\ln L$ 的方式趋近临界点，而非传统热力学一阶相变中的 $L^{-d}$ 标度。

Conclusion: 二维几何约束从根本上改变了 $k$-核逾渗在有限维中的相变性质，连续与一阶相变之间的分离及对数有限尺寸漂移支持了由稀有空洞（rare voids）触发的成核驱动机制。

Abstract: We perform large-scale numerical simulations to investigate the critical behavior of $k$-core percolation in two dimensions with an extended interaction range $r$. By systematically varying both the core index $k$ and the interaction range $r$, we construct a comprehensive phase diagram in the $(k,r)$ plane. In contrast to $k$-core percolation in infinite dimensions, no hybrid transition is observed in two dimensions: the phase diagram contains only a continuous transition regime and a strictly first-order regime, separated by a tricritical or critical-end point $(k_s,r_s)$. For $k<k_s$ and $r<r_s$, the transition is continuous and belongs to the universality class of standard two-dimensional (2D) percolation. For $k>k_s$ and finite $r>r_s$, the transition is discontinuous, with no hybrid features or critical singularities. In this first-order regime, the pseudocritical point approaches the critical point as $1/\ln L$, where $L$ is the linear system size, distinct from the $L^{-d}$ scaling typical of conventional thermodynamic first-order transitions in $d$ dimensions. This logarithmic finite-size drift is consistent with a nucleation-driven mechanism, in which rare voids trigger the collapse of the finite-range $k$-core. These results demonstrate that geometric constraints can fundamentally alter the nature of $k$-core percolation found in finite dimensions.

### [89] [Scaling features for the stress fluctuations in the OFC model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25884)
*Naveen Kumar,Rahul Chhimpa,Avinash Chand Yadav*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本研究分析了Olami-Feder-Christensen (OFC)地震模型在方形二维格子上的雪崩性质与应力涨落，发现局域守恒情形下雪崩尺寸与面积之差服从指数接近1的幂律，而局域耗散情形（α=0.21）下该标度行为消失；对比BTW与Manna沙堆模型验证了局域守恒动力学对幂律行为的关键作用；应力涨落的功率谱有限尺寸标度分析表明，从保守到耗散动力学，动态标度指数从接近弹道运动变为扩散行为，且局域应力在中频段呈现近似的1/f噪声特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 地震雪崩的尺寸与面积之差这一统计量此前尚未被探索，但在地震研究中具有重要潜在意义，因此本文旨在填补这一空白并探究其标度性质及其对动力学参数的依赖性。

Method: 在具有开放边界条件的正方形二维格点上运行Olami-Feder-Christensen (OFC)模型，通过控制参数α区分局域耗散（α<0.25）与局域守恒（α=0.25）动力学；同时对比BTW和Manna沙堆模型，并采用有限尺寸标度分析（finite-size scaling）方法研究应力涨落的功率谱（power spectra）。

Result: 在局域守恒OFC模型中，雪崩尺寸与面积之差服从幂律分布，标度指数接近1；但该标度行为在α=0.21（物理相关情形）下消失。BTW和Manna沙堆模型中因局域守恒动力学，该幂律行为得以保持。应力涨落的动力学标度指数从保守情形的近弹道运动（nearly ballistic）转变为耗散情形的扩散行为（diffusive behavior）；局域应力在中频段呈现近似1/f噪声，高频段以1/f²型标度为主。

Conclusion: 雪崩尺寸与面积之差的幂律标度强烈依赖于局域守恒动力学，在局域耗散条件下不再成立；OFC模型中应力涨落的动态行为在保守与耗散情形下定性相似但定量差异显著，揭示了耗散对系统临界动力学行为的根本影响。

Abstract: We consider the Olami-Feder-Christensen (OFC) model on a square two-dimensional lattice with open boundary conditions. The model exhibits self-organized criticality and explains the Gutenberg-Richter law observed for earthquakes. A parameter $α$ controls the level of local dissipation: $α< 0.25$ corresponds to locally dissipative and $α= 0.25$ marks locally conservative dynamics. The avalanche size distribution follows a decaying power-law, with a non-universal critical exponent. Here, we examine the probability distribution of the difference between avalanche size and area. This quantity remains unexplored despite being of significant interest in earthquakes. We find a power-law with a scaling exponent close to one in the conservative OFC model. The scaling feature vanishes even for the physically relevant case $α= 0.21$. To examine the robustness of such features, we also examine the same quantity in the BTW and Manna sandpile models on a square lattice. We find that the power-law behavior survives for these systems due to locally conservative dynamics. We further examine the local and total stress fluctuations in the OFC model for both locally conservative and dissipative dynamics. The finite-size scaling analysis of the power spectra for the stress fluctuations reveals qualitatively the same but quantitatively significantly different behavior. The dynamic exponent describing the divergence of the correlation time with system size changes from nearly ballistic in the conservative to diffusive behavior in the locally dissipative dynamics with $α= 0.21$. The local stress also exhibits a signature of nearly canonical $1/f$ noise in the intermediate regime, and $1/f^2$-type scaling dominates the high-frequency regime.

</details>


### [90] [Freezing of the tetrahedral amorphous network in supercooled water triggers crystallization towards LDA ice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25926)
*Ashutosh Srivastava,Pankaj A. Apte*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本研究通过分子动力学模拟，揭示了过冷水在其稳定性极限附近形成冰的初期机制，特别是低于稳定性极限时，结晶并非直接由成核主导，而是经历动力学交叉、四面体网络冻结等过程，最终通过立方和六方晶体基序的中程有序增长引发结晶，形成低密度无定形冰（LDA ice）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解过冷水在稳定性极限附近形成冰的初期机制，因为在此条件下，经典晶体成核（crystal nucleation）并非相关机制。

Method: 采用TIP4P/2005势函数的分子动力学模拟（molecular dynamics simulation），在恒定压力下以5至10 K/ns的冷却速率对水进行冷却。

Result: 冷却至最大密度温度（T_0 = 277 K）以下时，体系四面体序（tetrahedrality）持续增加；冷却至水的稳定性极限（T_s ≈ 235 K）附近时，出现动力学交叉（dynamical crossover）：大尺度热涨落消散，小尺度涨落维持热平衡，液态终结；随后四面体网络驱动能量和密度下降，网络“冻结”（freezing）后，弛豫机制转变为通过增加结构有序度（即结晶）进行，其中立方和六方晶体基序（cubic and hexagonal crystalline motifs）在冻结点附近迅速增长。

Conclusion: 确定了过冷水越过稳定性极限后引发结晶（形成低密度无定形冰）的具体机制，其中立方冰在整体结晶中贡献显著，与实验发现一致。

Abstract: In this work, we provide mechanistic insight into the initial stages of formation of ice across the limit of stability of supercooled water. Such an analysis is particularly important since crystal nucleation is not a relevant mechanism under these conditions. Using molecular dynamics simulation with the TIP4P/2005 potential, water is cooled at a constant pressure with cooling rates of 5 to 10 K per nanosecond. As the liquid is cooled across the temperature of maximum density (T_0 = 277 K), we find that there is a continuous increase in the tetrahedrality of the system. As the cooling continues across the limit of stability of water (T_s $\approx$ 235 K), large scale thermal fluctuations dissipate while the thermal equilibration is achieved through small scale fluctuations. This phenomenon, known as the dynamical crossover [Goutam et. al. in J. Stat. Phys., 168: 1302--1318 (2017)], ends the existence of the liquid state. Subsequently, we find that the tetrahedral network drives the decrease of energy and density. This process terminates when the network undergoes `freezing' (i.e., the bonds of the network acquire sufficient rigidity), due to which the network evolution, as a whole, stops. This triggers a qualitative change in the relaxation mechanism: subsequent relaxation occurs through crystallization, i.e., an increase in the structural order. In particular, we find that the cubic and hexagonal crystalline motifs, which possess medium range order, increase rapidly across the freezing point. In the resulting LDA ice states, cubic ice is found to have a significant contribution in the overall extent of crystallization, which is consistent with the experimental findings. Overall, our work provides the specific mechanism by which crystallization (leading to LDA ice) is initiated across the limit of stability of supercooled water.

</details>


### [91] [Generalized field mixing for endpoint criticality with marginal flow: resolving the four-state Potts endpoint in the square-lattice $J_1$--$J_2$ Ising model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25946)
*Yihua Sun,Yuchen Fan*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文发展了一个广义场混合（field-mixing）框架，用于处理受单一相关标度场（relevant scaling field）和边缘无关标度场（marginally irrelevant scaling field）共同控制的端点临界性（endpoint criticality）。通过构造有限尺寸赝临界流形（finite-size pseudocritical manifold），该框架消除了正常的相关失谐（relevant detuning），暴露出残留的边缘漂移（marginal drift），从而实现对端点渐近临界性的可控有限尺寸分析。将该方法应用于阻挫方形晶格 $J_1$--$J_2$ Ising 模型，直接识别出其条状序端点（stripe-ordering endpoint）为孤立的奇异点，并证明其渐近临界性遵循具有对数修正的四态 Potts 普适类（four-state Potts universality with logarithmic corrections）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 识别临界端点（critical endpoint）的渐近临界性（asymptotic criticality）具有挑战性，因为伪一级相变（pseudo-first-order）特征在可及的系统尺寸上持续存在，掩盖了其潜在的临界本质。当端点受边缘无关标度场控制时，对数流（logarithmic flow）会延迟渐近标度的出现，进一步放大了这种模糊性。此外，阻挫方形晶格 $J_1$--$J_2$ Ising 模型中条状序端点的位置乃至性质长期存在争议，亟待一种能够提取存在边缘流（marginal flow）时端点渐近临界性的通用框架。

Method: 发展了一个广义场混合框架，将端点临界性描述为一个相关标度场与一个边缘无关标度场共同作用的设定——这超出了传统两相关场（two-relevant-field）表述的范围。通过构造有限尺寸赝临界流形，该方法移除了正常的相关失谐，暴露出残留的边缘漂移，从而实现了基于直方图（histogram）和 Binder 比的有限尺寸分析（finite-size analysis）。

Result: 在 $J_1$--$J_2$ Ising 模型中，端点被直接识别为孤立的奇异点，而非从相边界最像 Potts 模型的位置推断得出。其渐近临界性被证明遵循四态 Potts 普适类并伴有对数修正。这一结论独立得到了与 Ashkin--Teller 模型中 Potts 点的直接比较以及磁性和向列（nematic）扇区中一致的 Binder 标度行为的支持。

Conclusion: 解决了阻挫 Ising 系统中长期存在的数值模糊性问题，建立了一个在存在边缘流时提取端点渐近临界性的通用框架。

Abstract: Identifying the asymptotic criticality of a critical endpoint is challenging, as pseudo-first-order signatures persist over accessible system sizes and mask its underlying critical nature. This ambiguity is amplified at endpoints controlled by a marginally irrelevant scaling field, where logarithmic flow delays the onset of asymptotic scaling. Here we develop a generalized field-mixing framework for endpoint criticality governed by one relevant scaling field together with a marginally irrelevant one, a setting that lies outside the conventional two-relevant-field formulation. By constructing a finite-size pseudocritical manifold, the framework removes the normal relevant detuning and exposes the residual marginal drift, enabling controlled histogram- and Binder-based finite-size analyses. We apply this approach to the frustrated square-lattice $J_1$--$J_2$ Ising model, where the location and even the nature of the stripe-ordering endpoint have remained controversial for decades. The endpoint is isolated directly as a distinct singular point, rather than inferred from where the phase boundary appears most Potts-like, and its asymptotic criticality is shown to follow four-state Potts universality with logarithmic corrections. This identification is independently supported by direct comparison with the Potts point of the Ashkin--Teller model and by consistent Binder scaling in both the magnetic and nematic sectors. Our results resolve a longstanding numerical ambiguity in a paradigmatic frustrated Ising system and establish a general framework for extracting asymptotic endpoint criticality in the presence of marginal flow.

</details>


### [92] [Boltzmann Distribution from Invariance of Coarse-Graining-Scale and Energy-Shift](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25987)
*Weicheng Fu,Yisen Wang,Yong Zhang,Hong Zhao*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种从粗粒化尺度不变性和能量零点平移不变性出发，简洁推导经典多体哈密顿系统中玻尔兹曼单粒子能量分布的方法，并通过模拟验证了其在一维双原子硬核气体和非线性晶格链中的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对玻尔兹曼分布（Boltzmann distribution）的推导通常依赖于统计力学（statistical mechanics）中的系综理论或最大熵原理。该论文试图寻找一种更简洁、更基础的推导方式，仅基于两条物理事实——经验分布的粗粒化尺度不变性（coarse-graining-scale invariance）和能量零点的均匀平移不变性（invariance under a uniform shift of the energy zero），从而揭示玻尔兹曼因子的唯一来源。

Method: 从经典多体哈密顿系统（classical many-body Hamiltonian systems）出发，假设单粒子能量经验分布满足粗粒化尺度不变性和能量零点平移不变性。利用这两条公理性条件唯一地导出玻尔兹曼因子（Boltzmann factor），其参数由平均每粒子能量确定。对于可分离哈密顿量（separable Hamiltonians），平衡权重因子分解为动能和位形贡献，共享同一参数，该参数由动能部分识别为逆动能温度（inverse kinetic temperature）。该原理还可推广到任何具有稳态分布和平移不变性的物理量。

Result: 在一维双原子硬核气体（one-dimensional diatomic hard-core gas）和非线性晶格链（nonlinear lattice chain）中，该方法成功预测了速度、能量、间距、碰撞时间和压力依赖位移等分布，与模拟结果一致。在晶格模型中，谐波弹性、非谐修正、内压和热膨胀等均从相同的指数平衡权重中涌现。

Conclusion: 该工作表明，玻尔兹曼分布可以从粗粒化尺度不变性和能量零点平移不变性这两条基本物理事实中唯一导出，为统计力学的基础提供了一种新的简洁视角。论文还简要讨论了不同系综（ensembles）之间的关系。

Abstract: We present a concise derivation of the Boltzmann form for single-particle energy distributions in classical many-body Hamiltonian systems. The derivation relies on two physical facts: coarse-graining-scale invariance of the empirical distribution and invariance under a uniform shift of the energy zero. These conditions uniquely yield the Boltzmann factor, whose parameter is fixed by the mean energy per particle. For separable Hamiltonians, the equilibrium weight factorizes into kinetic and configurational contributions sharing the same parameter, identified from the kinetic part as the inverse kinetic temperature. The principle extends to any physical quantity with a stationary distribution and translational invariance. It is illustrated in a one-dimensional diatomic hard-core gas and a nonlinear lattice chain, where it predicts velocity, energy, spacing, collision-time, and pressure-dependent displacement distributions in agreement with simulations. The lattice model further shows how harmonic elasticity, anharmonic corrections, internal pressure, and thermal expansion emerge from the same exponential equilibrium weights. Finally, the relationships among different ensembles are briefly discussed.

</details>

### [93] [Vacuum-Sealed Thermal Treatment Regulates Trap States and Red Persistent Luminescence in CaTiO3: Pr3+,Al3+ Phosphors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24836)
*Ziyi Guo,Duanting Yan*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文通过高温固相法在真空密封石英管（QT）和空气两种条件下制备CaTiO3:0.3%Pr3+,0.3%Al3+红色长余辉荧光粉，发现QT处理（尤其是QT-1300°C）能显著提升余辉强度（1200秒时比空气处理样品高3.6倍），并通过热释光分析揭示了低氧环境调控氧空位相关缺陷陷阱的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 红色长余辉荧光粉（red persistent phosphors）的余辉通常较弱且衰减快，其成熟度远低于绿色和蓝绿色体系，因此需要在材料制备与陷阱调控方面寻求改进策略。

Method: 采用高温固相反应法（high-temperature solid-state route），分别在空气和真空密封石英管（quartz-tube, QT）条件下合成CaTiO3:0.3%Pr3+,0.3%Al3+荧光粉；利用X射线衍射（XRD）、拉曼光谱（Raman spectra）、扫描电子显微镜（SEM）、能谱分析（EDS）、稳态光致发光、余辉、热释光（thermoluminescence）和激发态衰减等手段进行表征。

Result: 所有样品均为正交CaTiO3钙钛矿相，无杂相；QT处理样品在612 nm附近的Pr3+红色发射更强，余辉性能显著优于空气处理样品；QT-1300°C样品余辉最佳，在1200秒时强度为空气处理样品的3.6倍；热释光显示QT处理增加了热活性陷阱（thermally active traps）的布居并增强了深陷阱组分。

Conclusion: 低氧密封环境（QT处理）可通过调控缺陷相关陷阱（最可能涉及氧空位相关中心）来改善载流子存储与释放，并利用Pr3+与Ti4+之间的间隔电荷转移路径（intervalence charge-transfer pathway）提升余辉性能；该工作为改善CaTiO3基红色长余辉荧光粉提供了一种实用的制备策略，并为低氧热处理下陷阱态调控提供了见解。

Abstract: Red persistent phosphors remain less mature than green and blue-green systems because their afterglow is often weak and decays rapidly. Here, CaTiO3:0.3%Pr3+,0.3%Al3+ phosphors were prepared by a high-temperature solid-state route under either air or vacuum-sealed quartz-tube (QT) conditions. The effects of processing atmosphere and sintering temperature on phase structure, microstructure, steady-state photoluminescence, afterglow, thermoluminescence, and excited-state decay were examined. X-ray diffraction and Raman spectra show that all samples retain the orthorhombic CaTiO3 perovskite phase, with no detectable secondary phase. SEM observations show particle coarsening at higher QT temperatures, while EDS mapping indicates a homogeneous distribution of Ca, Ti, O, Pr, and Al within the examined region. The QT-treated samples exhibit stronger Pr3+ red emission near 612 nm and markedly improved afterglow compared with the air-treated sample. The QT-1300 sample shows the best afterglow among the present samples, with a reported 3.6-fold higher intensity at 1200 s than Air-1200°C. Thermoluminescence results indicate that QT treatment increases the population of thermally active traps and enhances the deeper trap component. These results suggest that a low-oxygen sealed environment regulates defect-related traps, most likely involving oxygen-vacancy-associated centers, and improves carrier storage and release through the Pr3+ and Ti4+ intervalence charge-transfer pathway. This work provides a practical processing strategy for improving CaTiO3-based red persistent phosphors and offers insight into trap-state regulation under low-oxygen thermal treatment.

### [94] [Absolute measurement of the intrinsic helicity in nanophotonics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26058)
*Malo Bézard,Simon Garrigou,Jérémie Béal,Andreas Horrer,Yves Auad,Hugo Lourenço-Martins,Davy Gérard,Mathieu Kociak*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 该论文通过实验和理论证明，在纳米光子手性系统中，螺旋度（helicity）可以被严格定义并测量，方法是通过聚焦电子束近场激发圆偏振光发射，并对称化激发与探测几何结构，从而克服了传统圆二色性（circular dichroism）测量在手性光子系统中不适用的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 螺旋度是描述物体或场内部旋转的普适量，对于从基本粒子自旋到手性分子毒性等性质的表征至关重要。然而在等离激元纳米粒子或光子超表面等手性光子系统中，其定义与测量仍存在歧义——传统的圆偏振依赖光学性质观测并非螺旋度的有效度量，亟需建立严格的定义与测量方法。

Method: 论文同时采用实验与理论方法：在近场中通过聚焦电子束激发纳米光子系统，使其发射圆偏振光；以两个等离激元偶极子构成的Borm-Kuhn系统为模型，通过对称化激发与探测几何结构来测量光子模式的螺旋度。

Result: 在Born-Kuhn模型系统中，光子模式的螺旋度呈现出直观的形式，并可通过对称化激发与探测几何结构简单测量。该方法可推广至多种手性光子系统。

Conclusion: 该工作为手性光子系统中螺旋度的严格定义与测量提供了理论与实验基础，这些系统因其局域增强特性在手性工程（chirality engineering）领域具有广阔应用前景。

Abstract: Helicity is a universal quantity describing the internal rotation of an object or a field. Whether it characterizes fundamental properties such as the spin of elementary particles or leads to practical consequences such as the toxicity or harmlessness of chiral molecules, defining and measuring it is essential. However, this remains ambiguous in the case of chiral photonic systems such as plasmonic nanoparticles or photonic metasurfaces, where contrary to common knowledge, the observation of circularly polarized dependent optical properties is not a relevant measure for the helicity. We demonstrate experimentally and theoretically that the helicity can be rigorously defined and measured in a nanophotonic system emitting circularly polarized light after excitation in the near-field by a focused electron beam. In the case of a model system composed of two plasmonic dipoles (Born-Kuhn systems), we show that the helicity of photonic modes takes on a very intuitive form and can be simply measured by symmetrizing the geometry of excitation and detection. The method could be extended to a variety of chiral photonic systems, whose locally enhanced properties make them promising for the engineering of local chirality.

### [95] [Reinforcement Learning for Laser Additive Manufacturing Scan-Order Optimisation: A Bilevel Proxy--FEA Diagnostic Framework for Reward and World-Model Diagnosis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25063)
*Xian Wu,Haoran Li,Dongbin Zhao,Ruiyao Zhang,Yuanqi Chu,Bin Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种双层 Proxy–FEA 诊断框架，用于激光增材制造中基于强化学习的扫描顺序优化问题。下层使用轻量热启发式代理（proxy）快速生成候选路径，上层借助稀疏 Abaqus 有限元分析（FEA）提供参考标签。实验表明，当前低成本代理主要捕捉与垂直畸变（U3）相关的行为，而与 FEA 参考标签的相关性较弱，揭示仅依赖代理奖励可能导致强化学习训练中的目标错位。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 激光增材制造（laser additive manufacturing）中的扫描顺序优化对热积累、残余应力、畸变及最终质量影响显著。强化学习（reinforcement learning）被引入该问题，但面临奖励与世界模型保真度的核心挑战：全有限元分析（finite-element analysis, FEA）计算成本过高，而廉价热启发式代理（thermo-inspired proxy）虽高效，但仅能捕捉真实热-力学目标的部分信息。

Method: 提出一个双层 Proxy–FEA 诊断框架。下层采用轻量扫描路径与热启发式代理进行快速候选生成和策略侧初步筛选；上层利用稀疏的 Abaqus FEA 仿真提供基于仿真的参考标签。框架在一个包含十种代表性扫描策略的简化全轨道加热 LDED32 条纹基准（benchmark）上进行验证。

Result: 最终冷却残余 Mises 应力、U3 垂直畸变和 PEEQ 塑性指标显示存在应力-畸变权衡（stress–distortion trade-off），而非单一单调质量目标。在评估集中，center_out 策略是稳健的折衷候选，raster_left_to_right 和 edge_in 构成权衡的两个端点。Proxy–FEA 对齐分析表明，当前廉价基于路径的代理主要捕获畸变（U3）相关行为，与稀疏 FEA 参考标签的相关性较弱。

Conclusion: 仅依赖代理（proxy-only）的奖励设计在未来的强化学习训练中存在目标错位（misalignment）风险。稀疏的 FEA 参考信号在大规模策略优化（policy optimisation）之前，对于诊断引导的奖励与世界模型修正具有重要价值。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning offers a promising approach for scan-order optimisation in laser additive manufacturing, where sequential scan decisions critically influence thermal accumulation, residual stress, distortion, and final part quality. A central challenge in applying RL to this domain lies in reward and world-model fidelity: full finite-element analysis is computationally prohibitive for dense in-the-loop evaluation, while cheap thermo-inspired proxy metrics, though efficient, may capture only partial aspects of the true thermo-mechanical objectives. This paper investigates a bilevel Proxy--FEA diagnostic framework for reward and world-model diagnosis in reinforcement-learning-guided scan-order optimisation. The lower level employs lightweight scan-path and thermo-inspired proxies for rapid candidate generation and preliminary policy-side screening, while the upper level utilises sparse Abaqus FEA simulations to provide simulation-based reference labels. The framework is examined on a simplified whole-track heating LDED32 stripe benchmark comprising ten representative scan strategies. Final-cooling residual Mises stress, U3 vertical distortion, and PEEQ plasticity metrics reveal an observed stress--distortion trade-off rather than a single monotonic quality objective. Within the evaluated set, the center_out strategy emerges as a robust compromise candidate, while raster_left_to_right and edge_in form opposing endpoints of the trade-off. Proxy--FEA alignment analysis shows that current cheap path-based metrics predominantly capture distortion-related (U3) behaviour and exhibit only weak correlation with the sparse FEA reference labels. These findings highlight that proxy-only reward designs risk misalignment in future RL training and underscore the value of sparse FEA reference signals for diagnostic-guided reward and world-model refinement prior to large-scale policy optimisation.

### [96] [UNATE: UNsupervised ATomic Embedding for crystal structures property prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25866)
*Laura Solà-Garcia,Àlex Solé,Javier Ruiz-Hidalgo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出UNATE（无监督原子嵌入）框架，通过无监督去噪自编码器（denoising autoencoder）和自监督对比学习（self-supervised contrastive learning）从未标记晶体结构中学习稳健的原子表示（atomic representations），用于提升下游性质预测性能。实验表明该框架在完整数据下提升2.7%，在仅用25%标注数据时最高提升10%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 晶体性质预测（crystal property prediction）对加速材料发现至关重要，但常受限于稀缺的标注数据（labeled data）和高昂的理论计算成本。现有方法难以有效利用大量未标记的晶体结构信息。

Method: 提出UNATE框架，集成无监督去噪自编码器与自监督对比学习，从无标签的晶体结构中提取结构信息并学习稳健的原子级表示，再将这些预训练节点嵌入（node embeddings）作为下游性质预测任务的输入特征。

Result: 用UNATE预训练节点嵌入替换原始原子序数，在完整标注数据下相比基线提升2.7%；在标注数据有限时提升更为显著，仅使用25%标注数据时提升高达10%。

Conclusion: UNATE能有效利用无标注晶体结构数据提升下游预测性能，尤其在标注数据稀缺的场景下具有显著优势，为加速材料发现提供可行方案。

Abstract: Accurately predicting crystal properties is critical for accelerating materials discovery, but it is often limited by scarce labeled data and costly theoretical calculations. To alleviate this, we propose UNATE (Unsupervised Atomic Embedding), a framework that leverages structural information extracted from unlabeled crystal structures. UNATE integrates an unsupervised denoising autoencoder with self-supervised contrastive learning to learn robust atomic representations, which are then used as input features for downstream property prediction. Experimental results show that replacing raw atomic numbers with UNATE-pretrained node embeddings yields a 2.7\% improvement over the full-data baseline. Notably, the benefits become more pronounced in scenarios with limited labeled data, reaching improvements of up to 10\% when only 25\% of the labeled data is used.

### [97] [Topological analysis in $\mathcal{R}(p,q)-$anisotropic sector and nuclear space on $\mathcal{R}(p,q)-$quantum deformed algebra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24010)
*Kawèyim Lankpetre,Isiaka Aremua,Joseph Désiré Bukweli Kyemba*

Main category: math.QA

TL;DR: 本文在 $\mathcal{R}(p,q)-$ 微积分（$\mathcal{R}(p,q)-$calculus）框架下，引入并分析了经典核空间（classical nuclear space）的 $\mathcal{R}(p,q)-$ 拓扑分析。通过定义 $\mathcal{R}(p,q)-$Gamma 函数并建立其 Stirling 型渐近展开，进一步构造了 $\mathcal{R}(p,q)-$ 加权 Banach 空间与 Fréchet 空间，并证明了 Cauchy-Hadamard 定理、Borel-Carathéodory 不等式和 Phragmén-Lindelöf 增长原理的 $\mathcal{R}(p,q)-$ 类比，为 $\mathcal{R}(p,q)-$ 量子代数中的泛函分析奠定基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 发展 $\mathcal{R}(p,q)-$ 微积分框架下的拓扑分析与泛函分析工具，以支持 $\mathcal{R}(p,q)-$ 量子代数（quantum algebras）中一致泛函计算（consistent functional calculus）的构建。

Method: 首先引入 $\mathcal{R}(p,q)-$Gamma 函数，建立其变形阶乘（deformed factorial）连接与 Stirling 型渐近展开；基于渐近分析得到 $\mathcal{R}(p,q)-$ 整函数（entire functions）的系数界和 Cauchy 型不等式；进而构造 $\mathcal{R}(p,q)-$ 加权 Banach 空间与 Fréchet 空间，定义变形相关的伪范数（pseudo-norms）与赋值映射（valuation maps）；最后引入 $\mathcal{R}(p,q)-$ 圆盘（discs）和各向异性扇区（anisotropic sectors），证明多个经典复分析定理的 $\mathcal{R}(p,q)-$ 类比。

Result: 获得了 $\mathcal{R}(p,q)-$ 变形 Gamma 函数的指数二次增长估计 $\mathcal{R}!(p^n,q^n)\sim \exp(\lambda n^2)$；建立了 $\mathcal{R}(p,q)-$ 加权 Banach 空间和 Fréchet 空间上的严格分析框架；证明了 $\mathcal{R}(p,q)-$ 版本的 Cauchy-Hadamard 定理、Borel-Carathéodory 不等式和 Phragmén-Lindelöf 增长原理。

Conclusion: 本文为 $\mathcal{R}(p,q)-$ 量子代数中的泛函分析提供了严格的解析与泛函分析基础，其成果可推广至变形分数阶微分方程（deformed fractional differential equations）、算子理论（operator theory）、谱问题（spectral problems）及数学物理中的非交换模型（non commutative models）。

Abstract: The purpose of this article is to develop and analyze $\mathcal{R}(p,q)-$topological analysis of the classical nuclear space within the general framework of $\mathcal{R}(p,q)-$calculus. We begin by introducing the $\mathcal{R}(p,q)-$Gamma functions, establishing their main properties and their connection with the deformed factorials. We develop a rigorous analytic and functional-analytic framework for holomorphic functions governed by a general $\mathcal{R}(p,q)-$deformation, where $\mathcal{R}(u,v)$ is a meromorphic kernel satisfying $0<q<p\leq 1$, $\mathcal{R}(1,1)=0$, and $\mathcal{R}(p^n,q^n)>0$.
  A Stirling-type asymptotic expansion is established for the $\mathcal{R}(p,q)-$deformed Gamma function $Γ_{\mathcal{R}(p,q)}$, yielding precise exponential quadratic growth estimates driven by the asymptotics of the deformed factorial $\mathcal{R}!(p^n,q^n)\sim \exp(λn^2)$.
  These asymptotics induce sharp coefficient bounds and Cauchy-type inequalities for $\mathcal{R}(p,q)-$entire functions. Based on these estimates, we introduce $\mathcal{R}(p,q)-$weighted Banach and Fréchet spaces of holomorphic functions, together with deformation dependent pseudo-norms and valuation maps.
  Within this setting, we define $\mathcal{R}(p,q)-$discs and anisotropic sectors adapted to the deformation geometry and prove $\mathcal{R}(p,q)-$analogues of the Cauchy-Hadamard theorem, the Borel-Carathéodory inequality and Phragmén-Lindelöf type growth principles. These results contribute to the broader program of constructing a consistent functional calculus in $\mathcal{R}(p,q)-$quantum algebras, with potential applications to deformed fractional differential equations, operator theory, spectral problems, and non commutative models arising in mathematical physics.

### [98] [Elliptic Generalization of Cherednik-Macdonald-Mehta identities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25908)
*Shamil Shakirov*

Main category: math.QA

TL;DR: 本文提出了Cherednik-Macdonald-Mehta (CMM)恒等式的椭圆推广，其中三角范德蒙乘积被替换为θ函数，Macdonald多项式被提升为Shiraishi函数，并在椭圆参数的一阶近似下证明了所提出的恒等式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Macdonald多项式的积分恒等式在现代数学和数学物理中具有重要作用，尤其是CMM恒等式与双仿射Hecke代数（Double Affine Hecke Algebras, DAHA）及量子群表示论有深刻联系，并在精细Chern-Simons理论中居于核心地位。作者旨在将这些恒等式推广到椭圆情形。

Method: 将三角范德蒙乘积替换为θ函数，并将Macdonald多项式推广为Shiraishi函数——一类具有多种有趣表现形式的椭圆函数。从矩阵模型角度，引入了一个具有超可积性（superintegrability）性质的椭圆矩阵模型。恒等式在椭圆参数下展开至一阶进行证明。

Result: 提出了CMM恒等式的椭圆推广，并证明了该推广恒等式在椭圆参数的一阶近似下成立。

Conclusion: 该椭圆推广的CMM恒等式连接了多个领域：可积系统中的非定态Ruijsenaars问题、代数几何中仿射Laumon空间的等变K-理论特征（equivariant K-theory characters）、以及五维超Yang-Mills理论中的表面缺陷配分函数（surface defect partition functions）。从矩阵模型视角，所得椭圆矩阵模型具有超可积性。

Abstract: Integral identities for Macdonald polynomials play an important role in modern mathematics and mathematical physics. Especially interesting are the Cherednik-Macdonald-Mehta (CMM) identities, with profound connections to Double Affine Hecke Algebras (DAHA) and representation theory of quantum groups. These identities are central in refined Chern-Simons theory, where they lead to refined S and T matrices and ultimately to refined knot invariants. We suggest an elliptic generalization of CMM identities, where trigonometric Vandermonde products are replaced by theta functions. At the same time Macdonald polynomials are promoted to Shiraishi functions -- distinguished elliptic functions with several interesting avatars, from the non-stationary Ruijsenaars problem in integrable systems, to equivariant K-theory characters of the affine Laumon space in algebraic geometry, to surface defect partition functions in 5d super Yang-Mills theory. From the perspective of matrix models, we present an elliptic matrix model with a superintegrability property. We prove the suggested identities to the first order in the elliptic parameter.

### [99] [On the Statistical Interpretation of Discoveries in LHC Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24441)
*S. V. Chekanov,E. J. Weik*

Main category: physics.data-an

TL;DR: 本文在模型无关框架下重新审视大型强子对撞机（LHC）的新物理发现判据，特别关注由同时考虑多个不变质量分布（invariant-mass distributions）引发的“看别处效应”（look-elsewhere effects），并提出了一个统计保守的局部显著性（local significance）与全局显著性（global significance）之间的换算关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期LHC的搜索策略正从基于少量分布的模型特定搜索（model-specific searches）转向更广泛的模型无关策略（model-agnostic strategies）。这一转变显著提高了对意外现象的灵敏度，但也带来了多重检验问题，需要重新审视传统的5σ显著性判据是否仍然适用。

Method: 本文在模型无关框架下，系统分析了同时考虑多个不变质量分布时，由多重bin和多重分布共同导致的看别处效应，并推导出一个统计保守的局部与全局显著性之间的解析关系。

Result: 提出了一个在LHC多个不变质量分布存在条件下，用于联系局部显著性与全局显著性的简单且统计保守的换算关系，可作为未来实验规划的一个有用的一级近似（first approximation）。

Conclusion: 传统的5σ局部显著性阈值在模型无关的多分布搜索中需要修正，以正确计入多重检验带来的看别处效应，所提出的换算关系为这一修正提供了保守且实用的统计工具。

Abstract: We examine discovery criteria at the Large Hadron Collider (LHC) within a model-independent framework, with particular emphasis on the statistical signatures of new physics. This study is motivated by the recent shift from model-specific searches based on a small number of distributions to broad, model-agnostic strategies, which offer substantially greater sensitivity to unexpected phenomena. We revisit the well-known criterion of a local statistical significance of $5\,σ$ for the observation of new phenomena in invariant-mass distributions and discuss how this threshold should be modified to account for look-elsewhere effects arising not only from multiple bins within a given distribution, but also from the simultaneous consideration of multiple distributions. We present a simple but statistically conservative relation between local and global significances in the presence of multiple invariant-mass distributions at the LHC, which can serve as a useful first approximation for planning future measurements.

</details>

### [100] [Geodesics and Thermodynamics of a Schwarzschild Black Hole with Hernquist Dark Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24046)
*A. R. P. Moreira,A. Bouzenada,F. M. Belchior,F. C. E. Lima*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究浸没在Hernquist暗物质晕中的Schwarzschild黑洞的物理与几何性质，发现暗物质分布对黑洞的光学、热力学和微扰性质产生不可忽略的修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索暗物质晕（dark matter halo）对Schwarzschild黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole）物理与几何特性的影响，填补标准真空中黑洞解在暗物质环境下的理论空白。

Method: 将Hernquist暗物质晕轮廓（Hernquist dark matter profile）纳入Schwarzschild度规，构建浸没型黑洞度规；分析零测地线（null geodesic）和光子动力学，推导光轨迹变形；导出黑洞质量、视界条件、Hawking温度、熵、Gibbs自由能和热容等热力学表达式；研究标量微扰（scalar perturbations）以考察暗物质晕对标量场动态传播的影响。

Result: 暗物质晕改变了Schwarzschild黑洞的热力学结构和稳定性条件；Hernquist晕参数对光学性质、热力学性质和微扰性质均产生非平凡修正，导致与标准真空解存在系统性偏离。

Conclusion: 暗物质晕对Schwarzschild黑洞的光学、热力学和微扰特性具有显著影响，必须考虑暗物质环境才能准确描述黑洞在宇宙学背景下的行为。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the physical and geometrical properties of a Schwarzschild black hole (BH) immersed in a Hernquist dark matter halo. To accomplish our purpose, one builds the BH metric by incorporating the Hernquist dark matter profile into the Schwarzschild geometry. In addition, we verify the null geodesic solutions and the Halo effect on photon dynamics. Within this framework, one examines the corresponding light trajectories to determine the deformation of photon paths generated by the dark matter distribution. Furthermore, the thermodynamic properties of the system are studied by deriving expressions for the black hole mass, the horizon condition, the Hawking temperature, the entropy, the Gibbs free energy, and the heat capacity. Our results show that the dark matter halo modifies the thermal structure and stability conditions of the black hole configuration. Finally, we investigate the scalar perturbations to examine the influence of the Hernquist halo on the dynamical propagation of scalar fields in the BH background. In this framework, the results obtained demonstrate that the dark matter parameters yield nontrivial corrections to the optical, thermodynamic, and perturbative properties of the Schwarzschild black hole, producing deviations from the standard vacuum solution.

### [101] [Hawking atmosphere of anti-de Sitter black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24091)
*A. F. Cardona,C. Molina*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过半经典方法研究蒸发中的球对称反德西特黑洞的霍金大气演化，利用Parikh-Wilczek隧穿方法考虑反作用效应，并结合重整化能动张量计算，揭示了小adS黑洞蒸发过程中光度与温度关系的显著非黑体行为以及几何、量子场与热力学之间的相互作用机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解蒸发过程中反德西特（anti-de Sitter, adS）黑洞霍金大气（Hawking atmosphere）的半经典演化，澄清几何、量子场和热力学如何共同塑造霍金大气及黑洞蒸发动力学。

Method: 采用动力学框架，将霍金辐射视为通过黑洞视界的量子隧穿（quantum tunneling）过程；运用Parikh-Wilczek隧穿方法（Parikh-Wilczek tunneling method）纳入反作用（backreaction）效应，将发射概率与Bekenstein-Hawking熵变关联；计算时间依赖的光度；并计算Vaidya-adS几何中量子场的重整化能动张量（renormalized energy-momentum tensor）。

Result: 光度与理想黑体行为存在显著偏差，尤其对小adS黑洞而言，由于其蒸发过程中强烈的质量变化，光度并不随温度升高而增加。

Conclusion: 微观隧穿方法与连续几何方法相结合，阐明了几何、量子场和热力学在非渐近平坦adS时空中塑造霍金大气及蒸发动力学的协同作用。

Abstract: This work investigates the semiclassical evolution of the Hawking atmosphere surrounding evaporating, spherically symmetric anti-de Sitter (adS) black holes. We model the evaporation process within a dynamical framework, treating the emission of Hawking radiation as a quantum tunneling process through the black-hole horizon. Using the Parikh-Wilczek tunneling method, we incorporate backreaction effects, with the emission probability being linked to the resulting change in the Bekenstein-Hawking entropy of the black hole. This probability is then used to compute the time-dependent luminosity of the system, revealing significant deviations from ideal blackbody behavior, particularly for small adS black holes. For these objects, the luminosity does not increase with temperature due to strong mass variations during evaporation. To complement this microscopic approach, we compute the renormalized energy-momentum tensor for a quantum field propagating in the Vaidya-adS geometry modelling the evaporation process. Together, these approaches clarify the interplay between geometry, quantum fields, and thermodynamics in shaping the Hawking atmosphere and the evaporation dynamics of black holes in asymptotically adS spacetimes.

### [102] [Red/Blue shifts of photons in a Hayward black hole immersed in perfect fluid dark matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24102)
*L. Marlene. López,L. A. López*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文研究了在完美流体暗物质（PFDM）背景下的Hayward规则黑洞周围，沿稳定圆轨道运动粒子发出的光子的红移/蓝移现象。PFDM参数改变黑洞视界结构、光子球和ISCO半径，并显著影响频率移动模式与黑洞阴影大小，这些效应或可成为强引力场中暗物质存在的观测标志。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用由Dymnikova提出的Hayward规则黑洞解，嵌入完美流体暗物质（PFDM）背景；通过求解稳态圆轨道上的光子频率移动表达式，分析PFDM参数对红移与蓝移的影响；同时利用光线追迹方法计算黑洞阴影半径，并与Sgr A*的观测数据进行对比。

Result: 红移在纯Hayward情形下达到最小值，随PFDM参数增大而增大；蓝移行为与之相反。正的PFDM参数减小阴影半径，负的PFDM参数导致阴影半径偏离Schwarzschild情形的程度更大。

Conclusion: 频率移动与黑洞阴影可作为PFDM效应在强引力场中的潜在观测特征，有助于通过射电干涉测量等观测手段间接约束暗物质参数。

Abstract: We investigate the red/blue shifts of photons emitted by particles moving along stable circular orbits around a Hayward regular black hole immersed in perfect fluid dark matter (PFDM). The PFDM contribution modifies the horizon structure and shifts the characteristic radii associated with circular motion, including the photon sphere and the ISCO radius. We show that the redshift reaches its minimum in the pure Hayward case and increases for nonzero values of the PFDM parameter, whereas the blueshift exhibits the opposite behavior. We also analyze the black hole shadow and compare the results with the observational constraints from Sgr A*. Positive values of the PFDM parameter reduce the shadow radius, while negative values produce larger deviations from the Schwarzschild case. These results suggest that frequency shifts and black hole shadows may provide observational signatures of PFDM effects in strong gravitational fields.

### [103] [Probing the limits of the semiclassical Einstein equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24103)
*Gustavo Schranck Habermann,Daniel A. Turolla Vanzella*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在半经典引力（semiclassical gravity）框架下，利用引力的非线性特性构造了一个可控解析模型，证明弱引力态的退相干混合可将系统驱动至强引力区；通过分支简并可观测量（branch-degenerate observable），可对比量子引力与半经典引力的预测，从而界定半经典爱因斯坦方程的适用边界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 半经典爱因斯坦方程（semiclassical Einstein equation）在量子物质/场对时空的反作用（backreaction）问题中被广泛使用，但其成立前提（量子涨落很小）在实际中经常被违背——尤其是应力-能量张量（stress-energy tensor）的期望值的涨落形式上发散。因此，需要一种系统性的方法来探测该近似的失效边界。

Method: 利用引力的特殊非线性（nonlinearities of gravity），构造一个受控且可解析处理的设定：弱引力态（weak-gravity states）的非相干混合（incoherent mixture）会驱动系统进入强引力区（strong-gravity regime）。通过选定一个分支简并可观测量的响应，来对比量子引力与半经典引力的预测差异。

Result: 构造了一个原理验证（proof of principle）层面的可解析模型，展示了从弱引力到强引力的非平庸过渡；分支简并可观测量能够有效区分量子引力与半经典引力框架下的预测。

Conclusion: 该方法为界定半经典引力的有效范围（domain of validity）提供了新的理论探针，指出半经典近似在强引力或较大量子涨落情形下可能失效，并需借助量子引力进行修正。

Abstract: In the context of semiclassical gravity, the semiclassical Einstein equation is often invoked when backreaction of quantum matter/fields on the spacetime is at stake. It is expected to hold when quantum fluctuations are small. Yet, it is routinely used to justify the central role of the expectation value of the stress-energy tensor of quantum fields, whose fluctuations formally diverge. Here we propose a new way to probe the limits of this approximation by exploiting peculiar nonlinearities of gravity. As a proof of principle, we construct a controlled, analytically tractable setting where the incoherent mixture of weak-gravity states drives the system into a strong-gravity regime. By selecting a branch-degenerate observable, one can compare predictions of quantum and semiclassical gravity, potentially delimiting the validity of the latter.

</details>


### [104] [Towards a causal effective thermodynamics of scalar-tensor gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24133)
*Narayan Banerjee,Andrea Giusti,Valerio Faraoni,Luca Gallerani,Alain Maltais-Gosselin*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文将标量-张量引力（scalar-tensor gravity）有效流体与Eckart不可逆热力学之间的热类比，扩展至因果性的Israel-Stewart模型，通过将热流密度提升为类时矢量（timelike vector）这一最小假设，首次实现了有效温度$\mathcal{T}$与有效热导率$\mathcal{K}$的一致解耦，并保留了广义相对论作为$\mathcal{KT}$趋于零时动力学弛豫平衡态的解释，最后将该因果形式应用于宇宙学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的标量-张量引力有效流体与Eckart不可逆热力学的类比存在因果性问题，缺乏一个一致的形式来解耦有效温度$\mathcal{T}$与有效热导率$\mathcal{K}$，从而限制了对广义相对论作为平衡态弛豫过程的理解。

Method: 采用最小假设（minimal ansatz），将热流密度（heat flux density）提升为类时矢量（timelike vector），将热类比从Eckart模型扩展至因果性的Israel-Stewart模型，从而获得解析可处理的本构方程（constitutive equations）。

Result: 首次实现标量-张量引力中有效温度$\mathcal{T}$与有效热导率$\mathcal{K}$的一致解耦；保留了广义相对论在$\mathcal{KT}$极限（vanishing-$\mathcal{KT}$ limit）下作为动力学弛豫平衡态的解释。

Conclusion: 该因果形式（causal formalism）可应用于宇宙学场景，为进一步研究标量-张量引力中的不可逆过程提供了理论框架。

Abstract: The thermal analogy between the effective fluid of scalar-tensor gravity and Eckart's irreversible thermodynamics is extended to the causal Israel-Stewart model, adopting the minimal ansatz of promoting the heat flux density to a timelike vector. This choice yields analytically manageable constitutive equations, allowing for the first consistent decoupling of the effective temperature $\mathcal{T}$ and the effective thermal conductivity $\mathcal{K}$ of scalar-tensor gravity. Crucially, this new framework preserves the interpretation of general relativity as the equilibrium state approached via a dynamical relaxation process in the vanishing-$\mathcal {KT}$ limit. This new causal formalism is applied to cosmology.

</details>


### [105] [Inferring Neutron-Star Properties from Post-merger Gravitational-wave Spectra with Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24145)
*Dimitrios Pesios,Nikolaos Stergioulas*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了从双中子星并合后的引力波频谱直接反演中子星性质的反问题（inverse problem）。利用数值相对论目录中的无噪声频谱，训练并比较了三种人工神经网络（ANN）回归模型和两种多元线性回归基线模型，以预测恒星质量、四极潮汐形变性和质量-半径关系的斜率。神经网络模型优于线性基线，其中单任务网络集成表现最佳，且模型预测在物理上具有一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统方法难以直接从并合后引力波频谱（post-merger gravitational-wave spectrum）中反演中子星性质，因为正映射（direct mapping）的解析反演不可行，且反问题本身具有非线性特征。本文旨在探索神经网络代理模型（neural-network surrogate）作为解决该反问题的新途径，以期为未来第三代引力波探测器提供数据解释工具。

Method: 采用无噪声的数值相对论（numerical relativity）频谱数据，训练三种人工神经网络回归模型和两种多元线性回归（multivariate linear regression）基线。反演代理模型（inverse surrogate）通过两阶段训练过程构建：第一阶段残差定义第二阶段样本权重，并结合丢弃法（dropout）、高斯噪声注入（Gaussian-noise injection）和早停（early stopping）进行正则化。最终比较单任务网络集成（ensemble of single-task networks）、多任务模型（multi-task model）和混合专家架构（mixture-of-experts architecture）的性能。

Result: 神经网络模型一致优于线性基线，表明非线性代理模型能更有效地捕获并合后频谱与源性质之间的反演关系。单任务网络集成获得最佳性能；多任务模型在预测质量-半径斜率方面精度相当；混合专家架构提供了频谱区域重要性的洞察。最优模型能够复现主导并合后频率与潮汐形变性之间的经验关系，并恢复依赖于状态方程（equation of state）的质量-潮汐形变性趋势。

Conclusion: 尽管研究仅限于理想化的无噪声频谱，但结果表明神经网络代理模型为未来第三代探测器从并合后信号中提取中子星信息提供了有前景的技术路线。模型在点态精度（pointwise accuracy）之外还展示了物理一致性（physical consistency），证实了该方法的可靠性。

Abstract: We present a proof-of-concept study of the inverse problem of inferring neutron-star properties directly from the post-merger gravitational-wave spectrum of equal-mass binary neutron-star mergers. Using noise-free spectra from numerical-relativity catalogs, we train and compare three artificial-neural-network regression models and two multivariate linear-regression baselines to predict the stellar mass, $M$, the quadrupolar tidal deformability, $κ_2^τ$, and the slope of the mass--radius relation, $dR/dM$. Since the inverse mapping is nonlinear and cannot be obtained by analytically inverting the direct neural-network model, we construct inverse surrogates and train the networks with a two-stage procedure in which residuals from an initial pass define sample weights for a second pass, together with regularization via dropout, Gaussian-noise injection, and early stopping. We find that neural networks consistently outperform linear baselines, showing that nonlinear surrogates capture the inverse relation between post-merger spectra and source properties more effectively than algebraic inversion. The best performance is achieved by an ensemble of single-task networks, while a multi-task model gives comparable accuracy for predicting the mass--radius slope, and a mixture-of-experts architecture provides insight into spectral-region importance. We further show that the best model reproduces empirical relations between the dominant post-merger frequency and tidal deformability, and recovers equation-of-state-dependent mass--tidal-deformability trends, indicating physical consistency beyond pointwise accuracy. Although restricted to idealized noise-free spectra, the results show that neural-network surrogates provide a promising route for extracting neutron-star information from post-merger signals with future third-generation detectors.

### [106] [Stress-Energy Tensor for Modified General Relativity with Quantum-Deformed Metric in Riemann Spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24282)
*A. Tawfik,Saleh O. Allehabi,A. A. Alshehri,M. Nasar,M. Maher*

Abstract: The generalized noncommutative Heisenberg algebra, which is based on the generalized uncertainty principle, imposes a minimal length uncertainty on quantum mechanics (QM), on one hand. On the other hand, the quantum-induced spacetime which is based on quantum-deformed metric through geometric quantization is proposed as additional curvatures on the relativistic tangent bundle on Finsler manifold. An additional term that incorporates minimal length discretization along with second-order derivatives of tangent covectors, thereby suggesting an approach to reconcile the principles of QM with General Relativity (GR), is utilized for the construction of a torsion-free quantum-deformed metric on Riemann manifold. Consequently, it is proposed that quantum-induced revisions to the symmetric stress-energy tensor, source of spacetime curvature, along with the current density related to the gauge transformations of gravity, ought to be taken into account in the matter Lagrangian with electromagnetic and scalar components. Vanishing covariant derivative of the quantum-induced stress-energy tensor suggests that the corresponding continuity equation implies that the gravitational fields do work on the classical and quantum matter and vice versa and the non-gravitational energy and momentum are no longer entirely conserved. For vanishing tangent covector derivatives and/or minimal length uncertainty, the classical formulations of the Einstein stress-energy tensor are retained and accordingly that of GR and QM. We conclude that the proposed quantum-induced formulation of the stress-energy tensor is fundamentally suitable for both classical and quantum-induced field equations.

Abstract: The main objective of this study is to explore the shadow and polarization patterns of a Kerr-Sen-like BH induced from Bumblebee gravity, which, among other alternative theories of gravity beyond Einstein gravity, stands out as a promising candidate for explaining certain high-energy astrophysical phenomena. Finally, the polarization patterns trace the brightness distribution and vary with both $\ell$ and $Q$, reflecting the spacetime structure. ### [108] [Non-monotonic evolution of multipartite entanglement under the Unruh effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24424)
*Shu-Min Wu,Si-Han Shang,Si-Yu Liu,Rui-Yang Xu,Qianqian Liu,Xiao-Li Huang*

TL;DR: 本文通过Unruh-DeWitt探测器模型研究四量子比特Dicke态在相对论运动下的四方纠缠行为，发现纠缠呈现非单调演化——随加速度增加先下降后回升至有限值，表明Unruh效应在多方纠缠中具有双重角色，既能衰减也能增强纠缠。Dicke态因此对Unruh退相干更具鲁棒性，有利于相对论量子信息处理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用Unruh-DeWitt探测器模型（Unruh-DeWitt detector model），令其中一个探测器经历均匀加速度（uniform acceleration），分析四量子比特Dicke态在相对论运动下的四方纠缠（tetrapartite entanglement）变化。

Result: 纠缠呈现非单调演化（non-monotonic evolution）：随加速度增大，纠缠先下降后回升，最终趋于一个有限值。这表明Unruh效应在有限参数区间内反而能够增强多方纠缠，与传统预期的单调退化相反。

Conclusion: Unruh效应在多方纠缠系统中具有双重角色（dual role），既能导致纠缠退化也能促进纠缠增强。Dicke态作为对Unruh退相干（Unruh-induced decoherence）更具鲁棒性的多方量子资源，可能在相对论量子信息处理（relativistic quantum information processing）任务中提供优势。

Abstract: We investigate the behavior of tetrapartite entanglement in a four-qubit Dicke state under relativistic motion by employing the Unruh-DeWitt detector model, where one detector undergoes uniform acceleration. We show that the entanglement exhibits a non-monotonic evolution: it first decreases and subsequently increases toward a finite value as the acceleration grows. In contrast to the conventional view that the Unruh effect leads to a monotonic degradation of multipartite entanglement, our results demonstrate that it can instead enhance multipartite entanglement within a finite parameter regime. This behavior reveals a dual role of the Unruh effect in multipartite systems. Our findings therefore provide a refined understanding of relativistic multipartite quantum correlations, indicating that Dicke states constitute more robust multipartite quantum resources against Unruh-induced decoherence and may offer advantages for relativistic quantum information processing tasks.

### [109] [Shaping black hole resonances I. Black hole ringdown as a spectral filtering process](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24704)
*Alejandro Svyatkovskyy Kholyavka,Jose Antonio León Vega,Samuel Gómez Gómez,Xisco Jiménez Forteza,Sayak Datta*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文发现黑洞准正则模（QNM）的激发遵循一个简单的谱规则：每个模式的激发幅度由扰动在其特征频率处的傅里叶分量决定。黑洞充当共振谱滤波器（resonant spectral filters），当扰动的中心频率接近QNM频率的实部时激发最强。作者通过构造可独立调谐谱带宽和载波频率的局域化扰动，从解析和数值上验证了这一机制，并开发了新的拟合算法$\mathtt{QNMToolkit}$用于时域演化拟合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑洞扰动后的ringdown信号可由准正则模（quasinormal modes, QNMs）的叠加描述，但控制模式激发的物理机制尚不清晰，通常只能逐案例处理，缺乏统一的定量理解。

Method: 从激发系数的因子化分解出发，建立扰动频谱特性与ringdown幅度之间的直接定量联系；构造具有独立可调谱带宽和载波频率的局域化扰动；通过解析推导证明激发幅度等于初始数据在波数$k\simω_n$处的加权空间傅里叶变换；开发新拟合算法$\mathtt{QNMToolkit}$，对大量滑动时间窗口上的ringdown进行系综拟合并量化方差。

Result: 解析和数值结果均表明黑洞作为共振谱滤波器（resonant spectral filter），选择性激发频率位于扰动谱支撑（spectral support）内的QNM模式；当扰动主频接近QNM频率实部时激发最大化，该结论通过时域数值演化的百分比级精度拟合得到验证。

Conclusion: QNM激发由简单的谱规则控制，建立了扰动谱特性与ringdown幅度之间的定量联系，为理解黑洞激发的物理机制提供了统一框架，新算法$\mathtt{QNMToolkit}$提升了ringdown拟合的鲁棒性。

Abstract: The ringdown of a perturbed black hole (BH) can be described as a superposition of quasinormal modes (QNMs), whose frequencies are determined by the spacetime geometry while their amplitudes depend also on the perturbing source. However, the physical mechanism governing mode excitation remains unclear and is typically treated on a case by case basis. In this work, we show that QNM excitation is governed by a simple spectral rule: each mode is excited according to the Fourier content of the perturbation evaluated at its characteristic frequency. This result follows from the factorization of the excitation coefficients and establishes a direct, quantitative connection between the spectral properties of the perturbation and the resulting ringdown amplitudes. To make this mechanism explicit and controllable, we construct localized perturbations with independently tunable spectral bandwidth and carrier frequency. We demonstrate analytically and numerically that BHs act as resonant spectral filters. We show analytically that the excitation amplitude of each mode equals the weighted spatial Fourier transform of the initial data evaluated at wavenumber $k\simω_n$ so that the filter selectively excites modes whose frequencies lie within the spectral support of the perturbation while suppressing others. Consequently, the excitation is maximized when the dominant perturbation frequency lies close to the real part of the QNM frequency, and we validate this at the percent level with fits to time-domain numerical evolutions. To robustly perform these fits, we have developed a new fitting algorithm, $\mathtt{QNMToolkit}$, which performs ringdown fits over large ensembles of sliding time-domain windows and quantifies the resulting fitting variance.

</details>


### [110] [Spacetime discreteness via consistent microscopic measurement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24967)
*Weihu Ma,Yu-Gang Ma*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出时空离散性（spacetime discreteness）并非依赖于特定微观结构或模型假设，而是源自微观测量一致性的必然结果。通过建立微测量原理（Micro-Measurement Principle），将时空量子涨落编码于标度结构（scaling structure）中，从而在保持洛伦兹不变性（Lorentz invariance）和广义协变性（general covariance）的前提下，自然地导出有限微观长度和离散时空结构，而经典连续时空则对应不稳定的极限情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 时空离散性的物理起源是量子引力（quantum gravity）领域的一个核心开放问题，现有方法大多依赖于特定的微观结构或模型假设。本文旨在不引入人为截断（ad hoc cutoffs）或对称性破缺（symmetry breaking）的前提下，从更基本的测量一致性原理出发，为时空离散性提供统一的物理起源解释。

Method: 将无穷小时空间隔视为依赖于标度的测量结果（scale-dependent measurement outcomes），而非预定义的几何实体；提出微测量原理，将时空量子涨落直接编码于标度结构中；构建微观长度的等价对偶表示（dual representation），导出离散等距测量结果；引入标度形变的不确定关系（scaling-deformed uncertainty relation），并证明其可约化为标准海森堡形式（Heisenberg form）；利用几何重整化群流（renormalization-group flow）刻画微观长度，并验证有限长度不动点（finite-length fixed points）的存在性。

Result: 经典连续时空描述对应一个不稳定的极限情形；有限微观长度和离散时空结构作为微观测量一致性的基本要求而自然出现；该构造不依赖人为截断或对称性破缺，同时保持洛伦兹不变性和广义协变性。

Conclusion: 时空离散性可以从微观测量的一致性要求中衍生出来，而无需依赖具体的微观模型假设。经典连续时空仅是不稳定的极限情况，离散时空结构才是更基本的、由测量一致性原理所要求的自然结果。

Abstract: The physical origin of spacetime discreteness remains a central open problem in quantum gravity, with most existing approaches relying on specific microscopic structures or model-dependent assumptions. In this letter, spacetime discreteness can arise instead as a consequence of consistent microscopic measurement. By treating infinitesimal spacetime intervals as scale-dependent measurement outcomes rather than predefined geometric entities, we formulate a Micro-Measurement Principle in which spacetime quantum fluctuations are encoded directly in the scaling structure. An equivalent dual representation of microscopic lengths leads to discrete, equidistant measurement outcomes, with the corresponding scaling-deformed uncertainty relation thereby reducing to the standard Heisenberg form. The microscopic lengths are further governed by a geometric renormalization-group flow admitting finite-length fixed points. This construction preserves Lorentz invariance and general covariance without ad hoc cutoffs or symmetry breaking. Our results show that the classical continuous-spacetime description corresponds to an unstable limiting regime, whereas a finite microscopic length and a discrete spacetime structure arise naturally from the fundamental requirements of micro-measurement consistency.
