### [111] [Field Sources for Dark Matter Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25071)
*G. Alencar,C. R. Muniz,Francisco Tello-Ortiz*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在非线性电动力学（NED）与引力最小耦合的框架下，从暗物质晕（dark matter halo）的密度分布出发，通过场论重构（field-theoretic reconstruction）得到规则黑洞（regular black holes）的有效物质源和NED拉格朗日量（Lagrangian），并系统分析了Einasto、Dehnen、Burkert和伪等温（pseudo-isothermal）等典型晕轮廓的可容许性，发现有限中心密度的晕分布可自然产生de Sitter核心和渐近Schwarzschild行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在非线性电动力学与引力耦合的框架下，探索暗物质晕密度分布能否作为规则黑洞的有效物质源，进而建立晕结构与规则黑洞时空之间的统一几何与场论解释。

Method: 采用静态球对称几何，从暗物质晕密度分布ρ(r)出发重构质量函数和有效物质源；在磁扇区直接得到形如L(F)=-ρ(r(F))的NED拉格朗日量，在电扇区通过场方程参数化获得理论形式；通过分析原点正则性、渐近行为和能量条件检验模型的可容许性与自洽性。

Result: 有限中心密度的晕分布（如Burkert、伪等温等）能自然产生de Sitter核心和渐近Schwarzschild行为；Einasto、Dehnen、Burkert和伪等温等代表性轮廓均可实现有效的NED完成。

Conclusion: 广泛的暗物质晕轮廓族可被NED有效完成，为暗物质晕现象学与规则黑洞时空之间提供了统一且物理透明的几何与场论联系。

Abstract: We investigate the field-theoretic realization of regular black holes sourced by dark matter halo profiles within nonlinear electrodynamics (NED) minimally coupled to gravity. Starting from a static, spherically symmetric geometry determined by a halo density profile $ρ(r)$, we reconstruct the associated mass function and derive the effective matter source supporting the spacetime. In the magnetic sector, the reconstruction is direct and yields a NED Lagrangian of the form $L(F)=-ρ(r(F))$, while in the electric sector the theory is obtained parametrically through the field equations. We analyze the admissibility and consistency of the reconstructed models by studying regularity at the origin, asymptotic behavior, and the relevant energy conditions. The formalism is applied to representative halo profiles, including the Einasto, Dehnen, Burkert, and pseudo-isothermal families. For halo distributions with finite central density, the resulting geometries naturally exhibit de Sitter cores and asymptotically Schwarzschild behavior, providing a controlled and physically transparent link between dark matter halo phenomenology and regular black-hole spacetimes. Our results show that a broad class of halo profiles admits an effective NED completion, offering a unified geometric and field-theoretic interpretation of regular black holes sourced by dark matter halos.

### [112] [Grey-Body Factors and Thermodynamics of Asymptotically de Sitter Black Holes in Generalized Proca Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25076)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用六阶WKB势垒计算方法，对有质量标量场、电磁场和无质量狄拉克场三种测试场分别计算灰体因子与有效吸收截面，并将结果与拟正则模重建进行比较。

Result: WKB方法与拟正则模重建的结果在多数情形下一致，仅在低多极矩（lower multipoles）处存在微小可见差异；增大标量质量会使势垒升高并展宽，抑制固定频率处的透射率（transmission），并将有效透射推向更高频率；耦合参数对灰体因子和黑洞热力学均有显著影响。

Conclusion: 广义Procia黑洞背景上的灰体因子受标量质量与耦合参数调控，透射曲线与拟正则模重建整体吻合，验证了理论计算的可靠性；该结果为理解矢量毛发黑洞的辐射与吸收性质提供了定量依据。

Abstract: Generalized Proca theory supplements gravity with a massive vector field whose derivative self-interactions can support black holes carrying primary vector hair. In the asymptotically de Sitter branch considered here, the de Sitter scale is effective: it is generated by the vector sector rather than imposed through a bare cosmological-constant term. We compute grey-body factors and effective absorption cross-sections for massive scalar, electromagnetic, and massless Dirac test fields on this background. The transmission curves are obtained from a sixth-order WKB barrier calculation and are compared with the quasinormal-mode reconstruction; the two descriptions mostly agree, with small visible differences at lower mutlipoles. Increasing the scalar mass raises and broadens the scalar barrier, suppresses transmission at fixed frequency, and shifts efficient transmission to higher frequencies. The couplings considerably affect the grey-body factors and black hole thermodynamics.

### [113] [Chaotic motion of particles around a Schwarzschild black hole in a swirling electromagnetic background](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25094)
*Wenbin Li,Yu-Qi Lei,Xian-Hui Ge*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究在 swirling Bertotti-Robinson-Bonnor-Melvin 背景下的 Schwarzschild 黑洞周围的粒子运动，通过多种混沌分析方法（Poincaré 截面、最大 Lyapunov 指数、快速 Lyapunov 指标、递归分析和分岔图）发现，即使在没有 swirling 的 Schwarzschild-Bertotti-Robinson 黑洞中，混沌运动也可以出现，且两个电磁场对束缚轨道的存在性有复杂约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在含有两种不同电磁场分量及 swirling 形变的黑洞时空（swirling Bertotti-Robinson-Bonnor-Melvin 背景）中，这些复杂电磁背景和几何形变如何影响粒子动力学，特别是混沌行为的出现条件。

Method: 采用多种非线性动力学分析工具：Poincaré 截面（Poincaré sections）、最大 Lyapunov 指数（maximum Lyapunov exponent）、快速 Lyapunov 指标（Fast Lyapunov indicator）、递归分析（recurrence analysis）和分岔图（bifurcation diagrams），对广义相对论下的粒子运动方程进行数值求解和混沌诊断。

Result: 混沌运动可在非 swirling 的 Schwarzschild-Bertotti-Robinson 黑洞中出现，表明 swirling 背景并非该时空家族中混沌运动的必要条件，其主要作用是移动混沌发生的参数区域。两个电磁场的强度及相对方向强烈约束束缚轨道的存在性。

Conclusion: 粒子混沌运动与可达相空间（accessible phase space）、电磁反作用（electromagnetic backreaction）和 swirling 形变之间的非线性相互作用密切相关，数值结果提供了丰富的证据。

Abstract: We investigate the particle motion around a Schwarzschild black hole immersed in a swirling Bertotti-Robinson-Bonnor-Melvin background. This spacetime provides a physically well-motivated framework for studying how the two different electromagnetic components and the swirling deformation affect particle dynamics near compact objects. By employing Poincaré sections, the maximum Lyapunov exponent, the Fast Lyapunov indicator, recurrence analysis and bifurcation diagrams, we show that chaotic motion can already appear in the non-swirling Schwarzschild-Bertotti-Robinson black hole. This indicates that the swirling background is not a necessary condition for chaos in this family of spacetimes, it mainly shifts the parameter region where chaos occurs. We further find that the effects of the two electromagnetic fields are very complicated. In particular, the existence of bound orbits is strongly restricted by the strengths of the two electromagnetic fields and their relative direction. These results provide rich numerical evidence that the chaotic motion of particles is associated with the nonlinear interaction between the accessible phase space, the electromagnetic backreaction and the swirling deformation.

### [114] [Absorption and scattering spectra of massive scalar waves in charged regular black hole spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25148)
*Marco A. A. Paula,Carolina L. Benone,Luís C. B. Crispino*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本研究计算了有质量标量波在两类正则黑洞（Ayón-Beato-García 和 Bardeen 带电正则黑洞）上的吸收和散射截面，发现场质量的增加会降低总吸收截面，并在散射谱中展宽干涉条纹，且结果在适当极限下与经典和半经典近似吻合良好，同时与 Reissner-Nordström 度规的结果进行了对比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 正则黑洞（Regular black holes, RBHs）作为无曲率奇点的标准黑洞替代方案，理解其与天体物理环境的相互作用有助于检验这类几何结构的性质，并区分正则黑洞与标准黑洞的差异。

Method: 采用数值方法计算有质量标量波（massive scalar waves）在 Ayón-Beato-García 和 Bardeen 两种带电正则黑洞几何上的吸收截面（absorption cross section）和散射截面（scattering cross section），并与经典近似（classical approximation）和半经典近似（semiclassical approximation）以及 Reissner-Nordström 度规的结果进行对比。

Result: 在固定黑洞电荷下，场质量增加导致总吸收截面下降；散射谱中当场速度超过临界值 v_c 时，场质量增大会展宽干涉条纹宽度；数值结果在适当极限下与经典和半经典近似一致；在低至极值黑洞电荷范围内，正则黑洞与标准黑洞的谱可呈现相似性。

Conclusion: 场质量是调控正则黑洞吸收和散射谱的关键参数，可在一定条件下使正则黑洞与标准黑洞（如 Reissner-Nordström 度规）的散射行为趋同，为正则黑洞的可观测性提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Regular black holes (RBHs) can be seen as possible alternatives to standard black holes (BHs), since these geometries do not have a curvature singularity. As a way of improving our knowledge of such geometries, we can investigate how the astrophysical environment interacts with RBHs and compare the results with those obtained in the framework of standard BHs. In this work, we aim to study the absorption and scattering cross sections of massive scalar waves impinging on Ayón-Beato-García and Bardeen charged RBH geometries, focusing on understanding the role played by the field's mass. Concerning the absorption spectrum, our numerical results show that the total absorption cross section decreases as we increase the field's mass for fixed values of the BH charge. In turn, in the scattering spectrum, an increase in the mass of the field leads to wider interference widths for field velocities larger than a critical value, $v_c$. Moreover, we also compare our numerical results with the classical and semiclassical approximations, showing that they agree very well within the appropriate limits. We also draw comparisons with the results of the Reissner-Nordström metric. In particular, we show that the mass of the field contributes to finding situations in which the absorption and scattering spectra of regular and standard BHs are similar for arbitrary values of the field frequency and scattering angle, considering low- to near-extreme BH charges.

### [115] [Hairy Kiselev black hole with quintessential matter: themodynamic properties, sparsity of Hawking radiation, and greybody factors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25245)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于五重态流体背景下的毛状Kiselev黑洞度规，首先求解视界条件得到黑洞质量；然后导出霍金温度、热容和吉布斯自由能，分析局部与全局热力学行为；利用稀疏性参数评估霍金辐射的间歇性特征；最后将Klein-Gordon方程约化为径向方程，研究质量为零的标量微扰。

Result: 指数毛发修正主要改变小视界区域的热力学行为；五重态场和宇宙学常数显著影响黑洞的大尺度行为。热容显示发散点，对应二级相变；吉布斯自由能呈现潜在竞争性热力学分支。霍金辐射高度稀疏，表现为间歇性发射而非持续辐射。

Conclusion: 指数毛发与五重态流体的共同作用使毛状Kiselev黑洞的热力学结构更加丰富，尤其在小视界和大视界尺度上表现出不同的主导机制。霍金辐射的强间歇性提示该系统的量子引力特征可能更为显著，灰体因子和标量微扰的进一步分析将深化对该黑洞动力学和观测特征的理解。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the thermodynamic properties, Hawking-radiation sparsity, and greybody-factor bounds of a hairy Kiselev black hole surrounded by a quintessential fluid. The spacetime geometry contains, in addition to the Schwarzschild mass term, a quintessence contribution controlled by the intensity parameter $N$ and the state parameter $ω_q$, an exponential hair correction governed by the coupling $α$ and the primary hair scale $\ell$, and a cosmological constant $Λ$. We first examined the horizon structure and derived the black hole mass from the horizon condition. The Hawking temperature, heat capacity, and Gibbs free energy were then analyzed in order to identify the influence of the hair and surrounding-field parameters on local and global thermodynamic behavior. The results show that the exponential hair mainly affects the small-horizon regime, while the quintessential sector and the cosmological constant produce significant changes in the large-scale behavior of the black hole. In particular, the heat capacity exhibits divergences associated with second-order phase transitions, and the Gibbs free energy reveals the possibility of competing thermodynamic branches. We also analyzed the sparsity of Hawking radiation and showed that the emitted flux is highly intermittent rather than continuous. The sparsity parameter is controlled by the combination of the Hawking temperature, the effective emitting area, and the greybody factors. Finally, we studied massless scalar perturbations in this background by reducing the Klein-Gordon equation to a radial equation with an effective potential.

### [116] [On the boundary cost of source-consistent warp shells](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25417)
*An T. Le*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本研究分析了亚光速、正能量曲速壳层（warp shell）在经典能量条件（energy condition）下的可允许性。通过对多种源优先壳层（source-first shell）结构的系统性评估，发现能量条件破坏集中在源-真空过渡区域而非内部体区，所有构造均未能通过五项标准检验，且边界缺陷与过渡几何结构相关而非位移场（shift）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对曲速驱动（warp drive）构型中长期存在的能量条件违反问题，以及Barzegar、Buchert和Vigneron提出的源一致性批评（source-consistency critique），需要建立更严格的评估标准来检验亚光速正能量曲速壳层的物理可允许性。

Method: 提出了两种源优先壳层拟设（ansätze）：无位移S壳层（shift-free S-shell）和位移来自动量约束的T壳层（T-shell）。建立了包含正则性、约束满足、显式物质模型、框架无关能量条件裕度和全局诊断的五项标准，并对八种典型曲速驱动构型及600种参数配置进行了框架无关的数值扫描验证。

Result: 所有八种曲速驱动构型均未通过完整五项标准；Fuchs常速度壳层内部满足能量条件（13个内部探针未违反），但在标称壳层以外的平滑尾区出现Hawking–Ellis Type IV违反；600种配置的框架无关扫描未发现任何可允许构型；边界缺陷在静态$v_0=0$极限下依然存在，表明其源于过渡几何而非位移场；沿代表性类光射线（null ray）的零能量线积分（null-energy line integral）对所有源预设壳层均为正值。

Conclusion: 曲速壳层的能量条件违反本质上是边界效应，与过渡几何结构紧密相关，而非体区或位移场导致。源优先方法未能产生任何完全满足五项标准的可允许构型，但零能量线积分的正定性提示点式违反在平均意义上可能被补偿，这为未来的曲速驱动研究提供了新的诊断方向和几何约束视角。

Abstract: We study classical energy-condition admissibility for subluminal, positive-energy warp shells. For the constructions examined here, the energy-condition failures are localized at the smooth source--vacuum transition rather than in the bulk interior. We introduce two \emph{source-first} shell ans"atze whose metric potentials are obtained from the Einstein constraints for a prescribed matter model: a shift-free S-shell and a T-shell whose shift is derived from the momentum constraint. We assess them with a five-criterion standard comprising regularity, constraint satisfaction, an explicit matter model, frame-independent energy-condition margins, and global diagnostics; the standard responds to the source-consistency critique of Barzegar, Buchert, and Vigneron. Applied to eight constructions spanning the canonical warp-drive classes, none passes the full standard. An independent frame-independent verification of the Fuchs constant-velocity shell confirms interior energy-condition compliance (0 of 13 interior probes violate) but reveals Hawking--Ellis Type~IV violations in the smoothing tail beyond the nominal shell. A frame-independent scan over shell compactness and thickness (600 configurations) yields no admissible configuration in either source-first class. The same boundary deficit appears in the shift-free S-shell and persists in the static $v_0=0$ limit, which ties it to the transition geometry rather than to the shift. Along a representative off-axis null ray the null-energy line integral is nevertheless positive for every source-prescribed shell; this is an exploratory diagnostic rather than a proof of the averaged null energy condition, but it shows that the pointwise boundary failures need not appear in that integral.

### [117] [Gravitational Wave Propagation in K-essence Cosmology: Theory and Observational Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25466)
*Sougata Bhunia,Eduardo Guendelman,Debashis Gangopadhyay,Ramón Herrera,Abhijit Bhattacharyya,Goutam Manna*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在 k-本质（k-essence）宇宙学框架下研究了线性引力波（gravitational waves, GWs）传播。在高频近似和 FLRW 背景的横迹无迹张量扇区中，推导出含有效质量项（effective mass-like term）的张量微扰修正演化方程，发现该质量项可在不引入额外自由度的前提下产生频率相关的累积相移，并可能有助于缓解哈勃常数（$H_0$）张力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波作为探测时空动力学结构和宇宙学背景的理论无关探针具有重要价值，而 k-本质宇宙学中非正则标量场对暗扇区的描述尚未在引力波线性传播层面得到充分研究。

Method: 在弗里德曼-勒梅特-罗伯逊-沃克（FLRW）背景下的高频（短波长）近似中，限于横迹无迹（transverse-traceless）张量扇区，推导出张量微扰的修正演化方程；随后利用宇宙时计（CC）、重子声学振荡（BAO）、Pantheon+SH0ES 以及 GWTC-2.1/3/4 标准汽笛数据的联合贝叶斯分析（joint Bayesian analysis）进行检验。

Result: 引力波速度保持光速（luminal），与 GW170817 等多信使观测一致；背景场诱导的类质量项 $m_{\rm eff}$ 导致色散关系修正并产生累积的、频率依赖的波形相移；$m_{\rm eff}$ 可表示为红移相关的函数 $m_{\rm eff}(z)$；引力波光度距离（luminosity distance）与电磁对应体一致，保持标准汽笛（standard siren）一致性；联合分析结果与当前观测约束相容，重现了晚期膨胀历史。

Conclusion: $m_{\rm eff}(z)$ 的演化提供了一种可能有助于缓解 $H_0$ 张力（$H_0$ tension）的新机制，并将引力波可观测量直接与标量场动力学联系起来。

Abstract: Gravitational waves (GWs) provide a powerful, theory-independent probe of the dynamical structure of spacetime and the cosmological background. We study linearized GW propagation in k-essence cosmology, where a non-canonical scalar field describes the dark sector. In the high-frequency (short-wavelength) approximation on a Friedmann--Lemaître--Robertson--Walker (FLRW) background, and restricting to the transverse-traceless tensor sector, we derive a modified evolution equation for tensor perturbations. The GW speed remains strictly luminal, consistent with multimessenger bounds such as GW170817, but the interaction with the background field $\barφ$ induces a time-dependent effective mass-like term $m_{\rm eff}$. This background-induced mass modifies the dispersion relation without introducing additional propagating degrees of freedom, leading to a cumulative, frequency-dependent phase shift in the waveform over cosmological distances. We show that $m_{\rm eff}$ is uniquely determined by background cosmological parameters and can be written as a redshift-dependent function, $m_{\rm eff}(z)$, directly linking GW observables to scalar-field dynamics, while the GW luminosity distance remains identical to its electromagnetic counterpart, preserving standard-siren consistency. We test the scenario through a joint Bayesian analysis that combines cosmic chronometers (CC), BAO, Pantheon+SH0ES, and standard-siren data from GWTC-2.1/3/4. The reconstruction is consistent with current constraints and reproduces the late-time expansion history, while the evolution of $m_{\rm eff}(z)$ offers a new mechanism that may help alleviate the $H_0$ tension.

### [118] [A New Self-Dual Gravitational Instanton Solution on a Local Conformal Kählerian Manifold in a Brane World Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25532)
*Reinoud Jan Slagter*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文在共形标量引力（conformal dilaton gravity）的类克尔翘曲时空（Kerr-like warped spacetime）中发现了一个精确的引力瞬子解（gravitational instanton），该解由一阶偏微分方程导出，关联自对偶性（self-duality），其奇点由五次多项式决定，并揭示了对跖边界条件（antipodal boundary condition）与霍金粒子纯态之间的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索共形标量引力框架下是否存在精确的引力瞬子解，特别是类克尔翘曲时空中的真空解，并分析其奇点结构、拓扑性质与自对偶性的联系。

Method: 通过求解一阶偏微分方程（first-order PDE）获得度规解，利用霍普夫纤维化（Hopf fibration）将黑洞视界描述为 $S^2$，引入克莱因瓶（Klein bottle）超曲面上的对跖边界条件（antipodal boundary condition）来描述蒸发过程中的霍金粒子，并应用5维投影外尔张量（projected Weyl tensor）在膜（brane）上构造有效4维自对偶凯勒流形（self-dual Kähler manifold）。

Result: 奇点由五次多项式（quintic polynomial）确定，表明这是描述Petrov D型轴对称流形黑洞奇点可能达到的最高多项式次数，且该解不符合由四次多项式决定的Plebanski-Demianski黑洞分类。引力瞬子的拓扑为 $S^3\times \mathbb{R}/\mathbb{Z}_2$，中心点位于克莱因瓶而非环面（torus）。该解与Janis-Newman-Winicour提出的施瓦西解在复坐标下的零质量标量场模型存在关联，并发展出一种异常不对称性（anomalous asymmetry）。

Conclusion: 所发现的引力瞬子解不需要“剪切粘贴”（cut and paste）操作，霍金粒子保持纯态（pure state），无需瞬时信息传输（instantaneous information transport）。该解扩展了对黑洞奇点结构和瞬子拓扑的理解，并建立了与已知解析模型之间的联系。

Abstract: An exact gravitational instanton solution on a vacuum Kerr-like warped spacetime in conformal dilaton gravity is found. Remarkably, the metric solution results from a first-order PDE, allowing the connection with self-duality. The singular points are determined by a quintic polynomial. This suggests that this is the highest possible polynomial in describing the singularities of black holes of Petrov type D axially symmetric manifolds and don't fits the Plebanski-Demianski classification of black holes which is determined by a fourth order polynomial. The solution can be described by a locally conformal Kählerian manifold with Euclidean signature and a Kähler potential. This is possible for the effective 4D manifold, despite the fact that a Kähler manifold in 5D cannot be modelled. We are dealing with an effective 4D self-dual Kähler manifold with a recurrent conformal structure. This happened by the projected Weyl tensor of 5D on the brane. The topology of the gravitational instanton would be $S^3\times \mathbb{R}/\mathbb{Z}_2$. The antipodal boundary condition on the hyper-surface of a Klein bottle $\sim \mathbb{C}^1\times\mathbb{C}^1$ is applied to describe the Hawking particles during the evaporation process. We used the Hopf fibration to get $S^2$ as the black hole horizon, where the centrix is not in a torus but in the Klein bottle. The twist fits very well with the antipodal identification of the points on the horizon. No 'cut and past' is necessary, so the Hawing particles remain pure without instantaneous information transport. Finally, we reveal a connection between the description of the interior of our new black hole solution and the similar model proposed by Janis, Newman and Winicour some time ago of the Schwarzschild solution in complex coordinates with a zero rest mass scalar field, which develops an anomalous asymmetry.

</details>


### [119] [A pre-merger-informed spectral-level ringdown inference framework for black-hole spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25623)
*Shitong Guo,Yan-Gang Miao*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出SPRING框架，将环信号（ringdown）的谱级（spectral-level）推断与理论解释解耦，同时利用并合前（pre-merger）信息改进了准正则模（quasinormal-mode, QNM）振幅估计，在GW250114数据上验证了该方法能提升贝叶斯支持度且保持后验一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有黑洞光谱学（black-hole spectroscopy）的环推断通常使用已内嵌Kerr或其它理论特定QNM谱关系的波形模型，导致谱测量与 remnant 参数推断纠缠；同时，传统分析多舍弃并合前数据，而这些数据包含QNM激发振幅与相位的信息。

Method: 引入SPRING（Spectral-level Pre-merger-informed RINGdown inference）框架，将环谱推断与理论侧解释分离，并通过振幅尺度估计传播并合前信息；采用不可知论的两分量阻尼正弦（two-component damped-sinusoid, 2DS）模型对Kerr remnant进行推断。

Result: 在GW250114上，SPRING使不可知论2DS信号模型的贝叶斯支持度相比未使用并合前信息的分析提升了Δln B ∼ 5–10；尽管引入了第二个DS分量的额外自由度，remnant后验仍与并合-环（inspiral-merger-ringdown）估计紧密一致。

Conclusion: 该工作架起了并合前信息与环推断之间的桥梁，为未来的黑洞光谱学建立了一条完全在谱级层面运行的路径。

Abstract: Black-hole spectroscopy aims to infer properties of the remnant spacetime from the quasinormal-mode (QNM) spectrum of the gravitational-wave ringdown signal. In most implementations, however, this inference is performed with waveform models that already incorporate Kerr or other theory-specific QNM spectral relations, thereby entangling spectral measurement with remnant or beyond-Kerr parameter inference. At the same time, conventional ringdown analyses commonly excise the pre-merger data, which in principle contain information about the excitation amplitudes and phases of the QNMs. We introduce \texttt{SPRING} (\textit{Spectral-level Pre-merger-informed RINGdown inference}), a framework designed to separate ringdown spectral inference from theory-side interpretation while propagating pre-merger information through amplitude-scale estimation. As a demonstration, we apply \texttt{SPRING} to GW250114 using an agnostic two-component damped-sinusoid (2DS) model for Kerr remnant inference. \texttt{SPRING} improves the Bayesian support for the agnostic 2DS signal model relative to analyses that do not use pre-merger information, with an increase of \(Δ\ln B\sim 5\)--\(10\). The resulting remnant posterior remains closely consistent with the inspiral-merger-ringdown estimate, despite the extra freedom introduced by the second DS component. This work bridges pre-merger information and ringdown inference, establishing a fully spectral-level route for future black-hole spectroscopy.

### [120] [Periodic orbits and gravitational waveforms around a Schwarzschild black hole with a cloud of strings embedded in perfect fluid dark matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25625)
*Ziqiang Cai,Zhi Li,Zhenglong Ban,Qi-Qi Liang,Zheng-Wen Long*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了位于弦云与完美流体暗物质介质中的史瓦西黑洞周围粒子轨道动力学及其引力波特征，分析了弦云参数 a 与暗物质参数 α 对轨道半径、角动量、能量及引力波形的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究在更现实的背景下（引入弦云与完美流体暗物质）史瓦西黑洞周围粒子轨道及引力波特征的变化，以区别于纯史瓦西时空。

Method: 通过引入弦云参数 a 和暗物质分布参数 α 构建模型，系统分析边缘束缚轨道（MBO）和最小稳定圆轨道（ISCO）对这两个参数的依赖关系，并进一步研究了有理数索引的周期轨道及其产生的引力波形。

Result: 轨道半径与角动量随 a 增加而增加、随 α 增加而减小，能量则呈现相反趋势；弦云参数 a 的增加导致波形出现显著相位延迟；低 a 值的波形在更短时间区间内振荡，高 a 值的波形则延展至更长时间尺度，且振幅差异明显，可与纯史瓦西时空区分。

Conclusion: 弦云和暗物质介质的引入显著改变了黑洞周围的轨道特性和引力波波形，这些特征性差异有望成为区分纯史瓦西黑洞与复杂介质环境黑洞的观测依据。

Abstract: In this study, we explore the dynamics of particle orbits and their corresponding gravitational wave signatures in the vicinity of a Schwarzschild black hole (BH) surrounded by a cloud of strings and embedded in a perfect fluid dark matter medium. The model is characterized by two parameters: $a$, associated with the string cloud, and $α$, representing the dark matter distribution. We systematically analyze how the marginally bound orbit (MBO) and the innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO) depend on these parameters. Our findings reveal that while both the orbital radius and angular momentum increase with increasing $a$, they decrease as $α$ increases; notably, the energy exhibits the opposite trend, decreasing with $a$ and increasing with $α$. Furthermore, we examine periodic orbits indexed by rational numbers $q$ and the gravitational waveforms they generate. The results demonstrate that an increase in the string cloud parameter $a$ induces a significant phase delay in the waveform. Specifically, waveforms with lower values of $a$ oscillate over shorter time intervals, whereas those with higher values extend to longer time scales. These distinct features, including noticeable differences in amplitude, allow the waveforms to be clearly distinguished from those in a pure Schwarzschild spacetime.

### [121] [Scalarization of dark matter stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25671)
*Junya Tanaka*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本研究在标量-张量理论（scalar-tensor theories）框架下，研究了由自相互作用暗物质（self-interacting dark matter）形成的致密星中的标量场增长（标量化的发生条件，发现负耦合参数 β_d 下的参数范围比传统中子星更宽，且该范围与暗物质自相互作用解决星系形成问题的参数区域重叠。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究已分别讨论过标量场与重子物质耦合导致的标量化（spontaneous scalarization），以及自相互作用暗物质可形成致密天体。然而，标量场与暗物质耦合在暗物质星中的标量化行为尚待系统研究，尤其是参数空间的范围。

Method: 在标量-张量理论框架下，考虑标量场不仅与重子物质耦合、也与暗物质耦合，并通过分析自相互作用暗物质形成的致密星模型，研究标量场增长的参数条件。

Result: 暗物质星在负耦合参数 β_d 下的大多数参数区域中都会发生标量化，且该参数范围比传统中子星中的标量化范围更宽。所考虑的暗物质参数与自相互作用暗物质解决星系形成问题的参数区域一致。

Conclusion: 如果暗物质星真实存在，它们可作为探测标量场与暗物质之间关系的探针（probe），为理解标量-张量理论中暗物质与标量场的相互作用提供新的观测窗口。

Abstract: We investigated scalarization in dark matter stars. In scalar tensor theories, the coupling between matter and a scalar field generates an effective mass, which is known to trigger the growth of the scalar field in stars and black holes (spontaneous scalarization). On the other hand, models in which the scalar field couples not only to baryonic matter but also to dark matter have been discussed in the literature. Moreover, in models with self interacting dark matter, it is known that dark matter can form compact objects. Within the framework of scalar tensor theories, we studied the parameter ranges in which the growth of the scalar field occurs in compact stars formed by self interacting dark matter. As a result, we found that scalarization occurs over most of the parameter region with a negative coupling parameter $β_d$. This parameter range is broader than that for scalarization in conventional neutron stars. Since the dark matter parameters considered correspond to those in which self-interacting dark matter resolves problems in galaxy formation, if dark matter stars actually exist, they could serve as probes for investigating the relationship between the scalar field and dark matter.

### [122] [Cesàro convergence of the high-order WKB method and its applications to black-hole overtones and long-lived modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25705)
*Roman A. Konoplya,Jerzy Matyjasek,Alexander Zhidenko*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于Bender-Wu算法，开发了一种全自动的高阶黑洞WKB方法Mathematica实现，并利用对角Padé近似（diagonal Padé approximants）提升了该方法在传统低阶WKB难以处理的区域（高泛音模式与长寿命准正规模）的效率；同时指出，对于非温和类黑洞度规，WKB序列可能出现表观收敛但实际偏离真实值的情况，而Cesàro均值（Cesàro means）可在足够高阶时提供内禀收敛判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 克服标准低阶WKB（Wentzel–Kramers–Brillouin）方法在处理两类黑洞准正规模（quasinormal modes）时的局限性：一是n>l的高泛音（overtone）模式，二是有质量场（massive fields）导致的极长寿命准正规模。同时，探索高阶WKB方法的可靠性极限与收敛判据。

Method: 基于Bender-Wu算法（Bender-Wu algorithm），在Mathematica中实现全自动的高阶黑洞WKB方法；通过对角Padé近似（diagonal Padé approximants）对WKB序列进行改进；引入Cesàro均值作为内禀收敛性判据。

Result: 该方法在n>l的高泛音模式和有质量场的长寿命模式中均表现出高效性；但发现在非温和类（non-moderate class）黑洞度规下，特别是近地平线参数化（near-horizon parametrization）的高阶系数较大时，WKB序列可能出现表观收敛（apparent convergence）而实际偏离精确准正规模频率；对角或近对角Padé近似不呈现逐阶单调收敛，但Cesàro均值在足够高阶后表现出单调收敛性。

Conclusion: 高阶WKB方法结合对角Padé近似可有效拓展至传统低阶WKB难以处理的参数区域；WKB输出的数值稳定性（numerical stabilization）本身不足以作为正确性判据；Cesàro均值的逐阶单调收敛行为可作为WKB方法的内禀收敛判据（internal convergence criterion）。

Abstract: We develop a fully automatic Mathematica implementation of the black-hole WKB method at very high orders based on the Bender-Wu algorithm, which in principle is limited only by memory and computational time, and show that when pushed to sufficiently high order and improved by diagonal Padé approximants the method becomes efficient for two regimes which are usually regarded as difficult for the standard low-order WKB treatment: the first several overtones with n>l and the very long-lived quasinormal modes of massive fields. At the same time, we show that this efficiency has a nontrivial limitation: for black-hole metrics belonging to the non-moderate class, especially when higher coefficients of the near-horizon parametrization become large, the WKB sequence may exhibit an apparent convergence to values which are nevertheless far from the accurate quasinormal frequencies. Thus, numerical stabilization of the WKB output alone is not always a sufficient criterion of correctness. However, we observe that although the WKB method with diagonal or near-diagonal Padé approximants does not exhibit monotonic convergence order by order, the corresponding Cesàro means become monotonically convergent once a sufficiently high WKB order is reached. This behavior may serve as an internal WKB criterion for the convergence of the method.

Abstract: We calculate the gamma ray emission from a black-to-white hole transition. Abstract: We investigate static, spherically symmetric (SS) spacetimes in covariant teleparallel \(F(T)\) gravity in the presence of electromagnetic sources. A general reconstruction procedure is established, allowing the systematic construction of nonlinear teleparallel \(F(T)\) models for arbitrary coframe ansätze. Focusing on power-law (PL) configurations, we obtain several classes of exact solutions, including constant-radius, black-hole-like (BH-like), and wormhole-like (WH-like) branches, and analyze their horizon structures, torsion singularities, and stability properties. The inclusion of electromagnetic sources leads to new charged solutions that generalize Reissner--Nordström (RN) spacetimes and reveal modified near-horizon and asymptotic behaviors. The results are further organized within an invariant classification framework, highlighting the role of torsion in shaping the solution space. Overall, this work provides a unified and covariant approach to the construction and interpretation of physically relevant compact-object, effective cosmological, and regularized strong-field sectors in nonlinear teleparallel gravity, with potential implications for strong-field tests beyond General Relativity (GR).

### [125] [Polarized Anisotropic Stochastic Gravitational Wave Background Search with Ground-Based Detector Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25772)
*Töre Boybeyi,Vuk Mandic*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文将引力波（gravitational waves）的完整斯托克斯分解（Stokes decomposition）方法引入地基探测器网络，实现了对强度（I）、圆偏振（V）和线偏振（Q, U）的最大似然联合制图（full-Stokes maximum-likelihood map-making）分析，并应用于LVK O3数据以约束偏振角功率谱。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 类比宇宙微波背景偏振测量（CMB polarimetry），在探测器网络中实现了完整斯托克斯参数的最大似然制图（maximum-likelihood map-making），将标准交叉关联数据产品推广至I、V、Q、U的联合重建，并利用Fisher内积（Fisher inner product）分析各斯托克斯响应之间的非正交性。

Result: 使用LVK O3数据约束了偏振角谱Cℓ^VV、Cℓ^EE、Cℓ^BB以及|Cℓ^IV|；发现纯强度模型在有偏振成分时存在偏差，且瞬态致密双星并合（transient CBC）前景的偏振散粒噪声（polarized shot noise）与强度散粒噪声相比不具有参数性压制。

Conclusion: 完整的斯托克斯框架能够分离各偏振扇区，同时提供对纯强度搜索无法见到的偏振各向异性（polarized anisotropies）的观测能力，为引力波背景的偏振分析奠定了方法学基础。

Abstract: Gravitational waves admit a Stokes decomposition into intensity ($I$), circular polarization ($V$), and linear polarization ($Q$, $U$), analogous to Cosmic Microwave Background (CMB) polarimetry. We implement a full-Stokes maximum-likelihood SGWB map-making analysis for ground-based detector networks, promoting the standard cross-correlation data products used in existing pipelines to a joint reconstruction of $I$, $V$, $Q$, $U$. Applied to LVK O3 data, we constrain the polarized angular spectra $C^{VV}_\ell$, $C^{EE}_\ell$, $C^{BB}_\ell$ and $|C^{IV}_\ell|$. We show that an intensity-only model is biased when polarized sky components are present, since the detector-network Fisher inner product does not generally make the Stokes responses orthogonal. For transient CBC foregrounds, polarized shot noise is not parametrically suppressed relative to ordinary CBC intensity shot noise. The full Stokes framework separates the Stokes sectors while providing access to polarized anisotropies invisible to conventional intensity-only searches.

### [126] [Generalising gravitationally induced decoherence beyond linear environmental interactions in a microscopic quantum mechanical toy model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25936)
*Max Joseph Fahn,Renata Ferrero,Kristina Giesel,Roman Kemper*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文推广了引力诱导退相干（gravitationally induced decoherence）的量子力学玩具模型，将系统哈密顿量与环境中谐振子位置算符的线性耦合替换为基于Weyl元（Weyl element）的指数型耦合，并推导了相应的主方程。通过两种互补方法计算环境关联函数，数值分析支持马尔可夫近似（Markov approximation）的有效性，且在小Weyl参数极限下恢复原线性耦合模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原有引力诱导退相干模型仅考虑了系统哈密顿量与环境中位置算符的线性耦合，而聚合物量子力学（polymer quantum mechanics）中的基本算符是Weyl元，且通过截断指数Weyl元可能产生非线性相互作用。本文旨在扩展该模型，引入Weyl元形式的耦合以探索更广泛的相互作用类型。

Method: 将耦合形式改为环境位置算符的Weyl元，聚焦于正弦型耦合（sinus-like coupling）并用薛定谔表象（Schrödinger representation）量子化。发展两种解析方法计算环境关联函数：第一种利用Wick定理（Wick's theorem）和产生湮灭算符；第二种基于短时傅里叶变换（short-time Fourier transform），避免使用产生湮灭算符。进一步推广了适用于指数耦合结构的谱密度（spectral density）。

Result: 两种方法得到的关联函数结果一致。数值分析表明环境关联函数随时间快速衰减，支持马尔可夫近似。对Weyl参数进行泰勒展开（Taylor expansion），一阶项重现了Xu, Blencowe (2022)和Domi et al. (2024)的退相干模型。推导得到了重整化主方程（renormalised master equation）的解。

Conclusion: 本文提出的Weyl元耦合框架成功推广了引力诱导退相干模型，既保留了聚合物量子力学的结构特征，又在小参数极限下与原有线性耦合模型相容。所发展的两种关联函数计算方法具有互补性，其中基于短时傅里叶变换的方法更容易推广到聚合物量子化方案。

Abstract: We generalise the quantum mechanical toy model for gravitationally induced decoherence presented in Xu, Blencowe (2022) and Domi et al. (2024). In contrast to earlier formulations, in which the Hamiltonian of the system of interest is linearly coupled to the position operators of the oscillators in the environment, we consider an interaction formulated in terms of Weyl elements of the environment's position operators. This extension is motivated by polymer quantum mechanics, in which Weyl elements are fundamental operators, as well as by the possibility of generating non-linear interactions through suitable truncations of the exponential Weyl elements. Here we focus on a sinus-like coupling that is still quantised using the Schrödinger representation and, in the limit of a small Weyl parameter, reproduces the conventional linear interaction. To derive the corresponding master equation, we developed two complementary methods for the analytical calculation of the environmental correlation functions. The first utilises Wick's theorem for thermal expectation values in conjunction with annihilation and creation operators, while the second is based on the short-time Fourier transform and completely avoids the use of annihilation and creation operators, making it more readily transferable and generalisable to a polymer quantisation. Both approaches yield identical results. We further generalise the spectral density required for the exponential coupling structure. A numerical analysis shows that the environmental correlation functions decay rapidly with time, which supports the validity of the Markov approximation. Using a Taylor expansion in the Weyl parameter, we show that the first-order term reproduces the decoherence model of Xu, Blencowe (2022) and Domi et al. (2024). Finally, we derive the solution to the renormalised master equation.

</details>


### [127] [Gravitational wave interactions with matter: beyond quadrupolar perturbations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25950)
*Ulrich K. Beckering Vinckers,Nigel T. Bishop*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用Bondi-Sachs形式论，将线性化引力波（gravitational wave, GW）与物质相互作用的理论从四极（quadrupolar, ℓ=2）扰动推广至一般ℓ≥2的闵可夫斯基背景情况，得到了任意ℓ下的阻尼与加热效应公式，并发现高阶ℓ模效应普遍增强，因而难以在双中子星并合或核心坍缩超新星的后并合信号中被观测到。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有工作利用Bondi-Sachs形式论发展了线性化引力波（gravitational wave, GW）与物质相互作用的理论，但扰动仅局限于四极（quadrupolar, ℓ=2）情形。本文旨在将该理论推广至闵可夫斯基背景下的任意ℓ≥2情况。

Method: 基于Bondi-Sachs形式论，将线性化引力波与物质相互作用的理论从ℓ=2的四极扰动推广至闵可夫斯基背景下的一般ℓ≥2情形，推导出任意ℓ下的引力波阻尼与加热效应公式。

Result: 获得了任意ℓ≥2下引力波阻尼与加热效应的公式，并发现高阶ℓ模（higher ℓ-modes）的效应普遍强于低阶模。

Conclusion: 由于高阶ℓ模的阻尼与加热效应更强，这些模式不太可能在双中子星并合（binary neutron star merger）或核心坍缩超新星（core collapse supernova）的后并合信号中被观测到。

Abstract: Previous work has developed the theory of linearized gravitational wave (GW) interactions with matter using the Bondi-Sachs formalism, but with the perturbations restricted to be quadrupolar, i.e., the angular dependence is spherical harmonic with $\ell=2$. Here, the theory is extended to the case of GWs on a Minkowski background with general $\ell$. Formulas for the GW damping and heating effects are obtained for arbitrary $\ell\ge 2$. It is found that the effects are, generally, enhanced, and this suggests that it is unlikely that higher $\ell$-modes will be seen in GW observations of the post-merger signal of a binary neutron star merger, or of a core collapse supernova.

</details>


### [128] [Hyperboloidal evolution for scalar scattering in Minkowski space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26028)
*Ekrem S Demirboğa,Anıl Zenginoğlu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于闵可夫斯基时空中全局标量波散射的时域数值框架，核心思想是通过精确的共形匹配（conformal matching）连接三个紧致化区域：过去双曲面域（$\mathscr I^-$ 附近）、彭罗斯域（空间无穷远 $i^0$ 邻域）和未来双曲面域（$\mathscr I^+$ 附近），从而在无人工类时外边界且无需插值的情况下实现从 $\mathscr I^-$ 经 $i^0$ 到 $\mathscr I^+$ 的全局演化。数值实验针对球对称标量波及多种非线性势进行了验证，展示了稳定传播、辐射提取和收敛性表现，同时指出了立方非线性情形下由于边界正则性不足带来的收敛性限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有全局散射数值方法通常依赖人工类时外边界或需要在 scri 固定规范（scri-fixing gauges）之间进行插值，这些做法会引入数值误差且难以准确处理空间无穷远 $i^0$ 区域。本文旨在建立一种无需人工边界和插值的全局演化方案，以在紧致化坐标下直接连接 $\mathscr I^-$、$i^0$ 和 $\mathscr I^+$。

Method: 构建时域数值框架，核心在于对闵可夫斯基时空进行三个紧致化区域的精确共形匹配：过去双曲面域（附着于 $\mathscr I^-$）、彭罗斯域（覆盖空间无穷远 $i^0$ 邻域）和未来双曲面域（附着于 $\mathscr I^+$）。匹配面为相邻图（chart）中的相同共形超曲面。针对球对称标量波实现该构造，涵盖自由传播、局域线性散射势（如 Pöschl–Teller 势）以及立方、五次、七次非线性的半线性波动方程（semilinear wave equations）。

Result: 数值实验表明：波在匹配界面间稳定传播；可直接在 $\mathscr I^+$ 提取辐射；自由传播和线性势测试达到四阶收敛；五次和七次非线性测试也呈现约四阶收敛，并恢复预期的晚期拖尾率；而立方非线性情形仅有一阶收敛，表明当共形标度后的非线性源在紧致化边界处非零时，当前处理方法存在局限。

Conclusion: 共形匹配策略（conformal matching strategy）在长时间模拟中是有效的，但立方非线性测试暴露了空间无穷远处边界正则性不足的问题，需要通过更稳健的处理方式加以改进。

Abstract: We develop a time-domain numerical framework for global scalar wave scattering in Minkowski spacetime. The main contribution is an exact conformal matching of three compactified regions: a past hyperboloidal domain attached to $\mathscr I^-$, a Penrose domain covering a neighborhood of spatial infinity $i^0$, and a future hyperboloidal domain attached to $\mathscr I^+$. The matching surfaces are identical conformal hypersurfaces in the adjacent charts. This yields a global evolution scheme connecting $\mathscr I^-$, the neighborhood of $i^0$, and $\mathscr I^+$ without artificial timelike outer boundaries and without interpolation between scri-fixing gauges.
  We implement the construction for spherically symmetric scalar waves, including free propagation, localized linear scattering potentials such as the Pöschl--Teller potential, and semilinear wave equations with cubic, quintic, and septic nonlinearities. The numerical experiments demonstrate stable propagation across the matching interfaces, direct extraction of radiation at $\mathscr I^+$, and fourth-order convergence for the free and linear-potential tests. The quintic and septic nonlinear tests exhibit approximately fourth-order convergence and recover the expected late-time tail rates. The cubic case, by contrast, shows only first-order convergence, revealing a limitation of our treatment near compactified boundaries when the conformally rescaled nonlinear source remains non-vanishing. These results validate the conformal matching strategy for long-time simulations, while identifying the boundary regularity issues that must be addressed using a more robust treatment of spatial infinity.

</details>


### [129] [Ringdown and echoes from compact objects: Debye series and Debye quasinormal modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15429)
*Mohamed Ould El Hadj,Sam R. Dolan*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于散射理论中德拜展开（Debye expansion）的波形分解方法，用于分析无水平面致密天体在弯曲时空中对标量场扰动的时域响应。该方法能将波形分解为直射传播、表面反射和内部透射等成分，并通过德拜-准正则模（Debye-QNM）描述与标准QNM描述形成互补。研究表明，该分解在早期时间也能收敛，并能准确刻画中子星模型和超致密天体模型中的波形特征，包括环降（ringdown）和回声波包（echo-like wavepackets）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准准正则模（quasinormal-mode, QNM）分解在早期时间收敛性较差，且难以直观解释无水平面致密天体（如中子星和超致密天体）中回声（echo）现象的物理机制。因此，论文旨在发展一种新的波形分解方法，以弥补标准QNM方法的不足。

Method: 论文借鉴散射理论中的德拜展开（Debye expansion），构造了一种新的波形级数分解，将时域波形分离为直射外传播、表面反射以及通过天体内部的连续透射等不同路径的贡献。通过分析每个德拜项中的准正则模（QNM）内容，建立了德拜-QNM描述（Debye-QNM description），并与标准QNM描述进行对比。

Result: 在两种“史瓦西星”（Schwarzschild star）致密天体模型（中子星模型 R>3M 和超致密天体模型 R<3M）中，德拜重构与精确波形高度吻合；与标准QNM重构不同，该分解在早期时间即可收敛，准确描述了包括即时响应在内的所有波形特征。在中子星情况下，低阶德拜项主要描述环降（ringdown）和与亚阈值分支割线（sub-threshold branch cut）相关的非模成分；在超致密情况下，德拜级数将波形组织为即时响应/环降以及一系列可分辨的回声波包（echo-like wavepackets）。

Conclusion: 德拜-QNM展开与标准QNM展开具有互补的谱解释：前者识别单个传播通道中的模式，后者描述前者的重求和所产生的集体共振（collective resonances）。这一区别澄清了回声结构如何通过内部重复传播产生，以及极点和分支割线贡献如何进入时域信号。

Abstract: We introduce a new series decomposition of the waveform constructed in the spirit of Debye expansions in scattering theory, and we use this to analyse the time-domain response of compact, horizonless bodies to scalar-field perturbations on curved spacetimes. The Debye decomposition separates out direct exterior propagation, surface reflection, and successive transmissions through the interior of a compact body, and it provides an intuitive interpretation of the waveform in terms of geodesic trajectories. By analysing the quasinormal-mode (QNM) content of individual Debye terms, we set out a Debye-QNM description that is complementary to the standard QNM description. With this framework, we examine a scalar field propagating on two illustrative `Schwarzschild star' compact-body spacetimes: a neutron-star-like model \(R>3M\) and an ultracompact object \(R<3M\). We show that the Debye reconstruction matches well with the exact waveform, and that (unlike the standard QNM reconstruction) it converges even at early times, giving an accurate description of all waveform features including the prompt response. In the neutron-star case, the low-order Debye terms mainly describe the ringdown and a non-modal component associated with the sub-threshold branch cut. In the ultracompact case, the Debye series organizes the waveform into a prompt/ringdown contribution followed by a succession of individually resolved echo-like wavepackets. The new Debye-QNM expansion and the standard QNM expansion have complementary spectral interpretations: the former identifies modes in individual propagation channels, whereas the latter describes collective resonances that are resummations of the former. This distinction clarifies how echo-like structures emerge from repeated interior propagation, and how pole and branch-cut contributions enter the time-domain signal.

</details>

### [130] [Hamilton-Jacobi Approach to Inflationary Scenarios through Extended Entropies: An Observational Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23990)
*H R M Zarandi,Esmaiel Ebrahimi,Yo Toda*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文在非标准熵形式框架下系统推广慢滚暴胀范式，利用Hamilton–Jacobi形式建立暴胀势、广义熵函数与宇宙学观测量之间的直接联系，并引入一种新的非线性哈勃参数化方案。通过对Tsallis、Rényi和Kaniadakis三种广义熵参数进行观测约束，获得了与最新数据一致的参数估计，并采用双途径分析方法（主参数约束与观测不确定性影响评估）限制熵基暴胀模型的有效参数空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用Hamilton–Jacobi形式建立暴胀势、广义熵函数与宇宙学观测量之间的直接联系；引入一种新颖的非线性哈勃参数化方案（non-linear parametrization of the Hubble parameter）；采用双途径分析：首先用谱指数标量（$n_s$）和张量标量比（$r$）约束模型，其次通过改变$r$的上限观测不确定性（$\sigma_r$）评估其对参数估计的影响。

Result: 获得了与近期观测数据一致的参数估计：Tsallis参数$\delta \simeq 1.1-1.2$、Rényi参数$\alpha \sim \mathcal{O}(10^{-14})$、Kaniadakis统计参数$K \sim \mathcal{O}(10^{-17})$；双途径分析产生了互补的后验分布（posterior distributions），有效限制了熵基暴胀模型的可行参数空间。

Conclusion: Hamilton–Jacobi方法对暴胀时期动力学、再加热过程（reheating process）以及后期宇宙结构的演化具有重要意义；基于广义熵的暴胀模型在观测约束下具有可行且受限的参数空间。

Abstract: The slow-roll inflation paradigm can be systematically generalized within the framework of non-standard entropy formalisms, giving rise to a broad class of inflationary models that deviate from the conventional Bekenstein--Hawking case. We adopt a pragmatic observational strategy, employing the Hamilton--Jacobi formalism to establish a direct link between the inflationary potential, the generalized entropy function, and the resulting cosmological observables. In this approach we introduce a novel non-linear parametrization of the Hubble parameter, yielding sensible results, including consistency with recent observational data and new estimates of the cosmological parameters of the generalized entropy framework: the Tsallis parameter $δ\simeq1.1-1.2$, the Rényi parameter $α\sim\mathcal{O}(10^{-14})$, and the Kaniadakis statistics parameter $K\sim\mathcal{O}(10^{-17})$. Our analysis proceeds in two regimes: first, by constraining models directly with the primary inflationary parameters including the scalar spectral index ($n_s$) and the tensor-to-scalar ratio ($r$); second, by exploring the impact of the observational uncertainty on the upper bound of $r$ ($σ_r$), which we vary to assess its influence on parameter estimation. This dual approach yields complementary posterior distributions that restrict the viable parameter space of entropy-based inflationary models. We further highlight the implications of the Hamilton--Jacobi method for the dynamics of the inflationary epoch, the reheating process, and, as a secondary objective, the subsequent evolution of cosmic structure in the late universe.

*William Giarè,Jeremy Sakstein*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文通过自底向上和自顶向下相结合的方法，论证了要利用单个标量场同时解释早期和晚期暗能量，其势能必须具有“陡-更陡-缓”的三段式斜率层级结构，且该结论在引入与暗物质共形耦合时仍成立。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索早期暗能量（early dark energy）与晚期暗能量（late-time dark energy）是否可由同一个标量场统一描述，从而同时缓解哈勃张力（Hubble tension）并解释宇宙晚期加速膨胀。

Method: 采用自底向上（bottom-up）方法，首先识别统一场景必须经历的一系列动力学阶段，推导对标量能量密度和状态方程（equation of state）的要求；再采用自顶向下（top-down）方法，将这些要求转化为具有跟踪动力学（tracking-like dynamics）的极小耦合标量场相空间结构约束。

Result: 满足所有要求要求势能（potential）具有三种不同的斜率，按“陡-更陡-缓”层级排列；该结论在引入与暗物质的共形耦合（conformal couplings）时保持不变。

Conclusion: 所得结果对构建早期和晚期暗能量统一模型施加了严格约束，并讨论了模型构建方面的启示。

Abstract: We investigate whether early- and late-time dark energy could arise from a single scalar field. Adopting a bottom-up perspective, we first identify the sequence of dynamical regimes that any unified scenario must traverse to account for both an early dark energy phase relevant for pre-recombination solutions of the Hubble tension and the late-time acceleration of the Universe. We derive the corresponding requirements on the scalar energy density and equation of state. We then adopt a complementary top-down perspective and translate these requirements into constraints on the phase-space structure of minimally coupled scalar fields with tracking-like dynamics. We show that satisfying all requirements necessitates a potential with three distinct slopes, arranged in a steep-steeper-shallow hierarchy. This conclusion remains unchanged in the presence of conformal couplings to dark matter. These results place strong constraints on attempts to construct unified models of early- and late-time dark energy. We discuss implications for model-building.

### [132] [Mutual Friction in Dissipative Gross-Pitaevskii Thermal Counterflow Turbulence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25915)
*Kyo Yoshida,Hideaki Miura,Yoshiyuki Tsuji*

TL;DR: 本文通过数值模拟耗散Gross-Pitaevskii方程，研究了热逆流湍流体区的准稳态行为，发现互摩擦加速度与平均相对速度呈立方标度关系，并分析了涡旋间距与涡旋线取向的各向同性特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解热逆流湍流（thermal-counterflow turbulence）中超流体（superfluid）与正常流体（normal-fluid）组分之间的相互作用机制，特别是互摩擦（mutual friction）加速度的标度行为及其与唯象阻尼参数（phenomenological damping parameter）的关系。

Method: 采用耗散Gross-Pitaevskii方程（dissipative Gross-Pitaevskii equation）对体区域（bulk region）的热逆流湍流进行数值模拟（numerical simulations），在一定的外力（forcing）、阻尼（damping）和愈合长度（healing-length）参数范围内获得准稳态（quasistationary states），并与直涡线模型（straight-vortex-line model）进行对比。

Result: 互摩擦加速度（mutual-friction acceleration）与超流体和正常流体之间的平均相对速度（mean relative velocity）呈立方标度（cubic scaling）关系，该标度系数与唯象阻尼参数相关；在弱外力条件下，涡旋间距（intervortex spacing）满足预期的量纲标度（dimensional scaling）；与直涡线模型的比较表明涡旋线取向（vortex-line orientations）接近各向同性（nearly isotropic）。

Conclusion: 耗散Gross-Pitaevskii方程能够有效描述热逆流湍流的准稳态特性；互摩擦的三次方标度关系为连接微观动力学与宏观唯象模型提供了定量桥梁；涡旋线取向的近各向同性暗示在体区域中涡旋缠结（vortex tangle）具有近似无规的统计特征。

Abstract: We report numerical simulations of the dissipative Gross-Pitaevskii equation for a bulk region of thermal-counterflow turbulence. Quasistationary states are obtained over a range of forcing, damping, and healing-length parameters. The mutual-friction acceleration exhibits cubic scaling with the mean relative velocity between the superfluid and normal-fluid components, and the coefficient of this scaling is linked to the phenomenological damping parameter. The intervortex spacing follows the expected dimensional scaling in the weak-forcing regime. Comparison with a straight-vortex-line model suggests that the vortex-line orientations are nearly isotropic.

### [133] [Modelling the photocatalytic oxidation of methane and other air pollutants for applications in ventilation systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23999)
*Samuel D. Tomlinson,Aliki Marina Tsopelakou,Tzia Ming Onn,Steven R. H. Barrett,Adam M. Boies,Shaun Fitzgerald*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文实验评估了TiO₂光催化氧化（PCO）在环境相关浓度（2–10 ppm）下对甲烷（CH₄）的去除效率，建立了可解释实验结果并评估通风应用潜力的模型。结果表明，实验室尺度下CH₄转化效率最高可达24.4%，但通风规模下因边界层薄和停留时间短，效率骤降至约0.017%。在利用现有UV-C光源的条件下，TiO₂基PCO可实现净气候效益（净负CO₂e排放率）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光催化氧化（PCO）被视为室内空气净化和室外污染物治理的有前景方案，可处理甲烷（CH₄）、氮氧化物（NOₓ）和挥发性有机化合物（VOCs）等与气候和健康相关的污染物。然而，PCO在环境相关浓度下的实际性能及其在通风应用中的可行性尚需系统评估。

Method: 实验采用二氧化钛（TiO₂）作为光催化剂，在UV-C光强度（4–59 W/m²）变化的条件下，评估了CH₄（2–10 ppm）的PCO性能。同时构建了一个数学模型，用于解释实验结果并评估PCO在通风应用中的潜力；该模型通过本研究的CH₄数据以及文献中甲醛（HCHO）和NOₓ的结果进行了验证。

Result: 在2 ppm CH₄浓度下，TiO₂在测试UV-C光强范围内实现最高转化效率24.4%和最高表观量子产率0.013%。实验室规模下高转化效率（如CH₄达24.4%），但通风规模下因浓度边界层薄和停留时间短，转化效率降至约0.017%。CH₄去除的CO₂e排放率估算表明，当模型预测的CO₂e去除率超过催化剂材料生产和UV运行的排放时，可产生净气候效益。

Conclusion: TiO₂基PCO在环境相关CH₄浓度下展现活性，实验室配置可实现高效转化。然而通风应用中的性能受限于流体动力学因素，转化效率大幅降低。若能利用现有UV-C光源，TiO₂基PCO在通风应用中可实现净负CO₂e排放率，具有净气候效益的潜力。

Abstract: Photocatalytic oxidation (PCO) is a promising strategy for indoor air purification and outdoor pollutant abatement, potentially offering treatment for climate- and health-relevant pollutants such as methane (CH$_4$), nitrogen oxides (NO$_\text{x}$) and volatile organic compounds (VOCs). In this work, we present experiments evaluating the PCO of CH$_4$ (2 to 10 ppm) under varying UV-C light intensities (4 to 59 W/m$^2$), using titanium dioxide (TiO$_2$) as the photocatalyst. At 2 ppm CH$_4$, TiO$_2$ achieves a maximum conversion efficiency of 24.4% and a maximum apparent quantum yield of $0.013$\% over the tested UV-C light intensities, demonstrating activity at environmentally relevant concentrations. We develop a model to interpret the experimental results and assess the potential of PCO for ventilation applications. The model is validated against our CH$_4$ data and literature results for formaldehyde (HCHO) and NO$_\text{x}$. While laboratory-scale configurations achieve high conversions (e.g., 24.4% for CH$_4$), ventilation-scale performance is predicted to be limited by thin concentration boundary layers and short residence times, with conversion efficiencies dropping to around $0.017$%. Finally, we estimate the climate impact of CH$_4$ removal in terms of CO$_2$e emission rates, demonstrating that TiO$_2$-based PCO in ventilation applications can yield a net climate benefit (i.e., a net-negative CO$_2$e emissions rate) when the modelled CO$_2$e removal rate exceeds the emissions from catalyst material production and UV operation, particularly when pre-existing UV-C irradiation is leveraged.

</details>


### [134] [Harnessing AtomisticSkills for Agentic Atomistic Research](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24002)
*Bowen Deng,Bohan Li,Matthew Cox,Hoje Chun,Juno Nam,Artur Lyssenko,Sathya Edamadaka,Jurgis Ruza,Xiaochen Du,Nofit Segal,Jesus Diaz Sanchez,Mingrou Xie,Ty Perez,Yu Yao,Miguel Steiner,Sauradeep Majumdar,Charles B. Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出AtomisticSkills，一个开源框架，通过将科学工作流分层分解为智能体技能（agent skills）和工具，赋予通用AI编程智能体在材料科学、化学和药物发现领域开展原子级研究的能力，集成了超过100项人工筛选的多学科技能，并在多个科学任务中验证了其鲁棒性。

Method: 提出了AtomisticSkills框架，通过分层分解（hierarchically decomposing）科学工作流为智能体技能（agent skills）和工具，提供模块化、可扩展、即插即用的研究能力。该框架集成了超过100项人工筛选的多学科技能，涵盖数据库访问、热力学与动力学建模，以及采用机器学习原子间势（machine learning interatomic potentials, MLIPs）和密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）的多种模拟引擎。

Result: 在多个科学任务中验证了框架的功能覆盖与鲁棒编排能力：锂离子固态电解质的生成式设计、用于CO2捕获的金属有机框架高通量筛选、自主MLIP基准测试与微调、药物设计的多阶段基于结构的虚拟筛选、多模态X射线衍射图谱分析以及析氧反应Fe氧化物催化剂的筛选。

Abstract: Computational materials science and chemistry span vast knowledge domains and fractured software ecosystems. Although large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated research capabilities, scaling monolithic agents to manage the rigor and complexity of atomistic research remains a challenge. Here, we introduce AtomisticSkills, an open-source harness framework that empowers general-purpose AI coding agents to conduct atomistic research across materials science, chemistry, and drug discovery. By hierarchically decomposing scientific workflows into agent skills and tools, AtomisticSkills provides agents with modular, extensible, and plug-and-play research capabilities. The framework integrates more than 100 human-curated multidisciplinary skills, including database access, thermodynamics and kinetics modeling, and diverse simulation engines employing machine learning interatomic potentials (MLIPs) and density functional theory (DFT). We validate its functional coverage against scientific literature and demonstrate robust orchestration capabilities across diverse scientific campaigns: generative design of Li-ion solid-state electrolytes, high-throughput screening of metal-organic frameworks for CO2 capture, autonomous MLIP benchmarking and fine-tuning, multi-stage structure-based virtual screening for drug design, multimodal X-ray diffraction pattern analysis, and screening of Fe-oxide catalysts for oxygen evolution reaction. AtomisticSkills provides a critical agent infrastructure towards building fully autonomous AI scientists.

### [135] [Separable Force Matching of PBE0 Hybrid-Functional Reference Forces for Path-Integral Simulations of Liquid Water](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25081)
*Jan Kessler,Thomas Spura,Kristof Karhan,Thomas D. Kühne*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出两种改进策略（基于PBE0混合泛函参考力和可分离非线性最小二乘参数化），用于从第一性原理参考数据构建力匹配水模型，在保持计算效率的同时提高准确性和可复现性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有力匹配水模型（如q-TIP4P/F）虽能复现液态水关键结构特征，但精度和可复现性仍有提升空间，亟需更系统化的参数化方案。

Method: 采用PBE0混合泛函（hybrid functional）参考力引入Hartree-Fock精确交换贡献；将参数化问题转化为可分离非线性最小二乘（separable nonlinear least-squares）问题，解析消去所有线性力场振幅，仅对非线性形状参数进行搜索。

Result: 优化协议降低非线性搜索维度，减少异质参数间补偿；Lennard-Jones与Buckingham氧-氧排斥项对比表明，Buckingham形式提供更灵活的短程排斥壁；最终模型在路径积分（path-integral）模拟中保持稳定，径向分布函数接近第一性原理和中子散射基准。

Conclusion: 该方法提供了一条透明的工作流，可从精确混合密度泛函参考力导出可直接用于分子模拟的水势能模型。

Abstract: Force-matched water models provide a practical route from first-principles reference data to long classical and path-integral molecular simulations. Previous flexible four-site potentials in the spirit of q-TIP4P/F showed that fitting analytic models to density-functional-theory forces can reproduce key structural features of liquid water while retaining the efficiency required for quantum-nuclear sampling. Here we introduce two refinements aimed at making this strategy more accurate and more reproducible for molecular simulation. First, the production fit is based on PBE0 hybrid-functional reference forces and therefore includes the Hartree--Fock exact-exchange contribution in the electronic-structure target. Second, the parametrization is formulated as a separable nonlinear least-squares problem in which all linear force-field amplitudes are eliminated analytically for every trial set of nonlinear shape parameters. The resulting force-matching protocol lowers the dimension of the nonlinear search, reduces compensation between heterogeneous parameters, and enables a controlled comparison of Lennard-Jones and Buckingham oxygen--oxygen repulsion terms. Applied to CP2K reference forces for liquid water, the projected optimization reproduces target force distributions and yields radial distribution functions close to first-principles and neutron-scattering benchmarks. The Buckingham representation gives a more flexible short-range repulsive wall than a purely Lennard-Jones form, and the final flexible model remains stable in path-integral simulations. The method provides a transparent workflow for deriving simulation-ready water potentials from accurate hybrid density-functional reference forces.

### [136] [A DMFT approach to evaluate electronic frictional effects near solid surfaces of strongly correlated systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25320)
*Yunhao Liu,Wenjie Dou*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文采用基于动力学平均场理论（DMFT）的全密度矩阵数值重整化群（FDM-NRG）方法，研究了二维 Hubbard-Holstein 模型中的电子摩擦（electronic friction），并发现 DMFT 能够捕获平均场理论（MFT）无法描述的费米共振峰，同时 EF-LD 模拟揭示了两种方法在电子布居演化上的显著差异，表明 MFT 不足以描述强关联系统中的非绝热动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电子摩擦-朗之万动力学（EF-LD）是描述固体表面非绝热效应（nonadiabatic effects）的有效框架，在电化学和分子电子学中具有重要应用。本文旨在利用动力学平均场理论（DMFT）探究强关联系统中的电子摩擦特征，并评估平均场理论（MFT）在描述此类非绝热动力学中的局限性。

Method: 研究采用动力学平均场理论（DMFT）分析二维 Hubbard-Holstein 模型中的电子摩擦，其中全密度矩阵数值重整化群（FDM-NRG）作为杂质求解器（impurity solver）。所得结果与平均场理论（MFT）进行基准对比，并进一步通过电子摩擦-朗之万动力学（EF-LD）模拟考察电子摩擦的动力学行为。

Result: DMFT 计算得到的电子摩擦谱呈现两个不同的峰，对应于电子附着/脱离（attachment/detachment）与固体费米能级（Fermi level）之间的共振；而 MFT 无法捕获这一费米共振（Fermi resonance）。EF-LD 模拟显示，MFT 与 DMFT 预测的电子布居（electronic population）演化存在显著差异。

Conclusion: 平均场理论（MFT）不足以准确描述强关联系统中的非绝热动力学。基于 DMFT 的方法兼具灵活性与计算效率，可被广泛扩展应用于更多领域。

Abstract: Electronic friction-Langevin dynamics (EF-LD) provides an efficient framework for capturing nonadiabatic effects at solid surfaces, with particular relevance to electrochemistry and molecular electronics. In this work, we investigate electronic friction in the two-dimensional Hubbard-Holstein model employing dynamical mean-field theory (DMFT), where the full density-matrix numerical renormalization group (FDM-NRG) serves as the impurity solver. Our results are benchmarked against mean-field theory (MFT). DMFT yields two distinct peaks in the electronic friction, arising from electron attachment/detachment resonances with the solid Fermi level, whereas MFT is unable to capture this Fermi resonance. We further examine the dynamics of electronic friction via EF-LD simulations. Our simulations uncover significant discrepancies mainly in the electronic population evolution predicted by MFT versus DMFT, indicating that MFT is inadequate for describing nonadiabatic dynamics in strongly correlated systems. Thanks to its flexibility and computational efficiency, the proposed DMFT-based approach can be readily extended to a broad range of applications.

### [137] [Machine Learning Multiscale Interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25710)
*Àlex Solé,Sergio Suárez-Dou,Albert Mosella-Montoro,Silvia Gómez-Coca,Eliseo Ruiz,Alexandre Tkatchenko,Javier Ruiz-Hidalgo*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为多尺度结构集成（Multiscale Structural Ensemble, MuSE）的分层模型，通过软粗粒化池化（Soft Coarse-Graining Pooling）构建多尺度表示，使机器学习力场（MLFF）模块能够跨多个长度和时间尺度捕捉长程多体效应，在分子与材料的量子力学相互作用预测中表现出色。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实物理系统存在跨多个长度与时间尺度的涌现相互作用（emergent interactions），而现有大多数科学机器学习（scientific ML）模型仅关注窄范围相互作用；同时，虽机器学习力场（machine learning force fields, MLFFs）具有近量子级精度，但其普遍使用的消息传递（message-passing）层会遗漏长程多体效应（long-range many-body effects）。

Method: MuSE采用软粗粒化池化（Soft Coarse-Graining Pooling）方法，通过原子到粗粒节点的平滑分数分配（smooth fractional assignments）构建粗粒化表示，使MLFF模块能够在多个尺度上运行；该模型具有架构无关性（architecture-agnostic），可与SO3krates、MACE及PaiNN等多种MLFF模型耦合，适用于分子与材料体系。

Result: 在基于Hessian矩阵的基准测试、生物分子折叠轨迹以及分子-石墨烯纳米结构中的能量分布等任务上，MuSE能够准确捕捉相关尺度的量子力学相互作用，其表现优于其他近期提出的长程机器学习模型（long-range ML models）。

Conclusion: MuSE作为一种多尺度分层模型，有效解决MLFF中长程多体效应缺失的问题，在分子与材料体系上展现了优于现有长程模型的准确性与通用性。

Abstract: Realistic physical systems are characterised by emergent interactions across multiple length and time scales, posing a significant challenge for predictive machine learning (ML) models. Most scientific ML models focus on a narrow range of interactions. While machine learning force fields (MLFFs) offer near-quantum accuracy, the ubiquitous message-passing layers miss long-range many-body effects. Here we introduce the Multiscale Structural Ensemble (MuSE), a hierarchical model that uses Soft Coarse-Graining Pooling to construct coarse representations from smooth fractional assignments of atoms to coarse nodes, enabling MLFF modules to operate across multiple scales. MuSE is architecture-agnostic and coupled with SO3krates, MACE, and PaiNN MLFFs for both molecules and materials. We demonstrate the power of MuSE through Hessian-based benchmarks, folding trajectories for biomolecules, and energy profiles in molecule-graphene nanostructures, where MuSE accurately captures quantum-mechanical interactions at relevant scales -- unlike other recent long-range ML models.

### [138] [AB2X4 spinel structures: similarity and difference between the centrosymmetric, Fd-3m, and non-centrosymmetric, F4132, space groups](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24198)
*Alla Arakcheeva,Arnaud Magrez,Gervais Chapuis*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文指出尖晶石（spinel）AB2X4结构中的反演对称性破缺（loss of inversion symmetry）可能无需原子位移即可发生，因为中心对称空间群Fd-3m与非中心对称空间群F4132基于X射线衍射数据的结构确定和精修是等价的；区分二者需依赖原子位移的非简谐模型（anharmonic model）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多尖晶石AB2X4化合物的物理性质与中心对称性（centrosymmetry）不符，传统解释是通过将对称性降低至非中心对称空间群F-43m并引入原子位移；但这一解释仍存在与实验不一致的情况，需要澄清结构对称性与物理性质之间的误解。

Method: 该文从空间群对称性分析出发，论证中心对称的Fd-3m与非中心对称的F4132空间群在X射线衍射结构测定和精修中彼此等价，从而说明反演对称性破缺可在无原子位移的条件下发生。

Result: 研究发现，Fd-3m与F4132空间群在X射线衍射数据层面无法区分；只有当实验证据支持时，采用原子位移的非简谐模型才能区分这两个空间群。

Conclusion: 尖晶石型化合物的反演对称性破缺不必依赖原子位移，传统上通过降对称性至F-43m来解释物理性质的做法需要重新审视；非简谐原子位移模型是区分这类对称性的关键手段。

Abstract: Many compounds belonging to the spinel AB2X4 structure play an important role due to their wide range of practical applications. Most of them are traditionally assigned to the centrosymmetric space group Fd-3m. However, the physical properties of some spinels are incompatible with centrosymmetry. This discrepancy is often accounted for by reducing the symmetry to the non-centrosymmetric space group F-43m, allowing thus small atomic displacements from their original position in Fd-3m. In this work, we demonstrate that the loss of the inversion symmetry can occur without any atomic displacements, since the centrosymmetric Fd-3m and non-centrosymmetric F4132 space groups are equivalent for structure determination and refinement based on X-ray diffraction data. If consistent with experiment, only the use of an anharmonic model of atomic displacements can distinguish these space groups. This study aims to clarify certain misconceptions regarding the structural symmetry and physical properties of spinel type compounds.

</details>


### [139] [The structure of a melt: The case of liquid bismuth](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24234)
*Flor B. Quiroga,Isaías Rodríguez,David Hinojosa,Alexander Valladares,Renela M. Valladares,Ariel A. Valladares*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文利用分子动力学（Molecular Dynamics, MD）模拟和逆蒙特卡洛（Reverse Monte Carlo, RMC）方法，对573 K下液态铋（bismuth）的原子结构进行了详细分析，通过配对分布函数（Pair Distribution Functions, PDFs）和平面角分布（Plane Angle Distributions, PADs）揭示了液态铋中存在变形三角形和四边形等局部几何结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 液态铋的微观结构对其物理性质有重要影响，但相关实验和理论研究尚不充分。本文旨在通过计算模拟方法系统表征液态铋在573 K下的原子排布与局部几何特征。

Method: 采用Materials Studio（MS）代码套件对含216个铋原子的超胞进行分子动力学模拟，温度从300 K逐步升至573 K，并在573 K下保持500步以维持液态。提取MD最后1、10、25和100步的PDFs和PADs数据，并以最后100步的平均结构作为液态代表，对四组不同的初始随机速度分别应用逆蒙特卡洛（RMC）方法获得四个原子结构。

Result: PDFs在3.25 Å和6.55 Å处出现两个显著峰，并在4.6 Å处出现一个肩峰（pseudo peak）。该肩峰与晶体Wyckoff结构中第三、第四近邻峰以及液态中变形正方形的对角线距离相关。MS计算的PADs在53°和85°处出现两个主峰，RMC计算的PADs则在58°和90°处出现两个主峰，表明液态铋中存在变形三角形和四边形；高阶几何结构相对较少。

Conclusion: 液态铋在573 K下的原子结构以变形三角形和四边形为主要局部几何单元，PDFs中的肩峰对应于晶体结构第三、第四近邻及变形正方形对角线特征。多种方法（MD、RMC）结果一致支持上述结构解释。

Abstract: Molecular Dynamics (MD) is performed on supercells of 216 atoms of bismuth, going from 300 K to 573 K in 100 steps and maintaining it in the liquid state, at 573 K, during 500 steps using the Materials Studio (MS) suite of codes. The Pair Distribution Functions (PDFs) and the Plane Angle Distributions (PADs) of the last 1, 10, 25 and 100 steps of the MD have been obtained. Averaging the last 100 steps, as representative of the liquid, Reverse Monte Carlo (RMC) was applied to obtain 4 atomic structures, one for each set of initial random velocities. Then, a detailed structural study of liquid bismuth at 573 K was undertaken; PDFs and PADs are calculated and reported. Two noticeable peaks appear for the PDFs, at 3.25 and 6.55 Å, along with a pseudo peak (shoulder) at 4.6 Å. This shoulder (after the first peak) of the PDFs is found to be related to the third and fourth neighbor peaks of the crystalline Wyckoff structure and also to the diagonal distances in deformed squares in the liquid structure. For completeness J(r)s are also reported. Two prominent peaks in the MS PADs are observed: 53° and 85°; and two for the RMC PADs: 58° and 90°, suggesting the existence of deformed triangles and squares. Less abundant are higher-order geometrical structures.

</details>


### [140] [ChatMOSP: A Chemistry-Grounded Mobile Agent for Working-State Catalyst Simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24265)
*Sanyang Ye,Rui Qi,Beien Zhu,Yi Gao*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出ChatMOSP，一个基于化学知识的移动科学智能体，能够将自然语言或语音表达的催化请求转化为参数验证的多尺度操作模拟（operando simulation），实现从实验条件到催化剂形貌-性能模拟的自动化翻译，并通过Pd和Pt的CO氧化案例验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 催化纳米颗粒在反应条件下会发生动态重构，其形貌与活性受温度、压力和气体组成调控。然而，将实验环境条件转化为计算模拟所需的能量、动力学和执行参数需要计算催化领域的专业知识，这阻碍了实验条件与物理上有意义的形貌-性能模拟之间的有效转换。

Method: ChatMOSP将催化剂身份、温度、压力、气体组成及目标可观测量映射到多尺度结构重构（multiscale structure reconstruction）和动力学蒙特卡洛（kinetic Monte Carlo）任务上；通过数据库检索或在线文献获取工作流（online literature-retrieval workflow）构建缺失输入参数；最终执行经过验证的MOSP工作流。该智能体可运行于移动设备，支持端到端研究。

Result: 在Pd纳米颗粒CO氧化案例中，ChatMOSP模拟捕捉到了原位TEM实验观察到的温度诱导的从刻面到圆润形貌的转变，参数既可来自内置数据库，也可在缺失时通过在线检索文献获取。在Pt CO氧化案例中，ChatMOSP在移动设备上实现了压力-覆盖度-形貌-活性反馈循环的端到端模拟，成功解释了振荡式CO转化行为。

Conclusion: ChatMOSP被确立为一个受物理约束的移动智能体，能够实现可访问且可解释的催化剂工作状态模拟。

Abstract: Catalytic nanoparticles restructure dynamically under reaction conditions, so their working morphology and activity are governed by temperature, pressure, and gas composition. However, converting experimentally specified environments into physically meaningful morphology-performance simulations remains difficult because the translation of reaction conditions into model-specific energetic, kinetic, and execution parameters requires the specialized knowledge in computational catalysis. Here we report ChatMOSP, a chemistry-grounded mobile scientific agent that translates natural-language and voice-expressed catalytic requests into parameter-validated simulations using the Multi-scale Operando Simulation Package. ChatMOSP maps catalyst identity, temperature, pressure, gas composition, and target observables onto multiscale structure reconstruction and kinetic Monte Carlo tasks, retrieves database parameters or constructs missing inputs from an online literature-retrieval workflow, and executes validated MOSP workflows. Using CO oxidation on Pd nanoparticles as an example, we verify the ChatMOSP simulations capture the temperature-induced transition from faceted to rounded morphologies observed by in-situ TEM experiments either by built-in database or from web-retrieved literature information when the parameters are absent. Moreover, we demonstrate the capability of ChatMOSP to perform end-to-end study at mobile devices to simulate a pressure-coverage-morphology-activity feedback cycle for Pt CO oxidation to interpret the oscillatory CO conversion. These results establish ChatMOSP as a physically constrained mobile agent for accessible and interpretable catalyst working-state simulations.

### [141] [Ultrafast Magneto-optical Fingerprints of Altermagnetism in MnTe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24320)
*Xu Yang,Xingkai Cheng,Zhuo Deng,Yu-Han Gao,Qing-Lin Yang,Zheng Chang,Peng-Tao Yang,Hong-Mei Feng,Xiang-Qun Zhang,Wei He,Junwei Liu,Zhao-Hua Cheng*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过时间分辨泵浦-探测磁光测量，在交变磁体（altermagnet）MnTe中发现克尔效应（Kerr effect）与沃伊特效应（Voigt effect）的共存，直接揭示了交变磁体独特的双空间（dual-space）本质：动量空间中的自旋分裂能带与实空间中的完全补偿磁化。克尔效应源于交变磁性的贝里曲率（Berry curvature），沃伊特效应源于面内奈尔序（Néel order）诱导的各向异性介电常数，二者不同的弛豫动力学进一步证实了其不同起源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交变磁体（altermagnets）具有独特的双空间本质：动量空间中类似铁磁体（ferromagnets）的自旋分裂能带，以及实空间中类似反铁磁体（antiferromagnets）的完全补偿磁化。这种源于同一晶体对称性的双重性产生了多种新奇的物理现象，因此迫切需要一种稳健且高效的实验手段来揭示这一双重特性。磁光克尔效应和沃伊特效应分别对铁磁性和反铁磁性高度敏感，是探测这种双重性的理想工具。

Method: 采用时间分辨泵浦-探测磁光测量（time-resolved pump-probe magneto-optical measurements），并结合磁化测量（magnetization measurement）与第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations），对交变磁体MnTe的磁光响应进行系统研究。

Result: 在交变磁体MnTe中观测到显著的克尔效应与沃伊特效应共存现象。克尔效应源于动量空间中交变磁性分布的内在贝里曲率（intrinsic Berry curvature），而沃伊特效应则源于实空间面内奈尔序诱导的各向异性介电常数（anisotropic permittivity）。瞬态克尔信号的弛豫动力学快于瞬态沃伊特信号，表明二者分别起源于贝里曲率和奈尔序。

Conclusion: 瞬态磁光响应是交变磁性的独特指纹（fingerprint），交变磁体可作为超快自旋光电子学（ultrafast spin optoelectronics）中操控磁光现象的有前景的平台。

Abstract: Recently identified altermagnets exhibit a distinctive dual-space nature: they possess spin-split electronic bands akin to ferromagnets in momentum space while maintaining the fully compensated magnetization of antiferromagnets in real space. This inherent duality, originating from the same crystal symmetry, gives rise to various intriguing physical phenomena unique to altermagnets. Consequently, a robust and efficient experimental signature capable of revealing this dual character is critically needed. The magneto-optical Kerr and Voigt effects, given their high sensitivity to ferromagnetism and antiferromagnetism, respectively, are ideally suited to probe this duality. Here, using time-resolved pump-probe magneto-optical measurements, we report the coexistence of pronounced Kerr and Voigt effects in the altermagnet MnTe. Combining the magnetization measurement and first-principles calculations, we demonstrate that the Kerr effect originates from the intrinsic Berry curvature of altermagnetism distribution in momentum space, while the Voigt effect arises from an anisotropic permittivity induced by the in-plane Néel order in real space, directly revealing the dual-space nature of altermagnets. Furthermore, the transient Kerr signal exhibits faster relaxation dynamics than the transient Voigt signal, underscoring their distinct origins in Berry curvature and Néel order, respectively. These findings establish transient magneto-optical responses as distinctive fingerprints of altermagnetism and position altermagnets as promising platforms for manipulating magneto-optical phenomena in ultrafast spin optoelectronics.

### [142] [Systematic comparison of approximations and functionals in first-principle calculations of aluminum-based III-V ferroelectric nitrides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24334)
*Alejandro Mercado Tejerina,Peng Chen,Keisuke Yazawa,Andriy Zakutayev,Laurent Bellaiche,Charles Paillard*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文基于第一性原理计算，系统比较了不同化学无序处理方法（VCA与SQS）和交换关联泛函（PBE、PBESol、SCAN、SCAN+rVV10）对Al₁₋ₓScₓN和Al₁₋ₓBₓN合金结构、铁电和电子性质的预测差异，指出SQS结合SCAN是最一致的理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铝基III-V族氮化物合金（如Al₁₋ₓScₓN和Al₁₋ₓBₓN）在铁电材料中具有重要应用前景，但不同理论方法对其性质预测存在显著分歧。作者旨在通过统一超胞框架下的系统对比，揭示化学无序（chemical disorder）和交换关联近似（exchange-correlation approximation）对预测结果的关键影响。

Method: 采用第一性原理密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT），在统一的48原子超胞框架内，对比虚晶近似（virtual crystal approximation, VCA）与特殊准随机结构（special quasirandom structures, SQS）两种化学无序处理方法，并比较PBE、PBESol、SCAN和SCAN+rVV10四种交换关联泛函的性能。

Result: 即使是相似的PBE和PBESol泛函，预测结果也存在显著的定量和定性差异；VCA或SQS PBESol严重低估Al₁₋ₓScₓN中铁电纤锌矿相（ferroelectric wurtzite phase）的稳定域。发现2002年Farrer与Bellaiche预测的五重配位六方相（five-fold coordinated hexagonal phase）是介于四重配位纤锌矿相与六重配位岩盐相（rocksalt phase）之间的低能亚稳态。Al₁₋ₓBₓN中纤锌矿铁电相更快失稳，出现键断裂、结构强扭曲及极化增强，最终趋向闪锌矿相（zincblende phase）和三重配位六方层状相。

Conclusion: 局部无序（local disorder）和交换关联处理方式对于III-V族氮化物铁电体功能性质的预测至关重要；SQS结合SCAN泛函是最一致的理论框架，可用于理解和优化新型氮化物基铁电材料。

Abstract: We revisit first-principles predictions of structural, ferroelectric, and electronic properties in aluminum-based III-V nitride alloys, focusing on Al1-xScxN and Al1-xBxN. Using density functional theory within a unified 48-atom supercell framework, we systematically assess the role of chemical disorder and exchange-correlation approximations by comparing the virtual crystal approximation (VCA) and special quasirandom structures (SQS), as well as PBE, PBESol, SCAN, and SCAN+rVV10 functionals. We demonstrate that, even amongst the similar PBE and PBESol functionals, big quantitative and qualitative differences emerge. In particular, the VCA or SQS PBESol (a popular functional) strongly underestimate the stability domain of the ferroelectric wurtzite phase in Al1-xScxN compared to SQS PBE or SQS SCAN. We demonstrate that the 5-fold coordinated hexagonal phase predicted in 2002 by Farrer and Bellaiche [Phys. Rev. B 66, 201203] is a low-energy metastable state between the four-fold coordinated ferroelectric wurtzite phase and the six-fold coordinated rocksalt phase near the transition point upon increasing the Sc content. In contrast, Al1-xBxN shows a much faster destabilization of the wurtzite ferroelectric phase, with bond breaking which strongly distorts the wurtzite structure (with enhanced polarization) and eventually favor a zincblende phase and a threefold coordinated hexagonal layer phase. Our analysis highlights the critical importance of both local disorder and exchange-correlation treatment in predicting the functional properties of III-V nitride ferroelectrics. Overall, SQS combined with SCAN provides the most consistent theoretical framework for understanding and optimizing emerging nitride-based ferroelectric materials.

### [143] [Dilute Magnetism and Edge-State Engineering in Monolayer SnO](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24376)

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT），在大超胞（supercell）中计算过渡金属（Mn、Fe、Co、W）掺杂SnO单层的电子与磁性质；并构建纳米带（nanoribbon）几何结构研究维度效应，分析边缘局域态及手性纳米带在不同终止面下的稳定性与导电性。

Conclusion: 过渡金属掺杂与边缘工程是调控SnO单层电子性质的有效手段，使其成为未来自旋电子学与纳电子学应用中的有前景候选材料。

Abstract: Tin monoxide (SnO) is a p-type oxide semiconductor whose electronic properties can be widely modified via atomic-scale engineering. Using density functional theory, we investigate the electronic and magnetic properties of transition-metal (TM = Mn, Fe, Co and W) doped SnO monolayer within a large supercell. We find that all dopants induce finite localized magnetic moments, primarily originating from $d$-orbitals of the impurity atoms. We show that these localized magnetic states give rise to nearly
  dispersionless bands in the vicinity of the Fermi energy (taking Co doped SnO as an example). In addition, we investigate dimensional effects by constructing nanoribbon geometries of SnO monolayer. The ribbons exhibit intrinsic edge-localized states that are largely independent of ribbon width. For chiral nanoribbons oriented along a low-symmetry direction of the square lattice, we find that oxygen-rich edges are thermodynamically most stable and remain semiconducting, whereas Sn-terminated edges host metallic one-dimensional conduction channels. Our results demonstrate that transition-metal doping and edge engineering provide effective routes to tailor the electronic properties of SnO monolayer, making it a promising candidate for future spintronic and nanoelectronic applications.

### [144] [Light-Driven Ferroic Switching Enables Reversible Control of Hydrogen Adsorption Thermodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24378)
*Xueqing Wan,Zhenlong Zhang,Charles Paillard,Jian Zhou,Jinyang Ni,Chuanlu Yang,Zhijun Jiang,Laurent Bellaiche*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用光致载流子密度驱动的过渡金属3d轨道占据数重新分布，诱导二维离子铁电单层（ferroelectric monolayers）从铁电基态向具有交错或Zig-Zag反铁磁序（antiferromagnetic order）的顺电相（paraelectric phases）依次转变，从而调控氢吸附自由能。

Result: 在TiGeSe₃中，光致铁性序切换使氢吸附自由能从0.33 eV连续调至1.11 eV，界面从近热中性（near-thermoneutrality）转变为自发脱附。非绝热动力学（nonadiabatic dynamics）表明电子-声子耦合（electron-phonon coupling）促进非热H释放，皮秒级载流子重组快速恢复初始铁性序，形成超快可逆循环。该方法在AgBiP₂Se₆和CuInP₂S₆中同样有效。

Conclusion: 铁性序（ferroic order）可作为光学可寻址的调控旋钮，实现超越静态设计的动态热力学重构（dynamic thermodynamic reconfiguration）。

Abstract: Reversible ultrafast switching of surface thermodynamics is highly desirable for hydrogen storage and catalysis yet remains elusive at the nanoscale. Here we demonstrate that photoinduced ferroic-order switching in two-dimensional ionic ferroelectric monolayers enables rapid, reversible control of hydrogen binding. In TiGeSe$_3$, carrier-density-driven redistribution of transition-metal 3\textit{d} orbital occupations triggers a sequential evolution from the ferroelectric ground state to paraelectric phases with staggered or Zig-Zag antiferromagnetic order. This switch continuously tunes the hydrogen adsorption free energy from 0.33 to 1.11 eV, shifting the interface from near-thermoneutrality to spontaneous desorption. Nonadiabatic dynamics indicate that electron-phonon coupling promotes nonthermal H release, while picosecond carrier recombination rapidly restores the initial ferroic order, closing an ultrafast reversible cycle. Generality is further validated in AgBiP$_2$Se$_6$ and CuInP$_2$S$_6$, establishing ferroic order as an optically addressable knob for dynamic thermodynamic reconfiguration beyond static design.

### [145] [Colossal Type-II Multiferroic Polarization Driven by Collinear Spin Orders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24382)
*Chengxi Huang,Xinhai Tu,Jintao Jiang,Xiangang Wan,Erjun Kan*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文基于自旋群（spin-group）对称性，提出一种不依赖自旋-轨道耦合（SOC）和自旋-晶格耦合（SLC）的新型磁电耦合（MEC）机制，在共线3d磁性系统中实现强MEC与巨大铁电极化（monolayer 2H-VS2中面内极化达25.00 μC/cm²，比典型II型多铁性材料高出约两个数量级），并通过第一性原理计算和微观模型揭示其起源于电子hopping主导的p-d杂化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在II型多铁性材料（type-II multiferroics）中，同时实现强磁电耦合（MEC）与大铁电极化一直是核心挑战。传统自旋驱动多铁性材料中，极化由自旋-轨道耦合（SOC）或自旋-晶格耦合（SLC）诱导，但由于3d过渡金属离子的SOC较弱且SLC引起的晶格畸变有限，其极化通常远小于本征铁电体，且螺旋自旋序往往导致磁转变温度较低。

Method: 利用自旋群（spin-group）对称性分析，提出一条不依赖SOC和SLC的磁电耦合路径；结合第一性原理计算（排除SOC）对单层2H-VS2进行验证，并构建微观模型解释极化起源。

Result: 在非中心对称晶格中，不同共线（collinear）磁构型可分别允许或禁止电极化，表明可直接通过磁性控制极化，从而实现强MEC。单层2H-VS2的共线条纹反铁磁序（stripy antiferromagnetic order）诱导出高达25.00 μC/cm²的面内铁电极化，比典型II型多铁性材料大两个数量级。微观模型表明，诱导极化来源于由电子hopping（electronic hopping）控制的、不依赖SOC的p-d杂化（p-d hybridization）。

Conclusion: 本文结果表明，在共线3d磁性系统中，有望通过所提出的SOC/SLC无关路线，实现兼具强MEC与大电子极化的新型II型多铁性材料。

Abstract: Achieving strong magnetoelectric coupling (MEC) together with large ferroelectric polarization remains a central challenge in type-II multiferroics. In conventional spin-driven multiferroics, the induced polarization is usually mediated by spin-orbit coupling (SOC) or spin-lattice coupling (SLC). Since many representative systems are based on 3d transition-metal ions, where SOC is relatively weak and SLC-induced lattice distortions are often limited, their polarizations are typically much smaller than those of proper ferroelectrics. Moreover, electric polarizations in type-II multiferroics are generally induced by spiral spin orders stabilized by competing magnetic interactions, which often leads to relatively low magnetic transition temperatures. In this Letter, using spin-group symmetry, we propose an SOC- and SLC-independent route to MEC in collinear 3d magnetic systems. We show that, even for a noncentrosymmetric lattice structure, different collinear magnetic configurations can either forbid or allow electric polarization, indicating direct magnetic control of polarization and hence strong MEC. The first-principles calculations excluding SOC on monolayer 2H-VS2 support this picture: a collinear stripy antiferromagnetic order induces an in-plane ferroelectric polarization up to 25.00 μC/cm2, about two orders of magnitude larger than that of typical type-II multiferroics. Furthermore, our microscopic model suggests that the induced polarization originates from SOC-independent p-d hybridization governed by electronic hopping. Our results suggest a possible route toward type-II multiferroics combining strong MEC with large electronic polarization in collinear 3d magnetic systems.
