### [188] [Derivation of the focusing $Φ^6_1$ measure in the optimal mass regime from many-body quantum Gibbs states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25755)
*Lin Lü,Phan Thành Nam,Rongchan Zhu*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文推导了聚焦Φ⁶₁测度作为多体量子吉布斯态的高温/平均场极限，达到了最优质量阈值，并建立了量子级相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在聚焦（focusing）设定下，将经典质量截断（mass cutoff）与量子粒子数截断（particle-number cutoff）联系起来是主要困难；本文旨在实现Oh、Sosoe和Tolomeo（2022）识别的最优质量阈值（optimal mass threshold），并扩展Rout和Sohinger（2025）的早期工作。

Method: 发展了Lewin、Nam和Rougerie（2015）在聚焦设定下的变分框架（variational framework）；引入了两个新工具：非因子化试验态构造（non-factorized trial state construction）和相互作用下符号（interacting lower symbol）的精细尾部估计（tail estimate）。

Result: 在临界阈值下，短程相互作用允许在对数尺度上收缩为狄拉克δ函数（Dirac delta function）；严格低于阈值时，收敛在温度参数上呈多项式依赖（polynomial dependence）。此外，在同一质量阈值处建立了量子级相变（quantum-level phase transition）。

Conclusion: 该方法通过控制粒子数截断引起的局域化误差（localization error）和相对熵误差（relative entropy error）以及聚焦指数权重（focusing exponential weight）的贡献，成功建立了量子到经典极限的收敛性。

Abstract: We derive the focusing $Φ^6_1$ measure on the torus $\mathbb{T}$ as the high-temperature/mean-field limit of many-body quantum Gibbs states with an attractive three-body interaction. The main difficulty in the focusing setting is to relate the classical mass cutoff to the quantum particle-number cutoff. Our result reaches the optimal mass threshold for the classical field identified by Oh, Sosoe, and Tolomeo (2022), and thereby extends the earlier work of Rout and Sohinger (2025). At the critical threshold, the short-range interaction is allowed to shrink to a Dirac delta function on a logarithmic scale in the temperature parameter. Strictly below the threshold, the same convergence holds with a polynomial dependence on the temperature. Moreover, we establish a quantum-level phase transition at the same mass threshold. The proof develops the variational framework of Lewin, Nam, and Rougerie (2015) in the focusing setting and relies on two new ingredients: a non-factorized trial state construction and a delicate tail estimate for the interacting lower symbol. These allow us to control the localization and relative entropy errors caused by the particle-number cutoff, as well as the contribution of the focusing exponential weight.

</details>


### [189] [Chern numbers in quantum graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25899)
*Or Swartzberg,Omri Gat,Boris Gutkin*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文通过在二维正方晶格量子图（quantum graph）中建立简并条件，揭示了两个拓扑相：平庸相（所有能带的陈数（Chern number）为0）和非平庸相（相邻能带陈数在±1之间交替），并解析计算了陈数相图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子图提供了一个解析可处理的框架来研究周期性系统中的陈数和能带简并，但此前缺乏对其拓扑相结构的系统分析。

Method: 将二维正方晶格量子图映射为一个具有两条等长磁通环路的单顶点量子图，并通过建立能级简并条件来刻画拓扑相。

Result: 模型存在两个拓扑相：平庸相（所有能带陈数为0）和非平庸相（相邻能带陈数在±1之间交替）；陈数相图可作为节点散射矩阵参数的解析函数计算，并与数值结果吻合。

Conclusion: 量子图框架能够解析地揭示周期性系统中的拓扑相变和陈数交替模式，为相关拓扑现象的研究提供了可解析处理的理论模型。

Abstract: Quantum graphs provide an analytically tractable setting for the study of Chern numbers and band degeneracies in periodic systems. We study the Chern numbers of energy bands in a two-dimensional square lattice quantum graph. We approach the problem by mapping the lattice to a single-vertex quantum graph with two loops of equal lengths pierced by magnetic fluxes. By establishing the degeneracy condition for its energy levels, we show that the model possesses two topological phases: a trivial phase, where the Chern numbers of all energy bands are $0$, and the nontrivial one, where the Chern numbers of successive energy bands alternate between $\pm1$. By applying the degeneracy condition, we calculate Chern-number phase diagrams analytically as a function of the node scattering matrix parameters and compare the results with numerical calculations.

</details>


### [190] [Field theory of $\mathfrak{su}(n)$: the absence of non-zero scatterings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26024)
*Eugenia Boffo,Ján Pulmann,Ľuboš Ravas*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文以 $\mathfrak{su}(n)$ 形式（特别对 $n=2,3$ 详述）作为有限维规范对称场论中的玩具模型，利用同调微扰理论（homological perturbation theory）证明除相互作用顶点外不存在三叉树图散射振幅，从而将 Cattaneo–Mnëv 的已知论证推广到任意 $n$；同时展示了当转移至更大场空间时如何获得非平凡的高阶乘积。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于 Cattaneo–Mnëv 的已有论证，将其推广到任意 $n$ 的 $\mathfrak{su}(n)$ 情形，并探讨在扩大场空间时能否产生非平凡的高阶结构。

Method: 采用同调微扰理论（homological perturbation theory），以 $\mathfrak{su}(n)$ 形式（$\mathfrak{su}(2)$ 和 $\mathfrak{su}(3)$ 为重点案例）作为有限维规范对称场论的玩具模型进行分析。

Result: 除相互作用顶点外，不存在三叉树图（trivalent tree-level diagrams）对应的散射振幅；该结论成立对任意 $n$；在转移至更大场空间时可以获得非平凡的高阶乘积（higher products）。

Conclusion: 将 Cattaneo–Mnëv 的论证从特定情形推广到了任意 $\mathfrak{su}(n)$ 的一般情形，并且指出在扩大场空间的设置下仍能产生非平凡的高阶结构，对理解规范对称场论的结构有参考意义。

Abstract: We inspect $\mathfrak{su}(n)$ forms, providing greater detail for $n=2,3$, as a toy model for a field theory in finite dimensions and with gauge symmetries. Relying on homological perturbation theory, we show that there are no scattering amplitudes with trivalent tree-level diagrams, except for the interaction vertex, thus extending a known argument of Cattaneo--Mnëv to arbitrary $n$. In contrast to this, we show how to obtain non-trivial higher products when transferring to a larger space of fields.

</details>


### [191] [Universal cumulants and conformal invariance in annihilating random walks with pair deposition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2505.16046)
*Dragi Karevski,Gunter M Schütz,Ali Zahra*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了一维有限整数环上粒子对沉积条件下湮灭随机游走（annihilating random walks）的异常跳跃活动。在临界点处，所有活动累积量（cumulants）均以系统尺寸L的领头阶封闭形式给出，并在热力学极限下经历属于一维横向场量子伊辛模型（quantum Ising model）普适类（universality class）的相变。临界点附近距离为1/L量级时，累积量的生成函数由两个普适量给出：表征伊辛普适类的Virasoro代数中心荷c=1/2，以及一个明确的普适标度函数（universal scaling function）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究受异常跳跃活动条件约束的非平衡统计力学系统，特别是湮灭随机游走模型在有限系统中的临界行为，以揭示其与量子伊辛模型普适类之间的联系。

Method: 将稀有事件条件（异常跳跃活动）引入湮灭随机游走模型，在有限一维环上通过累积量生成函数进行统计分析，并在临界点附近通过系统尺寸L展开得到主导阶封闭解。

Result: 在临界点处，所有活动累积量均以系统尺寸L的领头阶封闭形式给出；在距离临界点约1/L的范围内，累积量生成函数由中心荷c=1/2和普适标度函数两个普适量共同决定。

Conclusion: 该条件湮灭随机游走过程在热力学极限下的相变属于一维横向场量子伊辛模型的普适类，其临界行为由Virasoro代数中心荷c=1/2刻画，并呈现普适的标度性质。

Abstract: We consider annihilating random walks on the finite one-dimensional integer torus with deposition of pairs of particles, conditioned on an atypical jump activity. All cumulants of the activity, defined as the number of particle jumps up to some time t, are obtained in closed form to leading order in system size L at the critical point, where in the thermodynamic limit the conditioned process undergoes a phase transition in the universality class of the one-dimensional quantum Ising model in a transverse field. The generating function of the cumulants at a distance of order 1/L away from the critical point is proved to be given by two universal quantities, viz., by the central charge c = 1/2 of the Virasoro algebra that characterizes the Ising universality class and by an explicit universal scaling function.

</details>

### [192] [Linac: linear algebra with CUDA over finite fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25863)
*Giuseppe De Laurentis,Jack Franklin*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: Linac 是一个高性能、开源的高斯消元（Gaussian elimination）并行实现，支持有限域（finite fields）和浮点运算，专为量子场论（quantum field theory）中散射振幅（scattering amplitudes）的解析重构而设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 求解多项式方程组（polynomial equations）是一个普适问题，但标准的高斯消元法计算复杂度为三次方，且在大系统规模下存在数值精度损失问题。

Method: Linac 利用 GPU（graphics processing unit）实现高斯消元的高度并行化，并采用有限域算术替代浮点运算以解决数值精度损失。

Result: 该工具是一个开源实现，同时支持有限域和浮点运算两种计算模式。

Conclusion: Linac 面向量子场论中散射振幅的解析重建应用，提供了一种可扩展且高精度的线性系统求解方案。

Abstract: Solving linear systems of polynomial equations is a ubiquitous problem in both mathematics and physics. The standard approach, Gaussian elimination, scales cubically with system size and often constitutes a computational bottleneck. The algorithm's inherent parallelism makes it well-suited for modern computing architectures, namely graphics processing units (GPUs), which offer significantly higher throughput than CPUs. Additionally, the use of finite fields -- integers modulo a prime -- in place of floating-point arithmetic offers a scalable solution to the issue of numerical precision loss, which becomes increasingly problematic at large system sizes. With Linac, we present a high-performance, open-source, parallel implementation of Gaussian elimination over finite fields and floating-point arithmetic. This tool has been developed for applications to analytic reconstruction of scattering amplitudes in quantum field theory.

</details>


### [193] [Machine-learned atomistic simulations reveal the basis of hydrogen-induced crack-plane transition in alpha-Fe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24880)
*Jiaqin Xu,Zhiqiang Zhao,Kazuma Ito,Shuhei Shinzato,Fanshun Meng,Shihao Zhang,Shigenobu Ogata*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过构建α-Fe/H的神经网络势，结合大规模分子动力学与巨正则蒙特卡洛（grand-canonical Monte Carlo, GCMC）方法，发现氢致体心立方（body-centered cubic, bcc）Fe中穿晶准解理断裂的裂纹面从{100}向{110}转变的原子尺度证据，并揭示了其双重能量起源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 体心立方（body-centered cubic, bcc）Fe及铁素体钢中的氢致断裂常表现为穿晶准解理（transgranular quasi-cleavage）而非纯晶间断裂，但氢是否导致解理面从{100}向{110}转变的原子尺度证据尚不明确。

Method: 构建了一种高效的α-Fe/H神经网络势（neural-network potential），并将大规模三维分子动力学（molecular dynamics）与巨正则蒙特卡洛（grand-canonical Monte Carlo, GCMC）方法结合，使GCMC域内的近尖端裂纹表面区域和裂纹尖端能与固定化学势的氢储库交换氢原子。

Result: 比较四种裂纹体系后发现：(100)[010]、(100)[011]和(110)[001]仍以解理为主，而(110)[1-10]裂纹在纯Fe中本为位错发射（dislocation emission），在充氢条件下转变为解理（cleavage）。

Conclusion: 氢对{110}解理面族的Griffith解理阈值降低程度大于对{100}的降低；对于控制性裂纹，Rice型能量描述符表明表面能控制的解理抗力下降速度快于不稳定层错能控制的发射抗力下降速度，这与位错发射屏蔽效应被削弱一致。这些结果为氢致Fe中穿晶裂纹面转变提供了热力学一致的原子尺度基础。

Abstract: Hydrogen-related fracture in body-centered cubic Fe and ferritic steels often appears as transgranular quasi-cleavage rather than purely intergranular failure, especially at low to moderate hydrogen contents. Fractography has suggested that hydrogen may change the dominant cleavage faceting from {100} toward {110}, but atomic-scale evidence for this possible crack-plane transition remains unclear. Here we construct an efficient neural-network potential for α-Fe/H and combine large-scale, three-dimensional molecular dynamics with grand-canonical Monte Carlo (GCMC), allowing the near-tip crack-surface region and crack tip within a defined GCMC domain to exchange hydrogen with a reservoir at fixed chemical potential. A comparison of four crack systems identifies the controlling response: (100)[010], (100)[011], and (110)[001] remain cleavage-dominated, whereas the (110)[1-10] crack changes from dislocation emission in pure Fe to cleavage under hydrogen charging. The energetic origin is twofold. Hydrogen lowers the Griffith cleavage threshold of the {110} cleavage-plane family more strongly than that of {100}, and, for the controlling crack, a Rice-type energetic descriptor indicates that the surface-energy-controlled cleavage resistance decreases faster than the unstable-stacking-fault-controlled emission resistance, consistent with a weakened dislocation-emission shield. These results provide a thermodynamically consistent atomistic basis for a hydrogen-induced transgranular crack-plane transition in Fe.

</details>


### [194] [Uncovering multi-channel magnetic hopfion annihilation via a single-node, billion-spin-scale atomistic framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26016)
*Qichen Xu,Anna Delin*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出 SpinX，一个基于 GPU 的原子自旋模拟框架，通过晶格子格分解将平移不变的自旋相互作用重构为多通道张量卷积，支持多种计算后端和混合精度模式，在单加速器上峰值吞吐量超过 100 亿自旋点位操作/秒，并利用该框架在百万自旋晶格上发现了磁 hopfion 的两种竞争湮灭通道。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有原子自旋模拟（atomistic spin simulation）在大晶格上进行三维磁织构计算时，因需重复评估自旋哈密顿量（spin Hamiltonian）而面临高昂的计算成本，亟需高效的 GPU 原生模拟框架以支撑长随机轨迹、热力学采样、静态优化和多像过渡路径等复杂工作流。

Method: SpinX 以统一哈密顿量接口和多种用户可选计算后端为核心，引入晶格子格分解（crystallographic sublattice decomposition）将平移不变自旋相互作用重构为多通道张量卷积（multi-channel tensor convolutions），支持稠密、稀疏及基于 FFT 的卷积后端；不规则系统采用配对列表（pair-list）评估，长程偶极场通过倒易空间 FFT 处理。框架基于 JAX 实现，支持确定性/随机 Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert 动力学、蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）采样、静态优化、动态谱学及弦/测地线 nudged elastic band 过渡路径计算，并配备 fp32 场评估与 fp64 自旋态传播的混合精度模式。

Result: 通过解析单自旋动力学、bcc Fe 的有限大小热力学及横向动态结构因子完成验证。性能基准测试表明，单加速器峰值吞吐量超过 100 亿自旋点位操作/秒，单节点聚合工作负载超过 10 亿原子自旋。在百万自旋晶格上对交换稳定磁 hopfion 的应用揭示了两种竞争湮灭通道：轴向塌缩路径（axial-collapse pathway）和横向断裂路径（lateral-rupture pathway），二者具有不同的过渡形态和激活势垒。

Conclusion: SpinX 为大规模原子自旋模拟提供了高效的 GPU 原生解决方案，其子格分解与多后端设计在保证精度的同时显著提升了计算吞吐量；在磁 hopfion 研究中发现的横向断裂路径为三维磁织构的湮灭机制提供了新见解。

Abstract: Modern atomistic spin simulations combine long stochastic trajectories, thermodynamic sampling, static optimization and multi-image transition-path workflows, all of which rely on repeated evaluation of spin Hamiltonians and become computationally prohibitive on the large lattices required for three-dimensional magnetic textures. We introduce SpinX, a GPU-native atomistic spin simulation framework built around a unified Hamiltonian interface and multiple user-selectable computational backends. Its core is a crystallographic sublattice decomposition that reformulates translationally invariant spin interactions as multi-channel tensor convolutions, enabling dense, sparse and FFT-based convolution backends, while irregular systems are handled by pair-list evaluation and long-range dipolar fields by reciprocal-space FFT. Implemented in JAX, SpinX supports deterministic and stochastic Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert dynamics, Monte Carlo sampling, static optimization, dynamical spectroscopy and string and geodesic nudged elastic band transition-path calculations on heterogeneous accelerator platforms. A validated mixed-precision mode combines fp32 field evaluation with fp64 spin-state propagation. We validate SpinX against analytical single-spin dynamics, finite-size thermodynamics of bcc Fe and transverse dynamic structure factors. Performance benchmarks show peak throughput exceeding 10 billion spin-site operations per second on a single accelerator and aggregate single-node workloads of over 1 billion atomic spins. Applying this framework to an exchange-stabilized magnetic hopfion, we uncover two competing annihilation channels on a million-spin atomistic lattice: a previously reported axial-collapse pathway and a distinct lateral-rupture pathway with a different transition morphology and activation barrier.(Due to arXiv's limit, the abstract shown here is a shortened version)

</details>

### [195] [Semiclassical Propagation and the Dynamics of Configuration Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24373)
*V. S. Morales-Salgado*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了非相对论量子传播子（quantum propagator）$K(x,t)$作为薛定谔方程的解，通过引入附加指数因子$R$对标准WKB近似（WKB ansatz）进行推广，探讨$R$作为量子性（quantumness）度量的角色，并在多个系统上验证了该方法的有效性，同时提出了向场论推广的方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在标准的WKB近似中，传播子仅由作用量$S$的指数形式给出，但该方法未能充分刻画量子效应的贡献。本文旨在通过引入额外的指数因子$R$来弥补这一不足，并将$R$解释为一种量子性（quantumness）的度量，从而更系统地理解量子力学中经典与量子行为之间的过渡。

Method: 论文假设非相对论量子传播子$K(x,t)$具有形式${\rm exp}\left(\frac{\mathrm{i}}{\hbar}S+R\right)$，其中$S$满足哈密顿-雅可比方程（Hamilton-Jacobi equation），$R$是附加的指数因子。通过这一推广的WKB ansatz，作者研究了$R$的物理含义，在多个具体系统中进行了实例验证，并将其推广到场论情形，在简单系统中进行了检验。

Result: 通过多个具体系统的实例分析，验证了所提出的推广WKB方法的可行性；将该方法推广到场论后，也在一些简单系统中得到了检验；此外，还分析了将其应用于受哈密顿约束（Hamiltonian constraint）控制的动力学系统的可能性。

Conclusion: 引入附加指数因子$R$的推广WKB方法能够有效刻画量子性（quantumness），该方法不仅适用于非相对论量子力学的传播子，还可推广到场论框架，并有望应用于受哈密顿约束的动力学系统。

Abstract: This work explores the non-relativistic quantum propagator $K(x,t)$ as a solution of the Schrödinger equation. We suppose that the propagator takes the form ${\rm exp}\left(\frac{\mathrm{i}}{\hbar}S+R\right)$, generalizing the usual WKB ansatz by allowing an additive exponent $R$ whose role as a measure of quantumness is investigated. Since $S$ is subject to the assumption that it is a solution of the Hamilton-Jacobi equation, here we are further interested in the role of $R$ and its interpretation as a measure of quantumness. Several systems are studied as concrete examples to illustrate this approach. Furthermore, a proposal to generalize it for fields is put forward. This is tested for some simple systems. Finally, the possibilities to use this approach for the case of systems whose dynamics are controlled by the Hamiltonian constraint are analyzed.

</details>


### [196] [Algebraic Tomography of Non-Hermitian Floquet Systems from Observable Traces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24555)
*Syo Kamata*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种Floquet代数层析（Floquet algebraic tomography）框架，用于从可观测迹序列中重建有限维非厄米单值矩阵（non-Hermitian monodromy matrix），通过Cayley–Hamilton与Hankel方法提取谱数据，并分析了不同可观测量代数下的可识别性极限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Floquet系统中从可观测迹序列重建非厄米单值矩阵是一个逆问题，但现有方法常将其视为一般指数拟合，忽略了特征多项式（characteristic polynomial）约束导致的代数重建结构，因而需要建立更系统的代数层析框架。

Method: 利用可观测量的迹序列ζ_n^{(O)}=Tr(OM^n)受M的特征多项式约束这一事实，将逆问题转化为有限维代数重建问题。通过可观测量预解式（observable resolvent）、谱行列式（spectral determinant）和Dirichlet谱数据组织重建，分离公共谱骨架（spectral skeleton）与可观测量依赖的修饰。采用Cayley–Hamilton方法和Hankel方法恢复相似性不变的谱数据，并通过多可观测量和Liouville空间扩展将其与实现理论（realization theory）和层析重建联系起来。

Result: 明确了有限可观测量代数下的可识别性（identifiability）极限：数据决定一个可见代表元（visible representative），微运动（micromotion）可扩大采样到的可见算符空间，精确对称性则导致剩余不可见扇区（invisible sectors）。通过驱动transmon qutrit和有限非厄米Floquet SSH链两个例子，展示了漏泄诱导的可见性扩展、可观测量依赖的相位响应、例外点（EP）可达的分支几何以及无序/探针依赖的可观测量维度读数。

Conclusion: 所提出的Floquet代数层析框架为从迹序列重建非厄米单值矩阵提供了系统的代数途径，揭示了谱数据与可观测量之间的结构关系，并为理解受限测量下的可识别性提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We formulate a framework of Floquet algebraic tomography for finite-dimensional non-Hermitian monodromy matrices from observable trace sequences $ζ_n^{(O)}={\rm Tr}(OM^n)$. Since these sequences are constrained by the characteristic polynomial of $M$, the inverse problem is a finite-dimensional algebraic reconstruction problem rather than a generic exponential fit. We organize the reconstruction through the observable resolvent, spectral determinant, and Dirichlet spectral data, separating the common spectral skeleton from observable-dependent dressing. Cayley--Hamilton and Hankel methods recover the similarity-invariant spectral data, while multi-observable and Liouville-space extensions connect the construction to realization theory and tomography reconstruction. We further clarify the limits of identifiability from restricted observable algebras: the data determine a visible representative, micromotion can enlarge the sampled visible operator space, and exact symmetries impose residual invisible sectors. Two examples, a driven transmon qutrit and a finite non-Hermitian Floquet SSH chain, demonstrate leakage-induced visibility expansion, observable-dependent phase response, EP-accessible branch geometry, and disorder/probe-dependent observable-dimension readouts.

</details>


### [197] [Photon position eigenstates in configuration space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25857)
*Artemio González-López,Luis Martínez Alonso*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文推导了Hawton光子位置算符（photon position operator）在构型空间（configuration space）中的本征函数表达式，涵盖Riemann-Silberstein和Landau-Peierls两类波函数。这些本征函数可用完全椭圆积分（complete elliptic integrals）$K(κ)$和$E(κ)$的线性组合给出闭式表达，并展现出在位置本征值$\mathbf q$处及其所在平面上的发散行为，以及随距离呈幂律衰减的特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管Hawton光子位置算符的本征函数在动量空间（momentum space）中形式简单，但其在构型空间中的显式表示却相当复杂，因此需要给出闭合形式的解析表达式以深化理解。

Method: 针对Riemann-Silberstein和Landau-Peierls两类波函数，推导了Hawton光子位置算符在构型空间中的本征函数；通过将表达式用完全椭圆积分$K(κ)$和$E(κ)$的线性组合表示，得到了闭式解析解，其中模量（modulus）$κ$依赖于极角（polar angle）的三角函数。

Result: 给出了构型空间中本征函数的闭式表达式；发现本征函数不仅在位置本征值$\mathbf q$处发散，还在包含$\mathbf q$的一个平面上发散；本征函数随距$\mathbf q$距离的增加呈幂律衰减。

Conclusion: Hawton光子位置算符在构型空间中的本征函数具有由完全椭圆积分表达的解析形式，其发散结构与衰减行为揭示了该算符在位置表示中的非平凡特性。

Abstract: The expressions of the eigenfunctions of the Hawton photon position operator in the configuration space are derived for several classes of wave function, including the Riemann-Silberstein and Landau-Peierls cases. Although these eigenfunctions have a simple form in momentum space, the explicit characterization of their representations in the configuration space is rather more involved. We provide closed expressions of these eigenfunctions in terms of linear combinations of the complete elliptic integrals $K(κ)$ and $E(κ)$ with modulus $κ$ depending on trigonometric functions of the polar angle. We show that they diverge not only at the value $\mathbf q$ of the position eigenvalue, but also on a plane containing $\mathbf q$ and that they decay as inverse powers of the distance from $\mathbf q$.

</details>


### [198] [Dynamical self-dual criticality in Fibonacci-monitored quantum Ising chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24086)
*Finn Eckstein,Harald Schmid,Quinten Preiss,Simon Trebst,Felix von Oppen,Guo-Yi Zhu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了一维横场伊辛链（transverse-field Ising chain）在准周期斐波那契测量序列下的受控动力学，发现非可逆的Kramers-Wannier对偶性（Kramers-Wannier duality）可推广至非平衡情形，用于组织纠缠相的动力学相图、预测相变位置并保护普适临界行为。分析识别出两条与黄金分割比（golden ratio）相关的临界线，分别对应Born规则弱测量和随机Clifford投影测量，后者等同于纯虚时间演化（imaginary-time evolution）的相变。文章还确定了斐波那契时刻长时临界稳态的普适类（universality class），并揭示了瞬态动力学中测量变形的实时量子临界性（measurement-altered quantum criticality）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管Kramers-Wannier对偶性在平衡态量子相变中已被充分理解，但它在非平衡受控动力学（monitored dynamics）中的作用——尤其是在超越时间周期Floquet协议（time-periodic Floquet protocol）的准周期情形下——仍未被深入探索。本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 研究了一维伊辛/马约拉纳链（Ising/Majorana chain）在准周期斐波那契序列（quasiperiodic Fibonacci sequence）测量下的受控动力学，同时结合解析分析与数值模拟，分别考察了Born规则弱测量（Born-rule weak measurement）和随机Clifford投影测量（random Clifford projective measurement）两种情形。

Result: 发现了两条与黄金分割比相关的不同临界线，分别对应两种测量方案；随机Clifford投影测量的临界线与纯虚时间演化的相变重合。确定了斐波那契时刻长时临界稳态的普适类，并观察到瞬态动力学中测量变形的实时量子临界性（dynamical measurement-altered quantum criticality）。

Conclusion: 非可逆的Kramers-Wannier对偶性可被推广至准周期受控动力学，用于统一描述纠缠相的动力学相图，同时预测相变位置并保护普适临界行为。该结果表明，测量可实时变形量子临界性，为理解非平衡量子相变提供了新的视角。

Abstract: For the quantum phase transition in the transverse-field Ising chain, Kramers-Wannier duality not only protects its critical properties but also pinpoints the location of the phase transition. Its role in out-of-equilibrium, monitored dynamics, however, remains largely unexplored beyond time-periodic Floquet protocols where self-duality turns into a statistical average symmetry. Here we explore the emergence of dynamical self-duality in the absence of time-translation symmetry by investigating the monitored dynamics of one-dimensional Ising/Majorana chains where measurements are arranged in a quasiperiodic Fibonacci sequence. We find that the dynamical extension of this non-invertible symmetry to an out-of-equilibrium setting allows one to organize the dynamical phase diagram of entangled phases, both predicting the transition locations and protecting universal critical behavior. Analytically and numerically, we identify two distinct critical lines, both related to the golden ratio, for Born-rule weak measurements and for random Clifford projective measurements. The latter coincides with the transition of a pure imaginary-time evolution, which can be viewed as a post-selected trajectory. The universality classes of the long-time critical steady states at Fibonacci times are determined, while the transient dynamics between Fibonacci times is deformed by measurements, realizing dynamical measurement-altered quantum criticality in real time.

</details>


### [199] [Fermi-Dirac machines as quantizations of neurons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24386)
*Alexander He,Nana Liu,Mark M. Wilde*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文重新诠释Fermi-Dirac机器为经典神经元的正则量子化（canonical quantization），通过将经典变量替换为算符实现量子化，并开发了高效的量子-经典混合算法来训练这些量子神经元。实验表明量子神经元能学习经典神经元无法学习的函数，并通过BQP完全性（BQP-completeness）证明其不存在高效经典模拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Fermi-Dirac机器最初被提出用于在量子计算机上求解半定优化问题，但本文试图提供一个更根本的视角——将其视为经典神经元的量子化推广，从而为量子深度学习奠定理论基础。

Method: 采用标准正则量子化方法：将经典变量替换为算符，其中算符的本征值编码变量的可能取值。当哈密顿量由对易算符构成时，该方法退化回经典神经元；更一般情形下，激活函数作用于参数化量子哈密顿量得到激活观测量（activation observable），其期望值作为量子神经元的输出。算法依赖随机采样、哈密顿量模拟（Hamiltonian simulation）和阿达玛测试（Hadamard test）等基本原语。

Result: 数值实验表明，基于量子哈密顿量的神经元可以学习经典神经元无法学习的函数。此外，论文将Fermi-Dirac神经元对应的计算决策问题证明为BQP完全的（BQP-complete），从计算复杂性理论上排除了高效经典模拟的可能性。方法还推广到连续量子变量，并提出了两种将量子神经元组合成网络的方式。

Conclusion: 本文建立的量子神经元框架不仅统一了Fermi-Dirac机器与经典神经网络，还为量子深度学习提供了新的理论基础和混合计算实现路径，同时通过复杂性理论保证了其在表达能力上的超越性。

Abstract: Fermi-Dirac machines were proposed recently as an approach to solving semidefinite optimization problems on quantum computers. Here, we reinterpret them as canonical quantizations of classical neurons. By viewing a classical neuron as an activation function applied to a parameterized classical Hamiltonian, we quantize this model by replacing classical variables with operators whose eigenvalues encode their possible values. This follows the standard approach to canonical quantization in quantum mechanics. Crucially, when the Hamiltonian consists of commuting operators, our construction reduces exactly to a classical neuron. More generally, our approach yields an activation observable, defined as an activation function applied to a parameterized quantum Hamiltonian. The output of this quantized neuron is a random variable with expectation value equal to that of the activation observable with respect to an input state. We develop efficient hybrid quantum-classical algorithms for evaluating outputs and gradients of our quantized neurons, enabling evaluation and training. These algorithms rely on basic primitives that include random sampling, Hamiltonian simulation, and the Hadamard test. We also quantize a whole host of other activation functions, including the smooth rectified linear unit (ReLU), sigmoid linear unit, Gaussian-smoothed ReLU, and Gaussian error linear unit (GeLU), which are known to be useful for deep learning applications. Numerical experiments indicate that neurons based on quantum Hamiltonians can learn functions that classical neurons cannot. We further define a computational decision problem based on Fermi-Dirac neurons and prove that it is BQP-complete, providing complexity-theoretic evidence against efficient classical simulation. Finally, we generalize our approach to continuous quantum variables and sketch two different ways of composing these neurons into networks.

</details>


### [200] [Dissipative acousto-mechanical parametric interface between high-overtone acoustics and flexural phonons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24581)
*Xun Ji,Huanying Sun,Longhao Wu,Qichun Liu,Yulong Liu,Mika A. Sillanpää,Tiefu Li*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文在悬浮氮化硅薄膜中实现了GHz高频体声波谐振器（HBAR）与低频弯曲模之间的辐射压力型参量相互作用，利用耗散声-力耦合（dissipative acousto-mechanical coupling）在室温下进入分辨边带区（resolved-sideband regime），观察到声-力诱导透明（acousto-mechanically induced transparency）、可调Kerr非线性以及HBAR频率梳，且耗散耦合强度是色散耦合的20倍，创下同类混合系统最高比值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高频体声波谐振器（HBAR）在先进声子学（phononics）中具有重要前景，但实现非线性（nonlinearity）仍然是一个挑战。本研究旨在通过耗散型声-力耦合机制克服这一困难。

Method: 在悬浮氮化硅（silicon nitride）薄膜中，利用机械位移调制外部耗散率，实现GHz HBAR与低频弯曲模（flexural modes）之间的辐射压力型（radiation-pressure-type）参量相互作用，从而构建耗散声-力耦合（dissipative acousto-mechanical coupling）系统。

Result: 系统在室温下进入分辨边带区（resolved-sideband regime），观察到声-力诱导透明（acousto-mechanically induced transparency）；实现了可调Kerr非线性（tunable Kerr nonlinearity），并通过双音驱动（two-tone driving）生成了相干的HBAR频率梳（frequency combs）。耗散耦合强度是色散耦合（dispersive coupling）的20倍，为已报道混合耗散-色散耦合系统中的最高比值，并在红边带驱动（red-sideband driving）下观测到反射谱中的放大现象。

Conclusion: 将密集HBAR模式与公共机械谐振器接口的能力，为多模声子信息处理（multimode phononic information processing）提供了可扩展的片上平台，并在亚开尔文（sub-Kelvin）温度下有望实现量子声子学（quantum phononics）。

Abstract: High-overtone bulk acoustic wave resonators (HBARs) promise advanced phononics, yet achieving nonlinearity remains challenging. We demonstrate a radiation-pressure-type parametric interaction between GHz HBARs and low-frequency flexural modes in a suspended silicon nitride membrane, where mechanical displacement modulates the external dissipation rate to enable dissipative acousto-mechanical coupling. Benefiting from the high quality factor, the system enters the resolved-sideband regime at room temperature, yielding acousto-mechanically induced transparency. We observe tunable Kerr nonlinearity and generate coherent HBAR frequency combs via two-tone driving. Notably, our dissipative coupling strength is 20 times larger than the dispersive coupling, the highest ratio among reported hybrid dissipative-dispersive coupling systems, resulting in the experimental observation of amplification in the reflection spectra under red-sideband driving. The ability to interface dense HBAR modes with a common mechanical resonator provides a scalable on-chip platform for multimode phononic information processing, with quantum phononics potentially achievable at sub-Kelvin temperatures.

### [201] [Dissipative preparation of injective tensor network states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25089)
*Drishti Baruah,Georgios Styliaris,J. Ignacio Cirac,Rahul Trivedi*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对张量网络态（tensor network states）的耗散制备（dissipative state preparation）问题，构建了连续时间和离散时间的几何局域耗散过程，其唯一稳态为给定的内射张量网络态（injective tensor network state）。该方法在$N$个格点上制备所有内射矩阵乘积态（matrix product state）的时间复杂度为$O(\log (N/\varepsilon))$，相较于已知耗散方案实现了指数级提升；对于高维张量网络态，在“高度内射”（highly injective）条件下同样达到$O(\log (N/\varepsilon))$的快速混合时间，并在数值模拟中验证了该协议在超出高度内射假设情形下的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 制备张量网络态是众多量子模拟任务的基本前提。虽然已有大量幺正协议（unitary protocols）被研究，但耗散态制备（dissipative state preparation）因其对噪声和初始化误差具有鲁棒性，成为一类强有力的替代方案。此前已知的耗散制备方案效率有限，亟需更快速的方法。

Method: 作者构造了连续时间与离散时间两种几何局域耗散过程（geometrically local dissipative processes），其唯一稳态（unique steady state）被设定为给定的内射张量网络态。针对内射矩阵乘积态与高度内射的高维张量网络态，分别利用耗散过程的快速混合性质（rapid-mixing property）推导出混合时间上界。

Result: 对于$N$个格点上的所有内射矩阵乘积态，该方案在$O(\log (N/\varepsilon))$时间内达到误差$\varepsilon$，相比已知耗散方案呈指数级加速。对于二维及以上维度的张量网络态，当张量满足高度内射条件时，耗散过程同样在$O(\log (N/\varepsilon))$时间内完成制备：相较于定义在格点上的幺正方法实现多项式加速，对于一般有界度图（bounded-degree graphs）上的态则实现指数级加速。数值模拟表明该协议在超出高度内射假设时仍可快速制备目标态。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一类高效的耗散态制备协议，在内射张量网络态上实现了对数时间的指数级或多项式级加速，显著优于现有耗散方案和幺正方案。数值结果进一步暗示该方法可能适用于更广泛的张量网络态类别。

Abstract: The preparation of tensor network states is a fundamental prerequisite for a wide range of quantum simulation tasks. While many unitary protocols for preparing these states have been investigated, dissipative state preparation provides a powerful alternative since it can be robust to noise and initialization errors. In this paper, we construct both continuous-time and discrete-time geometrically local dissipative processes whose unique steady state is a given injective tensor network state. Our method prepares all injective matrix product states on $N$ sites to an error $\varepsilon$ in $O(\log (N/\varepsilon))$ time, yielding an exponential improvement over previously known dissipative preparation schemes. For two and higher-dimensional tensor network states, we prove that when the tensors of the state are \emph{highly injective}, the constructed dissipative processes are rapid-mixing i.e., they prepare a state $\varepsilon$-close to the $N$-site target state in $O(
  \log (N/\varepsilon))$ time. For these states, our approach provides a polynomial speedup over known unitary methods for states defined on lattices and an exponential speedup for states on general bounded-degree graphs. We corroborate our theoretical results with numerical studies that indicate that the dissipative protocol can rapidly prepares states outside the high-injectivity assumption.

### [202] [Extracting Universal Entanglement Scaling from Mixed Fermionic Gaussian States via Entanglement Projected Entropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25102)
*Jia-Wen Tao,Hui-Ke Jin*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出“纠缠投影熵（entanglement projected entropy）”，一种从混合费米子高斯态（mixed fermionic Gaussian states）中提取边界敏感量子关联的诊断方法。该方法通过将子系统熵分解为高斯纠缠通道（Gaussian entanglement channels），并将净化伙伴投影到物理补集上，得到以物理协方差矩阵表示的闭式表达式。在一维自由费米子链中，该方法去除了体律混合态背景，恢复了零温共形标度（conformal scaling）与c/3系数；在二维半填充π-流模型中，揭示了由有效狄拉克红外长度（effective Dirac infrared length）控制的普适有限温标度坍缩。这些结果确立了纠缠投影熵作为混合态熵中隐藏的边界敏感量子关联的高斯空间滤波器（Gaussian spatial filter）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 识别混合态中的空间量子关联非常困难，因为热混合态贡献掩盖了子系统熵中编码的纠缠信息。现有方法难以在有限温度下有效提取边界敏感的量子关联。

Method: 引入纠缠投影熵（entanglement projected entropy），将子系统熵分解为高斯纠缠通道（Gaussian entanglement channels），并将其净化伙伴投影到物理补集上，最终得到以物理协方差矩阵（covariance matrix）表示的闭式表达式。

Result: 在一维自由费米子链中，该方法去除了体律混合态背景，恢复了零温共形场论（conformal field theory）的c/3标度行为；在二维半填充π-流模型中，揭示了由有效狄拉克红外长度（effective Dirac infrared length）控制的普适有限温标度坍缩。

Conclusion: 纠缠投影熵可作为一种高斯空间滤波器（Gaussian spatial filter），用于从混合态熵中提取边界敏感的量子关联。

Abstract: Identifying spatial quantum correlations in mixed states is challenging because thermal mixed-state contributions obscure the entanglement encoded in subsystem entropy. Here, we introduce the entanglement projected entropy, a diagnostic for extracting boundary-sensitive quantum correlations from mixed fermionic Gaussian states. By resolving subsystem entropy into Gaussian entanglement channels and projecting their purification partners onto the physical complement, we obtain a closed-form expression in terms of the physical covariance matrix. In a one-dimensional free-fermion chain, it removes the volume-law mixed-state background and recovers the zero-temperature conformal scaling with the $c/3$ coefficient. In a two-dimensional half-filled $π$-flux model, it reveals a universal finite-temperature scaling collapse governed by an effective Dirac infrared length. These results establish entanglement projected entropy as a Gaussian spatial filter for boundary-sensitive quantum correlations hidden in mixed-state entropy.

### [203] [Sideband fingerprints of antibunched light in cascaded quantum wave mixing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25828)
*R. D. Ivanovskikh,W. V. Pogosov,A. A. Elistratov,A. Yu. Dmitriev,T. R. Sabirov,A. V. Vasenin,S. A. Gunin,O. V. Astafiev*

TL;DR: 本文研究在单个超导量子比特（superconducting qubit）上发生的量子波混频（quantum wave mixing）现象，发现其会产生与弹性多光子散射路径（elastic multiphoton scattering pathways）相关的相干边峰层级结构。在级联源-探针（cascaded source-probe）几何结构中，这些路径对源量子比特辐射的光子统计特性敏感。作者从弱驱动（weak-driving）条件下的级联主方程（cascaded master equation）出发，建立了该效应的解析理论，并通过数值解验证了标度律（scaling laws）。该边带层级结构为反聚束行波微波光（antibunched itinerant microwave light）提供了频域指纹。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 从弱驱动条件下的级联主方程出发，建立该效应的解析理论；在相干滤波极限（coherent-filtering limit）和相反极限下分别推导标度律，并通过数值解进行验证。

Result: 在γ_s≫γ_pr的相干滤波极限下恢复到标准相干-相干波混频层级；在γ_pr≫γ_s的相反极限下，与来自反聚束源场的多光子吸收相关的边峰被参数化抑制。数值解确认了解析标度律。

Conclusion: 该边带层级结构可作为反聚束行波微波光的频域指纹，揭示了光子统计对量子波混频谱的调制作用。

Abstract: Quantum wave mixing on a single superconducting qubit produces a hierarchy of coherent side peaks associated with elastic multiphoton scattering pathways. In a cascaded source--probe geometry these pathways become sensitive to the photon statistics of the radiation emitted by the source qubit. We develop an analytical theory of this effect starting from the cascaded master equation in the weak-driving regime. In the coherent-filtering limit $γ_{\rm s}\ggγ_{\rm pr}$, the standard coherent--coherent wave-mixing hierarchy is recovered. In the opposite limit $γ_{\rm pr}\ggγ_{\rm s}$, side peaks associated with multiphoton absorption from the antibunched source field are parametrically suppressed. Numerical solutions confirm the analytical scaling laws. The resulting sideband hierarchy provides a frequency-domain fingerprint of antibunched itinerant microwave light.

### [204] [Native topological readout on qubit hardware: a Fibonacci-chain benchmark of measurement-compilation trade-offs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25913)
*Babatunde Moses Ayeni*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文以斐波那契任意子链（Fibonacci anyons chain）为模型，系统比较了融合读取（fusion readout）方法与分组泡利（grouped-Pauli）基方法在含噪中等规模量子（NISQ）硬件上实现拓扑任意子哈密顿量时的测量代价与编译代价权衡。研究发现，两种方法在不同类型的量子电路（Floquet时间演化电路与变分量子本征求解器电路）上表现各异，并给出了参考预算交叉点（shot-budget crossover points）和标度律（scaling laws）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期在NISQ超导处理器上演示了图顶点的非阿贝尔编织（non-Abelian braiding），并在多种量子硬件平台上实验实现了拓扑序（topological order），这引出了一个关键问题：在NISQ硬件上实现拓扑任意子哈密顿量时，原生（拓扑）融合读取何时才能真正带来优势？本文旨在量化评估这一权衡。

Method: 以斐波那契任意子链为具体模型，将融合读取方法与简单的分组泡利基线方法进行对比，采用协方差感知均方误差（covariance-aware mean-squared-error, MSE）作为评分指标。基准测试覆盖两类量子电路：Floquet时间演化（Floquet time-evolved）电路与变分量子本征求解器（variational quantum eigensolver, VQE）电路，底层哈密顿量同时包含编织（braiding）与融合（fusion）相互作用。

Result: 分析发现不存在适用于所有问题的统一最优方法：融合读取方法在Floquet型电路上同时在MSE和协方差感知采样方差（covariance-aware sampling variance）两方面表现更优；而分组泡利方法在VQE上MSE更优但采样方差更差。论文还推导了标度律并计算了预算交叉点，即一种方法在操作上优于另一种方法的测量预算阈值。

Conclusion: 该工作的相关性不仅限于斐波那契链，还可推广至编译到超导及其他量子比特原生平台上的二维拓扑模型（two-dimensional topological models），为指导何时应在目标物理的原生算符基（native operator basis）下进行测量、何时应退回到泡利基重构（Pauli-basis reconstruction）提供了参考依据。

Abstract: Recent demonstrations of non-Abelian braiding of graph vertices on noisy intermediate-scale quantum (NISQ) superconducting processor, and the experimental realization of topological order in general on various quantum hardware platforms necessitate an important question: when does a native (topological) fusion readout genuinely help for topological anyonic Hamiltonians implemented on NISQ hardware? We use the Fibonacci anyons chain as a concrete model for understanding the trade-off between measurement cost and compilation cost in that setting. The comparison is made against a simple grouped-Pauli baseline, and is scored by a covariance-aware mean-squared-error (MSE) of the full energy estimator. We based our benchmark on two different important classes of quantum circuits, namely Floquet time-evolved and variational quantum eigensolver quantum circuits, with the underlying Hamiltonian consisting of both braiding and fusion interaction. Our analysis found that there is not a uniform best method across both problems: the fusion readout method performed better on Floquet-type circuits on both the MSE and covariance-aware sampling variance, while the grouped Pauli method performed better on VQE on the MSE but worse on sampling variance. We derive scaling laws, and compute shot-budget crossover points, where one method is operationally favored above the other. The relevance of this work extends beyond Fibonacci chains to two-dimensional topological models compiled on superconducting and other qubit-native platforms, and can be used as a guide in answering the question of when one should measure in the native operator basis of the target physics, or when it is better to fall back on Pauli-basis reconstruction.

</details>


### [205] [Rounding Almost Commuting Hamiltonians](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26096)
*Islam Faisal,Anand Natarajan,Alexander Poremba*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种保持局域性的算法舍入技术，可将任意几乎对易的2-局域量子比特哈密顿量高效近似为一个对易哈密顿量，并证明了在近似误差足够大时，基态能量的δ-近似属于NP类。该框架还应用于吉布斯采样和快速哈密顿模拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对易哈密顿量（commuting Hamiltonians）处于经典约束满足与量子多体物理的边界，具有丰富的量子结构且比非对易模型更易处理。然而实际物理哈密顿量很少严格对易，因此自然引出了几乎对易哈密顿量（almost commuting Hamiltonians）的研究。尽管其重要性显著，但近似对易的物理含义仍知之甚少。

Method: 本文提出了一种保持局域性（locality-preserving）的算法舍入（algorithmic rounding）技术，可将任意满足对易子范数$\|[h_i,h_j]\| \leq ε$的2-局域（2-local）量子比特哈密顿量$H=\sum_{i=1}^m h_i$映射到邻近的对易哈密顿量$\hat{H}$，且整体距离满足$\|H-\hat{H}\| = O(m\,ε^{1/6})$。

Result: 对于ε-几乎对易的2-局域量子比特哈密顿量，当δ ≫ mε^{1/6}时，基态能量的δ-近似（δ-approximation）属于NP类，将对易情形下的经典包含关系推广到了几乎对易的情形。此外，该舍入框架还可应用于吉布斯采样（Gibbs sampling）和快速哈密顿模拟（fast Hamiltonian simulation）。

Conclusion: 几乎所有对易的2-局域量子比特哈密顿量都可以被高效地近似为一个严格对易的哈密顿量，这一结果同时带来了计算复杂度上的突破——将对易哈密顿量基态能量近似问题属于NP这一性质扩展到误差容忍的近似对易情形，并展示了在统计力学和量子模拟领域的实际应用价值。

Abstract: Commuting Hamiltonians lie at the boundary between classical constraint satisfaction and quantum many-body physics, exhibiting rich quantum structure while remaining more tractable than general noncommuting models. In contrast, physical Hamiltonians are rarely exactly commuting, which naturally motivates the study of almost commuting Hamiltonians. Despite their relevance, the implications of approximate commutation are only poorly understood.
  In this work, we show how to efficiently approximate any almost commuting $2$-local qubit Hamiltonian by a commuting one: we give a locality-preserving algorithmic rounding technique that maps any $2$-local Hamiltonian $H=\sum_{i=1}^m h_i$ with $\|[h_i,h_j]\| \leq ε$ to a nearby Hamiltonian $\hat{H}$ whose terms pair-wise commute, and which is within overall distance $\|H-\hat{H}\| = O(m\,ε^{1/6})$. As a consequence, we show that $δ$-approximations to the ground energy for $ε$-almost commuting $2$-local qubit Hamiltonians lie in $\mathsf{NP}$ when $δ\gg mε^{1/6}$, extending the classical containment well beyond the commuting setting. Finally, we present two applications of our rounding framework: Gibbs sampling and fast Hamiltonian simulation for almost commuting systems.

</details>

### [206] [The Pseudospectral Method for the Dirac Equation with Confining Potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25390)
*Dengshan Liu,Huihui Xie,Pengxiang Du,Jian Li,Tomoya Naito*

Main category: physics.atom-ph

TL;DR: 本文发现广义赝谱（GPS）方法在处理受限势的狄拉克方程时，因一阶微分公式导致收敛性变差和波函数振荡；通过引入动力学平衡条件提出单动力学平衡广义赝谱（MKB-GPS）方法，首次应用于受限势并在小受限半径下验证了其有效性，获得收敛的能量本征值和光滑连续的波函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 广义赝谱（generalized pseudospectral, GPS）方法在求解受限势中狄拉克方程（Dirac equation）时，随着受限半径减小，能量本征值收敛性恶化且波函数出现高度振荡，需解决这一数值问题。

Method: 在广义赝谱（GPS）方法中引入动力学平衡条件（kinetically-balanced condition），形成单动力学平衡广义赝谱（mono-kinetically-balanced generalized pseudospectral, MKB-GPS）方法，以替代原有的仅基于一阶微分公式的离散方案。

Result: MKB-GPS方法能获得收敛的能量本征值（converged energy eigenvalues），并生成光滑、连续的波函数（smooth, continuous wave functions），在小受限半径下仍保持有效。

Conclusion: MKB-GPS方法首次成功应用于受限势（confined potentials），在小受限半径场景下验证了其可靠性与有效性，为解决GPS方法在狄拉克方程数值求解中的振荡与发散问题提供了有效途径。

Abstract: We observe that solving the Dirac equation for confined potentials using the generalized pseudospectral (GPS) method leads to deteriorating convergence of energy eigenvalues and highly oscillatory in wave functions as the confinement radius decreases. It is found that this issue stems from the first-order differentiation formulation employed in GPS method. Motivated by this insight, we adopt the kinetically balanced generalized pseudospectral method, which incorporates the kinetically-balanced condition into the GPS method. Numerical results demonstrate that the mono-kinetically-balanced generalized pseu dospectral (MKB-GPS) method yields converged energy eigenvalues and generates smooth, continuous wave functions. This is the first application of the MKB-GPS method to confined potentials, and its effectiveness is validated for small confinement radii.

</details>

### [207] [Finite scalar field theory with SU(1,1) spacetime symmetry from near-BPS limits of $\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24085)
*Roberto Auzzi,Stefano Baiguera,Lihan Guo,Troels Harmark,Giuseppe Nardelli*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了一个从$\mathcal{N}=4$超杨-米尔斯理论近BPS退耦极限导出的相互作用矩阵标量量子场论，该理论具有非洛伦兹性、SU(1,1)时空对称性和半局域作用量形式。证明了经典作用量在SU(1,1)群下是离壳不变的，并分析了重整化性质，表明该理论在所有微扰阶都是有限的，从而提供了一个非超对称且非洛伦兹的量子场论中成立非重整化定理（non-renormalization theorem）的罕见例子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该理论此前被认为在经典层面上与SU(1,1)自旋矩阵理论（Spin Matrix theory）等价，本文旨在从量子层面检验这一等价性，并分析其重整化性质。

Method: 从$\mathcal{N}=4$超杨-米尔斯理论的近BPS退耦极限出发，构建具有SU(1,1)时空对称性的非洛伦兹相互作用矩阵标量量子场论；通过作用量的离壳对称性分析及微扰论的重整化性质研究，证明该理论在所有阶都是有限的。

Result: 经典作用量在SU(1,1)对称群下是离壳不变的；该理论在所有微扰阶都是有限的，即满足非重整化定理。

Conclusion: 该理论提供了一个非超对称且非洛伦兹的量子场论中成立非重整化定理的罕见例子，并对SU(1,1)自旋矩阵理论的量子等价性给出了支持。

Abstract: In this work, we consider an interacting and matrix-valued scalar quantum field theory that emerges from a near-BPS decoupling limit of $\mathcal{N}=4$ super Yang-Mills. The theory is non-Lorentzian with SU(1,1) spacetime symmetry and admits a (semi-)local action formulation. The interaction can be viewed as arising from a non-abelian gauge field without propagating degrees of freedom. The proposed field theory action has previously been considered as classically equivalent to SU(1,1) Spin Matrix theory. In this work, we examine this equivalence at the quantum level. We show that the classical action is off-shell invariant under the SU(1,1) symmetry group. We then analyze the renormalization properties, showing the theory is finite at all orders in perturbation theory. This provides a rare example of a non-supersymmetric and non-Lorentzian quantum field theory where a non-renormalization theorem holds.

### [208] [Bremsstrahlung function in $\mathcal{N}=2$ SCFTs far beyond the supergravity limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24101)
*Lorenzo De Lillo,Paolo Vallarino*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过矩阵模型（matrix model）技术，研究了四维 $\mathcal{N}=2$ 超共形规范理论（superconformal gauge theories）中的轫致辐射函数（Bremsstrahlung function），包括 E-理论和 D-理论。在大 $N$ 展开的前几阶导出了任意耦合下的精确结果。在领头阶，两种理论均与 $\mathcal{N}=4$ 超 Yang-Mills 理论平面等价（planar equivalent）；而在非平面层次，两者行为显著不同。文章分别给出了两种理论在强耦合区亚领头修正的完整结构，包括非微扰贡献（non-perturbative contributions），并提供了超越超引力近似的全息对偶（holographic dual）精确预言。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究 $\mathcal{N}=2$ 超共形规范理论中轫致辐射函数的精确行为，特别是在强耦合和大 $N$ 展开的次领头阶（subleading order）水平上，考察不同物质表示（matter representation）下理论之间的差异，并为全息对偶（holographic dual）提供超越超引力近似（supergravity approximation）的精确预测。

Method: 采用矩阵模型（matrix model）技术，在大 $N$ 展开的前几阶推导任意耦合下的精确解析结果。对 E-理论，将亚领头修正表示为自由能（free energy）对耦合常数的导数；对 D-理论，则进行详细的强耦合分析，考察截断的逆幂展开以及非微扰贡献的闭式（closed-form）表达。

Result: 在领头阶，E-理论与 D-理论均与 $\mathcal{N}=4$ Super Yang-Mills 平面等价。E-理论的亚领头修正可精确表示为自由能对耦合的导数，从而可借助已知自由能结果获得完整的强耦合展开（包括非微扰贡献）。D-理论的精确表达式结构更复杂；强耦合亚领头大 $N$ 修正的展开在有限项后截断（truncate），非微扰效应也可得到闭式表达。

Conclusion: 这些结果为上述两种 $\mathcal{N}=2$ 超共形规范理论的全息对偶在超越超引力近似下提供了精确预言，揭示了大 $N$ 展开高阶项及强耦合区完整亚领头修正的行为。

Abstract: We study the Bremsstrahlung function in two four-dimensional $\mathcal{N}=2$ superconformal gauge theories: the E-theory, with hypermultiplets in the symmetric and antisymmetric representations, and the D-theory, with antisymmetric and fundamental matter. Using matrix model techniques, we derive exact results at arbitrary coupling for the first few orders in the large-$N$ expansion. At leading order, both theories are shown to be planar equivalent to $\mathcal{N}=4$ Super Yang-Mills, while beyond the planar limit their behavior differs significantly. For the E-theory, we prove that the subleading correction is exactly given by a derivative of the free energy with respect to the coupling. This relation enables us to determine the complete strong-coupling expansion for the Bremsstrahlung function, including non-perturbative contributions, by exploiting known results for the free energy. For the D-theory, the exact expressions have a more intricate structure. We perform a detailed analysis of the strong-coupling regime of the subleading large-$N$ corrections, showing that, in this case, there are expansions in inverse powers of the coupling which truncate after finitely many terms. We further analyze the non-perturbative effects at strong coupling and derive closed-form expressions also for these contributions. These results provide precise predictions for the holographic duals of both theories beyond the supergravity approximation, probing higher orders in the large-$N$ expansion and the full subleading corrections at strong coupling.

</details>

TL;DR: 本文构造了一个简单的双矩阵模型（two-matrix model），其1/N展开系数生成任意p值下的高亏格Fuss-Catalan数（Fuss-Catalan numbers），并给出了推广的Harer-Zagier公式（Harer-Zagier formula），同时讨论了这些数自旋-p曲线模空间（moduli space of spin-p curves）的交理论（intersection theory）和欧拉示性数（Euler characteristic）之间的关联。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构造了一个简单的双矩阵模型（two-matrix model），通过其1/N展开（1/N-expansion）的系数来生成任意p下的高亏格Fuss-Catalan数；并推导出精确求和规则（exact sum rules）以及推广的显式公式。

Result: 获得了精确求和规则和一个推广到p > 2的显式公式，该公式将著名的Harer-Zagier公式推广至一般p；并将高亏格Fuss-Catalan数与自旋-p曲线模空间的交理论（intersection numbers）及欧拉示性数（Euler characteristic）建立了联系。

Conclusion: 该双矩阵模型统一了任意p值下高亏格Fuss-Catalan数的生成机制，并揭示了这些数与自旋-p曲线模空间几何量之间的内在联系。

Abstract: The genus--g Fuss--Catalan (FC) number counts the number of ways to obtain a genus-g surface by identifying the edges of a pn--gon via p-valent hyperedges. For p=2 these are the genus--g Catalan numbers which are generated as the trace correlations in the Gaussian matrix model (GUE). Here we construct a simple two-matrix model which generates the higher-genus Fuss--Catalan numbers for any p as the coefficients of its 1/N-expansion. We obtain exact sum rules and an explicit formula for the higher-genus Fuss--Catalan numbers which generalises the Harer--Zagier formula to p>2. We discuss the relation of the higher-genus FC numbers to the intersection numbers and the Euler characteristic of the moduli space of spin-p curves.

*Moslem Shafiee,Ahmad Sheykhi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究施瓦西黑洞的蒸发过程，纳入由共形反常（conformal anomaly）和真空极化（vacuum polarization）产生的量子修正，发现黑洞具有最高温度，辐射随后下降直至终止，最终态为具有零霍金温度（Hawking temperature）的极值残余（extremal remnant），且熵获得对数修正，并通过隧穿方法（tunneling method）予以佐证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索霍金辐射（Hawking radiation）在量子修正下的演化路径，明确共形反常与真空极化对施瓦西黑洞热力学行为的实质影响。

Method: 通过引入共形反常和真空极化修正分析霍金辐射与黑洞热力学；同时采用隧穿方法（tunneling method）重新检验霍金辐射，提供一致的量子效应图像。

Result: 黑洞呈现最高温度，此后辐射递减直至停止；蒸发终结时黑洞成为具有零霍金温度的极值残余；黑洞熵获得对数修正。

Conclusion: 量子修正从根本上改变了黑洞蒸发过程，阻止完全蒸发，最终以极值残余状态终结，熵的对数修正进一步支持了该量子图像。

Abstract: This study investigates the evaporation process of a Schwarzschild black hole, incorporating quantum corrections arising from conformal anomaly and vacuum polarization. We demonstrate that these corrections significantly alter the Hawking radiation and the black hole's thermodynamic behavior. Specifically, the black hole exhibits a maximum temperature, after which the radiation begins to decrease, eventually leading to the cessation of Hawking radiation. The final state of the black hole at the end of the evaporation process is found to be an extremal remnant with a vanishing Hawking temperature. Furthermore, we show that the black hole entropy is modified, acquiring a logarithmic correction. Hawking radiation is also examined through the lens of the tunneling method, providing a consistent picture of these quantum effects.

### [211] [Graviton scattering in the null surface formulation. Part III: Fourth-order Bondi shear and the tree-level amplitude](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24512)
*C. N. Kozameh,G. O. Depaola*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在广义相对论的零曲面表述（null surface formulation, NSF）中完成了量子引力子散射的三部曲，通过计算四阶Bondi剪切σ⁺₄建立了三个具有普适性的结论：NSF的微扰S矩阵在所有圈阶都是紫外（UV）有限的；给出了区分2→2引力子散射拓扑贡献的简单圈计数公式；以及提出了广义Jordan-Pauli关系，为逐阶计算σ⁺_n提供了系统化程序。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 完成NSF框架下量子引力子散射的三部曲研究，建立该表述下微扰散射矩阵的紫外有限性、拓扑分类以及高阶修正的系统化计算方法。

Method: 通过对递归零锥散射方程（recursive null-cone scattering equation）进行归纳推导得到核标度关系K^(n)~ω_ext/q^{n-2}；利用圈计数公式L=(n₁+n₂-6)/2对2→2引力子散射的拓扑贡献进行分类；通过推广标准Jordan-Pauli论证，引入超前锥（advanced cone）上的δσ⁺_j修正，建立广义Jordan-Pauli关系以实现σ⁺_n的逐阶计算。

Result: NSF的微扰S矩阵在所有圈阶无需正则化即紫外有限；树图级（L=0）贡献由M^(22)、M^(33)和M^(24)组成，共同复现Weinberg–DeWitt振幅M_tree=-κ²s³/(4tu)；完整一圈振幅需要σ⁺₄、σ⁺₅和σ⁺₆三个场；σ⁺₄的计算使用了三个推迟锥对、共形因子δΩ⁻₄以及来自(1,3)和(2,2)对的超前锥修正。

Conclusion: NSF为量子引力散射提供了一种无需正则化即可获得紫外有限S矩阵的微扰框架，广义Jordan-Pauli关系为系统计算高阶引力子散射振幅铺平了道路。

Abstract: We complete a trilogy on quantum graviton scattering in the null surface formulation (NSF) of general relativity by computing the fourth-order Bondi shear $σ^+_4$ and establishing three results of general scope.
  The perturbative $S$-matrix of the NSF is UV-finite at every loop order. This follows from the kernel scaling $K^{(n)}\simω_{\mathrm{ext}}/q^{n-2}$, which we derive by induction on the recursive null-cone scattering equation; the $L$-loop integrand then scales as $dq/q^{4L}$, which is convergent for all $L\geq 1$ without regularization.
  We show that a simple loop-counting formula, $L=(n_1+n_2-6)/2$, classifies the topologically distinct contributions to $2\to 2$ graviton scattering by the perturbative orders $n_1$, $n_2$ of the out-operators. Tree level ($L=0$) is exhausted by $\mathcal{M}^{(22)}$, $\mathcal{M}^{(33)}$, and $\mathcal{M}^{(24)}$, which together reproduce the Weinberg--DeWitt amplitude $\mathcal{M}_{\mathrm{tree}}=-κ^2s^3/(4tu)$. The complete 1-loop amplitude requires, in addition to $σ^+_4$, the fields $σ^+_5$ and $σ^+_6$.
  At order $n\geq 4$ the standard Jordan--Pauli argument, which equates the advanced and retarded null-cone contributions, must be extended. The advanced cone receives additional contributions from $δσ^+_j$ ($j<n$), the nontrivial scattering corrections determined at previous orders. We formulate this as a generalized Jordan--Pauli relation that provides a systematic, order-by-order procedure for computing $σ^+_n$ from the free incoming datum $σ^-$.
  The computation of $σ^+_4$ uses three retarded-cone pairs, the conformal factor $δΩ^-_4$, and -- for the first time -- advanced-cone corrections from pairs $(1,3)$ and $(2,2)$ built from the known $σ^+_2$ and $σ^+_3$

</details>

Method: 通过数学分析将能隙方程拆解为两部分：一部分由高阶离散拉普拉斯模式定义，另一部分为超几何函数（hypergeometric function）截断渐近展开的截断依赖项；并结合内能（internal energy）与热模式熵态（entropic states of thermal modes）的平衡条件，以及 OPE 反演公式（OPE inversion formula）进行物理等价论证。

Result: 发现特定虚化学势值下的热质量（thermal mass）可由内能与热模式熵态的平衡固定；该物理图像与 OPE 反演公式技术等价，其中热质量值由超越方程组（transcendental sets of equations）决定。

Conclusion: 该模型在奇数时空维度 $d=4k+3$ 中展现的数学结构，暗示了奇数维热场论与精确可解一维量子问题之间存在更深层的对应关系。

Abstract: We observe a remarkable mathematical structure in the gap equations of the large-$N$ Gross--Neveu model at imaginary chemical potential in odd spacetime dimensions $d = 4k+3$. We show they can be written as the sum of two parts: one defined by higher-order discrete Laplacian patterns and a cut-off dependent part given by truncated asymptotic expansion of a hypergeometric function. We argue that this picture corresponds to a deeper relationship between thermal field theories in these odd $d$ and exactly-solvable one-dimensional quantum problems. We find that the thermal mass at specific imaginary chemical potential values is fixed where internal energy balances entropic states of thermal modes which is physically equivalent with OPE inversion formula techniques where thermal mass values arise from transcendental sets of equations.

Abstract: Active feedback between geometry and physics is woven throughout the study of Nature at its fundamental level, and is of key importance in string theory. ### [214] [Chirality loss during brane merging: a universal power law from the Jackiw-Rebbi index](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24739)
*H. P. Pinheiro,C. A. S. Almeida*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本研究在(1+1)维Jackiw-Rebbi框架下，发现畴壁（domain wall）合并时手征费米子零模空间分离遵循普适幂律|Δ_abs|∝d^γ，临界指数γ仅由Jackiw-Rebbi拓扑指数N_JR决定，与费米子质量间隙、标量场可积性及畴壁形状细节无关，从而证明四维Yukawa耦合坍缩率为拓扑不变量。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 以(1+1)维Jackiw-Rebbi框架为可控解析实验室，分析双畴壁合并时手征零模的空间分离。对比可积sine-Gordon模型与四个不可积double sine-Gordon模型（均满足N_JR=1），推导sine-Gordon模型的闭式重叠积分I(d)=2d/sinh(2d)，并引入局部有效指数γ_eff(d)解析幂律行为。

Result: 临界指数γ∈[0.930,0.985]（N_JR=1）。sine-Gordon模型的精确手征分离表现为双曲函数之比，无自由参数。γ可理解为γ_eff(d)的交叉平台值，其亚单位（sub-unit）性质源于N_JR=1零模的Pöschl-Teller结构。

Conclusion: γ的普适性表明，畴壁合并过程中四维Yukawa耦合的坍缩率是一个拓扑不变量（topological invariant），不受微观标量动力学细节影响。

Abstract: We investigate the rate at which chiral fermion localisation is lost when two domain walls merge in extra-dimensional braneworld scenarios, using the $(1+1)$-dimensional Jackiw-Rebbi framework as a controlled analytical laboratory. As the inter-brane separation $d$ decreases, left- and right-handed zero modes hybridise and chiral asymmetry is progressively lost. We show that the spatial separation between the chiral zero modes follows a universal power law $|Δ_{\mathrm{abs}}|\propto d^γ$ in the merging limit $d\to 0^{+}$, with the critical exponent $γ$ determined solely by the Jackiw-Rebbi topological index $N_{\mathrm{JR}}$, and independent of the fermionic mass gap, the integrability of the scalar sector, and the detailed shape of the domain wall profile. Comparing the integrable sine-Gordon model with four members of the non-integrable double sine-Gordon family, all sharing $N_{\mathrm{JR}}=1$, we find $γ\in[0.930,0.985]$. For the sine-Gordon model we derive the closed-form overlap integral $I(d)=2d/\sinh(2d)$, from which the exact chiral separation follows as a ratio of hyperbolic functions without free parameters. This result identifies $γ$ as the crossover plateau of a local effective exponent $γ_{\mathrm{eff}}(d)$, explaining the sub-unit value analytically and tracing the universality to the Pöschl-Teller structure of the $N_{\mathrm{JR}}=1$ zero mode. The universality of $γ$ implies that the rate of four-dimensional Yukawa coupling collapse during brane merging is a topological invariant, insensitive to the microscopic scalar dynamics generating the walls.

</details>


### [215] [Multicritical points of gravitational solitons and a black hole in four dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24783)
*Moaathe Belhaj Ahmed,Moisés Bravo-Gaete,Robert B. Mann,Constanza Quijada*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文首次在四维广义相对论中实现了多临界点，通过在Plebański非线性电动力学框架下使用多项式结构函数，建立了非线性电动力学耦合与热力学相结构之间的直接联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在引力系统中实现并系统构建多临界点（multicritical points）行为，将先前已知的三重点（triple points）推广到更一般的情形。

Method: 采用Plebański非线性电动力学（Plebański nonlinear electrodynamics）框架，引入多项式结构函数$\mathcal{H}(P)$；建立以Maxwell不变量（Maxwell invariant）$F$的幂级数表示的物质理论与Plebański表述之间的显式映射，构造带电渐近反德西特（anti-de Sitter）黑洞和磁荷孤子（magnetically charged solitons）的新族。

Result: 在巨正则系综（grand-canonical ensemble）中，孤子扇区展现出多重燕尾结构（swallowtail structures），标志着一级相变（first-order phase transitions），允许多个磁荷孤子与单个电荷黑洞共存；共存相的数量由多项式结构函数的次数控制。黑洞分支不呈现燕尾行为，不允许多个电荷黑洞与磁荷孤子共存。

Conclusion: 这些构型定义了推广先前三重点的多临界点，揭示了非线性电动力学耦合与热力学相结构之间的直接对应关系。

Abstract: We present the first realization of multicritical points in four-dimensional general relativity, specifically within the context of Plebański nonlinear electrodynamics, using a polynomial structural function denoted as $\mathcal{H}(P)$. We show that this construction provides a systematic mechanism to engineer multicritical behavior in gravitational systems. By establishing an explicit mapping between matter theories expressed as power series in the Maxwell invariant $F$ and the Plebański formulation, we construct new families of electrically charged asymptotically anti-de Sitter black holes and magnetically charged solitons. In the grand-canonical ensemble, we analyze their thermodynamic properties and uncover a rich phase structure. We demonstrate that the soliton sector develops multiple swallowtail structures, signaling first-order phase transitions and allowing the coexistence of several magnetically charged solitons with a single electrically charged black hole. These configurations define multicritical points that generalize previously known triple points. We further show that the number of coexisting phases is controlled by the degree of the polynomial structural function, providing a direct link between the nonlinear electrodynamics couplings and the thermodynamic phase structure. In contrast, the black hole branch does not display swallowtail behavior, and it does not allow multiple electrically charged black holes to coexist with a magnetically charged soliton.

### [216] [Defect Conformal Manifolds along RG Domain Walls between $\mathbb Z_N$-Parafermions and Minimal Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24978)
*Jin-Rui Zhang,Jing-Hao Jin,Ting-Kai Chen,Jin Chen*

Main category: hep-th

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用自底向上(bottom-up)方法，以“幻象流(phantom currents)”的涌现为核心，通过追踪沿重整化群流保持的非可逆对称性𝔰𝔬(3)_𝑁来提取定域在缺陷上的幻象流精确谱；利用簇分解原理(cluster decomposition principle)分析UV-IR应力张量混合，建立代数框架。

Result: 自旋-1幻象流使得界面可发生边际形变(marginally deformed)，动态生成连续缺陷共形流形(defect conformal manifold)；自旋-2算子作为𝑊^{(3)}-代数的后代，通过簇分解原理严格约束UV-IR应力张量混合；该代数框架可精确计算共形流形上依赖于参数的透射率(transmission rate)，且在N→∞极限下透射率严格为零，源于宏观靶空间坍缩(macroscopic target space collapse)。

Conclusion: 幻象流方法为构造非微扰RG畴壁提供了有效的代数框架；非可逆对称性在约束重整化群流与缺陷物理中起到关键作用；大N极限下的透射率消失揭示了靶空间坍缩的宏观效应。

Abstract: We investigate the renormalization group (RG) domain walls interpolating between the $\mathbb{Z}_N$ parafermion theory (the critical $N$-state Potts model) and the Virasoro minimal model $\mathcal{M}_{N+1}$. These flows are genuinely non-perturbative and an explicit construction of Gaiotto type RG domain wall remains elusive. We bypass this limitation by employing a bottom-up approach centered on the emergence of ``phantom currents". By tracking the preserved non-invertible symmetries ($\mathfrak{so}(3)_N$) along the flow, we extract the exact spectrum of these currents localized on the defect. We demonstrate that the presence of a spin-1 phantom current allows the interface to be marginally deformed, dynamically generating a continuous defect conformal manifold. Furthermore, we show that an extra spin-2 operator, crucially as a $W^{(3)}$-algebra descendant of the spin-1 phantom current, rigidly constrains the UV-IR stress tensor mixing via the cluster decomposition principle. This algebraic framework enables the exact computation of the parameter-dependent transmission rate across the conformal manifold, which we observe strictly vanishes in the large-$N$ limit as a consequence of macroscopic target space collapse.

Conclusion: 不稳定非阿贝尔上同调理论能够统一处理RR通量与NS-膜源引起的非线性效应，为M-理论中的膜通量量子化提供了更全面的数学框架。

Abstract: The traditional conjecture that RR-flux is quantized in stable K-cohomology fails to account for the presence of NS-brane sources: These impose nonlinear relations -- reductions of the famous quadratic relation on M-brane flux -- that can only be captured by unstable nonabelian cohomology theories. Here we consider a deformation of unstable K-theory which properly quantizes the fluxes coupling to D0/D2/NS5-branes, find a twisted version that quantizes also the fluxes coupling to NS1/D4-branes, and show that this oxidizes to a proper electromagnetic quantization of M-brane fluxes.

### [218] [Pseudorandom Dynamics in the SYK Model and Cryptographic Censorship in JT Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25178)

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文论证了SYK模型在JT引力中条件性地实现了密码学审查（Cryptographic Censorship），通过证明SYK无序系综是近似酉k-设计，并在planted-SYK困难性猜想下将其提升为引力赝随机酉，结合因果楔重建得出典型态必存在事件视界的结论，同时将正则化测地线长度识别为显式区分算子，将密码学审查与复杂度等于体积猜想联系起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用Weingarten微积分（Weingarten calculus）和随机矩阵普适性（random matrix universality），证明SYK无序系综对所有k = poly(N)构成近似酉k-设计（approximate unitary k-design），偏差由谱形状因子（spectral form factor）控制；随后提出planted-SYK困难性猜想，并借助谱普适性和低次多项式框架（low-degree polynomial framework）提供证据。

Result: 在planted-SYK困难性猜想下，近似酉设计升级为引力赝随机酉（gravitationally pseudorandom unitary）；结合JT引力中的因果楔重建（causal wedge reconstruction），证明SYK微正则窗口中的典型态在体对偶中必有事件视界（event horizon），无视界态的占比为双指数小；识别出最大内部切片的正则化测地线长度（regularized geodesic length）为显式区分算子，其预测差距随黑洞内部的拉伸而线性增长。

Conclusion: SYK模型在特定数学假设下实现了JT引力中的密码学审查，且密码学审查与复杂度等于体积猜想（complexity equals volume conjecture）之间存在直接联系。

Abstract: We argue that the SYK model provides a conditional realization of Cryptographic Censorship in JT gravity. By using the Weingarten calculus and random matrix universality, we prove that the SYK disorder ensemble is an approximate unitary $k$-design for all $k=\poly(N)$, with deviation controlled by the spectral form factor. We then formulate the planted-SYK hardness conjecture and provide evidence from spectral universality and the low-degree polynomial framework. Under this conjecture, the approximate design becomes a gravitationally pseudorandom unitary. Together with the efficient causal wedge reconstruction in JT gravity, this leads to the conclusion that typical states in the SYK microcanonical window must have event horizons in their bulk duals, with the horizonless fraction doubly exponentially small. We further identify the regularized geodesic length of the maximal interior slice as the explicit distinguishing operator. Its prediction gap grows linearly with time due to the stretching of the black hole interior, linking Cryptographic Censorship to the complexity equals volume conjecture.

### [219] [Quantum-Corrected Q-balls in the Friedberg-Lee-Sirlin Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25243)
*Yong-Xiang Su,Qi-Xin Xie,Shuang-Yong Zhou*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文在非均匀Hartree近似下，研究了Friedberg-Lee-Sirlin模型中Q-ball的实时量子动力学。通过重整化公式和经典极限标度，作者在3+1维空间中模拟了单Q-ball构型，发现了经典区与量子区的分离、Noether电荷在平均场与涨落模式间的周期性交换，以及量子涨落导致的稳定性变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用非均匀Hartree近似（inhomogeneous Hartree approximation），将平均场与领先阶量子两点函数（quantum two-point functions）自洽演化；通过随机系综表示（stochastic ensemble representation）实现数值求解；引入重整化表述（renormalized formulation）和经典极限标度（classical-limit scaling），在3+1维空间中模拟单Q-ball构型。

Result: 发现了经典区（classical regime）与量子区（quantum regime）的清晰分离：经典区中量子涨落较小，演化接近经典解；量子区中涨落部分携带显著比例的Noether电荷（Noether charge）。观测到平均场与涨落模式之间Noether电荷的周期性交换。还发现了一个中间窗口（intermediate window），在此窗口内经典稳定的构型在引入Hartree涨落后变得不稳定。

Conclusion: 该研究为可重整化两场孤子模型中Q-ball的实时量子模拟迈出了第一步，揭示了量子涨落对Q-ball动力学和稳定性的重要影响，为后续更全面的量子场论孤子研究提供了基础。

Abstract: We study the real-time quantum dynamics of Q-balls in the Friedberg-Lee-Sirlin model within the inhomogeneous Hartree approximation. The mean fields are evolved self-consistently with the leading quantum two-point functions, which are implemented numerically through a stochastic ensemble representation. After introducing a renormalized formulation and a classical-limit scaling, we simulate single-Q-ball configurations in $3+1$ dimensions and compare their quantum-corrected evolution with the corresponding classical dynamics. We find a clear separation between a classical regime, where quantum fluctuations remain small and the evolution closely follows the classical solution, and a quantum regime, where the fluctuation sector carries a sizable fraction of the Noether charge. We also observe a periodic exchange of Noether charge between the mean fields and the fluctuation modes within the Hartree approximation. We further investigate the stability of quantum-corrected Q-balls and find an intermediate window in which configurations that are classically stable become unstable once Hartree fluctuations are included. Our results provide a first step toward real-time quantum simulations of Q-balls in renormalizable two-field soliton models.

Abstract: In this work, first we discuss the connections between various low-dimensional quantum gravity models, including 3d Chern-Simons, 2d JT and 2d BF theory, 2d Liouville and 2d WZW, and 1d Schwarzian through holography and dimension reduction, and discuss some universalities in their partition functions. ### [221] [Negative entropy in scrambling black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25315)

Abstract: We present a microscopic statistical-mechanical foundation for interpreting the horizon area of a scrambling black hole as coherent information, equivalently negative conditional quantum entropy, in Hawking's pair-creation picture. We derive the entropy increase induced in a black hole when an infalling object is absorbed and scrambled into its microscopic degrees of freedom. Up to finite-reservoir corrections, this increase takes a canonical form at the Hawking temperature, regardless of the entropy carried by the infalling object. Applying this entropy formula to an incoming mode paired by time reversal with an outgoing Hawking radiation mode, we show that their partition-function contributions cancel in the coherent-information balance associated with the horizon area. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将先前工作中发展的天球RSVW形式体系从旋量坐标扩展到迷你扭量超空间（minitwistor superspace），以更自然地描述N=4超对称杨-米尔斯理论（N=4 SYM）中的天球振幅结构，并建立其与迷你扭量几何和半经典动力学之间的联系。

Method: 利用Drummond-Henn公式构建树图阶N^k-MHV天球叶振幅（celestial leaf amplitudes），并通过迷你扭量傅里叶变换（minitwistor-Fourier transform）将其转化为迷你扭量线族模空间上的积分；同时将Korchemsky-Sokatchev扭量变换技术（twistor-transform）适配到叶振幅的迷你扭量傅里叶变换。进而提出两种半经典动力学描述：1) 在迷你扭量超空间中定义基于代数环（algebraic cycles）的威尔逊算符（Wilson operators），将其半经典关联函数作为生成泛函；2) 构建半经典迷你扭量西格玛模型（minitwistor sigma model），识别其顶点算符并构造在S-代数下闭合的天球胶子算符。

Result: 树图阶N^k-MHV天球叶振幅的迷你扭量傅里叶变换可表示为迷你扭量线族模空间上的积分。两种半经典动力学构造——基于威尔逊算符的生成泛函和迷你扭量西格玛模型中的顶点算符——其半经典关联函数均能再现树图阶N^k-MHV叶振幅。此外，在迷你扭量西格玛模型中构造的天球胶子算符在半经典近似下对S-代数（S-algebra）闭合。

Conclusion: 成功将天球RSVW形式体系扩展到迷你扭量超空间，并建立了树图阶N^k-MHV叶振幅与迷你扭量几何和半经典动力学的多重联系，为后续通过天球版本的Brandhuber-Spence-Travaglini形式体系推广到单圈图乃至更高圈层次奠定了基础。

Abstract: We extend the celestial Roiban-Spradlin-Volovich-Witten (RSVW) formalism developed in our previous work to minitwistor superspace. Using the Drummond-Henn formula for all tree-level amplitudes in N=4 supersymmetric Yang-Mills (SYM) theory, we construct tree-level N^k-MHV celestial leaf amplitudes and show that their minitwistor-Fourier transforms are given by integrals over moduli spaces of families of minitwistor lines. We also adapt the Korchemsky-Sokatchev twistor-transform techniques for gluon amplitudes to the minitwistor-Fourier transforms of leaf amplitudes. We then describe two dynamical formulations of these celestial amplitudes. First, we show that semiclassical correlators of Wilson operators supported on algebraic cycles in minitwistor superspace act as generating functionals for tree-level N^k-MHV leaf-gluon amplitudes. Second, we analyse a semiclassical minitwistor sigma model, identify its vertex operators, and construct from them celestial gluon operators that close on the S-algebra in the semiclassical approximation; their leading-trace semiclassical correlators again reproduce the tree-level N^k-MHV leaf amplitudes. A companion paper extends this construction beyond tree level, in particular to one-loop amplitudes via a celestial version of the Brandhuber-Spence-Travaglini formalism.

</details>


### [223] [The Diagrammar of Quantum Magnusian](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25473)
*Li Guo,Joon-Hwi Kim,Jung-Wook Kim,Sungsoo Kim,Sangmin Lee,Jian-Rong Li*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过引入颜色基（color basis）和黑白基（black-and-white basis）两种互补视角，并结合指数化Wick收缩（exponentiated Wick contraction），提出了一种高效计算量子Magnusian中Murua系数的图解算法。该算法建立了一套边收缩规则（edge contraction rules），使得仅通过图操作即可直接从图解层次递归计算Murua系数，无需直接处理底层的Magnus展开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典Magnusian的图解展开已基于树图和Hopf代数得到完整建立，而近期工作将之推广到量子场论（quantum field theory），揭示了圈展开（loop expansion）的一般结构及不同图之间的有趣关系。本文旨在进一步推进圈展开，为量子Magnusian中每个图的权重因子——即Murua系数（Murua coefficient）——提供一种高效的图解计算算法。

Method: 本文同时采用颜色基和黑白基两种互补视角来刻画Magnusian，并利用指数化Wick收缩从Magnus级数（Magnus series）中提取Murua系数。在此基础上，识别出Murua递归公式的圈层次推广，最终建立一套边收缩规则，使得Murua系数可在纯图解层次上直接递归计算。

Result: 建立了一套适用于量子Magnusian的边收缩规则，使得Murua系数可以仅通过图操作即可计算，无需直接查阅或操纵底层的Magnus展开。这表明量子Magnusian的矩阵元可以完全依托图的操作来求解。

Conclusion: 量子Magnusian的矩阵元可以仅通过图操作计算，这为量子场论中高阶圈展开的计算提供了一种高效且结构清晰的图解途径。

Abstract: The logarithm of the time-evolution operator has been termed Magnusian, on account of the fact that its expansion describes the Magnus series. The diagrammatic expansion and computation of the classical Magnusian has been completely established in terms of tree graphs and their Hopf algebra. Recent works initiated extensions into quantum field theory, revealing general structures of loop expansions while finding intriguing relations between different diagrams. In this work, we advance the loop expansion further by providing an efficient diagrammatic algorithm to calculate the weight factor of each graph in the quantum Magnusian, known as the Murua coefficient. This is achieved by incorporating two complementary perspectives on the Magnusian at the same time: the color basis and the black-and-white basis. We extract the Murua coefficients from the Magnus series by utilizing these two bases while implementing an exponentiated Wick contraction. In turn, we identify the loop-level extension of Murua's recursive formula. Eventually, we establish a set of edge contraction rules which facilitate a direct recursive computation of the Murua coefficients at the purely diagrammatic level, without referencing or directly manipulating the underlying Magnus expansion. This shows that the matrix elements of the quantum Magnusian can be computed from graph manipulations alone.

### [224] [Bulk Motion in Global AdS$_3$ from the Boundary Energy-Density Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25481)
*Shiki Yoshikawa*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了全局 AdS₃ 中的体传播如何体现在对偶 CFT₂ 在柱面上的边界能量密度中，展示了边界能量密度的手征峰（chiral peaks）能够镜像全局 AdS₃ 中径向零测地线（radial null geodesic）的边界到边界周期传播。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在全局 AdS₃ 几何中，零激发从边界发射后，经过全局时间 Δτ=π 到达对径边界点，再经过 Δτ=2π 返回原边界点。这一边界到边界的周期传播特性在庞加莱片（Poincaré-patch）描述中缺失，因此需要研究该全局效应如何在边界共形场论（CFT）中编码。

Method: 从两类边界态出发进行分析：一是波包态（wave-packet state），计算其前导阶能量密度；二是由带有欧几里得正规子（Euclidean regulator）的重算子（heavy operator）制备的态，解析求解柱面上精确的应力张量（stress tensor）。

Result: 波包态的能量密度由两个沿边界光锥方向运动的手征峰组成，其相对权重编码了对应体零射线（null ray）的碰撞参数（impact parameter）。重算子态的能量密度给出两个沿边界光锥方向运动的周期手征脉冲（chiral pulses），这些脉冲到达对径点并返回原点的全局时间与体径向零测地线完全一致。

Conclusion: 边界能量密度能够捕获全局 AdS₃ 中定域体激发（localized bulk excitations）的边界到边界传播及其周期性，验证了全息对偶（holographic duality）中全局几何信息的边界编码能力。

Abstract: We study how bulk propagation in global AdS$_3$ is encoded in boundary energy densities of the dual CFT$_2$ on the cylinder. A key feature of the global geometry, which is absent in the Poincaré-patch description, is that a null excitation emitted from the boundary reaches the antipodal boundary point after $Δτ=π$ and returns to the original boundary point after $Δτ=2π$. We show that this periodic boundary-to-boundary propagation is reflected in the CFT energy density as chiral peaks that meet at the antipodal point and reappear after one global period. For a wave-packet state, the leading energy density consists of two chiral peaks moving along the boundary light-cone directions; their relative weights encode the impact parameter of the corresponding bulk null ray. For a state prepared by a heavy operator with Euclidean regulator, the exact cylinder stress tensor gives two periodic chiral pulses moving along the boundary light-cone directions. These pulses reach the antipodal point and return to the original point at the same global times as the radial null geodesic in the bulk. Thus the boundary energy density captures the boundary-to-boundary propagation and periodicity of localized bulk excitations in global AdS$_3$.

Method: 基于分岔方程（bifurcation equations）构造有效热力学景观（thermodynamic landscape），引入流参数 τ（弛豫时间，relaxation time）描述黑洞在热力学状态空间（thermodynamic state space）中向平衡不动点（equilibrium fixed points）的弛豫过程，并利用临界点附近的普适约化行为进行分类。

Result: 在临界点附近，热力学流动（thermodynamic flow）简化为普适数学形式，使得不同黑洞可根据其临界行为被归入不同的普适类（universality classes）；同时观察到临界减速现象，弛豫时间尺度由局部分岔结构（local bifurcation structure）完全决定。

Conclusion: 该动力学系统方法为黑洞热力学临界性提供了一种基于分岔理论的统一框架，实现了对不同黑洞临界行为的普适分类，并揭示了弛豫动力学与分岔结构之间的内在联系。

Abstract: We present a dynamical systems approach to black hole thermodynamic criticality based on bifurcation equations. We construct an effective thermodynamic landscape in which black holes relax toward equilibrium fixed points. To describe this process, we introduce a flow parameter $τ$, interpreted as a phenomenological relaxation time, which governs the approach toward equilibrium configurations in thermodynamic state space. Near critical points, the thermodynamic flow simplifies into universal mathematical forms, which allows different black holes to be grouped into different universality classes based on their critical behaviour. Our analysis further shows critical slowing down, with relaxation timescales determined entirely by the local bifurcation structure.

### [226] [Finite-$N$ BMN index across all vacuum sectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25560)
*Chi-Ming Chang,Sarthak Duary,Kangning Liu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过对称群特征标展开和留数展开两种互补方法，计算了BMN矩阵量子力学在所有分划标记的超对称真空扇区上的有限N Witten指数，发现电荷j~N²附近的系数呈现N²量级的熵增长，并揭示了主导扇区随N变化的“主导切换”现象，为将BMN指数用作受保护平面波黑洞微观态的诊断工具提供了定量有限N基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为BMN指数作为受保护平面波黑洞微观态诊断工具建立定量有限N基础，并理解其扇区组织结构与熵增长行为。

Method: 对每个扇区的酉矩阵积分，发展两种互补方法：对称群特征标展开（symmetric-group character expansion），将每个固定阶次约化为有限组合和；留数展开（residue expansion），其中贡献极点由有根树组织，多分划扇区引入彩色树（colored-tree）推广。通过直接积分和常数项提取进行独立验证。

Result: 计算了N≤9的所有真空扇区。等阶次展开中电荷j~N²附近的系数呈现N²量级的熵增长，且扇区求和未抵消该增长。有限N数据揭示非平凡扇区组织结构：在j=N²附近，给出最大贡献的扇区随N变化，从小秩的单分划扇区（single-partition sector）切换到N=5开始的双分划扇区（double-partition sector），称为主导切换（dominance switching）。

Conclusion: 结果为使用BMN指数诊断受保护平面波黑洞微观态提供了定量有限N基础，并暗示了在平面波黑洞被宏观M2巨引力子（giant graviton）修饰下的体对偶解释，类似于AdS₅×S⁵中对偶修饰黑洞。

Abstract: We compute the finite-$N$ Witten index of BMN matrix quantum mechanics after summing over all partition-labeled supersymmetric vacuum sectors. Starting from the unitary-matrix integral for each sector, we develop two complementary evaluation methods: a symmetric-group character expansion, which reduces each fixed fugacity order to a finite combinatorial sum, and a residue expansion in which the contributing poles are organized by rooted trees, with a colored-tree generalization for multi-partition sectors. Direct integration and constant-term extraction provide independent checks in explicit examples. We evaluate every vacuum sector for $N\leq 9$. In the equal-fugacity expansion, the coefficients near charges $j\sim N^2$ show entropy growth of order $N^2$, and the sector sum does not cancel this growth. The finite-$N$ data also reveal a nontrivial sectoral organization: near $j=N^2$, the sector giving the largest contribution changes with $N$, from single-partition sectors at small rank to double-partition sectors starting at $N=5$. We call this phenomenon dominance switching. These results provide a quantitative finite-$N$ foundation for using the BMN index as a diagnostic of protected plane-wave black-hole microstates and suggest a bulk interpretation in terms of plane-wave black holes dressed by macroscopic M2 giant gravitons, analogous to dual dressed black holes in $AdS_5\times S^5$.

Abstract: We investigate the renormalized fermion-gluon vertex, the fermion effective mass, and the fermion condensate when the fermion propagates in an external Yang-Mills gauge field. We use an exact Green's function for the Dirac operator in a non-Abelian plane-wave gauge field to construct the renormalized vertex function, calculate the on-shell fermion self-energy, and the background-dependent condensate. We consider both the background and operator fields in the axial gauge $k^{μ} \mathcal{A}_{μ}^{a}=0$, thereby preserving the gauge. Its applications to strong-field QCD and non-Abelian Schwinger physics are discussed.

### [228] [A Casimir obstruction to asymptotically flat black-brane completions of non-supersymmetric 7-branes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25588)

Result: 无卡西米尔能量时，系统可解析求解，存在渐近局部平坦（locally flat asymptotics）的解但含有限固有距离处的裸奇点；引入卡西米尔反馈后，该奇点无法被正则的有限视界黑膜核心取代。

Abstract: We study axisymmetric 7-brane solutions in the dilaton-gravity sector of 10d supergravity, including the backreaction of the Casimir energy induced by monodromies around the transverse circle. Without Casimir energy, we find that the system is analytically solvable and admits locally flat asymptotics with arbitrary deficit angles, but the corresponding solutions contain a naked singularity at finite proper distance. We investigate whether this singularity can be replaced by a regular finite-horizon black-brane core once Casimir backreaction is included.
