### [229] [Endpoint formulation and Molien--Weyl structure for the \(N=2\), large--\(d\) BFSS/BMN models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25647)
*Badis Ydri*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了高斯区间的BFSS/BMN型矩阵量子力学中N=2、大d扇区的径向端点形式，建立了端点配分函数与Molien-Weyl描述之间的等价关系，并分析了连续极限下的二次系数分解、完整势的几何结构以及非多项式玩具模型对D通道贡献的重现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究对BFSS/BMN型矩阵量子力学在高斯区间的端点形式及其与规范投影配分函数的关系尚不清楚，且连续极限下完整势（holonomy potential）的几何行为和D通道贡献的物理来源有待阐明。

Method: 采用径向端点形式（radial endpoint formulation），将体、规范及纵向自由度积分掉，保留由有效完整势（effective holonomy potential）支配的横向端点变量。通过平面端点形式与角向Molien-Weyl描述（angular Molien-Weyl description）的对比建立等价关系，并引入非多项式玩具模型\(V_{\rm toy}(B)=-\log\cosh B\)完成横向展开的收敛。

Result: 平面端点形式等价于Molien-Weyl描述（除一个普适旁观因子外）；低温展开的二次系数\(d(d+1)/2\)计数真空以上的高斯单重态（Gaussian singlet states）。连续极限下二次系数分离为高斯贡献、D通道和β通道，其中高斯项变为平庸，完整核（holonomy kernel）通过端点高斯宽度和各向异性耦合的奇异依赖性产生有限连续贡献。相关鞍点（relevant saddle）是约束边界鞍点（constrained boundary saddle），而非无约束临界点。非多项式玩具模型精确重现连续极限下的D通道贡献\(-2d\)，将其解释为Wishart-Stiefel熵（Wishart-Stiefel entropy）。

Conclusion: D通道贡献的几何起源可理解为端点形式中嵌入\(\mathbb R^d\)的涌现四维几何所对应的Wishart-Stiefel熵，为理解BFSS/BMN型矩阵量子力学中完整势的几何结构提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We study the \(N=2\), large--\(d\) sector of BFSS/BMN-type matrix quantum mechanics on the lattice in the Gaussian regime. We develop a radial endpoint formulation in which the bulk, gauge, and longitudinal degrees of freedom are integrated out, leaving transverse endpoint variables governed by an effective holonomy potential. We show that this planar endpoint formulation is equivalent to the angular Molien--Weyl description of the gauge-projected partition function, up to a universal spectator factor. This relation allows the low-temperature expansion of the endpoint partition function to be obtained from the Molien--Weyl result, whose quadratic coefficient \(d(d+1)/2\) counts Gaussian singlet states above the vacuum.
  We then analyze the continuum limit of the quadratic coefficient and show that it separates into a Gaussian contribution, a \(D\)-channel, and a \(β\)-channel. The naive Gaussian term becomes trivial, while the exact holonomy kernel generates finite continuum contributions through singular dependence on the endpoint Gaussian width and anisotropic coupling.
  We then study the geometry of the holonomy potential and show that its relevant saddle is a constrained boundary saddle on the aligned branch, rather than an unconstrained critical point. The associated transverse expansion captures the local saddle geometry, but any finite polynomial truncation has a trivial continuum limit. Finally, we introduce a non-polynomial toy model based on \(V_{\rm toy}(B)=-\log\cosh B\), which provides a completion of the transverse expansion and reproduces exactly the continuum \(D\)-channel contribution \(-2d\). This prepares the geometric interpretation of the \(D\)-channel as a Wishart--Stiefel entropy associated with an emergent four-dimensional geometry embedded \(\mathbb R^d\) in the endpoint formulation.

</details>

### [231] [Null Strings Gauged and Reloaded, I: Null Strings Have Carroll-Weyl Gauge Symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25817)
*M. M. Sheikh-Jabbari,H. Yavartanoo*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过Carroll几何（Carrollian geometry）重新审视空弦（null strings）理论，发现传统ILST作用量存在被忽视的部分规范对称性，进而在两个Carroll-Weyl标度变换（Carroll-Weyl scalings）下构建了新的空弦作用量，揭示了该对称性的Carroll几何起源，为一致量子化奠定基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统描述空弦的ILST作用量（Isberg-Lindström-Sundborg-Theodoridis action）存在一个此前被忽视的部分规范对称性（partial-gauge symmetry），这一发现使得文献中已有的标准空弦分析的一致性受到质疑。因此，有必要从Carroll几何出发重新构建空弦理论，澄清该对称性的起源。

Method: 利用Carroll几何，作者注意到空弦在世界面上拥有两个Weyl标度选项（Weyl scaling options），而普通拉伸弦（tensile string）只有一个。基于此，将两个Carroll-Weyl标度（Carroll-Weyl scalings）与二维微分同胚（2D diffeomorphisms）同时作为局域规范对称性，构建新的空弦作用量。

Result: 新构建的作用量在固定其中一个Carroll-Weyl标度后约化为传统的ILST作用量，且该对称性的残余部分正是此前被忽视的部分规范对称性。这阐明了该对称性的Carroll几何起源。

Conclusion: 澄清了空弦理论中被忽视的对称性的几何根源，为后续对空弦进行一致量子化（consistent quantization）铺平了道路。

Abstract: Null strings, strings with Carrollian worldsheets, are traditionally described by the Isberg-Lindström-Sundborg-Theodoridis (ILST) action, which is obtained via a tensionless limit of standard tensile strings. In a recent work, we observed that the ILST action enjoys an overlooked partial-gauge symmetry whose existence calls into question the consistency of {standard} null strings analysis found in the literature. In this paper, we show that the Carrollian geometry provides us with two Weyl scaling options, in contrast to a single Weyl scaling available for the ordinary tensile string worldsheet. Defining the null string theory by the action that realizes the two Carroll-Weyl scalings as well as the 2D diffeomorphisms as local (gauge) symmetries, we construct the new null string action. We show that the ILST action is obtained after fixing one of the two Carroll-Weyl scalings of the action that we construct, and that the residual part of this symmetry is precisely the overlooked partial-gauge symmetry. We hence clarify the Carroll-geometric origin of the overlooked symmetry and pave the way for a consistent quantization of null strings.

### [232] [Hard cutoff and gauge theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25827)
*V. Branchina,F. Contino,R. Gandolfo,A. Pernace*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出一种在威尔逊有效场论框架下，通过硬截断保持规范不变性的方法（以Euler-Heisenberg修正为例），从而缓解规范理论与Wilsonian有效场论之间的张力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 规范理论（gauge theory）中使用硬截断（hard cutoff）通常会导致规范不变性（gauge invariance）的破坏，这似乎与Wilsonian有效场论（Wilsonian effective field theory）范式产生了矛盾。本文旨在解决这一冲突。

Method: 以Euler-Heisenberg对自由Maxwell作用的修正为例，引入保持量子层面规范不变性的Wilsonian硬紫外截断（hard UV cutoff），分别对标量QED和费米子QED进行了分析。

Result: 除了被截断压低的项（generally cutoff-suppressed）外，恢复了在固有时间正规化（proper-time regularization）下得到的经典Euler-Heisenberg结果。这些项在反背景场（inverse background field）中具有周期性，并在背景场探测尺度接近截断尺度时变得相关。

Conclusion: 本文发展的方法为在规范理论中实现更接近Wegner-Houghton构造精神的Wilsonian重整化群（renormalization group）方案迈出了第一步。

Abstract: According to usual calculations, the use of a hard cutoff $Λ$ in gauge theories leads to a violation of gauge invariance. This seems to generate a tension between gauge theories and the Wilsonian effective field theory (EFT) paradigm, where $Λ$ has the physical meaning of ultimate scale of the theory, the scale above which the latter has to be replaced by its UV completion. In the present work, considering the Euler-Heisenberg correction to the free Maxwell action, we present a way to introduce the Wilsonian hard UV cutoff $Λ$ that preserves gauge invariance at the quantum level. For both scalar and fermionic QED, we recover the well-known Euler-Heisenberg result obtained within proper-time regularization, apart from terms that are generically cutoff-suppressed. These terms, periodic in the inverse background field, might become relevant in regimes where the latter probes scales not much smaller than $Λ$. On the theoretical side, the methods developed in the present work represent a first step towards a new (closer in spirit to the Wegner-Houghton construction) realization of the Wilsonian renormalization group program in gauge theories.

</details>

Method: 通过对矩阵模型进行$N=3$和$N=4$表示的系统约化，分别进行Krylov态复杂度和Krylov算子增长的哈密顿量分析，计算对应的Lanczos系数。

Abstract: We study Krylov complexity in BMN Plane Wave Matrix Model at large mass deformation. We consider various consistent reductions of the matrix model that allow us to perform a Hamiltonian analysis which leads to different notions of the Krylov complexity. In the first part of the paper, we study the Krylov state complexity considering systematic reduction of $N=3$ and $N=4$ representations of the matrix model, which reveals a universal characteristic scaling for the Lanczos coefficients and fix them completely in terms of the mass deformation parameter. In the second part of the paper, we study the Krylov operator growth in the matrix model and compute the corresponding Lanczos coefficients. In both cases, we observe a \emph{linear} scaling of Lanczos coefficients with the mass parameter. The early time growth in Krylov complexity receives quadratic correction due to the presence of the massive deformation in the matrix model. Our analysis reveals that such massive corrections appear at same order in time for both the notion of the Krylov complexity.

### [235] [On Perturbatively Dressed Observables](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26077)
*Clifford Cheung,Allic Sivaramakrishnan,Jordan Wilson-Gerow,Lihang Zhou*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过微扰计算展示了电动力学和广义相对论中局域算符的引力修正矩阵元（gravitationally-dressed matrix elements），证明修鉓（dressing）并非装饰性，而是普遍引入运动学奇点（kinematic singularities），并揭示修鉓与规范固定（gauge fixing）在数学上等价，具体表现为一种动力学时间规范（dynamical temporal gauge）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力理论的核心教训是局域可观测量（local observables）难以精确定义，坐标本身是描述中的冗余；尽管已有大量形式化工作，但对由此产生的引力修鉓可观测量（gravitationally-dressed observables）的显式计算仍较缺乏，本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 采用微扰计算方法，同时考虑势能光子与辐射光子（potential and radiative photons）以及引力子（gravitons），对电动力学和广义相对论中局域算符的修鉓矩阵元进行显式计算。

Result: 计算表明修鉓并非装饰性，而是普遍引入运动学奇点，这些奇点能够实质性地重塑可观测量；此外，修鉓在数学上等价于规范固定，具体表现为一种动力学时间规范，其中规范固定矢量（gauge-fixing vector）本身构成测地线流（geodesic fluid）。

Conclusion: 修鉓在引力与规范理论中具有实质性物理效应，不可被忽略；修鉓与规范固定的等价性为理解引力系统中的可观测量提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: A central lesson of gravity is that local observables are ill-defined. Coordinates themselves are a redundancy of description, so any particular point in spacetime is only meaningful once defined relationally by clocks, rulers, or asymptotic data. Despite extensive formal work on this subject, explicit calculations of the resulting gravitationally-dressed observables are more scarce. In this paper we perturbatively compute dressed matrix elements of local operators in electrodynamics and general relativity, including both potential and radiative photons and gravitons. Our expressions indicate that dressing is not ornamental: it universally induces kinematic singularities that can substantively reshape observables. We further show how dressing is mathematically equivalent to gauge fixing, as demonstrated by a dynamical temporal gauge in which the gauge-fixing vector is itself a geodesic fluid.

### [236] [Intersecting Surface Operators in 6d Holomorphic Field Theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26080)
*Meer Ashwinkumar*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究六维全纯场论中的交叉曲面算子，发现其交点处的局域算符类似于有理R-矩阵的准经典展开首项，并证明该算符满足杨-巴克斯特型关系，进而推导出曲面算子手征代数的余积结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在通过研究六维全纯场论中的交叉曲面算子（intersecting surface operators），揭示与之关联的量子可积结构（quantum integrable structures）。

Method: 分析了六维全纯Chern-Simons理论中曲面算子的交叉关联函数，提取交点处局域算符的形式，并验证其满足杨-巴克斯特型方程；通过算子乘积展开（OPE）推导了相关手征代数（chiral algebra）的余积（coproduct）。在六维全纯BF理论中类似地导出了R-矩阵型算符的局域首项形式。

Result: 在六维全纯Chern-Simons理论中，交叉曲面算子的关联函数给出了一个类似于有理R-矩阵（rational R-matrix）准经典展开首项的局域算符，且该算符满足杨-巴克斯特型关系（Yang-Baxter-type relation）。在六维全纯BF理论中也得到了对应的R-矩阵型算符的局域首项形式。

Conclusion: 六维全纯场论中的交叉曲面算子为量子可积结构提供了局域构建模块，特别是在twistor空间上，该理论描述四维杨-米尔斯理论的自对偶扇区（self-dual sector），预示了该框架下量子可积结构的实现。

Abstract: We study intersecting surface operators in 6d holomorphic field theories with the aim of unraveling associated quantum integrable structures. We first study the intersections of surface operators in 6d holomorphic Chern-Simons theory on $\mathbb{C}^3$. Computing their correlation function, we find a local operator at the intersection of the surface operators with a form reminiscent of the leading nontrivial term in the quasi-classical expansion of a rational $R$-matrix, as predicted by Costello. We provide evidence that this $R$-matrix-like operator satisfies a Yang-Baxter-type relation. We then derive the associated coproduct of the chiral algebra supported by surface operators from their OPE. We also study intersecting surface operators in 6d holomorphic BF theory and derive the local leading form of the corresponding $R$-matrix-like operator. When this theory is placed on twistor space, where it describes the self-dual sector of 4d Yang-Mills theory, this operator is expected to provide a local building block for quantum integrable structures anticipated in that setting.

### [237] [From dual connections to gravitational field equations -- the curvature and Einstein tensors of the $α$ - connection of a quasi-statistical manifold](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23968)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We present a detailed review of the mathematical foundations of the theory of the statistical and quasi-statistical manifolds, which recently have found many applications in general relativity, quantum mechanics, and mathematical statistics. In particular, we fully develop, in a rigorous and coherent way, the formulas and concepts necessary for the understanding of the mathematical basis of the statistical and quasi-statistical manifolds, including the properties of the dual connections and of the equiaffine connections. For each geometrical structure the explicit expressions of the curvatures and the Einstein tensors are explicitly obtained. As possible applications to the field of gravitational theories we explicitly compute the curvatures of a family of $α$-connections {$\nabla^{(α)}:=\frac{1+α}{2}\nabla +\frac{1-α}{2}\nabla ^{*}$, where $\nabla :=\nabla ^{(1)}$ and $\nabla ^{*}:=\nabla ^{(-1)}$ } are the dual connections of a quasi-statistical manifold $M$. The Einstein vacuum field equations are also written down, and the physical relevance of the obtained results for gravity and cosmology is briefly discussed.

### [238] [Associative Structures in Pseudo-Riemannian Lie Algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24204)
*Santiago Castañeda Montoya,Edison Alberto Fernández-Culma*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文研究伪黎曼李代数（pseudo-Riemannian Lie algebra）上Levi-Civita联络对称部分 $U$ 的结合性（associativity）所产生的代数与几何后果。在黎曼（正定）情形下，结合性迫使 $U$ 张量恒为零，从而退化为双不变度量（bi-invariant metrics）类；在伪黎曼情形下，结合性结合幺模性（unimodularity）可保证测地完备性（geodesic completeness）。此外，对2步幂零（2-step nilpotent）和几乎阿贝尔（almost-abelian）李代数给出了结构分类，后者以三维海森堡代数（Heisenberg algebra）配备特定（反）洛伦兹度量或规范中性空间上的半直扩张为典型模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究Levi-Civita联络的对称部分$U$在伪黎曼李代数上的结合性条件，并对比其在黎曼与伪黎曼两种设定下的几何与代数约束，以揭示该条件对度量结构与测地完备性的影响。

Method: 在伪黎曼李代数 $(\mathfrak{g}, \langle \cdot, \cdot \rangle)$ 上，分析 $U$ 的张量结合性（associativity of $U$），并引入幺模性（unimodular）子类；结合代数与微分几何框架，对2步幂零和几乎阿贝尔李代数进行结构分类。

Result: 在黎曼（正定）情形下，$U$ 的结合性迫使其张量恒为零，从而恢复为双不变度量类。在伪黎曼结合幺模情形下，每个具有左不变伪黎曼度量的连通李群都是测地完备的。对于几乎阿贝尔李代数，获得了刚性结构分类，典型模型为三维海森堡代数配备特定（反）洛伦兹度量，或规范中性空间 $W \oplus W^*$ 上的半直扩张。

Conclusion: $U$ 的结合性在黎曼与伪黎曼两种设定下表现出根本差异：前者极端受限进而退化，后者则与非退化度量结构及测地完备性紧密关联；对特定李代数子类的分类结果揭示了该条件的刚性约束力。

Abstract: This paper investigates the algebraic and geometric consequences of the associativity of the symmetric part $U$ of the Levi-Civita connection on a pseudo-Riemannian Lie algebra $(\mathfrak{g}, \langle \cdot, \cdot \rangle)$. We demonstrate that in the Riemannian (positive-definite) setting, the associativity of $U$ is an extremely restrictive condition that forces the tensor to vanish identically, thereby recovering the class of bi-invariant metrics. In contrast, in the pseudo-Riemannian setting, we focus on the subclass where $(\mathfrak{g}, U)$ is associative and unimodular. As a primary result, we establish that every connected Lie group endowed with a left-invariant pseudo-Riemannian metric whose $U$-tensor is associative and unimodular is geodesically complete. Finally, we explore the families of 2-step nilpotent and almost-abelian Lie algebras. For the latter, we obtain some rigid structural classifications, showing that the paradigmatic models are the $3$-dimensional Heisenberg algebra with certain (anti)-Lorentzian metrics or a semi-direct extension involving a nondegenerate infinitesimal $β$-transformation on the canonical neutral space $W \oplus W^*$.

</details>


### [239] [Poincaré-Einstein 4-manifolds with cusps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25462)
*Mingyang Li,Hongyi Liu*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文在四维彭加莱–爱因斯坦（Poincaré-Einstein）流形上构造了多种尖端（cusp）结构，包括两类具有不同渐近行为的无穷族爱因斯坦（Einstein）度量，其万有覆盖给出$\mathbb{R}^4$上全新的完备负爱因斯坦度量，并由此否定了Anderson关于彭加莱–爱因斯坦四维流形尖端形成的一个问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通过构造具有多种尖端结构的庞加莱–爱因斯坦四维流形，探索爱因斯坦度量的几何与退化现象，并检验Anderson关于尖端形成问题的猜想。

Method: 在两类拓扑不同的底空间上构造无穷族爱因斯坦度量：一类以$(0,\infty)\times \mathscr{N}$为流形，其中$\mathscr{N}\to T^2$是环面上的主$\mathbb{S}^1$丛；另一类以$(0,\infty)\times P$为流形，其中$P\to Σ_{\mathtt{g}}$是亏格$\mathtt{g}\geq 2$的闭黎曼曲面（Riemann surface）上的主$\mathbb{S}^1$丛。两类度量均有一个庞加莱–爱因斯坦端和一个渐近于双曲尖端的端。

Result: 构造出的度量在万有覆盖（universal cover）下给出$\mathbb{R}^4$上新的完备负爱因斯坦度量，并且这些度量展现出有趣的退化（degeneration）现象，最终否定了Anderson关于四维庞加莱–爱因斯坦流形尖端形成的一个问题。

Conclusion: 本文构造了一类新的庞加莱–爱因斯坦四维流形及其尖端结构，提供了针对Anderson问题的反例，揭示了此类流形在尖端形成方面的更多可能性。

Abstract: In this paper, we construct Poincaré-Einstein 4-manifolds with various kinds of cusps. In particular, we construct:
  (1) Infinite families of Einstein metrics on $(0,\infty)\times \mathscr{N}$, where $\mathscr{N}\to T^2$ is a principal $\mathbb{S}^1$-bundle over $T^2$, with one Poincaré-Einstein end and one end asymptotic to a real or complex hyperbolic cusp.
  (2) Infinite families of Einstein metrics on $(0,\infty)\times P$, where $P\to Σ_{\mathtt{g}}$ is a principal $\mathbb{S}^1$-bundle over a closed Riemann surface $Σ_{\mathtt{g}}$ of genus $\mathtt{g}\geq 2$, with one Poincaré-Einstein end and one end asymptotic to a bundle of two-dimensional hyperbolic cusps over hyperbolic $Σ_{\mathtt{g}}$.
  Universal covers of (1) and (2) provide new complete negative Einstein metrics on $\mathbb{R}^4$. These Einstein metrics also exhibit interesting degeneration phenomena. With this construction, we give a negative answer to a question of Anderson concerning cusp formation for Poincaré-Einstein 4-manifolds.

</details>

### [240] [Physical Coherence and Time's Emergence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24970)
*Eugene Y. S. Chua*

Main category: physics.hist-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了“物理相干性判据”（criterion of physical coherence），用以评估量子引力中时间从无时间性（timelessness）中涌现的方案，并将其应用于半经典时间（semiclassical time）和热时间（thermal time）两个研究纲领，挑战支持时间涌现的学者澄清其概念基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在量子引力（quantum gravity）中，时间常被视为根本性缺失的，部分研究纲领试图在非基础层面上推导时间的涌现（emergence）。作者希望提供一种评估这类纲领是否成功的标准，而非像某些形而上学论证那样先验地否定时间涌现的可能性。

Method: 作者提出了“物理相干性判据”，并将其应用于两个具体研究纲领——半经典时间和热时间，依据Chua与Callender（2021）以及Chua（2025）的近期工作进行分析。该判据不同于自上而下、预先固定形而上学定义的做法，而是保留各纲领在其自身框架内成功的可能性。

Result: 物理相干性判据并不先验地排除所有时间涌现主张，而是为不同纲领的成功与否设定了检验标准。将其应用于半经典时间和热时间后，表明这些纲领在概念基础层面仍有待澄清。

Conclusion: 物理相干性判据为时间涌现的支持者设立了概念澄清的挑战，同时也作为判别纲领是否成功的试金石（litmus test），从而在量子引力中时间涌现的讨论中留出了更开放的理论空间。

Abstract: It is often said that time vanishes in quantum gravity. One general approach to quantum gravity accepts this fundamental timelessness but seeks to derive time's emergence at a non-fundamental level. To better assess such approaches, I develop the criterion of physical coherence and situate it in context by applying it to two programs for time's emergence, drawing from recent works by Chua and Callender (2021) and Chua (2025): semiclassical time and thermal time. Unlike some recent arguments for the metaphysical incoherence of time's emergence, which rule out all claims of time's emergence 'from on high' once we've fixed a definition of metaphysical emergence, my criterion of physical coherence leaves open the possibility that some programs in quantum gravity may succeed on their own terms in providing a physically coherent derivation of time from no-time. This sets a challenge for proponents of time's emergence to clarify the conceptual foundations of their program, while at the same time acting as a litmus test for a program's success.

</details>

### [242] [GDP-Driven Structural and Dynamical Heterogeneity in the Synchronization of Chaotic Macroeconomic Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21806)
*Thierry Njougouo,Fernando Fagundes Ferreira,Diego Garlaschelli*

Main category: nlin.AO

TL;DR: 本文研究了耦合混沌宏观经济系统的同步化涌现现象。每个节点代表一个经济体，包含储蓄、GDP和外国资本流入三个关键变量；经济体通过基于潜在GDP的适应度概率相互连接。通过数值模拟和平均场（mean-field）近似，分析了耦合强度和异质性（包括网络拓扑与节点动力学）对同步转变的影响。结果表明，平均场方法在均匀全连接网络中有效，但在强结构异质性网络中失效；异质网络中出现部分同步和开-关间歇（on–off intermittency），而层流相持续时间分布符合幂律标度，暗示全球经济周期同步具有内在脆弱性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究较少在统一框架下同时考虑结构异质性（网络连接不均匀性）和动力学异质性（局部参数差异）对宏观经济同步行为的影响。本文旨在填补这一空白，揭示耦合混沌宏观经济系统在网络异质性条件下的同步转变机制。

Method: 构建以储蓄、GDP和外国资本流入为变量的混沌宏观经济节点网络，节点间连接基于潜在GDP的适应度概率；采用数值模拟与平均场近似两种方法，通过改变耦合强度和网络拓扑及节点动力学的异质性程度来分析同步转变。

Result: 平均场方法在均匀全连接网络中能准确描述集体动力学，即使节点内在动力学存在异质性；但在网络结构异质性较强时失效。异质网络中系统表现为部分同步和开-关间歇，即全局同步的相干阶段与突发去同步爆发交替出现，层流相持续时间呈幂律分布。

Conclusion: 全球经济周期同步具有内在脆弱性：强整合虽能促进经济体间的暂时协调，但结构性和动力学差异不可避免地导致集体行为的间歇性崩溃。

Abstract: We investigate the emergence of synchronization in a network of coupled chaotic macroeconomic systems. Each node represents an economy characterized by three key variables savings, gross domestic product (GDP), and foreign capital inflows. These economies interact or are connected through a fitness-based probability that depends on the potential GDP of each node. This formulation allows both structural heterogeneity, arising from uneven network connectivity, and dynamical heterogeneity, due to differences in local parameters, to be explored within a unified framework. Using both numerical simulations and a mean-field approximation, by varying the coupling strength and the degree of heterogeneity of both network topology and dynamical behavior of the nodes, we analyze synchronization transitions. Our results show that the mean-field approach accurately captures the collective dynamics in homogeneous and fully connected networks even with heterogeneity within the intrinsic dynamic of the nodes but fails when strong heterogeneity in the structure of the network is introduced. In heterogeneous networks, the system exhibits partial synchronization and on--off intermittency, where coherent phases of global synchronization alternate with abrupt desynchronization bursts. The distribution of laminar phase durations follows a power-law scaling, consistent with theoretical predictions for intermittent synchronization. From an economic perspective, these results suggest that global business cycle synchronization is inherently fragile: strong integration can promote temporary coordination among economies, but structural and dynamical disparities inevitably lead to intermittent breakdowns of collective behavior.

### [243] [Memory Uncertainty Relation and Harmonic Memory in Random Recurrent Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24628)
*Taichi Haruna,Kohei Nakajima*

Main category: nlin.AO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种下界约束动力系统短期记忆能力的不等式，可被解释为短期记忆度量与输入信号引起的状态涨落大小度量之间的不确定关系（uncertainty relation），并在多种储层系统（reservoir systems）中进行了理论与数值验证。研究发现，在状态空间正则化（state-space regularization）下，输入噪声可诱导出额外记忆（noise-induced memory），且此时记忆不确定关系不再普遍成立。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动力系统的短期记忆能力是储层计算（reservoir computing）等领域的核心问题，但现有理论缺乏对记忆能力下限的严格刻画，尤其缺乏将记忆与状态涨落联系起来的统一框架。本文旨在建立一种不确定性关系，从理论上界定短期记忆的下界，并探讨输入噪声和正则化对其的影响。

Method: 作者提出了一个不等式，从理论上给出了动力系统短期记忆能力的下界，并将其解释为短期记忆度量与输入信号引起的状态涨落大小度量之间的不确定关系。该下界可通过特定的读出权重（readout weight）实现，被定义为次优记忆（suboptimal memory），称为谐波记忆（harmonic memory）。随后，在多种存在输入噪声的储层系统中，对不等式进行了解析和数值验证。

Result: 数值与解析分析展示了三种情况：不等式严格取等、渐近取等以及严格不等式的情形。在状态空间正则化下，一定的输入噪声强度可诱导出额外记忆（noise-induced memory）。此外，记忆不确定关系对于正则化后的记忆和谐波记忆并不普遍成立。

Conclusion: 本文建立的记忆不确定关系为理解动力系统的短期记忆能力提供了一个新视角。状态空间正则化下的噪声诱导记忆揭示了一种反直觉的机制，即噪声在一定条件下反而有助于提升记忆能力，这一发现挑战了不确定关系在正则化条件下的普适性。

Abstract: We present an inequality that bounds the short-term memory capability of dynamical systems from below. It can be interpreted as an uncertainty relation between a measure of short-term memory and that of the size of state fluctuations induced by input signals. The lower bound can be achieved by a readout weight and thus represents a suboptimal memory called harmonic memory. We examine analytically and numerically the inequality in a number of reservoir systems subject to input noise. We illustrate cases in which equality is achieved exactly, equality holds asymptotically, and the inequality is strict. We also study the effect of a state-space regularization to elucidate the inequality in terms of the fluctuation structure of the state-space. We find that a certain strength of input noise induces extra memory under the regularization, and we refer to this phenomenon as noise-induced memory. We observe that the memory uncertainty relation does not hold in general for the regularized memory and harmonic memory. This fact is explained in terms of the mechanism of noise-induced memory.

</details>


### [244] [Self-consistent analysis of the Kuramoto model with higher-order interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24701)
*Chanin Kumpeerakij,Juan G. Restrepo*

Main category: nlin.AO

TL;DR: 针对高阶相互作用Kuramoto模型，提出一种自洽分析框架，引入广义局域序参量以捕捉二元与三元相位关联，推导同步与双稳态临界条件，并在有限超图与频率实现下验证理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有解析方法依赖全连接耦合或平均场近似，虽能描述热力学极限下的典型网络，但无法有效处理有限超图与振子频率实现带来的涨落效应。

Method: 引入广义局域序参量（generalized local order parameters）以联合刻画二元（dyadic）和三元（triadic）相位关联，推导局域与全局同步序参量的层级近似方案，据此确定同步启动与双稳态的临界耦合强度。

Result: 发现控制双稳态启动的临界三元耦合强度依赖于二元邻接矩阵特征向量与三元交互结构之间的关联；在均匀与非均匀超图上的数值模拟验证了理论的正确性，并展示了不同近似方案的适用区域。

Conclusion: 该自洽分析框架成功将Kuramoto模型的高阶相互作用分析从全连接或平均场假设拓展至有限超图场景，为理解高阶耦合网络中的集体动力学（collective dynamics）提供了更精确的理论工具。

Abstract: The Kuramoto model with higher-order interactions has recently been shown to exhibit bistability, explosive synchronization transitions, and rich collective dynamics. Existing analytical approaches, however, typically rely on all-to-all coupling or mean-field approximations of the underlying hypergraph structure. While these methods describe typical networks in the thermodynamic limit, they generally fail to capture the effects of finite hypergraph and oscillator frequency realizations. To address this limitation, we develop a self-consistent analytical framework for the Kuramoto model with dyadic and triadic interactions on hypergraphs. We introduce generalized local order parameters that capture the combined effects of dyadic and triadic phase correlations, and derive a hierarchy of approximation schemes for the local and global synchronization order parameters. Using these approximations, we determine critical coupling strengths for the onset of synchronization and bistability. In particular, we show that the critical triadic coupling strength governing the onset of bistability depends on correlations between the eigenvectors of the dyadic adjacency matrix and the triadic interaction structure. Numerical simulations on homogeneous and heterogeneous hypergraphs validate the theory and illustrate the distinct regimes of applicability of the approximation schemes.

### [245] [Towards terahertz excitons in hydrogenated graphene superlattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24027)

Abstract: Carbon nanostructures, such as nanotubes and graphene nanoribbons, exhibit unique electronic and optical properties that make them very promising candidates for terahertz components. However, carbon nanotube and nanoribbon monolithic on-chip integration is challenging because it may results in significant change of their intrinsic properties after an embedment into a substrate. We investigate with first principles theoretical methods the successful routes of such integration and calculate electronic and optical properties of the integrated structures -- two-dimensional graphene superlattices, where quasi-metallic and dielectric regions alternate by selective hydrogenation of graphene. It is shown that chemical engineering of the graphene surface can lead to strong and well-isolated excitonic absorption peaks in the far-infrared and possibly even terahertz frequencies.

### [246] [Radiation conduction in polaritonic nanowires](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24030)
*Livia C. McCormack,Mathieu Francoeur*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文基于涨落电动力学（fluctuational electrodynamics）的离散系统格林函数方法，预测了SiO2纳米线中声子极化激元（phonon polaritons）在近室温扩散区（diffusive regime）的辐射热导率，发现表面声子极化激元主导的贡献较小，而动力学理论（kinetic theory）与麦克斯韦方程联立预测的热导率高出近两个数量级，修正有效平均自由程（effective mean free path）后部分改善但频谱分布仍不准确。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 声子极化激元被广泛视为抵消纳米结构中声子热导率降低（由边界散射增强引起）的重要途径，但目前实验数据有限，且缺乏预测固态系统中热电磁输运（thermal electromagnetic transport）的全波模型（full-wave models），阻碍了对声子极化激元介导导热的深入理解。

Method: 采用基于涨落电动力学（fluctuational electrodynamics）的离散系统格林函数方法（discrete system Green's function method），预测SiO2纳米线在近室温下扩散区的辐射热导率，并与基于动力学理论（kinetic theory）结合麦克斯韦方程导出的纳米线色散关系（dispersion relations）进行对比。

Result: 在400 K下，直径66 nm和132 nm的SiO2纳米线的辐射热导率分别为0.0264 W/m-K和0.0165 W/m-K，由表面声子极化激元（surface phonon polaritons）主导；而动力学理论预测值高出近两个数量级，且主要由在本体传播的体声子极化激元（bulk phonon polaritons）贡献。引入考虑Reststrahlen谱带外体声子极化激元平均自由程减少的有效平均自由程后，两者在总辐射热导率上的一致性有所改善，但频谱分布仍存在显著偏差。

Conclusion: 该工作为开发基于声子极化激元的微纳电子器件热管理系统奠定了理论基础，同时揭示了动力学理论在准确描述辐射热导率频谱分布方面的局限性。

Abstract: Phonon polaritons have attracted increasing interest as a means to offset the reduction in phonon thermal conductivity in nanostructures caused by enhanced boundary scattering. However, the interpretation of the limited experimental data on phonon polariton-mediated conduction is hindered by the lack of comprehensive full-wave models for predicting thermal electromagnetic transport in solid-state systems. Here, the radiative thermal conductivity in the diffusive regime along SiO2 nanowires near room temperature is predicted using the fluctuational electrodynamics-based discrete system Green's function method. At 400 K, for nanowire diameters of 66 nm and 132 nm, modest radiative conductivities of 0.0264 W/m-K and 0.0165 W/m-K, respectively, are obtained, with contributions dominated by surface phonon polaritons. In contrast, the kinetic theory combined with nanowire dispersion relations derived from Maxwell's equations predicts conductivities that can be nearly two orders of magnitude larger than those obtained from fluctuational electrodynamics, and are largely dominated by bulk phonon polaritons propagating within the nanowire volume. Improved agreement between the kinetic theory and fluctuational electrodynamics for the total radiative conductivity can be achieved by introducing an effective mean free path that accounts for the reduced mean free path of bulk phonon polaritons outside the Reststrahlen spectral bands of SiO2. However, even with this correction, the kinetic theory fails to accurately capture the spectral distribution of radiative conductivity. This work establishes a solid foundation for the development of phonon polariton-based systems for thermal management in micro/nanoelectronic devices.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用尖端诱导脱氢（tip-induced dehydrogenation）对选定的碳原子进行脱氢或氢钝化处理；采用双电离势运动方程耦合簇单双激发方法（double ionization potential equation-of-motion coupled-cluster singles and doubles，DIP-EOM-CCSD）精确计算单重态-三重态能隙（singlet-triplet gaps），该能隙直接对应交换耦合 $J$。

Result: 三角烯（triangulene）二聚体中脱氢（或氢钝化）位点的位置强烈调制单重态-三重态分裂（singlet-triplet splitting），使得 $J$ 的调控范围覆盖从几毫电子伏特（meV）到数十毫电子伏特。

Conclusion: 该策略提供了一种简单而强大的途径，用于设计具有交替或空间图案化自旋交换耦合（spin-exchange couplings）的定制自旋模型（tailored spin models）。

Abstract: We demonstrate that the effective spin-exchange coupling $J$ in open-shell nanographene dimers can be precisely tuned via tip-induced dehydrogenation of selected carbon atoms. Using the double ionization potential equation-of-motion coupled-cluster singles and doubles (DIP-EOM-CCSD) method, we accurately compute the singlet-triplet gaps, which correspond directly to the exchange coupling $J$. We show that the position of the dehydrogenated (or hydrogen-passivated) site in triangulene dimers strongly modulates the singlet-triplet splitting, allowing $J$ to be tuned over a wide range - from a few meV to several tens of meV. This strategy provides a simple yet powerful route for designing tailored spin models with alternating or spatially patterned spin-exchange couplings.

### [248] [Electrostatically stabilized surface flat bands in rhombohedral graphite at zero displacement field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24080)
*Kryštof Kolář,Andrea F. Young,Cyprian Lewandowski*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究表明，菱面体（ABC堆叠）多层石墨烯中，即使在无位移场条件下，自洽非线性静电学机制也能使表面能带平坦化并增强态密度。在强耦合极限下，该系统趋于均匀半填充，产生渐近平坦的表面能带；在真实相互作用强度下，可通过近端栅极调控平坦程度。研究结合解析分析与自洽计算，描绘了低场区域，并建立了连接有限层样品中对称破缺相的分析框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 菱面体多层石墨烯在强位移场下由表面平带（surface flat bands）驱动产生相互作用诱导相。然而，厚层样品中的强屏蔽会抑制内电场，使得同一实验范式下能否达到平带区域成为开放问题。

Method: 采用自洽非线性静电学理论（self-consistent nonlinear electrostatics）进行解析论证，并结合基于实际模型的全自洽计算（fully self-consistent calculations），分析近表面势场的非均匀分布对表面能带色散和态密度（density of states）的影响。

Result: 在强耦合极限下，静电学驱动系统在每个动量点趋于均匀半填充（uniform half-filling），无需栅极即可实现渐近平坦表面能带。在真实相互作用强度下，表面平带平坦度可通过近端栅极（proximal gate）调控，当能带为空且在空穴掺杂（hole doping）时达到最大平坦度。研究绘制了低场区域，并与有限层（N≈6–15）样品中的对称破缺相（symmetry-broken phases）建立了联系。

Conclusion: 结果为分析菱面体多层石墨烯中观察到的对称破缺相提供了理论框架，激励未来在大层数器件中进行实验探索，并确立了一个用于研究静电诱导平带物理（electrostatically induced flat-band physics）的低场区域。

Abstract: Rhombohedral (ABC-stacked) multilayer graphene hosts interaction-driven phases enabled by surface flat bands at large displacement fields. In thick flakes, however, strong screening suppresses internal electric fields, raising the question of whether a flat-band regime is accessible within the same experimental paradigm. Here, we show that self-consistent, nonlinear electrostatics provides a robust alternative mechanism: even in the absence of a displacement field, a nonuniform near-surface potential flattens the surface-band dispersion and enhances the density of states. In the strong-coupling limit, electrostatics drives the system toward uniform half-filling at each momentum, yielding an asymptotically flat surface band without any gating. At realistic interaction strengths, surface-band flatness is tuned by the proximal gate, with maximal flatness achieved at hole doping when the band is empty. Combining analytic arguments with fully self-consistent calculations in a realistic model, we map the resulting low-field regime and connect to finite $N\!\sim\! 6-15$ layered samples, providing a framework for analyzing the symmetry-broken phases observed in these systems. Our results motivate future experiments in large-$N$ devices and establish a low-field regime for exploring electrostatically induced flat-band physics.

Abstract: The thermal Hall effect has emerged as a fundamental tool for probing exotic quasiparticles and topological order, particularly in magnetic insulators where electronic conduction is suppressed. Although the effect is a well-established experimental phenomenon, current research points toward the existence of its quantum analogue: the quantized thermal Hall effect. In this paper, we provide a theoretical framework for this quantum version based on Sommerfeld's flux quantization. Furthermore, we demonstrate the potential existence of dissipationless thermal current vortices. Method: 利用拉盖尔-高斯脉冲（Laguerre-Gaussian pulses）的光学磁场空间结构直接印刻非共线磁纹理，并通过微磁学模拟（micromagnetic simulations）验证其效果，同时分析光学拓扑性质（optical topological properties）与偏振（polarization）对拓扑荷密度（topological charge density）的控制能力。

Abstract: Structured light has become a practical tool for controlling matter by applying tailored, space- and time-dependent electromagnetic fields. We show that Laguerre-Gaussian pulses imprint non-collinear magnetic textures via the spatial structure of optical magnetic field. Our route offers a direct spatial selectivity determined by the optical features without relying on material anisotropic interactions. The proposed printing approach does not require interfacial anisotropy or bulk chirality, current-driven torques, or thermal quenching. We use micromagnetic simulations to demonstrate the potential to create topological charge density emerging during the pulse and reveal control through the optical topological properties and polarization. These results suggest structured-light quantum printing as a viable approach for magnonics and motivate studies toward reconfigurable topological textures enabled by ultrafast THz optics and non-thermal control.

### [251] [High-fidelity EDSR in Si/SiGe Wiggle Wells](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24790)
*Hudaiba Soomro,Minyoung Kim,Avani Vivrekar,M. A. Eriksson,Benjamin D. Woods,Mark Friesen*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文系统分析了合金无序（alloy disorder）对基于长周期Wiggle Well的Si/SiGe量子阱中电偶极自旋共振（EDSR）的影响，发现无序会通过谷相位（valley phase）随机化Rabi频率，同时诱导新的Rabi驱动机制，尽管存在退相位风险，但通过识别“甜点”（sweet spots）仍可实现高保真度Rabi振荡，表明Wiggle Well是无微磁体量子门操作的有前景平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前人发现Wiggle Well可增强Dresselhaus自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling, SOC），有利于基于EDSR的自旋量子比特操作，但随机合金无序对谷物理（valley physics）的影响尚未在EDSR分析中被充分考虑，因此需要系统评估合金无序如何影响EDSR性能。

Method: 本文通过理论分析研究合金无序对Si/SiGe量子阱中EDSR的影响，重点考察无序引起的谷相位（valley phase）$φ_{s,s}$的空间随机化，以及由此产生的Rabi频率变化和新驱动机制；同时通过识别“甜点”区域评估高保真度Rabi振荡的可行性。

Result: 合金无序通过两种途径影响EDSR：(1) Rabi频率$Ω$依赖谷相位$\cosφ_{s,s}$，导致其空间随机化，但在多数位置仍可实现快速EDSR；(2) 无序与谷态杂化（hybridization）诱导的谷偶极子（valley dipole）产生新的Rabi驱动机制，在低谷劈裂（low valley splitting）区域占主导。无序可增强EDSR，但也会产生$Ω$梯度导致旋转框架中的退相位（dephasing）。通过识别甜点，可在存在实际电荷噪声（charge noise）时实现高保真度Rabi振荡。

Conclusion: Wiggle Well是无需外部微磁体的高质量量子门操作的有前景平台，合金无序虽带来挑战，但可通过甜点策略加以控制。

Abstract: Si/SiGe quantum wells that incorporate Ge concentration oscillations, known as long-period Wiggle Wells, have previously been shown to enhance the Dresselhaus spin-orbit coupling (SOC) of conduction-band electrons. Such intrinsic SOC is desirable when performing spin-qubit gate operations based on electric dipole spin resonance (EDSR) because it eliminates the need for external micromagnets. However, random-alloy disorder plays a key role in the valley physics of this materials system by spatially randomizing the valley phase $φ_{s,s}$, and has not been fully accounted for in recent EDSR analyses. Here, we show that alloy disorder affects EDSR in two main ways. First, the Rabi frequency $Ω$ acquires a dependence on the valley phase, given by $\cosφ_{s,s}$, which causes spatial randomization of $Ω$. Despite this variability, we show that fast EDSR can be achieved at most locations across a given sample. Second, a new Rabi driving mechanism emerges, enabled by valley dipoles that result from disorder and the hybridization of ground and excited valley states in response to an EDSR driving field. This mechanism is dominant in regions of low valley splitting. Alloy disorder can therefore strengthen EDSR, but it can also cause gradients in $Ω$ that lead to dephasing in the rotating frame. We explore this problem by first identifying "sweet spots," where EDSR is relatively insensitive to electric-field fluctuations. We then show that high-fidelity Rabi oscillations can be achieved in the presence of realistic charge noise. Our results demonstrate that the Wiggle Well is a promising platform for high-quality, micromagnet-free gate operations.

*Rachid El Aitouni,Hasna Chnafa,Clarence Cortes,David Laroze,Ahmed Jellal*

Result: 应变可重塑电子色散并强烈改变输运特性；透射率和电导表现出由量子干涉（quantum interference）和共振隧穿（resonant tunneling）驱动的显著振荡行为；自旋极化和谷极化均随应变、势垒高度及入射能量发生大幅且高度可控的变化。

Abstract: We present a comprehensive theoretical study of strain-engineered quantum transport in monolayer tungsten diselenide (WSe$_2$) in the presence of an electrostatic scalar potential. By incorporating strain effects within a low-energy Dirac framework, we analyze their impact on spin- and valley-resolved transmission, conductance, and polarization. The applied potential barrier partitions the system into three distinct regions, allowing for an analytical derivation of the wave functions in each domain. Enforcing continuity conditions at the interfaces yields exact expressions for the transmission and reflection amplitudes. The transmission probability is evaluated from the corresponding current densities, while the conductance is obtained using the Landauer-Büttiker formalism, enabling a quantitative determination of spin and valley polarizations. Our numerical analysis reveals that strain acts as a powerful tuning parameter that reshapes the electronic dispersion and strongly modifies transport characteristics. In particular, the transmission and conductance exhibit pronounced oscillatory behavior driven by quantum interference and resonant tunneling mechanisms. More importantly, both spin and valley polarizations display substantial and highly controllable variations as functions of strain, barrier height, and incident energy. These results demonstrate that strain and electrostatic engineering provide an efficient and versatile platform for manipulating spin-valley degrees of freedom in WSe$_2$. The ability to tailor polarization and interference effects suggests promising opportunities for the design of next-generation spintronic, valleytronic, and optoelectronic devices based on two-dimensional transition-metal dichalcogenides.

Motivation: 探索翘曲二维狄拉克材料中轨道霍尔（orbital Hall）效应的可控性及其与多种电子相（如量子自旋霍尔、谷霍尔、反常霍尔相）之间的关联，旨在建立轨道霍尔响应作为能带拓扑探测工具的理论基础。

Method: 采用包含反铁磁交换场（antiferromagnetic exchange field）、垂直电场（perpendicular electric field）和本征自旋-轨道耦合（intrinsic spin-orbit coupling）的统一框架，基于低能大质量狄拉克模型（massive Dirac model）和贝里曲率（Berry curvature）线性响应理论（linear response theory）进行计算分析。

Result: 轨道霍尔电导率（orbital Hall conductivity）在能带反转点附近显著增强；通过调节外场可依次实现量子自旋霍尔（quantum spin Hall）、谷霍尔（valley Hall）和反常霍尔（anomalous Hall）等多个电子相；轨道响应的演化受贝里曲率在自旋与谷自由度之间再分配的控制；有限温度下响应幅度因热展宽而抑制，但相依赖特征保持稳健。

Conclusion: 轨道霍尔电导率可作为狄拉克系统中灵敏的能带拓扑探针（band topology probe），而翘曲二维材料为轨道电子学（orbitronics）中可调轨道电流的工程化设计提供了灵活的平台。

Abstract: We study the orbital Hall response in buckled two-dimensional Dirac materials using a unified framework that includes an antiferromagnetic exchange field, a perpendicular electric field, and intrinsic spin-orbit coupling. We show that the orbital Hall conductivity is considerably boosted around band-inversion points and shows different signatures across multiple electronic phases using a low-energy massive Dirac model in conjunction with Berry-curvature-based linear response theory. We find a series of quantum spin Hall, valley Hall, and anomalous Hall regimes by methodically adjusting external fields, and demonstrate how the evolution of the orbital response is controlled by the redistribution of Berry curvature between spin and valley sectors. We examine the impacts of finite temperature in more detail and find that although the response s size is suppressed by thermal broadening, the distinctive phase-dependent features remain robust. Our findings demonstrate that orbital Hall conductivity offers a sensitive band topology probe in Dirac systems and emphasize buckled two-dimensional materials as a flexible platform for engineering tunable orbital currents for orbitronic applications.

</details>


### [255] [Non-Hermitian Twisting Theory under the open boundary condition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25386)
*Chen-Hao Zhao,Jia-Rui Li,Yuping Tian,Wei-Jiang Gong*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出基于局部缩放变换（LST）的非厄米（non-Hermitian）局域理论，引入局部扭曲量 $T_n$ 和度规算符 $\xi$，定义了Zahlen-Brillouin Zone（ZBZ）以将非厄米能带理论推广至非周期与无序晶格，并建立了度规-态对应（MSC）作为实空间局域化的统一原理，为晶体和非晶介质中的非厄米物理提供了普适范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非厄米趋肤效应（non-Hermitian skin effect, NHSE）的广义布里渊区（generalized Brillouin zone, GBZ）描述仅适用于周期系统，缺乏能够处理非周期和无序晶格的一般性理论框架。

Method: 通过局部缩放变换（local scaling transformation, LST）引入位点分辨的局部扭曲量 $T_n$，用以量化度规算符（metric operator）$\xi$ 的非平凡性；利用 $T_n$ 的平移无关性定义Zahlen-Brillouin Zone（ZBZ）；将 $\xi$ 与GBZ的黎曼几何（Riemannian geometry）统一，建立度规-态对应（metric and state correspondence, MSC）并定义全局趋肤指数（global skin index）$\mathbf{\Gamma}$。

Result: 阐明了NHSE的起源，揭示了广义多通道趋肤效应（multiple-channel skin effect, MCSE）；将非厄米能带理论推广至非周期和无序晶格；建立了实空间局域化的度规-态对应原理；以全局趋肤指数 $\mathbf{\Gamma}$ 描述相变。

Conclusion: 该工作为晶体和非晶介质中的非厄米物理提供了普适范式，拓展了非厄米趋肤效应理论的应用范围。

Abstract: The non-Hermitian skin effect (NHSE) is a hallmark of non-Hermitian system, yet its generalized Brillouin zone (GBZ) description is restricted to periodic systems. We develop a site-resolved theory via a local scaling transformation (LST), introducing local twisting $T_n$ to quantify metric operator $ξ$ nontriviality. This elucidates the NHSE's origin and uncovers the generalized multiple-channel skin effect (MCSE). Exploiting $T_n$'s translational independence, we define the Zahlen-Brillouin Zone (ZBZ), extending non-Hermitian band theory to nonperiodic and disordered lattices. Furthermore, we unify the $ξ$ with GBZ Riemannian geometry, establishing the metric and state correspondence (MSC) as the principle for real-space localization. With a global skin index $\mathbfΓ$ for phase transitions, our results provide a universal paradigm for non-Hermitian physics in both crystalline and amorphous media.

</details>


### [256] [Microfluidic Actuation by Einstein-de Haas Spin Torque](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25387)
*Xin Hu,Mamoru Matsuo*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出通过自旋电流（spin current）微流体驱动密封液态金属（liquid metal）的新方法。利用铂（Pt）触点注入的自旋角动量，通过爱因斯坦-德哈斯转矩（Einstein-de Haas torque）和微极角动量平衡（micropolar angular-momentum balance）转化为粘性流动，无需压力驱动、移动壁面、磁场、洛伦兹力或电荷流经液体。实验测得直流速度遵循普适的自旋扩散标度律，有限频率的自旋-机械导纳则揭示了液态金属通道中的粘性动量扩散、自旋输运、微旋转弛豫及界面透明度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统微流体驱动通常依赖压力梯度、机械移动部件或外加电磁场，这些方法在密封系统或对电荷流动敏感的场景中面临局限。本文旨在探索一种全新的驱动机制，即利用纯自旋角动量注入来驱动液态金属流动，避免电荷流动或外部场作用，从而实现更灵活的微流体控制。

Method: 从铂（Pt）触点向密封的液态金属注入自旋角动量，该角动量以爱因斯坦-德哈斯转矩（Einstein-de Haas torque）形式进入液体，并通过微极角动量平衡（micropolar angular-momentum balance）转换为粘性流动。实验测量了直流速度的频率响应，并通过有限频率自旋-机械导纳（spin-mechanical admittance）分析粘性动量扩散与自旋动力学。

Result: 直流速度表现出普适的自旋扩散标度律（spin-diffusion scaling）；有限频率下的自旋-机械导纳成功分辨出粘性动量扩散（viscous momentum diffusion）、自旋输运（spin transport）、微旋转弛豫（microrotation relaxation）以及液态金属通道的界面透明度（interface transparency）。

Conclusion: 本文证明了一种无需压力驱动、移动壁面、磁场或电荷流动的全新液态金属驱动方式，为自旋电子学（spintronics）与微流体力学（microfluidics）的交叉提供了实验基础，并展示了通过自旋注入控制微流体流动的可行性。

Abstract: We propose spin-current microfluidic actuation of a sealed liquid metal. Spin angular momentum injected from Pt contacts enters the liquid as an Einstein-de Haas torque and is converted through micropolar angular-momentum balance into viscous flow without pressure drive, moving walls, magnetic fields, Lorentz forces, or charge flow through the liquid. The dc velocity obeys universal spin-diffusion scaling, and the finite-frequency spin-mechanical admittance resolves viscous momentum diffusion, spin transport, microrotation relaxation, and interface transparency of the liquid-metal channel.

</details>


### [257] [AI-Driven SERS for Non-invasive and Label-Free Extracellular Vesicle Detection Across Cellular Origins in Tears and Sweat](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25465)
*Yang Li,Xiaoming Lyu,Ling Xia,Kuo Zhan,Haoyu Ji,Lei Qin,Seppo J. Vainio,Jian-An Huang*

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种基于AI辅助的表面增强拉曼光谱（SERS）方法，利用盐诱导纳米颗粒聚集实现泪液和汗液中细胞外囊泡（EVs）的无标记、快速、高准确率识别，准确率超过92%，为临床疾病的快速诊断提供了新思路。

Method: 提出了一种基于盐诱导纳米颗粒聚集的人工智能（AI）辅助SERS方法，实现泪液和汗液中EVs的快速高准确率识别。利用分子动力学模拟（molecular dynamics simulations）揭示银原子（Ag）与蛋白质中多个氨基酸残基的氧原子之间形成静电相互作用，表明存在高亲和力。

Conclusion: 该策略实现了对EVs的超灵敏、抗干扰检测，为临床疾病的快速诊断提供了新思路。

Abstract: Wearable sensing technology capable of point-of-care, continuous and non-invasive analysis of exosomes in biofluid such as tears and sweat is an essential part for future personalized medicine. Major detection and identification methods of cell secreted Extracellular Vesicles (EVs) often require labeling and are time-consuming, resulting in low efficiency in EV mechanism research and disease diagnosis. While the label-free Surface-enhanced Raman spectroscopy (SERS) has been combined with deep learning model for EV identification in blood, their application to non-invasive detection of EVs in tears and sweat are missing. Here, we filled this gap by developing an artificial intelligence (AI)-assisted Surface-enhanced Raman spectroscopy (SERS) method based on salt-induced nanoparticle aggregation for fast EV identification in tears and sweat with high accuracy. Significantly, our label-free detection and AI differentiation of EVs from 6 cell lines (HepG2, Hela, 143B, LO-2, BMSC, H8) achieved the identification of EVs in tear fluids from 7 different disease sources with accuracies >92%. Our results showed that this platform can not only distinguish EVs from multiple cell sources but also generate highly reproducible and selective EV signals in tear fluids without a need for chemical labeling or separation steps. Molecular dynamics simulations revealed that silver atoms (Ag) form electrostatic interactions with oxygen atoms of multiple amino acid residues in proteins, suggesting a high affinity. This strategy realizes ultra-sensitive and anti-interference detection of EVs, providing a new idea for the rapid diagnosis of clinical diseases.

### [258] [Topological fragility and bilinear magnetoelectric resistance in gapless edge states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25774)
*Cosimo Gorini,Matthieu Bard,Sophie Gueron,Hélène Bouchiat,Giovanni Vignale*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文揭示了时间反演对称系统中拓扑边缘态和铰链态的一种基本“拓扑脆弱性”：在施加中等外磁场时，自旋-动量锁定与随机自旋-轨道相互作用相结合会产生显著的双线性磁电电阻，其幅度远超二维系统，且无需能隙打开或复杂多体效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在时间反演对称（time-reversal symmetric）的拓扑绝缘体（topological insulators）和高阶拓扑绝缘体（higher-order topological insulators）中，一维自旋-动量锁定（spin-momentum locked）的边缘态和铰链态理论上为“完美导电”态，能够免疫非磁性无序的背散射。作者旨在检验并揭示这一理想图像在非线性输运条件下的脆弱性。

Method: 理论分析表明，该效应需要两个关键要素：(i) 自旋-动量锁定，它能在非线性（non-linear）输运 regime 中最大化时间反演对称性破缺（time-reversal symmetry breaking）；(ii) 随机自旋-轨道相互作用（random spin-orbit interaction），即重元素中 Elliott–Yafet 自旋弛豫（spin relaxation）的同一机制。两者结合在外磁场下产生稳健的背散射通道。

Result: 研究发现这些边缘态和铰链态表现出双线性磁电电阻（bilinear magnetoelectric resistance），其幅度显著大于二维系统。该机制无需能隙（gap）打开或复杂的多体效应（many-body effects），是一种简单且普适的效应。

Conclusion: 该理论定量解释了近期在铋（Bismuth）铰链态中观测到的实验现象，为非磁性无序下拓扑边缘态“完美导电”这一理想图像提供了关键的修正。

Abstract: In time-reversal symmetric systems such as topological and higher-order topological insulators, 1D spin-momentum locked edge and hinge states are theoretically ``perfectly conducting'', being immune to backscattering by non-magnetic disorder. Here, we reveal a fundamental ``topological fragility'': these states exhibit a bilinear magnetoelectric resistance significantly larger than in 2D systems. This effect requires two ingredients: (i) spin-momentum locking, which maximizes time-reversal symmetry breaking in the non-linear regime, and (ii) random spin-orbit interaction -- the same mechanism behind Elliott - Yafet spin relaxation in heavy elements. Together, these generate a robust backscattering channel when a modest external magnetic field is applied. Our theory requires no gap opening or complex many-body effects, offering a simple and general mechanism that quantitatively explains recent observations in Bismuth hinge states.

</details>


### [259] [Hybridization of Ferromagnetic and Cyclotron Resonances in a Two-Dimensional Electron System on a Ferromagnetic Film](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25839)
*A. A. Zabolotnykh,I. V. Zagorodnev,A. A. Matveev,D. A. Rodionov,O. Yu. Arkhipova,D. V. Kalyabin,A. R. Safin,S. A. Nikitov*

TL;DR: 该论文从理论上研究了置于介电铁磁薄膜上的二维电子系统在垂直静磁场中的微波响应，发现铁磁共振（ferromagnetic resonance）与回旋共振（cyclotron resonance）之间存在反交叉（anticrossing）现象，该区域不仅共振频率发生修正，共振线宽也发生显著变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索二维电子系统与铁磁薄膜在垂直静磁场中微波响应（microwave response）的耦合行为，特别是铁磁共振与回旋共振之间的相互作用。

Method: 采用理论分析方法，研究位于介电铁磁薄膜上的二维电子系统，整个体系置于垂直静磁场中，并置于导电金属（栅极）上。

Result: 发现铁磁共振与回旋共振在磁场中相互作用，导致共振频率相互排斥（反交叉现象）。反交叉区域不仅使共振频率相对于无铁磁衬底的二维系统和无二维系统的铁磁薄膜发生修正，还显著改变了共振线宽（resonance linewidth）。

Conclusion: 二维电子系统与铁磁薄膜之间的耦合可导致反交叉行为，同时影响共振频率和线宽，这为调控微波响应提供了物理机制。

Abstract: The microwave response of a two-dimensional (2D) electron system located on a dielectric ferromagnetic film, which in turn lies on a conducting metal (gate), has been theoretically studied. The entire system has been placed in the perpendicular static magnetic field. It has been found that the ferromagnetic resonance of the film and the cyclotron resonance of the electrons of the 2D system interact in the magnetic field, leading to their repulsion ('anticrossing'). It has been revealed that the anticrossing region is characterized not only by the modification of resonance frequencies compared to the cyclotron resonance in the 2D system without the ferromagnetic substrate and the ferromagnetic resonance in the film without the 2D system, but also by a strong change in the resonance linewidths.

</details>


### [260] [Observation of the Optical Phonons in α-MnTe films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26075)
*Himanshu Sheokand,Arun K Kumay,Mazharul Islam Mondal,Milo Sprague,Ravinder Sharma,Jayan Thomas,Dariusz Kaczorowski,Andrzej Ptok,Madhab Neupane*

TL;DR: 本文报道了在GaAs(111)B衬底上通过分子束外延（MBE）生长高质量α-MnTe薄膜，并结合拉曼光谱与第一性原理声子计算，完整解析了其全部对称性允许的拉曼活性声子模，表明外延α-MnTe是研究交变磁（altermagnetism）及其晶格耦合激发的可靠薄膜平台。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用分子束外延（molecular beam epitaxy, MBE）技术在GaAs(111)B衬底上生长α-MnTe薄膜，结合拉曼光谱（Raman spectroscopy）与第一性原理声子计算（first principles phonon calculations），对薄膜的生长演化与结构性质进行综合分析。

Result: 拉曼光谱观察到α-MnTe在121 cm⁻¹和140 cm⁻¹附近的多个振动特征，经第一性原理声子计算确认其为六方NiAs型晶格的拉曼活性声子模（Raman-active phonon modes）；高质量MBE生长实现了全部对称性允许的拉曼活性声子模的完整实验分辨。

Conclusion: 高质量MBE生长的α-MnTe薄膜能够完整分辨所有对称性允许的拉曼活性声子模，表明外延α-MnTe是研究交变磁（altermagnetism）及其晶格耦合激发的稳健薄膜平台。

Abstract: The altermagnetic materials have emerged as model systems for studying spin split electronic structures, yet controlled epitaxial growth on technologically relevant substrates remains challenging. Among the known candidates, MnTe stands out as a prominent altermagnetic material owing to its layered structure and high Neel temperature. Here, we report the molecular beam epitaxy (MBE) growth of high quality alpha MnTe thin films on GaAs(111)B substrates and provide a comprehensive analysis of the growth evolution and structural properties. Raman spectroscopy reveals multiple vibrational features of alpha MnTe including modes near 121, and 140 1/cm. Combined with first principles phonon calculations, these features are identified as the Raman-active phonons of the hexagonal NiAs type lattice. Our results show that the high crystalline quality of MBE grown alpha MnTe enables the complete experimental resolution of all symmetry allowed Raman active phonon modes, highlighting epitaxial alpha MnTe as a robust thin film platform for investigating altermagnetism and its lattice coupled excitations.

# math.AP [[Back]](#toc)

### [261] [New inverse problems for a time-switched system of wave and diffusion equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24189)
*E. T. Karimov,N. A. Murolimova*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究了一类时间切换系统中两种新的反问题，该系统在[0,a)区间由分数阶波动方程（Caputo导数阶数α∈(1,2)）主导，在(a,b]区间由分数阶扩散方程（关于切换点t=a的Caputo导数阶数β∈(0,1)）主导。通过谱展开法（spectral expansion method）将问题简化为耦合标量Cauchy问题的序列，推导了显式级数解，并建立了唯一性与存在性定理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索时间切换分数阶系统中两类新型反问题，其待定量分别为界面t=a处传输条件的不同未知部分；给出显式解的存在性、唯一性及正则性理论，为相关物理或工程系统的参数识别提供数学基础。

Method: 采用基于[0,1]上经典Sturm-Liouville本征系统的谱展开法，将每个反问题归约为涉及双参数Mittag-Leffler函数（two-parameter Mittag-Leffler function）的耦合标量Cauchy问题序列；利用Mittag-Leffler函数的衰减估计、分部积分、Cauchy-Schwarz不等式和Weierstrass M-判别法等工具，通过四个辅助引理建立无穷级数及其相关导数的一致收敛性。

Result: 推导了解u(t,x)及未知界面函数h(x)和\bar{h}(x)的显式级数表示；在数据满足显式Sobolev型正则性条件下，为问题1陈述了唯一性与存在性定理，并为问题2给出了类似结果。

Conclusion: 本文为时间切换分数阶系统中的两类反问题提供了完整的数学分析框架，包括解的显式构造和收敛性保障，并建立了相应适定性理论。

Abstract: We study two new classes of inverse problems for a time-switched system in which a fractional wave equation (with Caputo derivative of order $α\in (1,2)$) governs the dynamics on the interval $[0,a)$, and a fractional diffusion equation (with Caputo derivative of order $β\in (0,1)$ taken with respect to the switching point $t=a$) governs the dynamics on $(a,b]$. The two problems differ in which part of the transmitting condition at the interface $t=a$ is regarded as unknown. In both cases the overdetermination data consist of a single spatial measurement of the solution at a fixed time $ξ\in (a,b)$. Using the spectral expansion method with respect to the classical Sturm-Liouville eigensystem on $[0,1]$, we reduce each problem to a sequence of coupled scalar Cauchy problems involving the two-parameter Mittag-Leffler function. Explicit series representations for the solution $u(t,x)$ and the unknown interface functions $h(x)$ and $\bar{h}(x)$ are derived. Uniform convergence of the resulting infinite series and their relevant derivatives is established through four auxiliary lemmas, using the decay estimates for the Mittag-Leffler function, integration-by-parts arguments, the Cauchy--Schwarz inequality, and the Weierstrass $M$-test. A uniqueness and existence theorem is stated for Problem~1 under explicit Sobolev-type regularity conditions on the data, with an analogous result for Problem~2.

</details>

### [263] [On the asymptotics of ground states for a boundary value problem for the equation $-\varepsilon Δ_p u = a|u|^{q-2}u - b|u|^{γ-2}u$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24482)
*Yavdat Sh. Il'yasov,Elvira I. Turianova*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究了一类带竞争超线性项的p-拉普拉斯奇异摄动Dirichlet问题，通过非线性Rayleigh商方法引入两个临界参数值，证明了解的不存在性与多解性，并刻画了基态解在参数趋于零时的渐近行为，收敛至一个显式剖面函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解带竞争超线性项的p-拉普拉斯（p-Laplacian）奇异摄动Dirichlet问题的解结构，特别是当摄动参数ε很小时，多解的存在性、不存在性以及解族的渐近极限行为。

Method: 采用非线性Rayleigh商方法（nonlinear Rayleigh quotient method），引入两个临界参数值ε*和ε_e*，分别关联到Nehari流形（Nehari manifold）和零能量水平面（zero energy level）。

Result: 证明了当ε>ε*时无非平凡弱解；当0<ε<ε_e*时至少存在两个正弱解，其中一个是基态解（ground state）。当a≥σ_a>0时，正基态解族u_ε在Ω中依测度收敛到显式剖面ū_0(x)=(a(x)/b(x))^{1/(γ-q)}，并且在L^r(Ω)(1≤r<γ)中强收敛，在L^r(Ω)(1<r≤γ)中弱收敛。

Conclusion: 竞争超线性项与奇异摄动机制共同导致了临界阈值现象，基态解在ε→0^+时收敛到由系数比a(x)/b(x)决定的精确剖面，并呈现出不同L^r空间中的强弱收敛差异。

Abstract: We study a singularly perturbed Dirichlet problem for the $p$-Laplacian with competing superlinear terms, \[ -\varepsilon Δ_p u = a(x)|u|^{q-2}u - b(x)|u|^{γ-2}u, \qquad u|_{\partialΩ}=0, \] where $1<p<q<γ<p^*$, $a\geq 0$, $b\geqσ_b>0$, and $\varepsilon>0$ is small. By means of the nonlinear Rayleigh quotient method, we introduce two critical parameter values, $\varepsilon^*$ and $\varepsilon_e^*$, related respectively to the Nehari manifold and to the zero energy level. We prove the nonexistence of nontrivial weak solutions for $\varepsilon>\varepsilon^*$, and the existence of at least two positive weak solutions for $0<\varepsilon<\varepsilon_e^*$; one of them is a ground state. The main result describes the asymptotic behaviour of ground states as $\varepsilon\to 0^+$. If, in addition, $a\geqσ_a>0$, then every family of positive ground states $u_\varepsilon$ converges in measure in $Ω$ to the explicit profile \[ \bar u_0(x) = \left(\frac{a(x)}{b(x)}\right)^{1/(γ-q)}. \] Moreover, \[ u_\varepsilon\to\bar u_0 \quad\text{strongly in }L^r(Ω), \qquad 1\le r<γ, \] and \[ u_\varepsilon\rightharpoonup\bar u_0 \quad\text{weakly in }L^r(Ω), \qquad 1<r\leγ. \]

</details>


### [264] [On a class of sharp Sobolev type estimates with weights](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25637)
*Raul Hindov,Evgeniy Lokharu*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究了形如 ∫₀¹|u(x)|ρ(x)dx ≤ Λ(∫₀¹|u⁽ᵏ⁾(x)|²dx)^{1/2} 的尖锐加权Sobolev型不等式，其中 ρ 为非负权重。通过证明每个极小化子（minimizer）具有恒定符号且满足多调和型（polyharmonic type）非线性特征值问题，刻画了极小化子并确定了最优常数 Λ(k,ρ)。进一步给出了最优常数关于权重函数的显式计算，并由此恢复和推广了多个先前的尖锐估计与 Hardy 型不等式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 加权Sobolev型不等式是分析学中的基本工具，但此前尚缺乏对于权重为一般非负函数时最优常数与极小化子的系统刻画。本文旨在填补这一空白，建立一套统一的框架以明确极小化子的结构并显式计算最优常数。

Method: 通过证明极小化子具有恒定符号，将其归结为多调和型非线性特征值问题的解，从而建立最优常数 Λ(k,ρ) 与极小化子的显式联系。进一步利用该特征值问题的结构，推导出最优常数关于权重函数 ρ 的显式表达式。

Result: 对所有满足条件的非负权重 ρ，确定了最优常数 Λ(k,ρ) 的显式形式，并完全刻画了极小化子的符号性质与满足的方程。所得加权估计涵盖了有限区间上先前已知的多个尖锐 Sobolev 估计与 Hardy 型不等式。

Conclusion: 该工作为加权Sobolev型不等式提供了一个统一且显式的处理方法，所得结果在调和分析、偏微分方程与函数不等式理论中具有广泛的应用前景，并为相关极值问题的研究奠定了基础。

Abstract: We study sharp weighted Sobolev-type inequalities of the form
  \[
  \int_{0}^{1}|u(x)|ρ(x) \diff x
  \leqslant Λ
  \Bigl(\int_{0}^{1}|u^{(k)}(x)|^2 \diff x\Bigr)^{1/2},
  \qquad u\in H_0^k(0,1),
  \]
  where $ρ$ is a non-negative weight. We characterize the minimizers and
  identify the optimal constant $Λ(k,ρ)$ by showing that every minimizer has a constant sign and therefore solves a nonlinear eigenvalue problem of polyharmonic type. This yields an explicit characterization of extremizers for a broad class of weights. Moreover, we even provide with a an explicit computation of the optimal constant in terms of the weight function. The new weighted estimates turn to be very useful and, among other applications, allow us to recover several previous sharp estimates and Hardy type inequalities on finite intervals.

</details>


### [265] [Stability of dispersive boundary layers for scalar conservation laws in one space dimension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25853)
*Paolo Antonelli,Pierangelo Marcati,Laura V. Spinolo*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究半直线上KdV型初边值问题的零色散极限，针对出流机制（outflow regime）构造了由边界条件不匹配决定的边界层剖面（boundary layer profile），并通过加权能量范数中的定量估计证明了该边界层的稳定性，这是首个针对半直线上KdV型方程边界层的稳定性结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究半直线上KdV型初边值问题的零色散极限（zero-dispersion limit），特别是在出流机制下色散问题所施加的边界条件不被极限标量守恒律的解所满足时的边界层行为及其稳定性。

Method: 通过关联的定常三阶边界层方程（stationary third-order boundary layer equation），构造出依赖于快变量（fast variable）的边界层剖面；利用WKB展开（WKB expansion），将色散问题的解近似为守恒律的平滑解与边界层剖面之和；基于线性化能量泛函（linearized energy functional）的分析，对余项在加权能量范数中建立定量估计。

Result: 在数据满足适当正则性和相容性假设的条件下，色散解可由WKB展开良好近似，且边界层剖面在加权能量范数意义下稳定——余项在$H^1$中收敛到0，关于时间一致成立，且持续到守恒律平滑解的生命周期。

Conclusion: 该稳定性证明不依赖于完全可积性或反散射技术，适用于一般通量且不要求边界层振幅的小量假设，是半直线上KdV型方程边界层稳定性的首个结果。

Abstract: We study the zero-dispersion limit for a class of Korteweg--de Vries (KdV)-type initial-boundary value problems on the half-line, with Dirichlet boundary conditions assigned at \(x=0\). We focus on the outflow regime, where the solution of the limiting scalar conservation law does not attain the boundary condition imposed on the dispersive problem. We construct a boundary layer profile, depending on the fast variable, which is uniquely determined, through the associated stationary third-order boundary layer equation, by the mismatch between the boundary conditions, and by the exponential decay at infinity in the fast variable. Our main result shows that, under suitable regularity and compatibility assumptions on the data, the dispersive solution is well approximated by a WKB expansion given by the sum of the smooth solution of the conservation law and the boundary layer profile. In particular, we establish stability of the boundary layer profile by proving quantitative estimates for the remainder term in a weighted energy norm, and show that it converges to $0$ in $H^1$, uniformly in time and up to the lifespan of the smooth solution of the conservation law. The proof is based on the analysis of a linearized energy functional and does not rely on complete integrability or inverse scattering techniques. It applies to general fluxes and requires no smallness assumption on the amplitude of the boundary layer. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first stability result for boundary layers of KdV-type equation on the half line.

</details>


### [266] [From Bogoliubov-de Gennes to Ginzburg-Landau: Critical Points Near $T_{\rm c}$ in the Non-Magnetic Case](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26008)
*Rupert L. Frank,Christian Hainzl,Dong Hao Ou Yang*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究了无外场BCS模型中Bogoliubov-de Gennes方程与Ginzburg-Landau方程之间的关系，证明了在临界温度附近，BdG方程的任意小解可渐近分解为微观Cooper对轮廓与宏观序参量，后者在标度极限下满足Ginzburg-Landau方程，误差趋于零。分析基于Birman-Schwinger重构、Lyapunov-Schmidt约化以及低正则性下的半经典估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前从BCS理论严格推导Ginzburg-Landau理论的工作主要关注能量与极小元（minimizers），本文则希望处理相关能量区域内任意临界点（critical points）的情形，从而推广已有结论。

Method: 首先对BdG方程进行Birman-Schwinger重构（Birman-Schwinger reformulation），再运用Lyapunov-Schmidt型约化（Lyapunov-Schmidt type reduction），最后结合低正则性下的半经典估计（semiclassical estimates）完成分析。

Result: 对于接近临界温度的温度，BdG方程的每个充分小的解均可渐近分解为一个微观Cooper对轮廓（Cooper-pair profile）和一个宏观序参量（order parameter）；后者在标度极限（scaling limit）下满足Ginzburg-Landau方程，且误差随标度极限趋于零。

Conclusion: 本文在无外场BCS模型中建立了BdG方程与GL方程之间更一般化的严格联系，将已有结果从能量极小元推广到任意临界点，为从微观Bogoliubov-de Gennes理论到宏观Ginzburg-Landau理论的推导提供了更完整的数学基础。

Abstract: We study the relation between the Bogoliubov-de Gennes equation and the Ginzburg-Landau equation for a BCS model without external fields. While previous rigorous derivations of Ginzburg-Landau theory from BCS theory have focused on energies and minimizers, here we consider arbitrary critical points in the relevant energy regime. For temperatures close to the critical temperature, we prove that every sufficiently small solution of the BdG equation admits an asymptotic factorization into a microscopic Cooper-pair profile and a macroscopic order parameter. The latter satisfies the Ginzburg-Landau equation up to an error that vanishes in the scaling limit. Our analysis relies on a Birman-Schwinger reformulation of the BdG equation, a Lyapunov-Schmidt type reduction, and semiclassical estimates at low regularity.

Abstract: We discuss anomalous spin polarization on the surface of nuclear pasta in a neutron star, driven by a nuclear spin-orbit interaction. We present an effective two-band model of surface-localized neutrons near the nuclear pasta. Starting from a single-particle Hamiltonian with a central potential and a standard nuclear spin-orbit interaction, we show that the surface spin polarization occurs due to the thermal inhomogeneity even in the absence of a magnetic field. Our study links neutron-star physics and solid-state spintronics and would contribute to understanding the interplay between spin dynamics and strong magnetic fields.

### [268] [Pal's permanent conjecture: proof for block uniform matrices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25274)
*Andrea Ottolini,Shannon Starr*

Main category: math.CO

TL;DR: 本文证明了Soumik Pal关于一类对称函数矩阵的永久（permanent）渐近展开猜想在分块常数函数情形下的成立性，该猜想源于熵正则化最优输运（entropy regularized optimal transport）中的大偏差理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Soumik Pal针对满足$\mathcal{C}(x,y)=\mathcal{C}(1-x,1-y)$的对称光滑函数，提出了矩阵永久渐近行为的猜想。该猜想涉及已知的大偏差率函数（large deviation rate function）$\Lambda[\mathcal{C}]$（已由Sumit Mukherjee严格证明）和一个代数项$\mathcal{D}[\mathcal{C}]$，后者由Peter McCullagh关于双随机矩阵（doubly stochastic matrices）的公式给出，包括Fredholm行列式（Fredholm determinant）。本文旨在为该猜想提供部分严格证明。

Method: 研究聚焦于分块常数（block-constant）函数情形，利用Ross Pinsky关于置换在分块中组合分解（combinatorial decomposition of permutations in blocks）的经典结果，对矩阵的永久进行渐近分析。

Result: 成功证明了当函数$\mathcal{C}$为分块常数时，Pal猜想的渐近展开式成立。

Conclusion: 该结果部分验证了Pal猜想的正确性，为进一步证明一般光滑函数情形提供了重要基础和方法论支撑。

Abstract: Consider a symmetric function $\mathcal{C}(x,y)$ on $[0,1]\times[0,1]$ which is twice continuously differentiable up to the boundary, and which satisfies $ \mathcal{C}(x,y)=\mathcal{C}(1-x,1-y)$. Let $A^{(n)} = \big(a^{(n)}_{i,j}\, :\, i,j \in [n]\big)$ be the matrix with entries $a^{(n)}_{i,j}\, =\, \exp(-\mathcal{C}(i/n,j/n))$. Soumik Pal conjectured the asymptotics $$\operatorname{perm}\big(A^{(n)}\big)/n!\sim \exp\big(n Λ[\mathcal{C}]\big)/ \sqrt{\mathcal{D}[\mathcal{C}]}$$ as $n \to \infty$ for known functionals that arise naturally in the context of entropy regularized optimal transport. The functional $Λ[\mathcal{C}]$ is the known large deviation rate function, already proved rigorously by Sumit Mukherjee. It is $\int_{0}^1 \int_0^{1} (α(x)+β(y))\, dx\, dy$ where $α(x)+β(y)$ is chosen such that $ρ(x,y) := \exp(-\mathcal{C}(x,y)-α(x)-β(y))$ has uniform marginals. The algebraic term $\mathcal{D}[c]$ is given by Peter McCullagh's formula for doubly stochastic matrices: $\operatorname{det}_F(I+J-T^*T)$, the Fredholm determinant, where $I$ is the identity on $L^2([0,1])$, $Jf(x) \equiv \int_{0}^1 f(z)\, dz$ (for all $x$) and $Tf(x) = \int_0^1 ρ(x,y) f(y)\, dy$. We prove the conjecture for functions $\mathcal C$ that are constant on blocks, exploiting a well-known Ross Pinsky's combinatorial decomposition of permutations in blocks.

</details>

### [269] [Classification of the eternal solutions and multiple coalescing shocks in the KPZ fixed point](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26048)
*Sudeshna Bhattacharjee,Ofer Busani,Evan Sorensen*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 对 KPZ 不动点（KPZ fixed point）的永恒解（eternal solutions）进行了完整分类，将其描述为 Busemann 函数的拼接；这些解在边界处产生激波（shock），并随时间向前聚合、向后分裂，形成激波树（tree of shocks），同时刻画了该树的若干几何性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: KPZ 方程是随机界面生长领域的核心模型，其长期（永恒）解的结构对理解标度极限和普适类至关重要。此前缺乏对 KPZ 不动点永恒解的完整分类，该工作旨在填

Method: 通过将永恒解分解为已知的 Busemann 函数的（可能无限）拼接来构建分类；并分析拼接边界处激波的演化行为，包括向前与向后时间方向上的合并与生成。

Result: 所有永恒解均可由 Busemann 函数拼接而成，且在拼接边界处必然出现激波；激波在时间正向演化时发生合并（coalesce），在时间反向演化时则可能生成新激波。此外，给出了该激波树的若干几何性质。

Conclusion: 完成了 KPZ 不动点永恒解的完全分类，揭示了其激波树的动态演化规律与几何结构，为理解 KPZ 普适类（KPZ universality class）中长期解的全局行为提供了完整的理论刻画。

Abstract: We give a complete classification of the eternal solutions for the KPZ fixed point. Each of these is a (possibly infinite) patching together of the known eternal solutions, called Busemann functions. The resulting evolution of the KPZ fixed point exhibits a shock at each of the boundaries between the different Busemann functions. Moving forward in time, the shocks coalesce, while moving backwards in time, additional shocks can form. We describe several geometric properties of this tree of shocks.

</details>


### [270] [Exact Variance and Fano Factor for Arbitrary Level Crossings in Stationary Gaussian Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25278)
*Shivang Rawat,Flaviano Morone,David J. Heeger,Stefano Martiniani*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文针对光滑平稳高斯过程（smooth stationary Gaussian processes）中的任意水平穿越（level crossing）事件，推导出了方差（variance）和法诺因子（Fano factor）的精确解析公式，超越传统Kac-Rice公式仅能给出平均率的局限，揭示了时间相关结构如何决定穿越事件是聚集还是规则化出现，并通过阻尼谐振子和Ornstein-Uhlenbeck噪声驱动的均值回归过程等实例展示了丰富的统计行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统Kac-Rice公式仅能给出水平穿越的平均率（mean rate），但该平均率仅依赖于随机过程在某一时刻的局部性质，无法捕捉过程在时间上的相关结构（correlation structure），因而无法回答穿越事件（如神经元放电）在时间上是聚集、分散还是呈现更复杂的时间组织。为了理解这些高阶穿越统计特性，需要推导超越平均率的精确解析结果。

Method: 本文通过解析推导，得到了光滑平稳高斯过程中任意水平穿越的方差和法诺因子的精确解析公式（exact analytical formulae）。该方法将完整的时域相关结构纳入考量，从而揭示了穿越统计特性对过程相关性的依赖。

Result: 在具有振荡相关性的系统（如随机阻尼谐振子）中，一次穿越会抑制紧随其后的一次穿越，产生亚泊松统计（sub-Poissonian statistics）；当阻尼增大到振荡消失时，大幅且缓慢的阈值以上偏移可产生多次密集穿越，呈现超泊松统计（super-Poissonian statistics）。在纯弛豫非振荡系统（如Ornstein-Uhlenbeck噪声驱动的均值回归过程）中，驱动噪声与系统弛豫的时间尺度竞争产生了更丰富的景象，包括随阈值水平变化在亚泊松与超泊松统计之间的回返转变（reentrant transitions）。

Conclusion: 本文推导的精确方差和法诺因子补充了Kac-Rice平均率公式，在任意使用高斯过程的场景中，能够实现更稳健的参数估计（parameter estimation）和模型选择（model selection）。

Abstract: Understanding the statistics of level crossings in stochastic processes is crucial across many scientific disciplines. The traditional Kac-Rice formula gives the mean rate of level crossings and has found broad use. However, that mean rate captures only a coarse summary of the crossing process. It depends entirely on local properties of the stochastic process at a given instant and is therefore blind to the correlation structure of the process over time. To understand whether crossing events, such as neuronal spikes, tend to cluster in time, spread apart, or exhibit more complex temporal organization, one must go beyond the mean rate and study higher-order crossing statistics. Here we go beyond the mean by deriving the exact analytical formulae for the variance and Fano factor of arbitrary level crossings in smooth stationary Gaussian processes. Our exact solution reveals how the full temporal correlation structure dictates whether crossings cluster or become regular. In systems with oscillatory correlations, such as a stochastic damped harmonic oscillator, a recent crossing suppresses an immediate subsequent one, producing sub-Poissonian statistics. However, as damping increases and oscillations disappear, a large and slow excursion above the threshold can produce multiple closely spaced crossings, yielding super-Poissonian statistics. In purely relaxational, non-oscillatory systems, such as a mean-reverting process driven by Ornstein-Uhlenbeck noise, the competition between the timescales of the driving noise and system relaxation produces a richer landscape, including reentrant transitions between sub- and super-Poissonian statistics as the threshold level is varied. Taken together, the exact variance and Fano factor derived here complement the Kac-Rice mean rate, enabling more robust parameter estimation and model selection across any setting where Gaussian processes are used.

</details>


### [271] [Accelerated Simulation Algorithms for Extreme First-Passage Problems with General Emission Profiles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25295)
*Emmanuel Akame Mfoumou,David Holcman*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种高效模拟最快到达事件（fastest arrival events）的通用计算框架，通过利用渐近首次通过分布（asymptotic first-passage distributions），避免了模拟所有扩散粒子完整轨迹的高昂计算成本。该算法适用于有界域内局部吸收目标附近的扩散过程，包括一至三维布朗运动（Brownian motion），并支持瞬时发射和时变发射场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在分子随机系统中，最快到达事件（多粒子中首个到达目标的粒子）是触发信号启动的关键。传统方法需要生成所有粒子的完整轨迹，当粒子数量庞大时计算成本极高，亟需一种高效模拟算法。

Method: 利用渐近首次通过分布（asymptotic first-passage distributions），设计了一种递归逆变换算法（recursive inverse transform algorithm），用于在不追踪粒子轨迹的情况下模拟前k个到达时间（order statistics）。针对瞬时发射（instantaneous emission）场景，实现了该递归算法；针对时变发射（time-dependent emission）场景，则通过迭代方式扩展算法，涵盖从快速到缓慢发射的各种时间注入模式。

Result: 该算法能够高效生成前k个到达顺序统计量（order statistics），并提供最快到达时间均值的渐近估计（asymptotic estimates of the mean fastest arrival time），避免了布朗运动轨迹模拟（Brownian simulations of trajectories）。

Conclusion: 该加速算法可应用于空间反应网络（spatial reaction networks）、稀有事件检测（rare event detection）或扩散控制激活（diffusion-controlled activation）等场景。

Abstract: Fastest arrival events, where the first among many diffusing particles reaches a target, are central in triggering signal initiation in molecular stochastic systems. Classical approaches to simulate such events rely on full trajectory generation of all particles, leading to prohibitive computational costs in the large particle number regime. In this work, we present a general simulation framework for efficiently generating order statistics of arrival times by exploiting asymptotic first-passage distributions. This framework applies to diffusion processes in bounded domains with localized absorbing targets, for which short-time first-passage asymptotics are available, such as Brownian motion in dimensions one, two, and three. Starting with the case of instantaneous emission, we derive and implement a recursive inverse transform algorithm to simulate the first $k$ arrivals without tracking particle trajectories. We extend this algorithm to time-dependent emission profiles via an iterative approach, enabling the simulation of extreme statistics in systems with temporal injection, ranging from rapid to prolonged emission. Additionally, we provide asymptotic estimates of the mean fastest arrival time. To conclude, the present acceleration algorithm which bypasses Brownian simulations of trajectories can be used for spatial reaction networks, rare event detection, or diffusion-controlled activation.

</details>
