### [272] [Resonances in Overdamped Odd Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24276)
*Julius Kiln,Alexander Mietke*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过将经典的Papkovich-Neuber解法推广到活性材料，提出了奇Papkovich-Neuber（OPN）解，用于解析任意各向同性线性奇流体或奇固体（最多6个独立模量）的边界驱动响应，并揭示了奇粘弹性固体中三种物理上不同的共振模式，这些模式可通过阻尼谐振子的等价描述统一理解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 奇粘弹性（odd viscoelasticity）出现在宇称破缺（parity-violating）的非平衡材料中，可导致非常规力学响应和过阻尼系统中的振荡弛豫。虽然许多生命与活性手性材料是展示奇粘弹性的候选体系，但目前缺乏能够流变学推断一个最小各向同性奇粘弹性材料所依赖的大量弹性模量和粘性模量的方法。

Method: 将经典的Papkovich-Neuber解法推广至活性材料，提出奇Papkovich-Neuber（odd Papkovich-Neuber, OPN）解，这是一种适用于任意各向同性线性奇流体或奇固体的解析解，每种材料最多由6个独立模量描述。该方法可用于研究模拟常见流变学方法的几何构型中的边界驱动响应。

Result: OPN解揭示了奇粘弹性固体中存在三种物理上不同的共振（resonances），这些共振表征了潜在的材料模量特征，且可在单一的几何框架内进行解释。过阻尼奇粘弹性材料存在与阻尼谐振子（damped harmonic oscillators）等价的描述，当这些谐振子的有效阻尼系数消失时出现共振，此过程由驱动奇材料特性的活性（activity）所促进。

Conclusion: 奇Papkovich-Neuber（OPN）解为各向同性奇粘弹性材料的流变学推断提供了解析工具，并通过阻尼谐振子框架统一了多种共振现象，揭示了活性在奇粘弹性材料中的关键作用。

Abstract: Odd viscoelasticity arises in parity-violating nonequilibrium materials, where it leads to unconventional mechanical responses and oscillatory relaxation even in overdamped systems. While many living and active chiral materials present promising candidates to exhibit odd viscoelasticity, there is currently no approach that allows for a rheological inference of the large number of elastic and viscous moduli that even a minimal isotropic odd viscoelastic material can depend on. Generalizing the century-old Papkovich-Neuber ansatz to active materials, our work introduces an odd Papkovich-Neuber (OPN) solution -- an analytic solution for any isotropic linear odd fluid or solid, each described by up to 6 independent moduli -- that enable us to study the boundary-driven response in geometries that mimic common rheology methods. OPN solutions reveal three physically distinct resonances in odd viscoelastic solids that are characteristic of the underlying material moduli and can all be interpreted within a single geometric framework. Underlying this unification is an equivalent description of overdamped odd viscoelastic materials in terms of damped harmonic oscillators. Resonances appear as the effective damping coefficients of these oscillators vanish, which is facilitated by the activity that powers odd material properties.

</details>


### [273] [Rheotaxis of microswimmers in colloid-laden channel flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25003)
*Margam Ramprasad,Shubhadeep Mandal,Pallab Sinha Mahapatra*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文利用球形方均模型（spherical squirmer model）和多粒子碰撞动力学（multi-particle collision dynamics, MPCD）模拟，研究了微游泳体（microswimmers）在含硬球胶体（hard monodisperse spherical colloids）的通道流（channel flow）中的运动行为。结果表明，胶体的存在显著改变了不同游泳体类型（pusher/puller/neutral）的定向与速度分布：低流速下pusher向通道中心与上游游动，puller则远离中心；高流速下所有游泳体均被携带至中心并以上游方向为主，且puller沿流方向的局部速度低于pusher。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微游泳体常出现在狭窄管道内的非均匀、拥挤环境中，研究其运动机制有助于理解推进型（pusher）、牵引型（puller）及中性型（neutral）游泳体的迁移行为，并为靶向药物递送等应用提供理论基础。

Method: 采用球形方均模型（spherical squirmer model）描述微游泳体，并利用多粒子碰撞动力学（multi-particle collision dynamics, MPCD）介观模拟框架表示背景流体，在含硬单分散球状胶体的通道流中模拟游泳体运动。

Result: 无胶体时，流速增加使方均体远离壁面并在壁间振荡，近壁处以上游方向为主。有胶体时，低流速下pusher游向通道中心与上游，puller游离中心；高流速时所有游泳体均被携带至通道中心且上游方向占优，导致局部沿流速度下降；在恒定胶体填充分数下，puller的沿流局部速度幅值小于pusher。

Conclusion: 胶体的存在及其填充分数对微游泳体在通道流中的迁移方向与速度有显著调控作用，且不同游泳体类型（pusher/puller）表现出相反的趋向行为，揭示了拥挤环境对外部流动中微游泳体运动的影响规律。

Abstract: Microswimmers are often found in heterogeneous and crowded environments within narrow conduits under external flow conditions, enabling them to perform interesting translational and rotational maneuvers, such as swimming in the upstream direction, following walls, and oscillatory motion. Studying such systems helps us understand the motility behaviors of microswimmers (pushers, pullers, or neutrals) and develop applications such as targeted drug delivery. To study the motion of microswimmers in a channel flow with the presence of hard, monodisperse spherical colloids, we adopted the spherical squirmer model to represent the microswimmers, along with a mesoscale simulation framework, multi-particle collision dynamics (MPCD), to represent the background fluid. In the absence of colloids, a squirmer in a microchannel flow develops an increased probability of moving away from the walls and oscillates between the walls as the flow speed increases compared to the squirmer speed, with a dominant upstream orientation near the walls. However, the presence of the colloids makes the pusher swim towards the center of the channel and upstream direction, and the puller swim away from the center of the channel at low flow speeds. At high flow speeds, the flow carries all the squirmers, resulting in a dominant upstream direction in the channel center. We observe that this leads to a decrease in the local velocity of the squirmer in the flow direction for pusher, neutral, and puller-type squirmers. We also observe that, for a constant colloidal packing fraction, the local velocity magnitude of the puller along the flow direction is less than that of the pusher.

</details>


### [274] [Unfrustrated Self-Morphing of Bulk Liquid Crystal Elastomers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25187)
*Shachaf Rotem,Hillel Aharoni*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过推广薄片的几何方法到体液晶弹性体（LCEs），利用参考Ricci曲率分析，建立了无应力、无几何阻挫（frustration）三维变形所需的最小条件集，识别了两类几何兼容体系，为体LCE的正向与逆向设计提供了数学基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在软体机器人（soft robotics）和自适应结构中，精确操控形状变形材料至关重要。尽管薄二维片材已实现显著精度，但因几何阻挫（geometric frustration）产生的复杂残余弹性应力，使得准确的体积（volumetric）形状变形仍是一项重大挑战。

Method: 本文将薄片的几何方法推广至体液晶弹性体（Liquid Crystal Elastomers, LCEs）。通过考察其参考Ricci曲率（reference Ricci curvature），推导了三维向列指向矢场（nematic director field）在驱动下实现无应力、无阻挫变形所需的最小条件集。

Result: 识别出两类几何兼容的体系统。第一类为无扭转指向矢场，在所有温度下均保持无阻挫，对应“平面（Planar）”和“近晶（Smectic）”LCE子族。第二类为具有扭转构型（twisted configurations）的系统，表现出温度选择性兼容性，导致内弹性应力非单调累积，并在预定目标温度下完全松弛。

Conclusion: 该数学框架为体LCE中稳健的正向与逆向设计协议建立了坚实的数学基础。

Abstract: Precise manipulation of shape-morphing responsive materials is crucial for applications in soft robotics and adaptive structures. While notable precision has been achieved in thin two-dimensional sheets, an accurate volumetric shape-morphing remains a major challenge due to geometric frustration, which inevitably generates complex, residual elastic stresses. In this work, we extend the geometric approach used for thin sheets to bulk Liquid Crystal Elastomers (LCEs). By examining their reference Ricci curvature, we formulate the minimal set of conditions required for a three-dimensional nematic director field to undergo stress-free, frustration-free deformations upon actuation. Through this mathematical framework, we identify two distinct classes of geometrically compatible bulk systems. The first class comprises twistless director fields that remain frustration-free across all temperatures, leading to holographic design principles demonstrated through "Planar" and "Smectic" LCE subfamilies. The second class features twisted configurations that exhibit unique, temperature-selective compatibility, leading to non-monotonic accumulation of internal elastic stresses that relax completely at a predefined target temperature. Our framework establishes a firm mathematical foundation for robust forward and inverse design protocols in bulk LCEs.

### [275] [Non-equilibrium pathway to mesoscale ordering in ethanol-water binary liquid](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25457)
*Xinyue Jiang,Yating Shang,Jianhui Li,Zhaoyong Zou,Yanxia Zuo,Yuqun Xie*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过周期性热振荡驱动乙醇-水混合物沿层级自组装路径演化，证明其经典热力学反常（如体积收缩和负过剩熵）并非平衡态性质，而是受阻相变的量热指纹，并从动力学角度揭示了溶液中非理想性的结构起源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 乙醇-水混合物是热力学非理想性（thermodynamic non-ideality）的经典范例，但其体积收缩和负过剩熵（negative excess entropy）等显著反常现象的结构起源长期未解。

Method: 对50%（体积比）乙醇-水体系施加周期性热振荡（periodic thermal oscillations），并利用荧光光谱（fluorescence spectroscopy）、二维相关分析（two-dimensional correlation analysis）和核磁共振（nuclear magnetic resonance）追踪分子机制。

Result: 体系沿完整层级自组装（hierarchical self-assembly）路径演化：从乙醇团簇（ethanol clusters）到含水滴状结构（water-containing droplets），再到针状薄片（acicular flakes），最终形成微米级有序乙醇聚集体（micron-scale ordered ethanol aggregates）。分子机制为：周期扰动水主导的氢键网络（hydrogen-bond network）引发乙醇-水共存中间体，最终导致富乙醇相的有序组装。

Conclusion: 实验表明周期性物理扰动可在简单二元混合物中驱动多尺度自发有序化，这为软物质（soft matter）中非理想性的结构起源提供了动力学视角，并对自组装策略具有普适意义。

Abstract: Ethanol-water mixtures are a classic example of thermodynamic non-ideality, yet the structural origin of their pronounced anomalies, such as volume contraction and a large negative excess entropy, has remained a long-standing puzzle. Here, we demonstrate these anomalies are not equilibrium properties but calorimetric fingerprint of an arrested phase transition. By imposing periodic thermal oscillations, we drive a 50% (v/v) ethanol-water system along a complete hierarchical self-assembly pathway that progressed from ethanol clusters to water-containing droplets, then to acicular flakes, and finally to micron-scale ordered ethanol aggregates. Fluorescence spectroscopy, two-dimensional correlation analysis and nuclear magnetic resonance revealed the underlying non-equilibrium molecular mechanism: a periodic perturbation of the water-dominated hydrogen-bond network initiates a ethanol-water coexistence intermediate, ultimately leading to the stable ordered assembly of an ethanol-rich phase. Our finding demonstrated that periodic physical perturbations capable drive spontaneous ordering across multiple length scales in a simple binary mixture, providing a kinetic perspective on the structural origin of solution non-ideality, and carry general implications for self-assembly strategies in soft matter.

</details>


### [276] [A sweeping twist defect as a topological flagellum that drives colloid motion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25606)
*Qi Xing Zhang,Claire Dore,Mojtaba Rajabi,Edward B. Steager,Kathleen J. Stebe*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本论文研究了一种在外部场驱动下旋转的混合圆盘胶体（hybrid disk colloid），该胶体产生动态伴随拓扑缺陷（topological defect）。研究发现，该缺陷是一种非奇异扭曲壁（non-singular twist wall），其扫过圆盘表面时驱动圆盘加速运动。通过Landau-de Gennes建模表明，该缺陷如同鞭毛（flagellum）一般推动胶体游动，提供了一个利用耗散拓扑结构（dissipative topological structure）做功的实例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 向列相液晶（nematic liquid crystals）在动态驱动下可发生显著重构，为活性物质（active matter）研究提供了重要机遇。本文旨在探索外部场驱动的圆盘胶体系统中拓扑缺陷的运动机制及其对胶体推进的影响。

Method: 采用混合盘胶体系统，通过外部场驱动其旋转产生动态伴随拓扑缺陷。结合Landau-de Gennes建模，分析缺陷的拓扑结构与动力学行为，并考察缺陷扫过圆盘表面时指向矢场（director field）的传播纹理（propagating director texture）特征。

Result: 缺陷被识别为非奇异扭曲壁，其扫过圆盘表面会反转扭曲的手性（handedness of twist）并降低间隙流体的自由能（free energy）。圆盘在缺陷扫过时运动更快。模拟显示，扫过壁表现为传播的指向矢纹理：在壁的参考系中指向矢场几乎静止，而液晶分子（nematogens）局部旋转，从而在圆盘表面产生黏性应力（viscous stress），加速推进。

Conclusion: 该拓扑缺陷起到类似鞭毛的作用，驱动胶体游动。此工作机制提供了一个耗散拓扑结构动力学被用于实现有用功的范例。

Abstract: Nematic liquid crystals can dramatically reconfigure under dynamic forcing, providing exciting opportunities in active matter. Here, we study a hybrid disk colloid rotated by an external field which generates a dynamic companion topological defect. The disk moves faster when the defect sweeps across the disk's face. We identify the defect as a non-singular twist wall, characterize the twist energy landscape, and identify the sweeping motion as a topological instability. As the defect sweeps, it reverses the handedness of twist and lowers the free energy in the fluid in the gap above the disk. Landau-de Gennes modeling shows that the sweeping wall behaves as a propagating director texture: the director field is nearly stationary in the wall frame, while nematogens rotate locally as the wall passes. The nematogens' rotation generates a viscous stress on the surface of the disk that hastens its propulsion. Thus, the defect acts as a flagellum that powers colloid swimming, providing an example of a dissipative topological structure whose dynamics can be harnessed to perform useful work.

</details>


### [277] [Chain conformations in adsorbed layer during polymer capillary imbibition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25714)
*Tao Liang,Li Peng,Xianbo Huang,Jiajia Zhou*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该论文通过分子动力学模拟研究了聚合物毛细吸入过程中吸附层的链构象，发现受限条件下移动珠子密度出现异常偏差，循环结构比例逐渐增加，且链松弛动力学表现出长度依赖的延迟效应，解吸时间的尺度行为与标度预言定量吻合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解聚合物在纳米受限毛细吸入过程中的链构象演化与吸附层动态行为，揭示经典Lucas-Washburn方程之外的新物理机制，为实验观测（如介电谱）提供微观理论解释。

Method: 采用分子动力学模拟（molecular dynamics simulations）方法，系统分析吸附层内链构象、移动珠子密度、循环结构比例及松弛动力学随毛细浸润进程的变化规律。

Result: 浸润长度符合经典Lucas-Washburn方程，但强受限条件下移动珠子密度出现显著偏差，与原位介电谱实验一致；浸润过程中循环结构比例逐渐增加；链松弛动力学表现出链长依赖的延迟效应，尤其在高受限条件下更为显著；特征解吸时间与标度预言（scaling predictions）定量吻合。

Conclusion: 聚合物毛细吸入过程中，吸附层的构象演化与松弛动力学受纳米受限程度和链长的共同调控，经典标度行为在动态响应中仍保持适用，但需要纳入链构象弛豫效应以完整描述受限下的输运行为。

Abstract: We conducted molecular dynamics simulations to investigate chain conformations in adsorbed layers during polymer capillary imbibition. While the imbibition length adheres to the classical Lucas-Washburn equation, a notable deviation in mobile bead density emerges under strong confinement, consistent with \emph{in situ} dielectric spectroscopy experiments. The proportion of loop structures within adsorbed layers progressively increases during capillary infiltration, attributed to the relaxation of initially stretched chains toward equilibrium configurations. Furthermore, systematic analysis revealed that chain relaxation dynamics exhibit length-dependent retardation, especially under high confinement. The characteristic desorption time demonstrates chain-length dependence in quantitative agreement with scaling predictions.

</details>


### [278] [The Remodeling of Fiber Distributions in Biological Tissues: Rotation without Rotation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25732)
*Christian Cherubini,Marcello Vasta,Filippo Recrosi,Alessio Gizzi*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文从理论层面证明，马萨式增长动力学（Malthusian growth dynamics）与线性力学重塑关系的结合，能够自然导出广义双峰冯·米塞斯分布（generalized bimodal Von Mises distributions）作为生命物质（living matter）的涌现态（emergent states），揭示了一种“无旋转的旋转”（rotation without rotation）机制，并建立了从随机单纤维动力学到组织重塑的统计力学框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 活体组织中的胶原重塑（collagen remodeling）呈现各向异性（anisotropic）取向模式，通常用冯·米塞斯分布（Von Mises distributions）描述，但这种非平衡组织（nonequilibrium organization）的物理起源尚未明确。

Method: 通过分析推导，将马萨式增长动力学与线性力学重塑关系相结合，以归一化纤维密度作为概率分布函数，引入动态香农熵（Shannon entropy）框架，并推导出相应的福克-普朗克方程（Fokker--Planck equation）及其随机微分方程（stochastic differential equation）。

Result: 理论解析解定量复现了实验观测到的纤维分布；揭示了“无旋转的旋转”机制，即纤维通过沿偏好方向的选择性沉积与移除实现渐进重定向，无需角向力学耦合；推导出福克-普朗克方程的漂移项闭式解，表明组织重塑是噪声驱动的单纤维动力学的集体结果。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一个连接生物力学（biomechanics）、随机过程（stochastic processes）与非平衡统计组织（nonequilibrium statistical organization）的最小理论框架，为生物组织中方向统计学（directional statistics）提供了直接的力学生物学（mechanobiological）起源。

Abstract: Collagen remodeling in living tissues exhibits anisotropic orientation patterns commonly described by Von Mises distributions, yet the physical origin of such nonequilibrium organization remains unresolved. In the present work, we demonstrate analytically that the combined action of Malthusian growth dynamics and the introduction of linear relations governing mechanical remodeling naturally gives rise to generalized bimodal Von Mises distributions as emergent states of living matter. The theory reveals a {\it rotation without rotation} mechanism, in which fibers progressively reorient in the absence of angular mechanical coupling via selective deposition and removal along preferred directions. The resulting analytical solutions quantitatively reproduce experimentally observed distributions and establish a direct mechanobiological origin for directional statistics in biological tissues. By interpreting the evolving normalized fiber density as a probability distribution function, we formulate a dynamical Shannon entropy framework that captures the temporal emergence of microstructural organization. The theory further yields closed-form expressions for the drift of the associated Fokker--Planck equation, enabling the corresponding stochastic differential equation to be derived, thus revealing that tissue remodeling is the collective outcome of noisy single-fiber dynamics. These results establish a minimal theoretical framework that connects biomechanics, stochastic processes, and nonequilibrium statistical organization in living matter.

*Luca Casagrande,Alessandro Manacorda,Etienne Fodor*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过构建椭圆活性粒子（active elliptical particles）的微观模型，研究各向异性变形（anisotropic deformation）如何产生自组织波（self-organized waves），并通过粗粒化（coarse-graining）推导出流体力学描述（hydrodynamic description），揭示了向列序（nematic order）与同步变形（synchronized deformation）之间的耦合机制及其相图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 收缩性活体组织（contractile living tissues）中变形波（deformation waves）的产生机制尚不明确，现有模型主要基于活性可变形粒子（actively deformable particles）。受心肌细胞（cardiomyocytes）各向异性变形的启发，旨在理解椭圆粒子的脉动如何影响其在高密度组装（dense assemblies）中的集体行为。

Method: 引入两种变形模式，使每个粒子的偏心率（eccentricity）受到周期性驱动（periodic drive）；通过系统相图（phase diagram）考察向列序与同步变形的相互作用；采用粗粒化程序（coarse-graining procedure）推导流体力学描述。

Result: 微观动力学的流体力学描述（hydrodynamic description）能够定性捕捉主要的集体态（collective states）；活性各向异性变形（active anisotropic deformation）可产生自组织形成多种动力学模式（dynamical patterns）的波。

Conclusion: 该模型为理解活性各向异性变形如何产生并自组织为不同动力学模式提供了关键见解，有助于揭示心肌组织等收缩性活体组织中的波形涌现机制。

Abstract: Capturing the emergence of deformation waves in contractile living tissues is a challenge that has recently been tackled with models of actively deformable particles. Inspired by the anisotropic deformation of cardiomyocytes in cardiac tissues, we examine how the pulsation of elliptical particles affects their collective properties in dense assemblies. We introduce two types of deformation where the eccentricity of each particle is subject to a periodic drive, and examine the interplay between nematic order and synchronized deformation via a systematic phase diagram. We derive a hydrodynamic description through a coarse-graining procedure, and show that it qualitatively captures the main collective states of the microscopic dynamics. Overall, our model provides key insights into how an active anisotropic deformation yields waves that self-organize into various dynamical patterns.

### [280] [Excess entropy scaling of the transverse sound speed in simple fluids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25972)
*Sergey Khrapak*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文计算了若干简单流体的横向声速随过量熵（excess entropy）的变化关系，建立了该依赖关系的准普适性（quasi-universal character），将Rosenfeld的输运系数过量熵标度（excess-entropy scaling）拓展至横向声速，并从软球-硬球交叉（soft- to hard-sphere crossover）与Frenkel交叉（气体-液体动力学转变）角度进行了讨论。

Method: 对多种简单流体模型（Lennard-Jones、Yukawa、单组分等离子体（one-component plasma, OCP）、逆幂律（inverse-power law, 软球）及硬球（hard sphere））分别计算了横向声速随过量熵的函数关系。

Result: 建立了横向声速与过量熵之间依赖关系的准普适性，即不同简单流体在该标度下表现出相近的行为。

Conclusion: 该准普适性表明过量熵标度框架可扩展至横向声速；其结果可从软球-硬球交叉和Frenkel交叉（气体-液体动力学转变）两种物理图像加以解释。

Abstract: A calculation of the transverse sound velocity as a function of excess entropy is presented for several simple fluids, including the Lennard-Jones, Yukawa, one-component plasma, inverse-power law (soft sphere) and hard sphere models. A quasi-universal character of this dependence is established, extending Rosenfeld's excess-entropy scaling of transport coefficients to the transverse sound velocity. The results are discussed in terms of the soft- to hard-sphere crossover and the Frenkel crossover between gas-like and liquid-like dynamics.

### [281] [Beyond Gaussian Statistics in Polymer Melts: Statistical Masking of Persistent Local Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25989)
*José A. Martins*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该论文通过聚乙烯熔体的原子分子动力学模拟，揭示了高分子链从非高斯到高斯末端距统计行为的恢复并非源于库恩尺度异质性的消失，而是一种统计掩盖效应：随着链长增加，独立卷曲段（RCS）的积累逐渐掩盖了持久存在的延伸排列链段（ACS）的非高斯特征。论文引入q-高斯函数和Tsallis熵比作为量化异质性指标，系统描述了从短链（C50，q=0.67）到长链（C500，q=0.99）的熵指数演化过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 短聚合物链的末端距分布明显偏离高斯统计（Gaussian statistics），但长链恢复高斯行为的分子机制尚未建立，这一基本问题的解答对高分子物理理论具有重要意义。

Method: 采用全原子分子动力学（atomistic molecular dynamics）模拟聚乙烯熔体，分析不同链长（C50至C500）的末端距分布，使用q-高斯函数（q-Gaussian function）拟合分布，并直接从模拟数据计算Tsallis熵与Boltzmann-Gibbs熵之比（$S_q/S_1$）。

Result: 发现所有链长的库恩尺度上均存在构象异质性（conformational heterogeneity），包含缓慢弛豫的延伸排列链段（aligned chain segments, ACS）、随机构象序列（random conformational sequences, RCS）和链端（chain ends, CE）。熵指数q从C50的0.67单调增长至C500的0.99，Tsallis/Boltzmann-Gibbs熵比从1.80降至1.03。ACS域在所有链长中均持续存在（占比约>35%）。

Conclusion: 高斯统计的恢复并非由于库恩尺度异质性的消除，而是一种统计掩盖效应（statistical masking effect）：独立RCS段的累积逐渐遮掩了持久ACS域的非高斯信号。q可定量作为“异质性指数”（heterogeneity index），q<1是非广延统计（non-extensive statistics）的标志。

Abstract: Short polymer chains exhibit clear deviations from Gaussian end-to-end distance statistics, yet the molecular mechanism by which Gaussian behavior is recovered in long chains remains unestablished. Atomistic molecular dynamics simulations of polyethylene melts reveal that conformational heterogeneity persists at the Kuhn scale across all chain lengths, consisting of a mosaic of slow-relaxing, extended aligned chain segments (ACS) and coiled segments -- random conformational sequences (RCS) and chain ends (CE). We show that the end-to-end distance distributions for both unentangled and entangled chains are accurately described by a $q$-Gaussian function, with the entropic index $q$ increasing systematically from $0.67$ (C50) to $0.99$ (C500). This evolution tracks the emergence and accumulation of RCS segments, which are absent in short chains, establishing $q$ as a quantitative ``heterogeneity index''. The $q < 1$ values are a signature of non-extensive statistics, with the ratio of Tsallis to Boltzmann-Gibbs entropy ($S_q/S_1$), computed directly from simulation data without fitting, decreasing from $1.80$ (C50) to $1.03$ (C500). Crucially, we demonstrate that Gaussian recovery does not result from the erasure of Kuhn-scale heterogeneities, as ACS domains persist in all chain lengths above the critical mass ($\approx 35\%$). Instead, the transition to Gaussian statistics is a statistical masking effect, where the accumulation of independent RCS segments progressively obscures the non-Gaussian signatures of the persistent ACS domains.

</details>


### [282] [Topology of pulsating active matter: Defect asymmetry controls emergent motility](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25996)
*Luca Casagrande,Alessandro Manacorda,Etienne Fodor*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 在脉动活性物质（pulsating active matter）中，拓扑缺陷（topological defects）虽无宏观流动和微观自推进，但由于振荡与排斥相互作用的棘轮效应（ratchet effect）而具备运动能力，该机制调控了慢速缺陷与快速缺陷之间的波型交叉，类似于心肌组织中心律失常的起始过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示脉动活性物质中拓扑缺陷在缺乏宏观流动和微观自推进条件下仍可运动的物理机制。

Method: 通过棘轮效应解释局部振荡与排斥相互作用的机械化学耦合如何同时破坏空间对称性和时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry），从而驱动非对称旋转缺陷在涨落中漂移；并利用涨落流体力学（fluctuating hydrodynamics）对该过程进行理论描述。

Result: 调控了慢速缺陷连接的螺旋波（spiral waves）与快速缺陷连接的纤维状波（fiber-like waves）之间的交叉（crossover），这一行为与心肌组织中心律失常的起始具有类比性。

Conclusion: 该发现表明拓扑缺陷的自主运动源于对称性破缺（symmetry breaking）导致的棘轮效应，且涨落流体力学框架能够有效描述缺陷的自发成核（nucleation）与在有序背景中的运动。

Abstract: In pulsating active matter, topological defects are motile despite the absence of any macroscopic flows and microscopic self-propulsion. We reveal that this motility arises from a ratchet effect: the mechanochemical coupling between local oscillations and repulsive interactions breaks both spatial and time-reversal symmetries, thus leading asymmetric rotating defects to drift under fluctuations. This mechanism regulates a crossover between spiral waves connecting slow defects and fiber-like waves connecting fast defects, in analogy with the onset of heart rhythm disorder in cardiac tissues. We rationalize this crossover in terms of a fluctuating hydrodynamics that captures how motile defects spontaneously nucleate and move within an ordered background.

</details>


### [283] [Liquid-Liquid Phase Separation in a Minimal Explicit-Solvent Lattice Model Mimicking Protein Solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26027)
*Siddhartha Roy,Rakesh S. Singh*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究采用基于有淬火无序（quenched disorder）的晶格气体哈密顿量（lattice-gas Hamiltonian）的显式溶剂最小统计力学模型，系统分析了蛋白质-溶剂和蛋白质-拥挤剂（crowder）相互作用如何调控凝聚体（condensate）的相行为与形貌，揭示了包括上临界溶解温度（UCST）、闭合环（closed-loop）和重入（reentrant）型转变在内的丰富相图，并扩展至二元蛋白质混合物体系，指出蛋白质-溶剂与蛋白质-拥挤剂相互作用可作为调控凝聚体形态的关键参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生物分子凝聚体（biomolecular condensates）在细胞过程中发挥重要作用，理解其组装机制和理性设计原理是当前的研究焦点。该研究旨在系统探究蛋白质-溶剂及蛋白质-拥挤剂相互作用对凝聚体相行为（phase behavior）和形貌（morphology）的影响规律。

Method: 采用基于有淬火无序的晶格气体哈密顿量的显式溶剂最小统计力学模型（explicit-solvent minimal statistical mechanical model），其中淬火无序用于模拟拥挤剂。该模型分别在平衡与非平衡条件下计算相图，并进一步扩展至二元蛋白质混合物体系，研究有无淬火无序时的相分离形貌。

Result: 相图显示在变化蛋白质-溶剂相互作用下出现上临界溶解温度（UCST）、闭合环和重入型转变等丰富行为。无无序时，二元蛋白质混合物呈现部分润湿、完全润湿、分离型和结合型等多种相分离形貌，且相边界敏感依赖于蛋白质-溶剂相互作用。引入淬火无序后，由于蛋白质-蛋白质、蛋白质-溶剂和蛋白质-拥挤剂相互作用的共同影响，产生了更广泛的复杂形貌谱系。

Conclusion: 该工作强调了蛋白质-溶剂和蛋白质-拥挤剂相互作用与蛋白质-蛋白质相互作用一起，可作为调节凝聚体形貌的关键调控参数。这些发现有望为研究生物分子体系中液-液相分离（liquid-liquid phase separation）的计算与实验工作提供指导，以设计具有刺激响应性的凝聚体（stimuli-responsive condensates）。

Abstract: Biomolecular condensates play essential roles in cellular processes, and recent efforts have focused on understanding their assembly and rational design principles. In this study, we have employed an explicit-solvent minimal statistical mechanical model based on the lattice-gas Hamiltonian with quenched disorder -- which mimics crowders -- to investigate how protein-solvent and protein-crowder interactions influence condensate phase behavior and morphology. The computed phase diagrams reveal rich behavior, including upper critical solution temperature (UCST), closed-loop, and reentrant type transitions under varying protein-solvent interactions at both equilibrium and out-of-equilibrium conditions. We elucidated the origin of these phase behavior changes and examined the role of protein-crowder interactions in modulating condensed phase morphology and stability. We further extended this model to binary protein mixtures where we studied the phase behavior in the presence and absence of quenched disorder. Without disorder, the system exhibits diverse phase-separated morphologies -- partially wetted, fully wetted, segregative, and associative -- with phase boundaries delicately sensitive protein-solvent interactions. The introduction of quenched disorder (or crowder) leads to a broader spectrum of complex morphologies, dictated by the interplay among protein-protein, protein-solvent, and protein-crowder interaction parameters. In general, this work underscores that protein-solvent and protein-crowder interactions, together with protein-protein interactions, can act as key regulatory parameters for modulating condensate morphology. These insights may guide future computational and experimental studies of liquid-liquid phase separation in biomolecular systems aimed at designing stimuli-responsive condensates.

### [284] [Characterizing emergent multi-scale dynamics in colloidal nanoparticle gels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26083)
*William D. Brackett,Zachary M. Sherman,Felix Lehmkühler,Thomas M. Truskett,Delia J. Milliron*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文综述了基于纳米颗粒（nanoparticle, NP）的胶体凝胶（colloidal gel）研究现状，指出其层级结构与宏观网络性质之间的理论桥梁尚未建立；强调X射线光子相关光谱（XPCS）结合互补技术（如流变-XPCS、光散射、显微镜与模拟）可在多时空尺度上揭示凝胶化、老化与力学响应机制，并展望了第四代光源下从描述性研究向可编程材料设计转型的前景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 胶体凝胶的层级组织过程如何与宏观网络性质相关联，是软物质物理学（soft matter physics）中一个尚未解决的广泛问题；凝胶形成机制对相互作用路径的敏感依赖性，阻碍了从纳米尺度相互作用到结构演化与网络动力学的统一理论构建。

Method: 利用X射线光子相关光谱（X-ray photon correlation spectroscopy, XPCS）探测纳米颗粒凝胶中的纳米尺度运动；结合原位流变-XPCS（in situ rheo-XPCS）同时监测纳米尺度与宏观力学响应；辅以互补的光散射、显微镜或模拟手段以扩展时空表征能力；并采用具有可调一次纳米颗粒特征的模块化模型平台（modular model platform）系统性地调控纳米尺度特性。

Result: XPCS能够量化凝胶中颗粒与网络的运动，但单独使用无法解析驱动凝胶化、老化及网络力学性质的完整时空动态谱；而多种互补技术的整合可显著扩展对NP凝胶网络物理的理解。

Conclusion: 第四代光源快速扩展的XPCS能力，结合互补工具与稳健的模型系统，有望促使该领域从描述性基础研究转向具有自适应与可编程行为（adaptive and programmable behaviors）的纳米颗粒凝胶设计。

Abstract: Colloidal gels assembled from nanoparticles (NPs) are a versatile class of soft network-based materials capable of rich dynamic, mechanical, and even optical or magnetic responses to stimuli. Understanding how their hierarchically organized processes relate to macroscopic network properties remains a broad and unresolved problem in soft matter physics. The mechanisms of gel formation can depend sensitively on the pathway and the nature of NP interactions, thus far preventing a unified theoretical bridge between nanoscopic interactions and structural evolution and network dynamics. Indirect measurement of dynamics using light-scattering techniques provides an experimental means to quantify underlying particle and network motion. X-ray photon correlation spectroscopy (XPCS) has emerged as a powerful tool for probing nanoscopic motion in nanoparticle gels, but alone cannot resolve the full spatiotemporal spectrum of dynamics that drive gelation, aging, and network mechanical properties. While in situ rheo-XPCS enables simultaneous probing of nanoscale and bulk mechanical responses, complementary light scattering, microscopy, or simulations can extend spatiotemporal characterization and, consequently, understanding of NP gel network physics. Implementing a modular model platform with tunable primary nanoparticle features allows systematic variation of nanoscopic characteristics that drive emergent gel responses and inform the development of theoretical models for a wide range of soft, dynamic, nanostructured materials. The rapid expansion of XPCS capabilities at fourth-generation light sources, combined with complementary tools and robust model systems, positions the field to move beyond descriptive fundamental studies toward the design of nanoparticle gels with adaptive and programmable behaviors.

</details>

### [285] [Pressure and Size Dependence of Roton Emission and Vortex Creation by Moving Objects in He~II in $T \to 0$ Limit: Generalized Nonlocal Gross-Pitaevskii Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24075)
*Nicolás Pablo Müller,Ladislav Skrbek,Yuri A. Sergeev,Giorgio Krstulovic*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文在广义非局域Gross-Pitaevskii（GP）模型框架下，数值研究了超流$^4$He中运动物体诱发的旋子发射（roton emission）和涡旋成核（vortex nucleation）随压强和障碍物尺寸变化的机制，计算了两种临界速度并分析了压强依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前尚未有工作在单一理论框架内同时分析超流$^4$He中旋子发射和涡旋成核机制的压强依赖性及相关临界速度，作者试图填补这一空白。

Method: 采用广义非局域Gross-Pitaevskii（GP）模型，通过选择原子间相互作用势参数使理论激发谱与Godfrin等人实验测得的压强依赖色散曲线（dispersion curve）吻合；在二维近似下模拟圆形障碍物（圆盘）在静止超流$^4$He中的运动。

Result: 在0 bar到约25 bar凝固压强的范围内，针对多个压强值计算了两种临界速度——分别对应旋子发射和量子化涡旋（quantized vortices）成核——并得到它们随压强和障碍物尺寸的变化关系；此外还简要提及三维球状障碍物模拟的初步结果。

Conclusion: 该广义非局域GP模型能够统一描述超流$^4$He中旋子发射和涡旋成核的压强依赖机制，为理解相关临界速度行为提供了理论工具。

Abstract: In the framework of generalized, nonlocal Gross-Pitaevskii (GP) model, we study numerically the pressure- and size-dependent mechanisms of roton emission and vortex nucleation by objects moving in superfluid $^4$He. As far as the authors are aware, this is the first attempt to analyze the pressure dependence of these mechanisms and the associated critical velocities within a single theoretical framework. For each of several pressures in the range from 0 to the solidification pressure of $\approx25$~bar, we chose the parameters of the interatomic interaction potential such that the resulting excitation spectrum for the generalized, nonlocal GP equation approximates fairly accurately the pressure-dependent dispersion curve determined experimentally by Godfrin \textit{et al.}, Phys. Rev. B \textbf{103}, 104516 (2021). In the two-dimensional approximation, for circular obstacles (disks) moving in quiescent $^4$He, we calculated two critical velocities -- one corresponding to the roton emission and the other to the nucleation of quantized vortices -- as functions of pressure and the obstacle's size. We also comment briefly on three-dimensional simulations of the roton emission and vortex nucleation by moving spherical obstacles.

### [286] [Programmable dipolar interaction geometry selects stripe-family order in a molecular lattice quantum simulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25019)
*Chao Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过量子蒙特卡洛模拟，研究微波修饰极性分子在正方形光学晶格中的硬核玻色子模型，发现存在两类由 t/V 控制的相：大 t/V 时为具有方向刚度各向异性的超流相，小 t/V 时形成条纹固态相，并指出该条纹族序态可通过适中的有效缀饰偶极矩在 NaCs 晶格实验中实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微波修饰极性分子提供了一种新的途径，使得长程偶极相互作用的角向形式（而非仅强度）可被工程化调控，从而拓展晶格量子模拟器（lattice quantum simulators）的物理可能性。

Method: 采用蠕虫算法路径积分量子蒙特卡洛（worm-algorithm path-integral quantum Monte Carlo）模拟，辅以硬核自旋映射（hard-core spin mapping）和古茨威勒软模诊断（Gutzwiller soft-mode diagnostic）进行分析。

Result: 系统存在两个由 t/V 控制的相区：较大 t/V 时保持超流但出现方向刚度各向异性；较小 t/V 时形成沿 (q,0) 轴向族选择的条纹固态相（stripe solid），实空间条纹平行于 y 方向。条纹的序波矢保持在轴向族内但随填充率重排，表明序为条纹族（family of stripe states）而非单一共度布拉格峰。条纹叶瓣闭合附近平均观测量可模拟窄超固体信号，但测量分辨的结构因子直方图揭示超流与条纹固态之间的一级开关切换。

Conclusion: 预测的条纹族序态及其实验诊断与可及的分子量子模拟尺度相关联，NaCs 晶格估计显示相关 V/t 窗口可通过适中的有效缀饰偶极矩（modest effective dressed dipole moments）实现。

Abstract: Microwave-dressed polar molecules offer a route to lattice quantum simulators in which the angular form of long-range dipolar interactions, not only their overall strength, can be engineered. We study this setting in a minimal hard-core Bose lattice model on a square optical lattice, with particles interacting through a sign-changing non-axisymmetric dipolar tail \mathcal V(\mathbf r)\propto (x^2-y^2)/(x^2+y^2)^{5/2} that is repulsive along one lattice axis and attractive along the other. Using worm-algorithm path-integral quantum Monte Carlo simulations, supported by a hard-core spin mapping and a Gutzwiller soft-mode diagnostic, we find two regimes controlled by t/V: at larger t/V the system remains superfluid but develops a pronounced directional stiffness anisotropy, while at smaller t/V it forms a stripe solid selected in the (q,0) axial family, corresponding to real-space stripes parallel to y. The leading ordering wave vector remains in this axial family but reorganizes with filling, showing that the robust ordered object is a family of stripe states rather than one fixed commensurate Bragg peak. Near the closure of the stripe lobe, averaged observables can mimic a narrow supersolid signal; measurement-resolved stripe structure-factor histograms instead reveal first-order switching between superfluid and stripe-solid sectors. NaCs lattice estimates place the relevant V/t window within reach of modest effective dressed dipole moments, linking the predicted stripe-family order and its experimental diagnostics to accessible molecular quantum-simulation scales.

</details>


### [287] [Lattice polarons with extended interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25202)
*Enrique I. Ramírez-Juárez,Genaro Lopez-Olivera,Luis A. Peña Ardila,Arturo Camacho-Guardian*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过包含单激发介质的变分方法，研究了具有强在位排斥和可调最近邻相互作用的二维晶格极化子（lattice polaron），发现扩展相互作用（extended interaction）会产生具有偶极对称性等非平庸内部结构的暗杂质态（dark impurity state），从而超越传统的吸引与排斥极化子图像。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 晶格杂质（lattice impurity）为极化子（polaron）揭示自由空间中不存在的量子多体态以及探测强关联物质提供了新平台，但扩展相互作用对晶格极化子准粒子结构的影响尚未被充分理解。

Method: 采用包含最多一个介质激发的变分方法（variational approach），研究具有强在位排斥（on-site repulsion）和可调最近邻相互作用的二维晶格极化子系统。

Result: 扩展相互作用定性改变了准粒子结构，超越了传统的吸引与排斥极化子图像；本征值谱分析揭示了暗杂质态的存在，这些态与本征杂质正交且具有偶极对称性等非平庸实空间内部结构。

Conclusion: 长程相互作用（long-range interaction）会产生具有不同对称性质的多重准粒子激发，凸显了相互作用范围和晶格几何的关键作用，为通过光谱学与波函数分辨测量探测晶格系统中的隐藏准粒子态开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Lattice impurities have recently emerged as a platform in which polarons unveil new quantum many-body states absent in free space and can serve to probe strongly correlated matter. In this work, we investigate two-dimensional lattice polarons with strong on-site repulsion and tunable nearest-neighbor interactions using a variational approach including up to one excitation of the medium. We show that extended interactions qualitatively modify the quasiparticle structure beyond the conventional attractive and repulsive polaron picture. A direct analysis of the eigenvalue spectrum reveals the presence of dark impurity states, orthogonal to the bare impurity and therefore spectroscopically dark. These states exhibit nontrivial internal structure, including dipolar symmetries in real space. Our results demonstrate that long-range interactions generate multiple quasiparticle excitations with distinct symmetry properties, highlighting the crucial role of interaction range and lattice geometry. This work opens new avenues for probing hidden quasiparticle states in lattice systems through spectroscopic and wave-function-resolved measurements.

### [288] [Response of a dipolar BEC to Laguerre-Gaussian beam driven STIRAP](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26094)
*Deepu Singh,Hari Sadhan Ghosh,Arpana Saboo,Soumyadeep Halder,Sonjoy Majumder*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过数值模拟研究STIRAP技术将拉盖尔-高斯光束的轨道角动量相干转移至准二维偶极玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（dipolar BEC）的过程，发现角动量转移效率与涡旋成核取决于偶极BEC的三种相互作用驱动相（超流相、液滴相、超固相），并揭示了磁场取向对超固相中涡旋稳定性的关键调控作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验STIRAP技术在偶极玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（dipolar BEC）中是否有效率地转移拉盖尔-高斯（Laguerre-Gaussian, LG）光束的轨道角动量（orbital angular momentum）并成核量子涡旋（quantized vortex），该问题在常规BEC中已有研究但在偶极凝聚体中尚属开放。

Method: 采用准二维捕获偶极凝聚体模型，使用共传播的高斯（Gaussian）光束和拉盖尔-高斯激光束，通过STIRAP（受激拉曼绝热通道）实现相干光-物质耦合，数值求解偶极BEC的动力学演化。

Result: 在超流相（superfluid）中，STIRAP实现近完全布居转移并成核稳定长寿命量子涡旋；在液滴相（droplet phase）中，涡旋被钉扎于密度分布内，角动量部分保留且呈振荡性，伴随液滴碎裂与重组；在超固相（supersolid）中，当磁场垂直于LG光束传播方向时，调制密度分布与液滴间相干性减弱导致涡旋退定域并被沿磁场方向排出，平均角动量趋于零；将磁极化方向重新沿光束传播方向取向则恢复高效角动量转移并稳定涡旋。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，通过相干光-物质耦合可在偶极玻色气体中实现涡旋态工程与集体激发探测，STIRAP技术为调控不同相区内的涡旋动力学提供了通用途径。

Abstract: Coherent light-matter coupling via STIRAP can offer a versatile route to nucleate quantized vortices in Bose-Einstein condensates, yet its efficacy in dipolar condensates remains an open question. Can the orbital angular momentum of a Laguerre-Gaussian beam be coherently transferred to a dipolar BEC via STIRAP? We investigate this for a quasi-two-dimensional trapped dipolar condensate using co-propagating Gaussian and Laguerre-Gaussian laser beams. The interplay between long-range dipole-dipole interactions and short-range contact interactions enables access to three interaction-driven phases: superfluid, droplet, and supersolid. We find that the amount of angular momentum transferred from the optical field to the dipolar condensate, along with the nucleation and persistence of vortices, depends strongly on the underlying phases of the dipolar BEC. In the superfluid, STIRAP achieves near-complete population transfer and nucleates a stable, long-lived quantized vortex. In the droplet phase, although the vortex remains pinned within the density profile, the angular momentum is partially retained and oscillatory, accompanied by droplet fragmentation and recombination. In the supersolid phase, when the external magnetic field is oriented perpendicular to the LG beam's propagation direction, the emergence of a modulated density distribution along with a slight reduction in inter-droplet coherence leads to vortex delocalization and eventually expels it along the field direction, yielding a vanishing average angular momentum. However, reorienting the magnetic polarization along the beam propagation direction restores efficient angular momentum transfer and stabilizes the vortex within the supersolid phase. Overall, our results demonstrate a versatile route to engineer vortex states and probe collective excitations in dipolar Bose gases via coherent light-matter coupling.

</details>
